010101 The book of the genealogy of Jesus Christ, the son of David, the son of Abraham.
010102 Abraham became the father of Isaac. Isaac became the father of Jacob. Jacob became the father of Judah and his brothers.
010103 Judah became the father of Perez and Zerah by Tamar. Perez became the father of Hezron. Hezron became the father of Ram.
010104 Ram became the father of Amminadab. Amminadab became the father of Nahshon. Nahshon became the father of Salmon.
010105 Salmon became the father of Boaz by Rahab. Boaz became the father of Obed by Ruth. Obed became the father of Jesse.
010106 Jesse became the father of King David. David became the father of Solomon by her who had been the wife of Uriah.
010107 Solomon became the father of Rehoboam. Rehoboam became the father of Abijah. Abijah became the father of Asa.
010108 Asa became the father of Jehoshaphat. Jehoshaphat became the father of Joram. Joram became the father of Uzziah.
010109 Uzziah became the father of Jotham. Jotham became the father of Ahaz. Ahaz became the father of Hezekiah.
010110 Hezekiah became the father of Manasseh. Manasseh became the father of Amon. Amon became the father of Josiah.
010111 Josiah became the father of Jechoniah and his brothers, at the time of the exile to Babylon.
010112 After the exile to Babylon, Jechoniah became the father of Shealtiel. Shealtiel became the father of Zerubbabel.
010113 Zerubbabel became the father of Abiud. Abiud became the father of Eliakim. Eliakim became the father of Azor.
010114 Azor became the father of Sadoc. Sadoc became the father of Achim. Achim became the father of Eliud.
010115 Eliud became the father of Eleazar. Eleazar became the father of Matthan. Matthan became the father of Jacob.
010116 Jacob became the father of Joseph, the husband of Mary, from whom was born Jesus, who is called Christ.
010117 So all the generations from Abraham to David are fourteen generations; from David to the exile to Babylon fourteen generations; and from the carrying away to Babylon to the Christ, fourteen generations.
010118 Now the birth of Jesus Christ was like this; for after his mother, Mary, was engaged to Joseph, before they came together, she was found pregnant by the Holy Spirit.
010119 Joseph, her husband, being a righteous man, and not willing to make her a public example, intended to put her away secretly.
010120 But when he thought about these things, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared to him in a dream, saying, "Joseph, son of David, don't be afraid to take to yourself Mary, your wife, for that which is conceived in her is of the Holy Spirit.
010121 She shall bring forth a son. You shall call his name Jesus, for it is he who shall save his people from their sins."
010122 Now all this has happened, that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the Lord through the prophet, saying,
010123 "Behold, the virgin shall be with child, and shall bring forth a son. They shall call his name Immanuel;" which is, being interpreted, "God with us."
010124 Joseph arose from his sleep, and did as the angel of the Lord commanded him, and took his wife to himself;
010125 and didn't know her sexually until she had brought forth her firstborn son. He named him Jesus.
010201 Now when Jesus was born in Bethlehem of Judea in the days of King Herod, behold, wise men from the east came to Jerusalem, saying,
010202 "Where is he who is born King of the Jews? For we saw his star in the east, and have come to worship him."
010203 When King Herod heard it, he was troubled, and all Jerusalem with him.
010204 Gathering together all the chief priests and scribes of the people, he asked them where the Christ would be born.
010205 They said to him, "In Bethlehem of Judea, for thus it is written through the prophet,
010206 'You Bethlehem, land of Judah, are in no way least among the princes of Judah: for out of you shall come forth a governor, who shall shepherd my people, Israel.'"
010207 Then Herod secretly called the wise men, and learned from them exactly what time the star appeared.
010208 He sent them to Bethlehem, and said, "Go and search diligently for the young child. When you have found him, bring me word, so that I also may come and worship him."
010209 They, having heard the king, went their way; and behold, the star, which they saw in the east, went before them, until it came and stood over where the young child was.
010210 When they saw the star, they rejoiced with exceedingly great joy.
010211 They came into the house and saw the young child with Mary, his mother, and they fell down and worshiped him. Opening their treasures, they offered to him gifts: gold, frankincense, and myrrh.
010212 Being warned in a dream that they shouldn't return to Herod, they went back to their own country another way.
010213 Now when they had departed, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared to Joseph in a dream, saying, "Arise and take the young child and his mother, and flee into Egypt, and stay there until I tell you, for Herod will seek the young child to destroy him."
010214 He arose and took the young child and his mother by night, and departed into Egypt,
010215 and was there until the death of Herod; that it might be fulfilled which was spoken by the Lord through the prophet, saying, "Out of Egypt I called my son."
010216 Then Herod, when he saw that he was mocked by the wise men, was exceedingly angry, and sent out, and killed all the male children who were in Bethlehem and in all the surrounding countryside, from two years old and under, according to the exact time which he had learned from the wise men.
010217 Then that which was spoken by Jeremiah the prophet was fulfilled, saying,
010218 "A voice was heard in Ramah, lamentation, weeping and great mourning, Rachel weeping for her children; she wouldn't be comforted, because they are no more."
010219 But when Herod was dead, behold, an angel of the Lord appeared in a dream to Joseph in Egypt, saying,
010220 "Arise and take the young child and his mother, and go into the land of Israel, for those who sought the young child's life are dead."
010221 He arose and took the young child and his mother, and came into the land of Israel.
010222 But when he heard that Archelaus was reigning over Judea in the place of his father, Herod, he was afraid to go there. Being warned in a dream, he withdrew into the region of Galilee,
010223 and came and lived in a city called Nazareth; that it might be fulfilled which was spoken through the prophets: "He will be called a Nazarene."
010301 In those days, John the Baptizer came, preaching in the wilderness of Judea, saying,
010302 "Repent, for the Kingdom of Heaven is at hand!"
010303 For this is he who was spoken of by Isaiah the prophet, saying, "The voice of one crying in the wilderness, make ready the way of the Lord. Make his paths straight."
010304 Now John himself wore clothing made of camel's hair, with a leather belt around his waist. His food was locusts and wild honey.
010305 Then people from Jerusalem, all of Judea, and all the region around the Jordan went out to him.
010306 They were baptized by him in the Jordan, confessing their sins.
010307 But when he saw many of the Pharisees and Sadducees coming for his baptism, he said to them, "You offspring of vipers, who warned you to flee from the wrath to come?
010308 Therefore bring forth fruit worthy of repentance!
010309 Don't think to yourselves, 'We have Abraham for our father,' for I tell you that God is able to raise up children to Abraham from these stones.
010310 "Even now the axe lies at the root of the trees. Therefore, every tree that doesn't bring forth good fruit is cut down, and cast into the fire.
010311 I indeed baptize you in water for repentance, but he who comes after me is mightier than I, whose shoes I am not worthy to carry. He will baptize you in the Holy Spirit.
010312 His winnowing fork is in his hand, and he will thoroughly cleanse his threshing floor. He will gather his wheat into the barn, but the chaff he will burn up with unquenchable fire."
010313 Then Jesus came from Galilee to the Jordan to John, to be baptized by him.
010314 But John would have hindered him, saying, "I need to be baptized by you, and you come to me?"
010315 But Jesus, answering, said to him, "Allow it now, for this is the fitting way for us to fulfill all righteousness." Then he allowed him.
010316 Jesus, when he was baptized, went up directly from the water: and behold, the heavens were opened to him. He saw the Spirit of God descending as a dove, and coming on him.
010317 Behold, a voice out of the heavens said, "This is my beloved Son, with whom I am well pleased."
010401 Then Jesus was led up by the Spirit into the wilderness to be tempted by the devil.
010402 When he had fasted forty days and forty nights, he was hungry afterward.
010403 The tempter came and said to him, "If you are the Son of God, command that these stones become bread."
010404 But he answered, "It is written, 'Man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word that proceeds out of the mouth of God.'"
010405 Then the devil took him into the holy city. He set him on the pinnacle of the temple,
010406 and said to him, "If you are the Son of God, throw yourself down, for it is written, 'He will put his angels in charge of you.' and, 'On their hands they will bear you up, so that you don't dash your foot against a stone.'"
010407 Jesus said to him, "Again, it is written, 'You shall not test the Lord, your God.'"
010408 Again, the devil took him to an exceedingly high mountain, and showed him all the kingdoms of the world, and their glory.
010409 He said to him, "I will give you all of these things, if you will fall down and worship me."
010410 Then Jesus said to him, "Get behind me, Satan! For it is written, 'You shall worship the Lord your God, and you shall serve him only.'"
010411 Then the devil left him, and behold, angels came and served him.
010412 Now when Jesus heard that John was delivered up, he withdrew into Galilee.
010413 Leaving Nazareth, he came and lived in Capernaum, which is by the sea, in the region of Zebulun and Naphtali,
010414 that it might be fulfilled which was spoken through Isaiah the prophet, saying,
010415 "The land of Zebulun and the land of Naphtali, toward the sea, beyond the Jordan, Galilee of the Gentiles,
010416 the people who sat in darkness saw a great light, to those who sat in the region and shadow of death, to them light has dawned."
010417 From that time, Jesus began to preach, and to say, "Repent! For the Kingdom of Heaven is at hand."
010418 Walking by the sea of Galilee, he saw two brothers: Simon, who is called Peter, and Andrew, his brother, casting a net into the sea; for they were fishermen.
010419 He said to them, "Come after me, and I will make you fishers for men."
010420 They immediately left their nets and followed him.
010421 Going on from there, he saw two other brothers, James the son of Zebedee, and John his brother, in the boat with Zebedee their father, mending their nets. He called them.
010422 They immediately left the boat and their father, and followed him.
010423 Jesus went about in all Galilee, teaching in their synagogues, preaching the Good News of the Kingdom, and healing every disease and every sickness among the people.
010424 The report about him went out into all Syria. They brought to him all who were sick, afflicted with various diseases and torments, possessed with demons, epileptics, and paralytics; and he healed them.
010425 Great multitudes from Galilee, Decapolis, Jerusalem, Judea and from beyond the Jordan followed him.
010501 Seeing the multitudes, he went up onto the mountain. When he had sat down, his disciples came to him.
010502 He opened his mouth and taught them, saying,
010503 "Blessed are the poor in spirit, for theirs is the Kingdom of Heaven.
010504 Blessed are those who mourn, for they shall be comforted.
010505 Blessed are the gentle, for they shall inherit the earth.
010506 Blessed are those who hunger and thirst after righteousness, for they shall be filled.
010507 Blessed are the merciful, for they shall obtain mercy.
010508 Blessed are the pure in heart, for they shall see God.
010509 Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called children of God.
010510 Blessed are those who have been persecuted for righteousness' sake, for theirs is the Kingdom of Heaven.
010511 "Blessed are you when people reproach you, persecute you, and say all kinds of evil against you falsely, for my sake.
010512 Rejoice, and be exceedingly glad, for great is your reward in heaven. For that is how they persecuted the prophets who were before you.
010513 "You are the salt of the earth, but if the salt has lost its flavor, with what will it be salted? It is then good for nothing, but to be cast out and trodden under the feet of men.
010514 You are the light of the world. A city located on a hill can't be hidden.
010515 Neither do you light a lamp, and put it under a measuring basket, but on a stand; and it shines to all who are in the house.
010516 Even so, let your light shine before men; that they may see your good works, and glorify your Father who is in heaven.
010517 "Don't think that I came to destroy the law or the prophets. I didn't come to destroy, but to fulfill.
010518 For most certainly, I tell you, until heaven and earth pass away, not even one smallest letter or one tiny pen stroke shall in any way pass away from the law, until all things are accomplished.
010519 Whoever, therefore, shall break one of these least commandments, and teach others to do so, shall be called least in the Kingdom of Heaven; but whoever shall do and teach them shall be called great in the Kingdom of Heaven.
010520 For I tell you that unless your righteousness exceeds that of the scribes and Pharisees, there is no way you will enter into the Kingdom of Heaven.
010521 "You have heard that it was said to the ancient ones, 'You shall not murder;' and 'Whoever shall murder shall be in danger of the judgment.'
010522 But I tell you, that everyone who is angry with his brother without a cause shall be in danger of the judgment; and whoever shall say to his brother, 'Raca!' shall be in danger of the council; and whoever shall say, 'You fool!' shall be in danger of the fire of Gehenna.
010523 "If therefore you are offering your gift at the altar, and there remember that your brother has anything against you,
010524 leave your gift there before the altar, and go your way. First be reconciled to your brother, and then come and offer your gift.
010525 Agree with your adversary quickly, while you are with him in the way; lest perhaps the prosecutor deliver you to the judge, and the judge deliver you to the officer, and you be cast into prison.
010526 Most certainly I tell you, you shall by no means get out of there, until you have paid the last penny.
010527 "You have heard that it was said,  'You shall not commit adultery;'
010528 but I tell you that everyone who gazes at a woman to lust after her has committed adultery with her already in his heart.
010529 If your right eye causes you to stumble, pluck it out and throw it away from you. For it is more profitable for you that one of your members should perish, than for your whole body to be cast into Gehenna.
010530 If your right hand causes you to stumble, cut it off, and throw it away from you. For it is more profitable for you that one of your members should perish, than for your whole body to be cast into Gehenna.
010531 "It was also said, 'Whoever shall put away his wife, let him give her a writing of divorce,'
010532 but I tell you that whoever puts away his wife, except for the cause of sexual immorality, makes her an adulteress; and whoever marries her when she is put away commits adultery.
010533 "Again you have heard that it was said to them of old time, 'You shall not make false vows, but shall perform to the Lord your vows,'
010534 but I tell you, don't swear at all: neither by heaven, for it is the throne of God;
010535 nor by the earth, for it is the footstool of his feet; nor by Jerusalem, for it is the city of the great King.
010536 Neither shall you swear by your head, for you can't make one hair white or black.
010537 But let your 'Yes' be 'Yes' and your 'No' be 'No.' Whatever is more than these is of the evil one.
010538 "You have heard that it was said, 'An eye for an eye, and a tooth for a tooth.'
010539 But I tell you, don't resist him who is evil; but whoever strikes you on your right cheek, turn to him the other also.
010540 If anyone sues you to take away your coat, let him have your cloak also.
010541 Whoever compels you to go one mile, go with him two.
010542 Give to him who asks you, and don't turn away him who desires to borrow from you.
010543 "You have heard that it was said, 'You shall love your neighbor, and hate your enemy.'
010544 But I tell you, love your enemies, bless those who curse you, do good to those who hate you, and pray for those who mistreat you and persecute you,
010545 that you may be children of your Father who is in heaven. For he makes his sun to rise on the evil and the good, and sends rain on the just and the unjust.
010546 For if you love those who love you, what reward do you have? Don't even the tax collectors do the same?
010547 If you only greet your friends, what more do you do than others? Don't even the tax collectors do the same?
010548 Therefore you shall be perfect, just as your Father in heaven is perfect.
010601 "Be careful that you don't do your charitable giving before men, to be seen by them, or else you have no reward from your Father who is in heaven.
010602 Therefore when you do merciful deeds, don't sound a trumpet before yourself, as the hypocrites do in the synagogues and in the streets, that they may get glory from men. Most certainly I tell you, they have received their reward.
010603 But when you do merciful deeds, don't let your left hand know what your right hand does,
010604 so that your merciful deeds may be in secret, then your Father who sees in secret will reward you openly.
010605 "When you pray, you shall not be as the hypocrites, for they love to stand and pray in the synagogues and in the corners of the streets, that they may be seen by men. Most certainly, I tell you, they have received their reward.
010606 But you, when you pray, enter into your inner chamber, and having shut your door, pray to your Father who is in secret, and your Father who sees in secret will reward you openly.
010607 In praying, don't use vain repetitions, as the Gentiles do; for they think that they will be heard for their much speaking.
010608 Therefore don't be like them, for your Father knows what things you need, before you ask him.
010609 Pray like this: 'Our Father in heaven, may your name be kept holy.
010610 Let your Kingdom come. Let your will be done, as in heaven, so on earth.
010611 Give us today our daily bread.
010612 Forgive us our debts, as we also forgive our debtors.
010613 Bring us not into temptation, but deliver us from the evil one. For yours is the Kingdom, the power, and the glory forever. Amen.'
010614 "For if you forgive men their trespasses, your heavenly Father will also forgive you.
010615 But if you don't forgive men their trespasses, neither will your Father forgive your trespasses.
010616 "Moreover when you fast, don't be like the hypocrites, with sad faces. For they disfigure their faces, that they may be seen by men to be fasting. Most certainly I tell you, they have received their reward.
010617 But you, when you fast, anoint your head, and wash your face;
010618 so that you are not seen by men to be fasting, but by your Father who is in secret, and your Father, who sees in secret, will reward you.
010619 "Don't lay up treasures for yourselves on the earth, where moth and rust consume, and where thieves break through and steal;
010620 but lay up for yourselves treasures in heaven, where neither moth nor rust consume, and where thieves don't break through and steal;
010621 for where your treasure is, there your heart will be also.
010622 "The lamp of the body is the eye. If therefore your eye is sound, your whole body will be full of light.
010623 But if your eye is evil, your whole body will be full of darkness. If therefore the light that is in you is darkness, how great is the darkness!
010624 "No one can serve two masters, for either he will hate the one and love the other; or else he will be devoted to one and despise the other. You can't serve both God and Mammon.
010625 Therefore, I tell you, don't be anxious for your life: what you will eat, or what you will drink; nor yet for your body, what you will wear. Isn't life more than food, and the body more than clothing?
010626 See the birds of the sky, that they don't sow, neither do they reap, nor gather into barns. Your heavenly Father feeds them. Aren't you of much more value than they?
010627 "Which of you, by being anxious, can add one moment to his lifespan?
010628 Why are you anxious about clothing? Consider the lilies of the field, how they grow. They don't toil, neither do they spin,
010629 yet I tell you that even Solomon in all his glory was not dressed like one of these.
010630 But if God so clothes the grass of the field, which today exists, and tomorrow is thrown into the oven, won't he much more clothe you, you of little faith?
010631 "Therefore don't be anxious, saying, 'What will we eat?', 'What will we drink?' or, 'With what will we be clothed?'
010632 For the Gentiles seek after all these things, for your heavenly Father knows that you need all these things.
010633 But seek first God's Kingdom, and his righteousness; and all these things will be given to you as well.
010634 Therefore don't be anxious for tomorrow, for tomorrow will be anxious for itself. Each day's own evil is sufficient.
010701 "Don't judge, so that you won't be judged.
010702 For with whatever judgment you judge, you will be judged; and with whatever measure you measure, it will be measured to you.
010703 Why do you see the speck that is in your brother's eye, but don't consider the beam that is in your own eye?
010704 Or how will you tell your brother, 'Let me remove the speck from your eye;' and behold, the beam is in your own eye?
010705 You hypocrite! First remove the beam out of your own eye, and then you can see clearly to remove the speck out of your brother's eye.
010706 "Don't give that which is holy to the dogs, neither throw your pearls before the pigs, lest perhaps they trample them under their feet, and turn and tear you to pieces.
010707 "Ask, and it will be given you. Seek, and you will find. Knock, and it will be opened for you.
010708 For everyone who asks receives. He who seeks finds. To him who knocks it will be opened.
010709 Or who is there among you, who, if his son asks him for bread, will give him a stone?
010710 Or if he asks for a fish, who will give him a serpent?
010711 If you then, being evil, know how to give good gifts to your children, how much more will your Father who is in heaven give good things to those who ask him!
010712 Therefore whatever you desire for men to do to you, you shall also do to them; for this is the law and the prophets.
010713 "Enter in by the narrow gate; for wide is the gate and broad is the way that leads to destruction, and many are those who enter in by it.
010714 How narrow is the gate, and restricted is the way that leads to life! Few are those who find it.
010715 "Beware of false prophets, who come to you in sheep's clothing, but inwardly are ravening wolves.
010716 By their fruits you will know them. Do you gather grapes from thorns, or figs from thistles?
010717 Even so, every good tree produces good fruit; but the corrupt tree produces evil fruit.
010718 A good tree can't produce evil fruit, neither can a corrupt tree produce good fruit.
010719 Every tree that doesn't grow good fruit is cut down, and thrown into the fire.
010720 Therefore, by their fruits you will know them.
010721 Not everyone who says to me, 'Lord, Lord,' will enter into the Kingdom of Heaven; but he who does the will of my Father who is in heaven.
010722 Many will tell me in that day, 'Lord, Lord, didn't we prophesy in your name, in your name cast out demons, and in your name do many mighty works?'
010723 Then I will tell them, 'I never knew you. Depart from me, you who work iniquity.'
010724 "Everyone therefore who hears these words of mine, and does them, I will liken him to a wise man, who built his house on a rock.
010725 The rain came down, the floods came, and the winds blew, and beat on that house; and it didn't fall, for it was founded on the rock.
010726 Everyone who hears these words of mine, and doesn't do them will be like a foolish man, who built his house on the sand.
010727 The rain came down, the floods came, and the winds blew, and beat on that house; and it fell--and great was its fall."
010728 It happened, when Jesus had finished saying these things, that the multitudes were astonished at his teaching,
010729 for he taught them with authority, and not like the scribes.
010801 When he came down from the mountain, great multitudes followed him.
010802 Behold, a leper came to him and worshiped him, saying, "Lord, if you want to, you can make me clean."
010803 Jesus stretched out his hand, and touched him, saying, "I want to. Be made clean." Immediately his leprosy was cleansed.
010804 Jesus said to him, "See that you tell nobody, but go, show yourself to the priest, and offer the gift that Moses commanded, as a testimony to them."
010805 When he came into Capernaum, a centurion came to him, asking him,
010806 and saying, "Lord, my servant lies in the house paralyzed, grievously tormented."
010807 Jesus said to him, "I will come and heal him."
010808 The centurion answered, "Lord, I'm not worthy for you to come under my roof. Just say the word, and my servant will be healed.
010809 For I am also a man under authority, having under myself soldiers. I tell this one, 'Go,' and he goes; and tell another, 'Come,' and he comes; and tell my servant, 'Do this,' and he does it."
010810 When Jesus heard it, he marveled, and said to those who followed, "Most certainly I tell you, I haven't found so great a faith, not even in Israel.
010811 I tell you that many will come from the east and the west, and will sit down with Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob in the Kingdom of Heaven,
010812 but the children of the Kingdom will be thrown out into the outer darkness. There will be weeping and gnashing of teeth."
010813 Jesus said to the centurion, "Go your way. Let it be done for you as you have believed." His servant was healed in that hour.
010814 When Jesus came into Peter's house, he saw his wife's mother lying sick with a fever.
010815 He touched her hand, and the fever left her. She got up and served him.
010816 When evening came, they brought to him many possessed with demons. He cast out the spirits with a word, and healed all who were sick;
010817 that it might be fulfilled which was spoken through Isaiah the prophet, saying: "He took our infirmities, and bore our diseases."
010818 Now when Jesus saw great multitudes around him, he gave the order to depart to the other side.
010819 A scribe came, and said to him, "Teacher, I will follow you wherever you go."
010820 Jesus said to him, "The foxes have holes, and the birds of the sky have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay his head."
010821 Another of his disciples said to him, "Lord, allow me first to go and bury my father."
010822 But Jesus said to him, "Follow me, and leave the dead to bury their own dead."
010823 When he got into a boat, his disciples followed him.
010824 Behold, a violent storm came up on the sea, so much that the boat was covered with the waves, but he was asleep.
010825 They came to him, and woke him up, saying, "Save us, Lord! We are dying!"
010826 He said to them, "Why are you fearful, O you of little faith?" Then he got up, rebuked the wind and the sea, and there was a great calm.
010827 The men marveled, saying, "What kind of man is this, that even the wind and the sea obey him?"
010828 When he came to the other side, into the country of the Gergesenes, two people possessed by demons met him there, coming out of the tombs, exceedingly fierce, so that nobody could pass that way.
010829 Behold, they cried out, saying, "What do we have to do with you, Jesus, Son of God? Have you come here to torment us before the time?"
010830 Now there was a herd of many pigs feeding far away from them.
010831 The demons begged him, saying, "If you cast us out, permit us to go away into the herd of pigs."
010832 He said to them, "Go!" They came out, and went into the herd of pigs: and behold, the whole herd of pigs rushed down the cliff into the sea, and died in the water.
010833 Those who fed them fled, and went away into the city, and told everything, including what happened to those who were possessed with demons.
010834 Behold, all the city came out to meet Jesus. When they saw him, they begged that he would depart from their borders.
010901 He entered into a boat, and crossed over, and came into his own city.
010902 Behold, they brought to him a man who was paralyzed, lying on a bed. Jesus, seeing their faith, said to the paralytic, "Son, cheer up! Your sins are forgiven you."
010903 Behold, some of the scribes said to themselves, "This man blasphemes."
010904 Jesus, knowing their thoughts, said, "Why do you think evil in your hearts?
010905 For which is easier, to say, 'Your sins are forgiven;' or to say, 'Get up, and walk?'
010906 But that you may know that the Son of Man has authority on earth to forgive sins..." (then he said to the paralytic), "Get up, and take up your mat, and go up to your house."
010907 He arose and departed to his house.
010908 But when the multitudes saw it, they marveled and glorified God, who had given such authority to men.
010909 As Jesus passed by from there, he saw a man called Matthew sitting at the tax collection office. He said to him, "Follow me." He got up and followed him.
010910 It happened as he sat in the house, behold, many tax collectors and sinners came and sat down with Jesus and his disciples.
010911 When the Pharisees saw it, they said to his disciples, "Why does your teacher eat with tax collectors and sinners?"
010912 When Jesus heard it, he said to them, "Those who are healthy have no need for a physician, but those who are sick do.
010913 But you go and learn what this means: 'I desire mercy, and not sacrifice,' for I came not to call the righteous, but sinners to repentance."
010914 Then John's disciples came to him, saying, "Why do we and the Pharisees fast often, but your disciples don't fast?"
010915 Jesus said to them, "Can the friends of the bridegroom mourn, as long as the bridegroom is with them? But the days will come when the bridegroom will be taken away from them, and then they will fast.
010916 No one puts a piece of unshrunk cloth on an old garment; for the patch would tear away from the garment, and a worse hole is made.
010917 Neither do people put new wine into old wineskins, or else the skins would burst, and the wine be spilled, and the skins ruined. No, they put new wine into fresh wineskins, and both are preserved."
010918 While he told these things to them, behold, a ruler came and worshiped him, saying, "My daughter has just died, but come and lay your hand on her, and she will live."
010919 Jesus got up and followed him, as did his disciples.
010920 Behold, a woman who had an issue of blood for twelve years came behind him, and touched the fringe of his garment;
010921 for she said within herself, "If I just touch his garment, I will be made well."
010922 But Jesus, turning around and seeing her, said, "Daughter, cheer up! Your faith has made you well." And the woman was made well from that hour.
010923 When Jesus came into the ruler's house, and saw the flute players, and the crowd in noisy disorder,
010924 he said to them, "Make room, because the girl isn't dead, but sleeping." They were ridiculing him.
010925 But when the crowd was put out, he entered in, took her by the hand, and the girl arose.
010926 The report of this went out into all that land.
010927 As Jesus passed by from there, two blind men followed him, calling out and saying, "Have mercy on us, son of David!"
010928 When he had come into the house, the blind men came to him. Jesus said to them, "Do you believe that I am able to do this?" They told him, "Yes, Lord."
010929 Then he touched their eyes, saying, "According to your faith be it done to you."
010930 Their eyes were opened. Jesus strictly commanded them, saying, "See that no one knows about this."
010931 But they went out and spread abroad his fame in all that land.
010932 As they went out, behold, a mute man who was demon possessed was brought to him.
010933 When the demon was cast out, the mute man spoke. The multitudes marveled, saying, "Nothing like this has ever been seen in Israel!"
010934 But the Pharisees said, "By the prince of the demons, he casts out demons."
010935 Jesus went about all the cities and the villages, teaching in their synagogues, and preaching the Good News of the Kingdom, and healing every disease and every sickness among the people.
010936 But when he saw the multitudes, he was moved with compassion for them, because they were harassed and scattered, like sheep without a shepherd.
010937 Then he said to his disciples, "The harvest indeed is plentiful, but the laborers are few.
010938 Pray therefore that the Lord of the harvest will send out laborers into his harvest."
011001 He called to himself his twelve disciples, and gave them authority over unclean spirits, to cast them out, and to heal every disease and every sickness.
011002 Now the names of the twelve apostles are these. The first, Simon, who is called Peter; Andrew, his brother; James the son of Zebedee; John, his brother;
011003 Philip; Bartholomew; Thomas; Matthew the tax collector; James the son of Alphaeus; Lebbaeus, whose surname was Thaddaeus;
011004 Simon the Canaanite; and Judas Iscariot, who also betrayed him.
011005 Jesus sent these twelve out, and commanded them, saying, "Don't go among the Gentiles, and don't enter into any city of the Samaritans.
011006 Rather, go to the lost sheep of the house of Israel.
011007 As you go, preach, saying, 'The Kingdom of Heaven is at hand!'
011008 Heal the sick, cleanse the lepers, and cast out demons. Freely you received, so freely give.
011009 Don't take any gold, nor silver, nor brass in your money belts.
011010 Take no bag for your journey, neither two coats, nor shoes, nor staff: for the laborer is worthy of his food.
011011 Into whatever city or village you enter, find out who in it is worthy; and stay there until you go on.
011012 As you enter into the household, greet it.
011013 If the household is worthy, let your peace come on it, but if it isn't worthy, let your peace return to you.
011014 Whoever doesn't receive you, nor hear your words, as you go out of that house or that city, shake off the dust from your feet.
011015 Most certainly I tell you, it will be more tolerable for the land of Sodom and Gomorrah in the day of judgment than for that city.
011016 "Behold, I send you out as sheep in the midst of wolves. Therefore be wise as serpents, and harmless as doves.
011017 But beware of men: for they will deliver you up to councils, and in their synagogues they will scourge you.
011018 Yes, and you will be brought before governors and kings for my sake, for a testimony to them and to the nations.
011019 But when they deliver you up, don't be anxious how or what you will say, for it will be given you in that hour what you will say.
011020 For it is not you who speak, but the Spirit of your Father who speaks in you.
011021 "Brother will deliver up brother to death, and the father his child. Children will rise up against parents, and cause them to be put to death.
011022 You will be hated by all men for my name's sake, but he who endures to the end will be saved.
011023 But when they persecute you in this city, flee into the next, for most certainly I tell you, you will not have gone through the cities of Israel, until the Son of Man has come.
011024 "A disciple is not above his teacher, nor a servant above his lord.
011025 It is enough for the disciple that he be like his teacher, and the servant like his lord. If they have called the master of the house Beelzebul, how much more those of his household!
011026 Therefore don't be afraid of them, for there is nothing covered that will not be revealed; and hidden that will not be known.
011027 What I tell you in the darkness, speak in the light; and what you hear whispered in the ear, proclaim on the housetops.
011028 Don't be afraid of those who kill the body, but are not able to kill the soul. Rather, fear him who is able to destroy both soul and body in Gehenna.
011029 "Aren't two sparrows sold for an assarion coin? Not one of them falls on the ground apart from your Father's will,
011030 but the very hairs of your head are all numbered.
011031 Therefore don't be afraid. You are of more value than many sparrows.
011032 Everyone therefore who confesses me before men, him I will also confess before my Father who is in heaven.
011033 But whoever denies me before men, him I will also deny before my Father who is in heaven.
011034 "Don't think that I came to send peace on the earth. I didn't come to send peace, but a sword.
011035 For I came to set a man at odds against his father, and a daughter against her mother, and a daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law.
011036 A man's foes will be those of his own household.
011037 He who loves father or mother more than me is not worthy of me; and he who loves son or daughter more than me isn't worthy of me.
011038 He who doesn't take his cross and follow after me, isn't worthy of me.
011039 He who seeks his life will lose it; and he who loses his life for my sake will find it.
011040 He who receives you receives me, and he who receives me receives him who sent me.
011041 He who receives a prophet in the name of a prophet will receive a prophet's reward. He who receives a righteous man in the name of a righteous man will receive a righteous man's reward.
011042 Whoever gives one of these little ones just a cup of cold water to drink in the name of a disciple, most certainly I tell you he will in no way lose his reward."
011101 It happened that when Jesus had finished directing his twelve disciples, he departed from there to teach and preach in their cities.
011102 Now when John heard in the prison the works of Christ, he sent two of his disciples
011103 and said to him, "Are you he who comes, or should we look for another?"
011104 Jesus answered them, "Go and tell John the things which you hear and see:
011105 the blind receive their sight, the lame walk, the lepers are cleansed, the deaf hear, the dead are raised up, and the poor have good news preached to them.
011106 Blessed is he who finds no occasion for stumbling in me."
011107 As these went their way, Jesus began to say to the multitudes concerning John, "What did you go out into the wilderness to see? A reed shaken by the wind?
011108 But what did you go out to see? A man in soft clothing? Behold, those who wear soft clothing are in king's houses.
011109 But why did you go out? To see a prophet? Yes, I tell you, and much more than a prophet.
011110 For this is he, of whom it is written, 'Behold, I send my messenger before your face, who will prepare your way before you.'
011111 Most certainly I tell you, among those who are born of women there has not arisen anyone greater than John the Baptizer; yet he who is least in the Kingdom of Heaven is greater than he.
011112 From the days of John the Baptizer until now, the Kingdom of Heaven suffers violence, and the violent take it by force.
011113 For all the prophets and the law prophesied until John.
011114 If you are willing to receive it, this is Elijah, who is to come.
011115 He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
011116 "But to what shall I compare this generation? It is like children sitting in the marketplaces, who call to their companions
011117 and say, 'We played the flute for you, and you didn't dance. We mourned for you, and you didn't lament.'
011118 For John came neither eating nor drinking, and they say, 'He has a demon.'
011119 The Son of Man came eating and drinking, and they say, 'Behold, a gluttonous man and a drunkard, a friend of tax collectors and sinners!' But wisdom is justified by her children."
011120 Then he began to denounce the cities in which most of his mighty works had been done, because they didn't repent.
011121 "Woe to you, Chorazin! Woe to you, Bethsaida! For if the mighty works had been done in Tyre and Sidon which were done in you, they would have repented long ago in sackcloth and ashes.
011122 But I tell you, it will be more tolerable for Tyre and Sidon on the day of judgment than for you.
011123 You, Capernaum, who are exalted to heaven, you will go down to Hades. For if the mighty works had been done in Sodom which were done in you, it would have remained until this day.
011124 But I tell you that it will be more tolerable for the land of Sodom, on the day of judgment, than for you."
011125 At that time, Jesus answered, "I thank you, Father, Lord of heaven and earth, that you hid these things from the wise and understanding, and revealed them to infants.
011126 Yes, Father, for so it was well-pleasing in your sight.
011127 All things have been delivered to me by my Father. No one knows the Son, except the Father; neither does anyone know the Father, except the Son, and he to whom the Son desires to reveal him.
011128 "Come to me, all you who labor and are heavily burdened, and I will give you rest.
011129 Take my yoke upon you, and learn from me, for I am gentle and lowly in heart; and you will find rest for your souls.
011130 For my yoke is easy, and my burden is light."
011201 At that time, Jesus went on the Sabbath day through the grain fields. His disciples were hungry and began to pluck heads of grain and to eat.
011202 But the Pharisees, when they saw it, said to him, "Behold, your disciples do what is not lawful to do on the Sabbath."
011203 But he said to them, "Haven't you read what David did, when he was hungry, and those who were with him;
011204 how he entered into the house of God, and ate the show bread, which was not lawful for him to eat, neither for those who were with him, but only for the priests?
011205 Or have you not read in the law, that on the Sabbath day, the priests in the temple profane the Sabbath, and are guiltless?
011206 But I tell you that one greater than the temple is here.
011207 But if you had known what this means, 'I desire mercy, and not sacrifice,' you would not have condemned the guiltless.
011208 For the Son of Man is Lord of the Sabbath."
011209 He departed there, and went into their synagogue.
011210 And behold there was a man with a withered hand. They asked him, "Is it lawful to heal on the Sabbath day?" that they might accuse him.
011211 He said to them, "What man is there among you, who has one sheep, and if this one falls into a pit on the Sabbath day, won't he grab on to it, and lift it out?
011212 Of how much more value then is a man than a sheep! Therefore it is lawful to do good on the Sabbath day."
011213 Then he told the man, "Stretch out your hand." He stretched it out; and it was restored whole, just like the other.
011214 But the Pharisees went out, and conspired against him, how they might destroy him.
011215 Jesus, perceiving that, withdrew from there. Great multitudes followed him; and he healed them all,
011216 and commanded them that they should not make him known:
011217 that it might be fulfilled which was spoken through Isaiah the prophet, saying,
011218 "Behold, my servant whom I have chosen; my beloved in whom my soul is well pleased: I will put my Spirit on him. He will proclaim justice to the nations.
011219 He will not strive, nor shout; neither will anyone hear his voice in the streets.
011220 He won't break a bruised reed. He won't quench a smoking flax, until he leads justice to victory.
011221 In his name, the nations will hope."
011222 Then one possessed by a demon, blind and mute, was brought to him and he healed him, so that the blind and mute man both spoke and saw.
011223 All the multitudes were amazed, and said, "Can this be the son of David?"
011224 But when the Pharisees heard it, they said, "This man does not cast out demons, except by Beelzebul, the prince of the demons."
011225 Knowing their thoughts, Jesus said to them, "Every kingdom divided against itself is brought to desolation, and every city or house divided against itself will not stand.
011226 If Satan casts out Satan, he is divided against himself. How then will his kingdom stand?
011227 If I by Beelzebul cast out demons, by whom do your children cast them out? Therefore they will be your judges.
011228 But if I by the Spirit of God cast out demons, then the Kingdom of God has come upon you.
011229 Or how can one enter into the house of the strong man, and plunder his goods, unless he first bind the strong man? Then he will plunder his house.
011230 "He who is not with me is against me, and he who doesn't gather with me, scatters.
011231 Therefore I tell you, every sin and blasphemy will be forgiven men, but the blasphemy against the Spirit will not be forgiven men.
011232 Whoever speaks a word against the Son of Man, it will be forgiven him; but whoever speaks against the Holy Spirit, it will not be forgiven him, neither in this age, nor in that which is to come.
011233 "Either make the tree good, and its fruit good, or make the tree corrupt, and its fruit corrupt; for the tree is known by its fruit.
011234 You offspring of vipers, how can you, being evil, speak good things? For out of the abundance of the heart, the mouth speaks.
011235 The good man out of his good treasure brings out good things, and the evil man out of his evil treasure brings out evil things.
011236 I tell you that every idle word that men speak, they will give account of it in the day of judgment.
011237 For by your words you will be justified, and by your words you will be condemned."
011238 Then certain of the scribes and Pharisees answered, "Teacher, we want to see a sign from you."
011239 But he answered them, "An evil and adulterous generation seeks after a sign, but no sign will be given it but the sign of Jonah the prophet.
011240 For as Jonah was three days and three nights in the belly of the whale, so will the Son of Man be three days and three nights in the heart of the earth.
011241 The men of Nineveh will stand up in the judgment with this generation, and will condemn it, for they repented at the preaching of Jonah; and behold, someone greater than Jonah is here.
011242 The queen of the south will rise up in the judgment with this generation, and will condemn it, for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon; and behold, someone greater than Solomon is here.
011243 But the unclean spirit, when he is gone out of the man, passes through waterless places, seeking rest, and doesn't find it.
011244 Then he says, 'I will return into my house from which I came out,' and when he has come back, he finds it empty, swept, and put in order.
011245 Then he goes, and takes with himself seven other spirits more evil than he is, and they enter in and dwell there. The last state of that man becomes worse than the first. Even so will it be also to this evil generation."
011246 While he was yet speaking to the multitudes, behold, his mother and his brothers stood outside, seeking to speak to him.
011247 One said to him, "Behold, your mother and your brothers stand outside, seeking to speak to you."
011248 But he answered him who spoke to him, "Who is my mother? Who are my brothers?"
011249 He stretched out his hand towards his disciples, and said, "Behold, my mother and my brothers!
011250 For whoever does the will of my Father who is in heaven, he is my brother, and sister, and mother."
011301 On that day Jesus went out of the house, and sat by the seaside.
011302 Great multitudes gathered to him, so that he entered into a boat, and sat, and all the multitude stood on the beach.
011303 He spoke to them many things in parables, saying, "Behold, a farmer went out to sow.
011304 As he sowed, some seeds fell by the roadside, and the birds came and devoured them.
011305 Others fell on rocky ground, where they didn't have much soil, and immediately they sprang up, because they had no depth of earth.
011306 When the sun had risen, they were scorched. Because they had no root, they withered away.
011307 Others fell among thorns. The thorns grew up and choked them.
011308 Others fell on good soil, and yielded fruit: some one hundred times as much, some sixty, and some thirty.
011309 He who has ears to hear, let him hear."
011310 The disciples came, and said to him, "Why do you speak to them in parables?"
011311 He answered them, "To you it is given to know the mysteries of the Kingdom of Heaven, but it is not given to them.
011312 For whoever has, to him will be given, and he will have abundance, but whoever doesn't have, from him will be taken away even that which he has.
011313 Therefore I speak to them in parables, because seeing they don't see, and hearing, they don't hear, neither do they understand.
011314 In them the prophecy of Isaiah is fulfilled, which says, 'By hearing you will hear, and will in no way understand; Seeing you will see, and will in no way perceive:
011315 for this people's heart has grown callous, their ears are dull of hearing, they have closed their eyes; or else perhaps they might perceive with their eyes, hear with their ears, understand with their heart, and should turn again; and I would heal them.'
011316 "But blessed are your eyes, for they see; and your ears, for they hear.
011317 For most certainly I tell you that many prophets and righteous men desired to see the things which you see, and didn't see them; and to hear the things which you hear, and didn't hear them.
011318 "Hear, then, the parable of the farmer.
011319 When anyone hears the word of the Kingdom, and doesn't understand it, the evil one comes, and snatches away that which has been sown in his heart. This is what was sown by the roadside.
011320 What was sown on the rocky places, this is he who hears the word, and immediately with joy receives it;
011321 yet he has no root in himself, but endures for a while. When oppression or persecution arises because of the word, immediately he stumbles.
011322 What was sown among the thorns, this is he who hears the word, but the cares of this age and the deceitfulness of riches choke the word, and he becomes unfruitful.
011323 What was sown on the good ground, this is he who hears the word, and understands it, who most certainly bears fruit, and brings forth, some one hundred times as much, some sixty, and some thirty."
011324 He set another parable before them, saying, "The Kingdom of Heaven is like a man who sowed good seed in his field,
011325 but while people slept, his enemy came and sowed darnel weeds also among the wheat, and went away.
011326 But when the blade sprang up and brought forth fruit, then the darnel weeds appeared also.
011327 The servants of the householder came and said to him, 'Sir, didn't you sow good seed in your field? Where did this darnel come from?'
011328 "He said to them, 'An enemy has done this.' "The servants asked him, 'Do you want us to go and gather them up?'
011329 "But he said, 'No, lest perhaps while you gather up the darnel weeds, you root up the wheat with them.
011330 Let both grow together until the harvest, and in the harvest time I will tell the reapers, "First, gather up the darnel weeds, and bind them in bundles to burn them; but gather the wheat into my barn."'"
011331 He set another parable before them, saying, "The Kingdom of Heaven is like a grain of mustard seed, which a man took, and sowed in his field;
011332 which indeed is smaller than all seeds. But when it is grown, it is greater than the herbs, and becomes a tree, so that the birds of the air come and lodge in its branches."
011333 He spoke another parable to them. "The Kingdom of Heaven is like yeast, which a woman took, and hid in three measures of meal, until it was all leavened."
011334 Jesus spoke all these things in parables to the multitudes; and without a parable, he didn't speak to them,
011335 that it might be fulfilled which was spoken through the prophet, saying, "I will open my mouth in parables; I will utter things hidden from the foundation of the world."
011336 Then Jesus sent the multitudes away, and went into the house. His disciples came to him, saying, "Explain to us the parable of the darnel weeds of the field."
011337 He answered them, "He who sows the good seed is the Son of Man,
011338 the field is the world; and the good seed, these are the children of the Kingdom; and the darnel weeds are the children of the evil one.
011339 The enemy who sowed them is the devil. The harvest is the end of the age, and the reapers are angels.
011340 As therefore the darnel weeds are gathered up and burned with fire; so will it be at the end of this age.
011341 The Son of Man will send out his angels, and they will gather out of his Kingdom all things that cause stumbling, and those who do iniquity,
011342 and will cast them into the furnace of fire. There will be weeping and the gnashing of teeth.
011343 Then the righteous will shine forth like the sun in the Kingdom of their Father. He who has ears to hear, let him hear.
011344 "Again, the Kingdom of Heaven is like a treasure hidden in the field, which a man found, and hid. In his joy, he goes and sells all that he has, and buys that field.
011345 "Again, the Kingdom of Heaven is like a man who is a merchant seeking fine pearls,
011346 who having found one pearl of great price, he went and sold all that he had, and bought it.
011347 "Again, the Kingdom of Heaven is like a dragnet, that was cast into the sea, and gathered some fish of every kind,
011348 which, when it was filled, they drew up on the beach. They sat down, and gathered the good into containers, but the bad they threw away.
011349 So will it be in the end of the world. The angels will come forth, and separate the wicked from among the righteous,
011350 and will cast them into the furnace of fire. There will be the weeping and the gnashing of teeth."
011351 Jesus said to them, "Have you understood all these things?" They answered him, "Yes, Lord."
011352 He said to them, "Therefore, every scribe who has been made a disciple in the Kingdom of Heaven is like a man who is a householder, who brings out of his treasure new and old things."
011353 It happened that when Jesus had finished these parables, he departed from there.
011354 Coming into his own country, he taught them in their synagogue, so that they were astonished, and said, "Where did this man get this wisdom, and these mighty works?
011355 Isn't this the carpenter's son? Isn't his mother called Mary, and his brothers, James, Joses, Simon, and Judas?
011356 Aren't all of his sisters with us? Where then did this man get all of these things?"
011357 They were offended by him. But Jesus said to them, "A prophet is not without honor, except in his own country, and in his own house."
011358 He didn't do many mighty works there because of their unbelief.
011401 At that time, Herod the tetrarch heard the report concerning Jesus,
011402 and said to his servants, "This is John the Baptizer. He is risen from the dead. That is why these powers work in him."
011403 For Herod had laid hold of John, and bound him, and put him in prison for the sake of Herodias, his brother Philip's wife.
011404 For John said to him, "It is not lawful for you to have her."
011405 When he would have put him to death, he feared the multitude, because they counted him as a prophet.
011406 But when Herod's birthday came, the daughter of Herodias danced among them and pleased Herod.
011407 Whereupon he promised with an oath to give her whatever she should ask.
011408 She, being prompted by her mother, said, "Give me here on a platter the head of John the Baptizer."
011409 The king was grieved, but for the sake of his oaths, and of those who sat at the table with him, he commanded it to be given,
011410 and he sent and beheaded John in the prison.
011411 His head was brought on a platter, and given to the young lady: and she brought it to her mother.
011412 His disciples came, and took the body, and buried it; and they went and told Jesus.
011413 Now when Jesus heard this, he withdrew from there in a boat, to a deserted place apart. When the multitudes heard it, they followed him on foot from the cities.
011414 Jesus went out, and he saw a great multitude. He had compassion on them, and healed their sick.
011415 When evening had come, his disciples came to him, saying, "This place is deserted, and the hour is already late. Send the multitudes away, that they may go into the villages, and buy themselves food."
011416 But Jesus said to them, "They don't need to go away. You give them something to eat."
011417 They told him, "We only have here five loaves and two fish."
011418 He said, "Bring them here to me."
011419 He commanded the multitudes to sit down on the grass; and he took the five loaves and the two fish, and looking up to heaven, he blessed, broke and gave the loaves to the disciples, and the disciples gave to the multitudes.
011420 They all ate, and were filled. They took up twelve baskets full of that which remained left over from the broken pieces.
011421 Those who ate were about five thousand men, besides women and children.
011422 Immediately Jesus made the disciples get into the boat, and to go ahead of him to the other side, while he sent the multitudes away.
011423 After he had sent the multitudes away, he went up into the mountain by himself to pray. When evening had come, he was there alone.
011424 But the boat was now in the middle of the sea, distressed by the waves, for the wind was contrary.
011425 In the fourth watch of the night, Jesus came to them, walking on the sea.
011426 When the disciples saw him walking on the sea, they were troubled, saying, "It's a ghost!" and they cried out for fear.
011427 But immediately Jesus spoke to them, saying "Cheer up! It is I! Don't be afraid."
011428 Peter answered him and said, "Lord, if it is you, command me to come to you on the waters."
011429 He said, "Come!" Peter stepped down from the boat, and walked on the waters to come to Jesus.
011430 But when he saw that the wind was strong, he was afraid, and beginning to sink, he cried out, saying, "Lord, save me!"
011431 Immediately Jesus stretched out his hand, took hold of him, and said to him, "You of little faith, why did you doubt?"
011432 When they got up into the boat, the wind ceased.
011433 Those who were in the boat came and worshiped him, saying, "You are truly the Son of God!"
011434 When they had crossed over, they came to the land of Gennesaret.
011435 When the people of that place recognized him, they sent into all that surrounding region, and brought to him all who were sick,
011436 and they begged him that they might just touch the fringe of his garment. As many as touched it were made whole.
011501 Then Pharisees and scribes came to Jesus from Jerusalem, saying,
011502 "Why do your disciples disobey the tradition of the elders? For they don't wash their hands when they eat bread."
011503 He answered them, "Why do you also disobey the commandment of God because of your tradition?
011504 For God commanded, 'Honor your father and your mother,' and, 'He who speaks evil of father or mother, let him be put to death.'
011505 But you say, 'Whoever may tell his father or his mother, "Whatever help you might otherwise have gotten from me is a gift devoted to God,"
011506 he shall not honor his father or mother.' You have made the commandment of God void because of your tradition.
011507 You hypocrites! Well did Isaiah prophesy of you, saying,
011508 'These people draw near to me with their mouth, and honor me with their lips; but their heart is far from me.
011509 And in vain do they worship me, teaching as doctrine rules made by men.'"
011510 He summoned the multitude, and said to them, "Hear, and understand.
011511 That which enters into the mouth doesn't defile the man; but that which proceeds out of the mouth, this defiles the man."
011512 Then the disciples came, and said to him, "Do you know that the Pharisees were offended, when they heard this saying?"
011513 But he answered, "Every plant which my heavenly Father didn't plant will be uprooted.
011514 Leave them alone. They are blind guides of the blind. If the blind guide the blind, both will fall into a pit."
011515 Peter answered him, "Explain the parable to us."
011516 So Jesus said, "Do you also still not understand?
011517 Don't you understand that whatever goes into the mouth passes into the belly, and then out of the body?
011518 But the things which proceed out of the mouth come out of the heart, and they defile the man.
011519 For out of the heart come forth evil thoughts, murders, adulteries, sexual sins, thefts, false testimony, and blasphemies.
011520 These are the things which defile the man; but to eat with unwashed hands doesn't defile the man."
011521 Jesus went out from there, and withdrew into the region of Tyre and Sidon.
011522 Behold, a Canaanite woman came out from those borders, and cried, saying, "Have mercy on me, Lord, you son of David! My daughter is severely demonized!"
011523 But he answered her not a word. His disciples came and begged him, saying, "Send her away; for she cries after us."
011524 But he answered, "I wasn't sent to anyone but the lost sheep of the house of Israel."
011525 But she came and worshiped him, saying, "Lord, help me."
011526 But he answered, "It is not appropriate to take the children's bread and throw it to the dogs."
011527 But she said, "Yes, Lord, but even the dogs eat the crumbs which fall from their masters' table."
011528 Then Jesus answered her, "Woman, great is your faith! Be it done to you even as you desire." And her daughter was healed from that hour.
011529 Jesus departed there, and came near to the sea of Galilee; and he went up into the mountain, and sat there.
011530 Great multitudes came to him, having with them the lame, blind, mute, maimed, and many others, and they put them down at his feet. He healed them,
011531 so that the multitude wondered when they saw the mute speaking, injured whole, lame walking, and blind seeing--and they glorified the God of Israel.
011532 Jesus summoned his disciples and said, "I have compassion on the multitude, because they continue with me now three days and have nothing to eat. I don't want to send them away fasting, or they might faint on the way."
011533 The disciples said to him, "Where should we get so many loaves in a deserted place as to satisfy so great a multitude?"
011534 Jesus said to them, "How many loaves do you have?" They said, "Seven, and a few small fish."
011535 He commanded the multitude to sit down on the ground;
011536 and he took the seven loaves and the fish. He gave thanks and broke them, and gave to the disciples, and the disciples to the multitudes.
011537 They all ate, and were filled. They took up seven baskets full of the broken pieces that were left over.
011538 Those who ate were four thousand men, besides women and children.
011539 Then he sent away the multitudes, got into the boat, and came into the borders of Magdala.
011601 The Pharisees and Sadducees came, and testing him, asked him to show them a sign from heaven.
011602 But he answered them, "When it is evening, you say, 'It will be fair weather, for the sky is red.'
011603 In the morning, 'It will be foul weather today, for the sky is red and threatening.' Hypocrites! You know how to discern the appearance of the sky, but you can't discern the signs of the times!
011604 An evil and adulterous generation seeks after a sign, and there will be no sign given to it, except the sign of the prophet Jonah." He left them, and departed.
011605 The disciples came to the other side and had forgotten to take bread.
011606 Jesus said to them, "Take heed and beware of the yeast of the Pharisees and Sadducees."
011607 They reasoned among themselves, saying, "We brought no bread."
011608 Jesus, perceiving it, said, "Why do you reason among yourselves, you of little faith, 'because you have brought no bread?'
011609 Don't you yet perceive, neither remember the five loaves for the five thousand, and how many baskets you took up?
011610 Nor the seven loaves for the four thousand, and how many baskets you took up?
011611 How is it that you don't perceive that I didn't speak to you concerning bread? But beware of the yeast of the Pharisees and Sadducees."
011612 Then they understood that he didn't tell them to beware of the yeast of bread, but of the teaching of the Pharisees and Sadducees.
011613 Now when Jesus came into the parts of Caesarea Philippi, he asked his disciples, saying, "Who do men say that I, the Son of Man, am?"
011614 They said, "Some say John the Baptizer, some, Elijah, and others, Jeremiah, or one of the prophets."
011615 He said to them, "But who do you say that I am?"
011616 Simon Peter answered, "You are the Christ, the Son of the living God."
011617 Jesus answered him, "Blessed are you, Simon Bar Jonah, for flesh and blood has not revealed this to you, but my Father who is in heaven.
011618 I also tell you that you are Peter, and on this rock I will build my assembly, and the gates of Hades will not prevail against it.
011619 I will give to you the keys of the Kingdom of Heaven, and whatever you bind on earth will have been bound in heaven; and whatever you release on earth will have been released in heaven."
011620 Then he commanded the disciples that they should tell no one that he was Jesus the Christ.
011621 From that time, Jesus began to show his disciples that he must go to Jerusalem and suffer many things from the elders, chief priests, and scribes, and be killed, and the third day be raised up.
011622 Peter took him aside, and began to rebuke him, saying, "Far be it from you, Lord! This will never be done to you."
011623 But he turned, and said to Peter, "Get behind me, Satan! You are a stumbling block to me, for you are not setting your mind on the things of God, but on the things of men."
011624 Then Jesus said to his disciples, "If anyone desires to come after me, let him deny himself, and take up his cross, and follow me.
011625 For whoever desires to save his life will lose it, and whoever will lose his life for my sake will find it.
011626 For what will it profit a man, if he gains the whole world, and forfeits his life? Or what will a man give in exchange for his life?
011627 For the Son of Man will come in the glory of his Father with his angels, and then he will render to everyone according to his deeds.
011628 Most certainly I tell you, there are some standing here who will in no way taste of death, until they see the Son of Man coming in his Kingdom."
011701 After six days, Jesus took with him Peter, James, and John his brother, and brought them up into a high mountain by themselves.
011702 He was transfigured before them. His face shone like the sun, and his garments became as white as the light.
011703 Behold, Moses and Elijah appeared to them talking with him.
011704 Peter answered, and said to Jesus, "Lord, it is good for us to be here. If you want, let's make three tents here: one for you, one for Moses, and one for Elijah."
011705 While he was still speaking, behold, a bright cloud overshadowed them. Behold, a voice came out of the cloud, saying, "This is my beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased. Listen to him."
011706 When the disciples heard it, they fell on their faces, and were very afraid.
011707 Jesus came and touched them and said, "Get up, and don't be afraid."
011708 Lifting up their eyes, they saw no one, except Jesus alone.
011709 As they were coming down from the mountain, Jesus commanded them, saying, "Don't tell anyone what you saw, until the Son of Man has risen from the dead."
011710 His disciples asked him, saying, "Then why do the scribes say that Elijah must come first?"
011711 Jesus answered them, "Elijah indeed comes first, and will restore all things,
011712 but I tell you that Elijah has come already, and they didn't recognize him, but did to him whatever they wanted to. Even so the Son of Man will also suffer by them."
011713 Then the disciples understood that he spoke to them of John the Baptizer.
011714 When they came to the multitude, a man came to him, kneeling down to him, saying,
011715 "Lord, have mercy on my son, for he is epileptic, and suffers grievously; for he often falls into the fire, and often into the water.
011716 So I brought him to your disciples, and they could not cure him."
011717 Jesus answered, "Faithless and perverse generation! How long will I be with you? How long will I bear with you? Bring him here to me."
011718 Jesus rebuked him, the demon went out of him, and the boy was cured from that hour.
011719 Then the disciples came to Jesus privately, and said, "Why weren't we able to cast it out?"
011720 He said to them, "Because of your unbelief. For most certainly I tell you, if you have faith as a grain of mustard seed, you will tell this mountain, 'Move from here to there,' and it will move; and nothing will be impossible for you.
011721 But this kind doesn't go out except by prayer and fasting."
011722 While they were staying in Galilee, Jesus said to them, "The Son of Man is about to be delivered up into the hands of men,
011723 and they will kill him, and the third day he will be raised up." They were exceedingly sorry.
011724 When they had come to Capernaum, those who collected the didrachma coins came to Peter, and said, "Doesn't your teacher pay the didrachma?"
011725 He said, "Yes." When he came into the house, Jesus anticipated him, saying, "What do you think, Simon? From whom do the kings of the earth receive toll or tribute? From their children, or from strangers?"
011726 Peter said to him, "From strangers." Jesus said to him, "Therefore the children are exempt.
011727 But, lest we cause them to stumble, go to the sea, cast a hook, and take up the first fish that comes up. When you have opened its mouth, you will find a stater coin. Take that, and give it to them for me and you."
011801 In that hour the disciples came to Jesus, saying, "Who then is greatest in the Kingdom of Heaven?"
011802 Jesus called a little child to himself, and set him in the midst of them,
011803 and said, "Most certainly I tell you, unless you turn, and become as little children, you will in no way enter into the Kingdom of Heaven.
011804 Whoever therefore humbles himself as this little child, the same is the greatest in the Kingdom of Heaven.
011805 Whoever receives one such little child in my name receives me,
011806 but whoever causes one of these little ones who believe in me to stumble, it would be better for him that a huge millstone should be hung around his neck, and that he should be sunk in the depths of the sea.
011807 "Woe to the world because of occasions of stumbling! For it must be that the occasions come, but woe to that person through whom the occasion comes!
011808 If your hand or your foot causes you to stumble, cut it off, and cast it from you. It is better for you to enter into life maimed or crippled, rather than having two hands or two feet to be cast into the eternal fire.
011809 If your eye causes you to stumble, pluck it out, and cast it from you. It is better for you to enter into life with one eye, rather than having two eyes to be cast into the Gehenna of fire.
011810 See that you don't despise one of these little ones, for I tell you that in heaven their angels always see the face of my Father who is in heaven.
011811 For the Son of Man came to save that which was lost.
011812 "What do you think? If a man has one hundred sheep, and one of them goes astray, doesn't he leave the ninety-nine, go to the mountains, and seek that which has gone astray?
011813 If he finds it, most certainly I tell you, he rejoices over it more than over the ninety-nine which have not gone astray.
011814 Even so it is not the will of your Father who is in heaven that one of these little ones should perish.
011815 "If your brother sins against you, go, show him his fault between you and him alone. If he listens to you, you have gained back your brother.
011816 But if he doesn't listen, take one or two more with you, that at the mouth of two or three witnesses every word may be established.
011817 If he refuses to listen to them, tell it to the assembly. If he refuses to hear the assembly also, let him be to you as a Gentile or a tax collector.
011818 Most certainly I tell you, whatever things you bind on earth will have been bound in heaven, and whatever things you release on earth will have been released in heaven.
011819 Again, assuredly I tell you, that if two of you will agree on earth concerning anything that they will ask, it will be done for them by my Father who is in heaven.
011820 For where two or three are gathered together in my name, there I am in the midst of them."
011821 Then Peter came and said to him, "Lord, how often shall my brother sin against me, and I forgive him? Until seven times?"
011822 Jesus said to him, "I don't tell you until seven times, but, until seventy times seven.
011823 Therefore the Kingdom of Heaven is like a certain king, who wanted to reconcile accounts with his servants.
011824 When he had begun to reconcile, one was brought to him who owed him ten thousand talents.
011825 But because he couldn't pay, his lord commanded him to be sold, with his wife, his children, and all that he had, and payment to be made.
011826 The servant therefore fell down and kneeled before him, saying, 'Lord, have patience with me, and I will repay you all!'
011827 The lord of that servant, being moved with compassion, released him, and forgave him the debt.
011828 "But that servant went out, and found one of his fellow servants, who owed him one hundred denarii, and he grabbed him, and took him by the throat, saying, 'Pay me what you owe!'
011829 "So his fellow servant fell down at his feet and begged him, saying, 'Have patience with me, and I will repay you!'
011830 He would not, but went and cast him into prison, until he should pay back that which was due.
011831 So when his fellow servants saw what was done, they were exceedingly sorry, and came and told to their lord all that was done.
011832 Then his lord called him in, and said to him, 'You wicked servant! I forgave you all that debt, because you begged me.
011833 Shouldn't you also have had mercy on your fellow servant, even as I had mercy on you?'
011834 His lord was angry, and delivered him to the tormentors, until he should pay all that was due to him.
011835 So my heavenly Father will also do to you, if you don't each forgive your brother from your hearts for his misdeeds."
011901 It happened when Jesus had finished these words, he departed from Galilee, and came into the borders of Judea beyond the Jordan.
011902 Great multitudes followed him, and he healed them there.
011903 Pharisees came to him, testing him, and saying, "Is it lawful for a man to divorce his wife for any reason?"
011904 He answered, "Haven't you read that he who made them from the beginning made them male and female,
011905 and said, 'For this cause a man shall leave his father and mother, and shall join to his wife; and the two shall become one flesh?'
011906 So that they are no more two, but one flesh. What therefore God has joined together, don't let man tear apart."
011907 They asked him, "Why then did Moses command us to give her a bill of divorce, and divorce her?"
011908 He said to them, "Moses, because of the hardness of your hearts, allowed you to divorce your wives, but from the beginning it has not been so.
011909 I tell you that whoever divorces his wife, except for sexual immorality, and marries another, commits adultery; and he who marries her when she is divorced commits adultery."
011910 His disciples said to him, "If this is the case of the man with his wife, it is not expedient to marry."
011911 But he said to them, "Not all men can receive this saying, but those to whom it is given.
011912 For there are eunuchs who were born that way from their mother's womb, and there are eunuchs who were made eunuchs by men; and there are eunuchs who made themselves eunuchs for the Kingdom of Heaven's sake. He who is able to receive it, let him receive it."
011913 Then little children were brought to him, that he should lay his hands on them and pray; and the disciples rebuked them.
011914 But Jesus said, "Allow the little children, and don't forbid them to come to me; for the Kingdom of Heaven belongs to ones like these."
011915 He laid his hands on them, and departed from there.
011916 Behold, one came to him and said, "Good teacher, what good thing shall I do, that I may have eternal life?"
011917 He said to him, "Why do you call me good? No one is good but one, that is, God. But if you want to enter into life, keep the commandments."
011918 He said to him, "Which ones?" Jesus said, "'You shall not murder.' 'You shall not commit adultery.' 'You shall not steal.' 'You shall not offer false testimony.'
011919 'Honor your father and mother.' And, 'You shall love your neighbor as yourself.'"
011920 The young man said to him, "All these things I have observed from my youth. What do I still lack?"
011921 Jesus said to him, "If you want to be perfect, go, sell what you have, and give to the poor, and you will have treasure in heaven; and come, follow me."
011922 But when the young man heard the saying, he went away sad, for he was one who had great possessions.
011923 Jesus said to his disciples, "Most certainly I say to you, a rich man will enter into the Kingdom of Heaven with difficulty.
011924 Again I tell you, it is easier for a camel to go through a needle's eye, than for a rich man to enter into the Kingdom of God."
011925 When the disciples heard it, they were exceedingly astonished, saying, "Who then can be saved?"
011926 Looking at them, Jesus said, "With men this is impossible, but with God all things are possible."
011927 Then Peter answered, "Behold, we have left everything, and followed you. What then will we have?"
011928 Jesus said to them, "Most certainly I tell you that you who have followed me, in the regeneration when the Son of Man will sit on the throne of his glory, you also will sit on twelve thrones, judging the twelve tribes of Israel.
011929 Everyone who has left houses, or brothers, or sisters, or father, or mother, or wife, or children, or lands, for my name's sake, will receive one hundred times, and will inherit eternal life.
011930 But many will be last who are first; and first who are last.
012001 "For the Kingdom of Heaven is like a man who was the master of a household, who went out early in the morning to hire laborers for his vineyard.
012002 When he had agreed with the laborers for a denarius a day, he sent them into his vineyard.
012003 He went out about the third hour, and saw others standing idle in the marketplace.
012004 To them he said, 'You also go into the vineyard, and whatever is right I will give you.' So they went their way.
012005 Again he went out about the sixth and the ninth hour, and did likewise.
