020718 He said to them, "Are you thus without understanding also? Don't you perceive that whatever goes into the man from outside can't defile him,
020719 because it doesn't go into his heart, but into his stomach, then into the latrine, thus purifying all foods?"
020720 He said, "That which proceeds out of the man, that defiles the man.
020721 For from within, out of the hearts of men, proceed evil thoughts, adulteries, sexual sins, murders, thefts,
020722 covetings, wickedness, deceit, lustful desires, an evil eye, blasphemy, pride, and foolishness.
020723 All these evil things come from within, and defile the man."
020724 From there he arose, and went away into the borders of Tyre and Sidon. He entered into a house, and didn't want anyone to know it, but he couldn't escape notice.
020725 For a woman, whose little daughter had an unclean spirit, having heard of him, came and fell down at his feet.
020726 Now the woman was a Greek, a Syrophoenician by race. She begged him that he would cast the demon out of her daughter.
020727 But Jesus said to her, "Let the children be filled first, for it is not appropriate to take the children's bread and throw it to the dogs."
020728 But she answered him, "Yes, Lord. Yet even the dogs under the table eat the children's crumbs."
020729 He said to her, "For this saying, go your way. The demon has gone out of your daughter."
020730 She went away to her house, and found the child having been laid on the bed, with the demon gone out.
020731 Again he departed from the borders of Tyre and Sidon, and came to the sea of Galilee, through the midst of the region of Decapolis.
020732 They brought to him one who was deaf and had an impediment in his speech. They begged him to lay his hand on him.
020733 He took him aside from the multitude, privately, and put his fingers into his ears, and he spat, and touched his tongue.
020734 Looking up to heaven, he sighed, and said to him, "Ephphatha!" that is, "Be opened!"
020735 Immediately his ears were opened, and the impediment of his tongue was released, and he spoke clearly.
020736 He commanded them that they should tell no one, but the more he commanded them, so much the more widely they proclaimed it.
020737 They were astonished beyond measure, saying, "He has done all things well. He makes even the deaf hear, and the mute speak!"
020801 In those days, when there was a very great multitude, and they had nothing to eat, Jesus called his disciples to himself, and said to them,
020802 "I have compassion on the multitude, because they have stayed with me now three days, and have nothing to eat.
020803 If I send them away fasting to their home, they will faint on the way, for some of them have come a long way."
020804 His disciples answered him, "From where could one satisfy these people with bread here in a deserted place?"
020805 He asked them, "How many loaves do you have?" They said, "Seven."
020806 He commanded the multitude to sit down on the ground, and he took the seven loaves. Having given thanks, he broke them, and gave them to his disciples to serve, and they served the multitude.
020807 They had a few small fish. Having blessed them, he said to serve these also.
020808 They ate, and were filled. They took up seven baskets of broken pieces that were left over.
020809 Those who had eaten were about four thousand. Then he sent them away.
020810 Immediately he entered into the boat with his disciples, and came into the region of Dalmanutha.
020811 The Pharisees came out and began to question him, seeking from him a sign from heaven, and testing him.
020812 He sighed deeply in his spirit, and said, "Why does this generation seek a sign? Most certainly I tell you, no sign will be given to this generation."
020813 He left them, and again entering into the boat, departed to the other side.
020814 They forgot to take bread; and they didn't have more than one loaf in the boat with them.
020815 He warned them, saying, "Take heed: beware of the yeast of the Pharisees and the yeast of Herod."
020816 They reasoned with one another, saying, "It's because we have no bread."
020817 Jesus, perceiving it, said to them, "Why do you reason that it's because you have no bread? Don't you perceive yet, neither understand? Is your heart still hardened?
020818 Having eyes, don't you see? Having ears, don't you hear? Don't you remember?
020819 When I broke the five loaves among the five thousand, how many baskets full of broken pieces did you take up?" They told him, "Twelve."
020820 "When the seven loaves fed the four thousand, how many baskets full of broken pieces did you take up?" They told him, "Seven."
020821 He asked them, "Don't you understand, yet?"
020822 He came to Bethsaida. They brought a blind man to him, and begged him to touch him.
020823 He took hold of the blind man by the hand, and brought him out of the village. When he had spit on his eyes, and laid his hands on him, he asked him if he saw anything.
020824 He looked up, and said, "I see men; for I see them like trees walking."
020825 Then again he laid his hands on his eyes. He looked intently, and was restored, and saw everyone clearly.
020826 He sent him away to his house, saying, "Don't enter into the village, nor tell anyone in the village."
020827 Jesus went out, with his disciples, into the villages of Caesarea Philippi. On the way he asked his disciples, "Who do men say that I am?"
020828 They told him, "John the Baptizer, and others say Elijah, but others: one of the prophets."
020829 He said to them, "But who do you say that I am?" Peter answered, "You are the Christ."
020830 He commanded them that they should tell no one about him.
020831 He began to teach them that the Son of Man must suffer many things, and be rejected by the elders, the chief priests, and the scribes, and be killed, and after three days rise again.
020832 He spoke to them openly. Peter took him, and began to rebuke him.
020833 But he, turning around, and seeing his disciples, rebuked Peter, and said, "Get behind me, Satan! For you have in mind not the things of God, but the things of men."
020834 He called the multitude to himself with his disciples, and said to them, "Whoever wants to come after me, let him deny himself, and take up his cross, and follow me.
020835 For whoever wants to save his life will lose it; and whoever will lose his life for my sake and the sake of the Good News will save it.
020836 For what does it profit a man, to gain the whole world, and forfeit his life?
020837 For what will a man give in exchange for his life?
020838 For whoever will be ashamed of me and of my words in this adulterous and sinful generation, the Son of Man also will be ashamed of him, when he comes in the glory of his Father with the holy angels."
020901 He said to them, "Most certainly I tell you, there are some standing here who will in no way taste death until they see the Kingdom of God come with power."
020902 After six days Jesus took with him Peter, James, and John, and brought them up onto a high mountain privately by themselves, and he was changed into another form in front of them.
020903 His clothing became glistening, exceedingly white, like snow, such as no launderer on earth can whiten them.
020904 Elijah and Moses appeared to them, and they were talking with Jesus.
020905 Peter answered Jesus, "Rabbi, it is good for us to be here. Let's make three tents: one for you, one for Moses, and one for Elijah."
020906 For he didn't know what to say, for they were very afraid.
020907 A cloud came, overshadowing them, and a voice came out of the cloud, "This is my beloved Son. Listen to him."
020908 Suddenly looking around, they saw no one with them any more, except Jesus only.
020909 As they were coming down from the mountain, he commanded them that they should tell no one what things they had seen, until after the Son of Man had risen from the dead.
020910 They kept this saying to themselves, questioning what the "rising from the dead" meant.
020911 They asked him, saying, "Why do the scribes say that Elijah must come first?"
020912 He said to them, "Elijah indeed comes first, and restores all things. How is it written about the Son of Man, that he should suffer many things and be despised?
020913 But I tell you that Elijah has come, and they have also done to him whatever they wanted to, even as it is written about him."
020914 Coming to the disciples, he saw a great multitude around them, and scribes questioning them.
020915 Immediately all the multitude, when they saw him, were greatly amazed, and running to him greeted him.
020916 He asked the scribes, "What are you asking them?"
020917 One of the multitude answered, "Teacher, I brought to you my son, who has a mute spirit;
020918 and wherever it seizes him, it throws him down, and he foams at the mouth, and grinds his teeth, and wastes away. I asked your disciples to cast it out, and they weren't able."
020919 He answered him, "Unbelieving generation, how long shall I be with you? How long shall I bear with you? Bring him to me."
020920 They brought him to him, and when he saw him, immediately the spirit convulsed him, and he fell on the ground, wallowing and foaming at the mouth.
020921 He asked his father, "How long has it been since this has come to him?" He said, "From childhood.
020922 Often it has cast him both into the fire and into the water, to destroy him. But if you can do anything, have compassion on us, and help us."
020923 Jesus said to him, "If you can believe, all things are possible to him who believes."
020924 Immediately the father of the child cried out with tears, "I believe. Help my unbelief!"
020925 When Jesus saw that a multitude came running together, he rebuked the unclean spirit, saying to him, "You mute and deaf spirit, I command you, come out of him, and never enter him again!"
020926 Having cried out, and convulsed greatly, it came out of him. The boy became like one dead; so much that most of them said, "He is dead."
020927 But Jesus took him by the hand, and raised him up; and he arose.
020928 When he had come into the house, his disciples asked him privately, "Why couldn't we cast it out?"
020929 He said to them, "This kind can come out by nothing, except by prayer and fasting."
020930 They went out from there, and passed through Galilee. He didn't want anyone to know it.
020931 For he was teaching his disciples, and said to them, "The Son of Man is being handed over to the hands of men, and they will kill him; and when he is killed, on the third day he will rise again."
020932 But they didn't understand the saying, and were afraid to ask him.
020933 He came to Capernaum, and when he was in the house he asked them, "What were you arguing among yourselves on the way?"
020934 But they were silent, for they had disputed one with another on the way about who was the greatest.
020935 He sat down, and called the twelve; and he said to them, "If any man wants to be first, he shall be last of all, and servant of all."
020936 He took a little child, and set him in the midst of them. Taking him in his arms, he said to them,
020937 "Whoever receives one such little child in my name, receives me, and whoever receives me, doesn't receive me, but him who sent me."
020938 John said to him, "Teacher, we saw someone who doesn't follow us casting out demons in your name; and we forbade him, because he doesn't follow us."
020939 But Jesus said, "Don't forbid him, for there is no one who will do a mighty work in my name, and be able quickly to speak evil of me.
020940 For whoever is not against us is on our side.
020941 For whoever will give you a cup of water to drink in my name, because you are Christ's, most certainly I tell you, he will in no way lose his reward.
020942 Whoever will cause one of these little ones who believe in me to stumble, it would be better for him if he was thrown into the sea with a millstone hung around his neck.
020943 If your hand causes you to stumble, cut it off. It is better for you to enter into life maimed, rather than having your two hands to go into Gehenna, into the unquenchable fire,
020944 'where their worm doesn't die, and the fire is not quenched.'
020945 If your foot causes you to stumble, cut it off. It is better for you to enter into life lame, rather than having your two feet to be cast into Gehenna, into the fire that will never be quenched--
020946 'where their worm doesn't die, and the fire is not quenched.'
020947 If your eye causes you to stumble, cast it out. It is better for you to enter into the Kingdom of God with one eye, rather than having two eyes to be cast into the Gehenna of fire,
020948 'where their worm doesn't die, and the fire is not quenched.'
020949 For everyone will be salted with fire, and every sacrifice will be seasoned with salt.
020950 Salt is good, but if the salt has lost its saltiness, with what will you season it? Have salt in yourselves, and be at peace with one another."
021001 He arose from there and came into the borders of Judea and beyond the Jordan. Multitudes came together to him again. As he usually did, he was again teaching them.
021002 Pharisees came to him testing him, and asked him, "Is it lawful for a man to divorce his wife?"
021003 He answered, "What did Moses command you?"
021004 They said, "Moses allowed a certificate of divorce to be written, and to divorce her."
021005 But Jesus said to them, "For your hardness of heart, he wrote you this commandment.
021006 But from the beginning of the creation, God made them male and female.
021007 For this cause a man will leave his father and mother, and will join to his wife,
021008 and the two will become one flesh, so that they are no longer two, but one flesh.
021009 What therefore God has joined together, let no man separate."
021010 In the house, his disciples asked him again about the same matter.
021011 He said to them, "Whoever divorces his wife, and marries another, commits adultery against her.
021012 If a woman herself divorces her husband, and marries another, she commits adultery."
021013 They were bringing to him little children, that he should touch them, but the disciples rebuked those who were bringing them.
021014 But when Jesus saw it, he was moved with indignation, and said to them, "Allow the little children to come to me! Don't forbid them, for the Kingdom of God belongs to such as these.
021015 Most certainly I tell you, whoever will not receive the Kingdom of God like a little child, he will in no way enter into it."
021016 He took them in his arms, and blessed them, laying his hands on them.
021017 As he was going out into the way, one ran to him, knelt before him, and asked him, "Good Teacher, what shall I do that I may inherit eternal life?"
021018 Jesus said to him, "Why do you call me good? No one is good except one--God.
021019 You know the commandments: 'Do not murder,' 'Do not commit adultery,' 'Do not steal,' 'Do not give false testimony,' 'Do not defraud,' 'Honor your father and mother.'"
021020 He said to him, "Teacher, I have observed all these things from my youth."
021021 Jesus looking at him loved him, and said to him, "One thing you lack. Go, sell whatever you have, and give to the poor, and you will have treasure in heaven; and come, follow me, taking up the cross."
021022 But his face fell at that saying, and he went away sorrowful, for he was one who had great possessions.
021023 Jesus looked around, and said to his disciples, "How difficult it is for those who have riches to enter into the Kingdom of God!"
021024 The disciples were amazed at his words. But Jesus answered again, "Children, how hard is it for those who trust in riches to enter into the Kingdom of God!
021025 It is easier for a camel to go through a needle's eye than for a rich man to enter into the Kingdom of God."
021026 They were exceedingly astonished, saying to him, "Then who can be saved?"
021027 Jesus, looking at them, said, "With men it is impossible, but not with God, for all things are possible with God."
021028 Peter began to tell him, "Behold, we have left all, and have followed you."
021029 Jesus said, "Most certainly I tell you, there is no one who has left house, or brothers, or sisters, or father, or mother, or wife, or children, or land, for my sake, and for the sake of the Good News,
021030 but he will receive one hundred times more now in this time, houses, brothers, sisters, mothers, children, and land, with persecutions; and in the age to come eternal life.
021031 But many who are first will be last; and the last first."
021032 They were on the way, going up to Jerusalem; and Jesus was going in front of them, and they were amazed; and those who followed were afraid. He again took the twelve, and began to tell them the things that were going to happen to him.
021033 "Behold, we are going up to Jerusalem. The Son of Man will be delivered to the chief priests and the scribes. They will condemn him to death, and will deliver him to the Gentiles.
021034 They will mock him, spit on him, scourge him, and kill him. On the third day he will rise again."
021035 James and John, the sons of Zebedee, came near to him, saying, "Teacher, we want you to do for us whatever we will ask."
021036 He said to them, "What do you want me to do for you?"
021037 They said to him, "Grant to us that we may sit, one at your right hand, and one at your left hand, in your glory."
021038 But Jesus said to them, "You don't know what you are asking. Are you able to drink the cup that I drink, and to be baptized with the baptism that I am baptized with?"
021039 They said to him, "We are able." Jesus said to them, "You shall indeed drink the cup that I drink, and you shall be baptized with the baptism that I am baptized with;
021040 but to sit at my right hand and at my left hand is not mine to give, but for whom it has been prepared."
021041 When the ten heard it, they began to be indignant towards James and John.
021042 Jesus summoned them, and said to them, "You know that they who are recognized as rulers over the nations lord it over them, and their great ones exercise authority over them.
021043 But it shall not be so among you, but whoever wants to become great among you shall be your servant.
021044 Whoever of you wants to become first among you, shall be bondservant of all.
021045 For the Son of Man also came not to be served, but to serve, and to give his life as a ransom for many."
021046 They came to Jericho. As he went out from Jericho, with his disciples and a great multitude, the son of Timaeus, Bartimaeus, a blind beggar, was sitting by the road.
021047 When he heard that it was Jesus the Nazarene, he began to cry out, and say, "Jesus, you son of David, have mercy on me!"
021048 Many rebuked him, that he should be quiet, but he cried out much more, "You son of David, have mercy on me!"
021049 Jesus stood still, and said, "Call him." They called the blind man, saying to him, "Cheer up! Get up. He is calling you!"
021050 He, casting away his cloak, sprang up, and came to Jesus.
021051 Jesus asked him, "What do you want me to do for you?" The blind man said to him, "Rabboni, that I may see again."
021052 Jesus said to him, "Go your way. Your faith has made you well." Immediately he received his sight, and followed Jesus in the way.
021101 When they drew near to Jerusalem, to Bethsphage and Bethany, at the Mount of Olives, he sent two of his disciples,
021102 and said to them, "Go your way into the village that is opposite you. Immediately as you enter into it, you will find a young donkey tied, on which no one has sat. Untie him, and bring him.
021103 If anyone asks you, 'Why are you doing this?' say, 'The Lord needs him;' and immediately he will send him back here."
021104 They went away, and found a young donkey tied at the door outside in the open street, and they untied him.
021105 Some of those who stood there asked them, "What are you doing, untying the young donkey?"
021106 They said to them just as Jesus had said, and they let them go.
021107 They brought the young donkey to Jesus, and threw their garments on it, and Jesus sat on it.
021108 Many spread their garments on the way, and others were cutting down branches from the trees, and spreading them on the road.
021109 Those who went in front, and those who followed, cried out, "Hosanna! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord!
021110 Blessed is the kingdom of our father David that is coming in the name of the Lord! Hosanna in the highest!"
021111 Jesus entered into the temple in Jerusalem. When he had looked around at everything, it being now evening, he went out to Bethany with the twelve.
021112 The next day, when they had come out from Bethany, he was hungry.
021113 Seeing a fig tree afar off having leaves, he came to see if perhaps he might find anything on it. When he came to it, he found nothing but leaves, for it was not the season for figs.
021114 Jesus told it, "May no one ever eat fruit from you again!" and his disciples heard it.
021115 They came to Jerusalem, and Jesus entered into the temple, and began to throw out those who sold and those who bought in the temple, and overthrew the tables of the money changers, and the seats of those who sold the doves.
021116 He would not allow anyone to carry a container through the temple.
021117 He taught, saying to them, "Isn't it written, 'My house will be called a house of prayer for all the nations?' But you have made it a den of robbers!"
021118 The chief priests and the scribes heard it, and sought how they might destroy him. For they feared him, because all the multitude was astonished at his teaching.
021119 When evening came, he went out of the city.
021120 As they passed by in the morning, they saw the fig tree withered away from the roots.
021121 Peter, remembering, said to him, "Rabbi, look! The fig tree which you cursed has withered away."
021122 Jesus answered them, "Have faith in God.
021123 For most certainly I tell you, whoever may tell this mountain, 'Be taken up and cast into the sea,' and doesn't doubt in his heart, but believes that what he says is happening; he shall have whatever he says.
021124 Therefore I tell you, all things whatever you pray and ask for, believe that you have received them, and you shall have them.
021125 Whenever you stand praying, forgive, if you have anything against anyone; so that your Father, who is in heaven, may also forgive you your transgressions.
021126 But if you do not forgive, neither will your Father in heaven forgive your transgressions."
021127 They came again to Jerusalem, and as he was walking in the temple, the chief priests, and the scribes, and the elders came to him,
021128 and they began saying to him, "By what authority do you do these things? Or who gave you this authority to do these things?"
021129 Jesus said to them, "I will ask you one question. Answer me, and I will tell you by what authority I do these things.
021130 The baptism of John--was it from heaven, or from men? Answer me."
021131 They reasoned with themselves, saying, "If we should say, 'From heaven;' he will say, 'Why then did you not believe him?'
021132 If we should say, 'From men'"--they feared the people, for all held John to really be a prophet.
021133 They answered Jesus, "We don't know." Jesus said to them, "Neither do I tell you by what authority I do these things."
021201 He began to speak to them in parables. "A man planted a vineyard, put a hedge around it, dug a pit for the winepress, built a tower, rented it out to a farmer, and went into another country.
021202 When it was time, he sent a servant to the farmer to get from the farmer his share of the fruit of the vineyard.
021203 They took him, beat him, and sent him away empty.
021204 Again, he sent another servant to them; and they threw stones at him, wounded him in the head, and sent him away shamefully treated.
021205 Again he sent another; and they killed him; and many others, beating some, and killing some.
021206 Therefore still having one, his beloved son, he sent him last to them, saying, 'They will respect my son.'
021207 But those farmers said among themselves, 'This is the heir. Come, let's kill him, and the inheritance will be ours.'
021208 They took him, killed him, and cast him out of the vineyard.
021209 What therefore will the lord of the vineyard do? He will come and destroy the farmers, and will give the vineyard to others.
021210 Haven't you even read this Scripture: 'The stone which the builders rejected, the same was made the head of the corner.
021211 This was from the Lord, it is marvelous in our eyes'?"
021212 They tried to seize him, but they feared the multitude; for they perceived that he spoke the parable against them. They left him, and went away.
021213 They sent some of the Pharisees and of the Herodians to him, that they might trap him with words.
021214 When they had come, they asked him, "Teacher, we know that you are honest, and don't defer to anyone; for you aren't partial to anyone, but truly teach the way of God. Is it lawful to pay taxes to Caesar, or not?
021215 Shall we give, or shall we not give?" But he, knowing their hypocrisy, said to them, "Why do you test me? Bring me a denarius, that I may see it."
021216 They brought it. He said to them, "Whose is this image and inscription?" They said to him, "Caesar's."
021217 Jesus answered them, "Render to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things that are God's." They marveled greatly at him.
021218 There came to him Sadducees, who say that there is no resurrection. They asked him, saying,
021219 "Teacher, Moses wrote to us, 'If a man's brother dies, and leaves a wife behind him, and leaves no children, that his brother should take his wife, and raise up offspring for his brother.'
021220 There were seven brothers. The first took a wife, and dying left no offspring.
021221 The second took her, and died, leaving no children behind him. The third likewise;
021222 and the seven took her and left no children. Last of all the woman also died.
021223 In the resurrection, when they rise, whose wife will she be of them? For the seven had her as a wife."
021224 Jesus answered them, "Isn't this because you are mistaken, not knowing the Scriptures, nor the power of God?
021225 For when they will rise from the dead, they neither marry, nor are given in marriage, but are like angels in heaven.
021226 But about the dead, that they are raised; haven't you read in the book of Moses, about the Bush, how God spoke to him, saying, 'I am the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob'?
021227 He is not the God of the dead, but of the living. You are therefore badly mistaken."
021228 One of the scribes came, and heard them questioning together. Knowing that he had answered them well, asked him, "Which commandment is the greatest of all?"
021229 Jesus answered, "The greatest is, 'Hear, Israel, the Lord our God, the Lord is one:
021230 you shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your mind, and with all your strength.' This is the first commandment.
021231 The second is like this, 'You shall love your neighbor as yourself.' There is no other commandment greater than these."
021232 The scribe said to him, "Truly, teacher, you have said well that he is one, and there is none other but he,
021233 and to love him with all the heart, and with all the understanding, with all the soul, and with all the strength, and to love his neighbor as himself, is more important than all whole burnt offerings and sacrifices."
021234 When Jesus saw that he answered wisely, he said to him, "You are not far from the Kingdom of God." No one dared ask him any question after that.
021235 Jesus responded, as he taught in the temple, "How is it that the scribes say that the Christ is the son of David?
021236 For David himself said in the Holy Spirit, 'The Lord said to my Lord, "Sit at my right hand, until I make your enemies the footstool of your feet."'
021237 Therefore David himself calls him Lord, so how can he be his son?" The common people heard him gladly.
021238 In his teaching he said to them, "Beware of the scribes, who like to walk in long robes, and to get greetings in the marketplaces,
021239 and the best seats in the synagogues, and the best places at feasts:
021240 those who devour widows' houses, and for a pretense make long prayers. These will receive greater condemnation."
021241 Jesus sat down opposite the treasury, and saw how the multitude cast money into the treasury. Many who were rich cast in much.
021242 A poor widow came, and she cast in two small brass coins, which equal a quadrans coin.
021243 He called his disciples to himself, and said to them, "Most certainly I tell you, this poor widow gave more than all those who are giving into the treasury,
021244 for they all gave out of their abundance, but she, out of her poverty, gave all that she had to live on."
021301 As he went out of the temple, one of his disciples said to him, "Teacher, see what kind of stones and what kind of buildings!"
021302 Jesus said to him, "Do you see these great buildings? There will not be left here one stone on another, which will not be thrown down."
021303 As he sat on the Mount of Olives opposite the temple, Peter, James, John, and Andrew asked him privately,
021304 "Tell us, when will these things be? What is the sign that these things are all about to be fulfilled?"
021305 Jesus, answering, began to tell them, "Be careful that no one leads you astray.
021306 For many will come in my name, saying, 'I am he!' and will lead many astray.
021307 "When you hear of wars and rumors of wars, don't be troubled. For those must happen, but the end is not yet.
021308 For nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom. There will be earthquakes in various places. There will be famines and troubles. These things are the beginning of birth pains.
021309 But watch yourselves, for they will deliver you up to councils. You will be beaten in synagogues. You will stand before rulers and kings for my sake, for a testimony to them.
021310 The Good News must first be preached to all the nations.
021311 When they lead you away and deliver you up, don't be anxious beforehand, or premeditate what you will say, but say whatever will be given you in that hour. For it is not you who speak, but the Holy Spirit.
021312 "Brother will deliver up brother to death, and the father his child. Children will rise up against parents, and cause them to be put to death.
021313 You will be hated by all men for my name's sake, but he who endures to the end, the same will be saved.
021314 But when you see the abomination of desolation, spoken of by Daniel the prophet, standing where it ought not (let the reader understand), then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains,
021315 and let him who is on the housetop not go down, nor enter in, to take anything out of his house.
021316 Let him who is in the field not return back to take his cloak.
021317 But woe to those who are with child and to those who nurse babies in those days!
021318 Pray that your flight won't be in the winter.
021319 For in those days there will be oppression, such as there has not been the like from the beginning of the creation which God created until now, and never will be.
021320 Unless the Lord had shortened the days, no flesh would have been saved; but for the sake of the chosen ones, whom he picked out, he shortened the days.
021321 Then if anyone tells you, 'Look, here is the Christ!' or, 'Look, there!' don't believe it.
021322 For there will arise false christs and false prophets, and will show signs and wonders, that they may lead astray, if possible, even the chosen ones.
021323 But you watch. "Behold, I have told you all things beforehand.
021324 But in those days, after that oppression, the sun will be darkened, the moon will not give its light,
021325 the stars will be falling from the sky, and the powers that are in the heavens will be shaken.
021326 Then they will see the Son of Man coming in clouds with great power and glory.
021327 Then he will send out his angels, and will gather together his chosen ones from the four winds, from the ends of the earth to the ends of the sky.
021328 "Now from the fig tree, learn this parable. When the branch has now become tender, and puts forth its leaves, you know that the summer is near;
021329 even so you also, when you see these things coming to pass, know that it is near, at the doors.
021330 Most certainly I say to you, this generation will not pass away until all these things happen.
021331 Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will not pass away.
021332 But of that day or that hour no one knows, not even the angels in heaven, nor the Son, but only the Father.
021333 Watch, keep alert, and pray; for you don't know when the time is.
021334 "It is like a man, traveling to another country, having left his house, and given authority to his servants, and to each one his work, and also commanded the doorkeeper to keep watch.
021335 Watch therefore, for you don't know when the lord of the house is coming, whether at evening, or at midnight, or when the rooster crows, or in the morning;
021336 lest coming suddenly he might find you sleeping.
021337 What I tell you, I tell all: Watch."
021401 It was now two days before the feast of the Passover and the unleavened bread, and the chief priests and the scribes sought how they might seize him by deception, and kill him.
021402 For they said, "Not during the feast, because there might be a riot of the people."
021403 While he was at Bethany, in the house of Simon the leper, as he sat at the table, a woman came having an alabaster jar of ointment of pure nard--very costly. She broke the jar, and poured it over his head.
021404 But there were some who were indignant among themselves, saying, "Why has this ointment been wasted?
021405 For this might have been sold for more than three hundred denarii, and given to the poor." They grumbled against her.
021406 But Jesus said, "Leave her alone. Why do you trouble her? She has done a good work for me.
021407 For you always have the poor with you, and whenever you want to, you can do them good; but you will not always have me.
021408 She has done what she could. She has anointed my body beforehand for the burying.
021409 Most certainly I tell you, wherever this Good News may be preached throughout the whole world, that which this woman has done will also be spoken of for a memorial of her."
021410 Judas Iscariot, who was one of the twelve, went away to the chief priests, that he might deliver him to them.
021411 They, when they heard it, were glad, and promised to give him money. He sought how he might conveniently deliver him.
021412 On the first day of unleavened bread, when they sacrificed the Passover, his disciples asked him, "Where do you want us to go and make ready that you may eat the Passover?"
021413 He sent two of his disciples, and said to them, "Go into the city, and there you will meet a man carrying a pitcher of water. Follow him,
021414 and wherever he enters in, tell the master of the house, 'The Teacher says, "Where is the guest room, where I may eat the Passover with my disciples?"'
021415 He will himself show you a large upper room furnished and ready. Make ready for us there."
021416 His disciples went out, and came into the city, and found things as he had said to them, and they prepared the Passover.
021417 When it was evening he came with the twelve.
021418 As they sat and were eating, Jesus said, "Most certainly I tell you, one of you will betray me--he who eats with me."
021419 They began to be sorrowful, and to ask him one by one, "Surely not I?" And another said, "Surely not I?"
021420 He answered them, "It is one of the twelve, he who dips with me in the dish.
021421 For the Son of Man goes, even as it is written about him, but woe to that man by whom the Son of Man is betrayed! It would be better for that man if he had not been born."
021422 As they were eating, Jesus took bread, and when he had blessed, he broke it, and gave to them, and said, "Take, eat. This is my body."
021423 He took the cup, and when he had given thanks, he gave to them. They all drank of it.
021424 He said to them, "This is my blood of the new covenant, which is poured out for many.
021425 Most certainly I tell you, I will no more drink of the fruit of the vine, until that day when I drink it anew in the Kingdom of God."
021426 When they had sung a hymn, they went out to the Mount of Olives.
021427 Jesus said to them, "All of you will be made to stumble because of me tonight, for it is written, 'I will strike the shepherd, and the sheep will be scattered.'
021428 However, after I am raised up, I will go before you into Galilee."
021429 But Peter said to him, "Although all will be offended, yet I will not."
021430 Jesus said to him, "Most certainly I tell you, that you today, even this night, before the rooster crows twice, you will deny me three times."
021431 But he spoke all the more, "If I must die with you, I will not deny you." They all said the same thing.
021432 They came to a place which was named Gethsemane. He said to his disciples, "Sit here, while I pray."
021433 He took with him Peter, James, and John, and began to be greatly troubled and distressed.
021434 He said to them, "My soul is exceedingly sorrowful, even to death. Stay here, and watch."
021435 He went forward a little, and fell on the ground, and prayed that, if it were possible, the hour might pass away from him.
021436 He said, "Abba, Father, all things are possible to you. Please remove this cup from me. However, not what I desire, but what you desire."
021437 He came and found them sleeping, and said to Peter, "Simon, are you sleeping? Couldn't you watch one hour?
021438 Watch and pray, that you may not enter into temptation. The spirit indeed is willing, but the flesh is weak."
021439 Again he went away, and prayed, saying the same words.
021440 Again he returned, and found them sleeping, for their eyes were very heavy, and they didn't know what to answer him.
021441 He came the third time, and said to them, "Sleep on now, and take your rest. It is enough. The hour has come. Behold, the Son of Man is betrayed into the hands of sinners.
021442 Arise, let us be going. Behold, he who betrays me is at hand."
021443 Immediately, while he was still speaking, Judas, one of the twelve, came--and with him a multitude with swords and clubs, from the chief priests, the scribes, and the elders.
021444 Now he who betrayed him had given them a sign, saying, "Whoever I will kiss, that is he. Seize him, and lead him away safely."
021445 When he had come, immediately he came to him, and said, "Rabbi! Rabbi!" and kissed him.
021446 They laid their hands on him, and seized him.
021447 But a certain one of those who stood by drew his sword, and struck the servant of the high priest, and cut off his ear.
021448 Jesus answered them, "Have you come out, as against a robber, with swords and clubs to seize me?
021449 I was daily with you in the temple teaching, and you didn't arrest me. But this is so that the Scriptures might be fulfilled."
021450 They all left him, and fled.
021451 A certain young man followed him, having a linen cloth thrown around himself, over his naked body. The young men grabbed him,
021452 but he left the linen cloth, and fled from them naked.
021453 They led Jesus away to the high priest. All the chief priests, the elders, and the scribes came together with him.
021454 Peter had followed him from a distance, until he came into the court of the high priest. He was sitting with the officers, and warming himself in the light of the fire.
021455 Now the chief priests and the whole council sought witnesses against Jesus to put him to death, and found none.
021456 For many gave false testimony against him, and their testimony didn't agree with each other.
021457 Some stood up, and gave false testimony against him, saying,
021458 "We heard him say, 'I will destroy this temple that is made with hands, and in three days I will build another made without hands.'"
021459 Even so, their testimony did not agree.
021460 The high priest stood up in the midst, and asked Jesus, "Have you no answer? What is it which these testify against you?"
021461 But he stayed quiet, and answered nothing. Again the high priest asked him, "Are you the Christ, the Son of the Blessed?"
021462 Jesus said, "I am. You will see the Son of Man sitting at the right hand of Power, and coming with the clouds of the sky."
021463 The high priest tore his clothes, and said, "What further need have we of witnesses?
021464 You have heard the blasphemy! What do you think?" They all condemned him to be worthy of death.
021465 Some began to spit on him, and to cover his face, and to beat him with fists, and to tell him, "Prophesy!" The officers struck him with the palms of their hands.
021466 As Peter was in the courtyard below, one of the maids of the high priest came,
021467 and seeing Peter warming himself, she looked at him, and said, "You were also with the Nazarene, Jesus!"
021468 But he denied it, saying, "I neither know, nor understand what you are saying." He went out on the porch, and the rooster crowed.
021469 The maid saw him, and began again to tell those who stood by, "This is one of them."
021470 But he again denied it. After a little while again those who stood by said to Peter, "You truly are one of them, for you are a Galilean, and your speech shows it."
021471 But he began to curse, and to swear, "I don't know this man of whom you speak!"
021472 The rooster crowed the second time. Peter remembered the word, how that Jesus said to him, "Before the rooster crows twice, you will deny me three times." When he thought about that, he wept.
021501 Immediately in the morning the chief priests, with the elders and scribes, and the whole council, held a consultation, and bound Jesus, and carried him away, and delivered him up to Pilate.
021502 Pilate asked him, "Are you the King of the Jews?" He answered, "So you say."
021503 The chief priests accused him of many things.
021504 Pilate again asked him, "Have you no answer? See how many things they testify against you!"
021505 But Jesus made no further answer, so that Pilate marveled.
021506 Now at the feast he used to release to them one prisoner, whom they asked of him.
021507 There was one called Barabbas, bound with those who had made insurrection, men who in the insurrection had committed murder.
021508 The multitude, crying aloud, began to ask him to do as he always did for them.
021509 Pilate answered them, saying, "Do you want me to release to you the King of the Jews?"
021510 For he perceived that for envy the chief priests had delivered him up.
021511 But the chief priests stirred up the multitude, that he should release Barabbas to them instead.
021512 Pilate again asked them, "What then should I do to him whom you call the King of the Jews?"
021513 They cried out again, "Crucify him!"
021514 Pilate said to them, "Why, what evil has he done?" But they cried out exceedingly, "Crucify him!"
021515 Pilate, wishing to please the multitude, released Barabbas to them, and handed over Jesus, when he had flogged him, to be crucified.
021516 The soldiers led him away within the court, which is the Praetorium; and they called together the whole cohort.
021517 They clothed him with purple, and weaving a crown of thorns, they put it on him.
021518 They began to salute him, "Hail, King of the Jews!"
021519 They struck his head with a reed, and spat on him, and bowing their knees, did homage to him.
021520 When they had mocked him, they took the purple off of him, and put his own garments on him. They led him out to crucify him.
021521 They compelled one passing by, coming from the country, Simon of Cyrene, the father of Alexander and Rufus, to go with them, that he might bear his cross.
021522 They brought him to the place called Golgotha, which is, being interpreted, "The place of a skull."
021523 They offered him wine mixed with myrrh to drink, but he didn't take it.
021524 Crucifying him, they parted his garments among them, casting lots on them, what each should take.
021525 It was the third hour, and they crucified him.
021526 The superscription of his accusation was written over him, "THE KING OF THE JEWS."
021527 With him they crucified two robbers; one on his right hand, and one on his left.
021528 The Scripture was fulfilled, which says, "He was numbered with transgressors."
021529 Those who passed by blasphemed him, wagging their heads, and saying, "Ha! You who destroy the temple, and build it in three days,
021530 save yourself, and come down from the cross!"
021531 Likewise, also the chief priests mocking among themselves with the scribes said, "He saved others. He can't save himself.
021532 Let the Christ, the King of Israel, now come down from the cross, that we may see and believe him." Those who were crucified with him insulted him.
021533 When the sixth hour had come, there was darkness over the whole land until the ninth hour.
021534 At the ninth hour Jesus cried with a loud voice, saying, "Eloi, Eloi, lama sabachthani?" which is, being interpreted, "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?"
021535 Some of those who stood by, when they heard it, said, "Behold, he is calling Elijah."
021536 One ran, and filling a sponge full of vinegar, put it on a reed, and gave it to him to drink, saying, "Let him be. Let's see whether Elijah comes to take him down."
021537 Jesus cried out with a loud voice, and gave up the spirit.
021538 The veil of the temple was torn in two from the top to the bottom.
021539 When the centurion, who stood by opposite him, saw that he cried out like this and breathed his last, he said, "Truly this man was the Son of God!"
021540 There were also women watching from afar, among whom were both Mary Magdalene, and Mary the mother of James the less and of Joses, and Salome;
021541 who, when he was in Galilee, followed him, and served him; and many other women who came up with him to Jerusalem.
021542 When evening had now come, because it was the Preparation Day, that is, the day before the Sabbath,
021543 Joseph of Arimathaea, a prominent council member who also himself was looking for the Kingdom of God, came. He boldly went in to Pilate, and asked for Jesus' body.
021544 Pilate marveled if he were already dead; and summoning the centurion, he asked him whether he had been dead long.
021545 When he found out from the centurion, he granted the body to Joseph.
021546 He bought a linen cloth, and taking him down, wound him in the linen cloth, and laid him in a tomb which had been cut out of a rock. He rolled a stone against the door of the tomb.
021547 Mary Magdalene and Mary, the mother of Joses, saw where he was laid.
021601 When the Sabbath was past, Mary Magdalene, and Mary the mother of James, and Salome, bought spices, that they might come and anoint him.
021602 Very early on the first day of the week, they came to the tomb when the sun had risen.
021603 They were saying among themselves, "Who will roll away the stone from the door of the tomb for us?"
021604 for it was very big. Looking up, they saw that the stone was rolled back.
021605 Entering into the tomb, they saw a young man sitting on the right side, dressed in a white robe, and they were amazed.
021606 He said to them, "Don't be amazed. You seek Jesus, the Nazarene, who has been crucified. He has risen. He is not here. Behold, the place where they laid him!
021607 But go, tell his disciples and Peter, 'He goes before you into Galilee. There you will see him, as he said to you.'"
021608 They went out, and fled from the tomb, for trembling and astonishment had come on them. They said nothing to anyone; for they were afraid.
021609 Now when he had risen early on the first day of the week, he appeared first to Mary Magdalene, from whom he had cast out seven demons.
021610 She went and told those who had been with him, as they mourned and wept.
021611 When they heard that he was alive, and had been seen by her, they disbelieved.
021612 After these things he was revealed in another form to two of them, as they walked, on their way into the country.
021613 They went away and told it to the rest. They didn't believe them, either.
021614 Afterward he was revealed to the eleven themselves as they sat at the table, and he rebuked them for their unbelief and hardness of heart, because they didn't believe those who had seen him after he had risen.
021615 He said to them, "Go into all the world, and preach the Good News to the whole creation.
021616 He who believes and is baptized will be saved; but he who disbelieves will be condemned.
021617 These signs will accompany those who believe: in my name they will cast out demons; they will speak with new languages;
021618 they will take up serpents; and if they drink any deadly thing, it will in no way hurt them; they will lay hands on the sick, and they will recover."
021619 So then the Lord Jesus, after he had spoken to them, was received up into heaven, and sat down at the right hand of God.
021620 They went out, and preached everywhere, the Lord working with them, and confirming the word by the signs that followed. Amen.
030101 Since many have undertaken to set in order a narrative concerning those matters which have been fulfilled among us,
030102 even as those who from the beginning were eyewitnesses and servants of the word delivered them to us,
030103 it seemed good to me also, having traced the course of all things accurately from the first, to write to you in order, most excellent Theophilus;
030104 that you might know the certainty concerning the things in which you were instructed.
030105 There was in the days of Herod, the king of Judea, a certain priest named Zacharias, of the priestly division of Abijah. He had a wife of the daughters of Aaron, and her name was Elizabeth.
030106 They were both righteous before God, walking blamelessly in all the commandments and ordinances of the Lord.
030107 But they had no child, because Elizabeth was barren, and they both were well advanced in years.
030108 Now it happened, while he executed the priest's office before God in the order of his division,
030109 according to the custom of the priest's office, his lot was to enter into the temple of the Lord and burn incense.
030110 The whole multitude of the people were praying outside at the hour of incense.
030111 An angel of the Lord appeared to him, standing on the right side of the altar of incense.
030112 Zacharias was troubled when he saw him, and fear fell upon him.
030113 But the angel said to him, "Don't be afraid, Zacharias, because your request has been heard, and your wife, Elizabeth, will bear you a son, and you shall call his name John.
030114 You will have joy and gladness; and many will rejoice at his birth.
030115 For he will be great in the sight of the Lord, and he will drink no wine nor strong drink. He will be filled with the Holy Spirit, even from his mother's womb.
030116 He will turn many of the children of Israel to the Lord, their God.
030117 He will go before him in the spirit and power of Elijah, 'to turn the hearts of the fathers to the children,' and the disobedient to the wisdom of the just; to make ready a people prepared for the Lord."
030118 Zacharias said to the angel, "How can I be sure of this? For I am an old man, and my wife is well advanced in years."
030119 The angel answered him, "I am Gabriel, who stands in the presence of God. I was sent to speak to you, and to bring you this good news.
030120 Behold, you will be silent and not able to speak, until the day that these things will happen, because you didn't believe my words, which will be fulfilled in their proper time."
030121 The people were waiting for Zacharias, and they marveled that he delayed in the temple.
030122 When he came out, he could not speak to them, and they perceived that he had seen a vision in the temple. He continued making signs to them, and remained mute.
030123 It happened, when the days of his service were fulfilled, he departed to his house.
030124 After these days Elizabeth, his wife, conceived, and she hid herself five months, saying,
030125 "Thus has the Lord done to me in the days in which he looked at me, to take away my reproach among men."
030126 Now in the sixth month, the angel Gabriel was sent from God to a city of Galilee, named Nazareth,
030127 to a virgin pledged to be married to a man whose name was Joseph, of the house of David. The virgin's name was Mary.
030128 Having come in, the angel said to her, "Rejoice, you highly favored one! The Lord is with you. Blessed are you among women!"
030129 But when she saw him, she was greatly troubled at the saying, and considered what kind of salutation this might be.
030130 The angel said to her, "Don't be afraid, Mary, for you have found favor with God.
030131 Behold, you will conceive in your womb, and bring forth a son, and will call his name 'Jesus.'
030132 He will be great, and will be called the Son of the Most High. The Lord God will give him the throne of his father, David,
030133 and he will reign over the house of Jacob forever. There will be no end to his Kingdom."
030134 Mary said to the angel, "How can this be, seeing I am a virgin?"
030135 The angel answered her, "The Holy Spirit will come on you, and the power of the Most High will overshadow you. Therefore also the holy one who is born from you will be called the Son of God.
030136 Behold, Elizabeth, your relative, also has conceived a son in her old age; and this is the sixth month with her who was called barren.
030137 For everything spoken by God is possible."
030138 Mary said, "Behold, the handmaid of the Lord; be it to me according to your word." The angel departed from her.
030139 Mary arose in those days and went into the hill country with haste, into a city of Judah,
030140 and entered into the house of Zacharias and greeted Elizabeth.
030141 It happened, when Elizabeth heard Mary's greeting, that the baby leaped in her womb, and Elizabeth was filled with the Holy Spirit.
030142 She called out with a loud voice, and said, "Blessed are you among women, and blessed is the fruit of your womb!
030143 Why am I so favored, that the mother of my Lord should come to me?
030144 For behold, when the voice of your greeting came into my ears, the baby leaped in my womb for joy!
030145 Blessed is she who believed, for there will be a fulfillment of the things which have been spoken to her from the Lord!"
030146 Mary said, "My soul magnifies the Lord.
030147 My spirit has rejoiced in God my Savior,
030148 for he has looked at the humble state of his handmaid. For behold, from now on, all generations will call me blessed.
030149 For he who is mighty has done great things for me. Holy is his name.
030150 His mercy is for generations of generations on those who fear him.
030151 He has shown strength with his arm. He has scattered the proud in the imagination of their hearts.
030152 He has put down princes from their thrones. And has exalted the lowly.
030153 He has filled the hungry with good things. He has sent the rich away empty.
030154 He has given help to Israel, his servant, that he might remember mercy,
030155 As he spoke to our fathers, to Abraham and his seed forever."
030156 Mary stayed with her about three months, and then returned to her house.
030157 Now the time that Elizabeth should give birth was fulfilled, and she brought forth a son.
030158 Her neighbors and her relatives heard that the Lord had magnified his mercy towards her, and they rejoiced with her.
030159 It happened on the eighth day, that they came to circumcise the child; and they would have called him Zacharias, after the name of the father.
030160 His mother answered, "Not so; but he will be called John."
030161 They said to her, "There is no one among your relatives who is called by this name."
030162 They made signs to his father, what he would have him called.
030163 He asked for a writing tablet, and wrote, "His name is John." They all marveled.
030164 His mouth was opened immediately, and his tongue freed, and he spoke, blessing God.
030165 Fear came on all who lived around them, and all these sayings were talked about throughout all the hill country of Judea.
030166 All who heard them laid them up in their heart, saying, "What then will this child be?" The hand of the Lord was with him.
030167 His father, Zacharias, was filled with the Holy Spirit, and prophesied, saying,
030168 "Blessed be the Lord, the God of Israel, for he has visited and worked redemption for his people;
030169 and has raised up a horn of salvation for us in the house of his servant David
030170 (as he spoke by the mouth of his holy prophets who have been from of old),
030171 salvation from our enemies, and from the hand of all who hate us;
030172 to show mercy towards our fathers, to remember his holy covenant,
030173 the oath which he spoke to Abraham, our father,
030174 to grant to us that we, being delivered out of the hand of our enemies, should serve him without fear,
030175 In holiness and righteousness before him all the days of our life.
030176 And you, child, will be called a prophet of the Most High, for you will go before the face of the Lord to make ready his ways,
030177 to give knowledge of salvation to his people by the remission of their sins,
030178 because of the tender mercy of our God, whereby the dawn from on high will visit us,
030179 to shine on those who sit in darkness and the shadow of death; to guide our feet into the way of peace."
030180 The child was growing, and becoming strong in spirit, and was in the desert until the day of his public appearance to Israel.
030201 Now it happened in those days, that a decree went out from Caesar Augustus that all the world should be enrolled.
030202 This was the first enrollment made when Quirinius was governor of Syria.
030203 All went to enroll themselves, everyone to his own city.
030204 Joseph also went up from Galilee, out of the city of Nazareth, into Judea, to the city of David, which is called Bethlehem, because he was of the house and family of David;
030205 to enroll himself with Mary, who was pledged to be married to him as wife, being pregnant.
030206 It happened, while they were there, that the day had come that she should give birth.
030207 She brought forth her firstborn son, and she wrapped him in bands of cloth, and laid him in a feeding trough, because there was no room for them in the inn.
030208 There were shepherds in the same country staying in the field, and keeping watch by night over their flock.
030209 Behold, an angel of the Lord stood by them, and the glory of the Lord shone around them, and they were terrified.
030210 The angel said to them, "Don't be afraid, for behold, I bring you good news of great joy which will be to all the people.
030211 For there is born to you, this day, in the city of David, a Savior, who is Christ the Lord.
030212 This is the sign to you: you will find a baby wrapped in strips of cloth, lying in a feeding trough."
030213 Suddenly, there was with the angel a multitude of the heavenly army praising God, and saying,
030214 "Glory to God in the highest, on earth peace, good will toward men."
030215 It happened, when the angels went away from them into the sky, that the shepherds said one to another, "Let's go to Bethlehem, now, and see this thing that has happened, which the Lord has made known to us."
030216 They came with haste, and found both Mary and Joseph, and the baby was lying in the feeding trough.
030217 When they saw it, they publicized widely the saying which was spoken to them about this child.
030218 All who heard it wondered at the things which were spoken to them by the shepherds.
030219 But Mary kept all these sayings, pondering them in her heart.
030220 The shepherds returned, glorifying and praising God for all the things that they had heard and seen, just as it was told them.
030221 When eight days were fulfilled for the circumcision of the child, his name was called Jesus, which was given by the angel before he was conceived in the womb.
030222 When the days of their purification according to the law of Moses were fulfilled, they brought him up to Jerusalem, to present him to the Lord
030223 (as it is written in the law of the Lord, "Every male who opens the womb shall be called holy to the Lord"),
030224 and to offer a sacrifice according to that which is said in the law of the Lord, "A pair of turtledoves, or two young pigeons."
030225 Behold, there was a man in Jerusalem whose name was Simeon. This man was righteous and devout, looking for the consolation of Israel, and the Holy Spirit was on him.
030226 It had been revealed to him by the Holy Spirit that he should not see death before he had seen the Lord's Christ.
030227 He came in the Spirit into the temple. When the parents brought in the child, Jesus, that they might do concerning him according to the custom of the law,
030228 then he received him into his arms, and blessed God, and said,
030229 "Now you are releasing your servant, Master, according to your word, in peace;
030230 for my eyes have seen your salvation,
030231 which you have prepared before the face of all peoples;
030232 a light for revelation to the nations, and the glory of your people Israel."
030233 Joseph and his mother were marveling at the things which were spoken concerning him,
030234 and Simeon blessed them, and said to Mary, his mother, "Behold, this child is set for the falling and the rising of many in Israel, and for a sign which is spoken against.
030235 Yes, a sword will pierce through your own soul, that the thoughts of many hearts may be revealed."
030236 There was one Anna, a prophetess, the daughter of Phanuel, of the tribe of Asher (she was of a great age, having lived with a husband seven years from her virginity,
030237 and she had been a widow for about eighty-four years), who didn't depart from the temple, worshipping with fastings and petitions night and day.
030238 Coming up at that very hour, she gave thanks to the Lord, and spoke of him to all those who were looking for redemption in Jerusalem.
030239 When they had accomplished all things that were according to the law of the Lord, they returned into Galilee, to their own city, Nazareth.
030240 The child was growing, and was becoming strong in spirit, being filled with wisdom, and the grace of God was upon him.
030241 His parents went every year to Jerusalem at the feast of the Passover.
030242 When he was twelve years old, they went up to Jerusalem according to the custom of the feast,
030243 and when they had fulfilled the days, as they were returning, the boy Jesus stayed behind in Jerusalem. Joseph and his mother didn't know it,
030244 but supposing him to be in the company, they went a day's journey, and they looked for him among their relatives and acquaintances.
030245 When they didn't find him, they returned to Jerusalem, looking for him.
030246 It happened after three days they found him in the temple, sitting in the midst of the teachers, both listening to them, and asking them questions.
030247 All who heard him were amazed at his understanding and his answers.
030248 When they saw him, they were astonished, and his mother said to him, "Son, why have you treated us this way? Behold, your father and I were anxiously looking for you."
030249 He said to them, "Why were you looking for me? Didn't you know that I must be in my Father's house?"
030250 They didn't understand the saying which he spoke to them.
030251 And he went down with them, and came to Nazareth. He was subject to them, and his mother kept all these sayings in her heart.
030252 And Jesus increased in wisdom and stature, and in favor with God and men.
030301 Now in the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiberius Caesar, Pontius Pilate being governor of Judea, and Herod being tetrarch of Galilee, and his brother Philip tetrarch of the region of Ituraea and Trachonitis, and Lysanias tetrarch of Abilene,
030302 in the high priesthood of Annas and Caiaphas, the word of God came to John, the son of Zacharias, in the wilderness.
030303 He came into all the region around the Jordan, preaching the baptism of repentance for remission of sins.
030304 As it is written in the book of the words of Isaiah the prophet, "The voice of one crying in the wilderness, 'Make ready the way of the Lord. Make his paths straight.
030305 Every valley will be filled. Every mountain and hill will be brought low. The crooked will become straight, and the rough ways smooth.
030306 All flesh will see God's salvation.'"
030307 He said therefore to the multitudes who went out to be baptized by him, "You offspring of vipers, who warned you to flee from the wrath to come?
030308 Bring forth therefore fruits worthy of repentance, and don't begin to say among yourselves, 'We have Abraham for our father;' for I tell you that God is able to raise up children to Abraham from these stones!
030309 Even now the axe also lies at the root of the trees. Every tree therefore that doesn't bring forth good fruit is cut down, and thrown into the fire."
030310 The multitudes asked him, "What then must we do?"
030311 He answered them, "He who has two coats, let him give to him who has none. He who has food, let him do likewise."
030312 Tax collectors also came to be baptized, and they said to him, "Teacher, what must we do?"
030313 He said to them, "Collect no more than that which is appointed to you."
030314 Soldiers also asked him, saying, "What about us? What must we do?" He said to them, "Extort from no one by violence, neither accuse anyone wrongfully. Be content with your wages."
030315 As the people were in expectation, and all men reasoned in their hearts concerning John, whether perhaps he was the Christ,
030316 John answered them all, "I indeed baptize you with water, but he comes who is mightier than I, the latchet of whose sandals I am not worthy to loosen. He will baptize you in the Holy Spirit and fire,
030317 whose fan is in his hand, and he will thoroughly cleanse his threshing floor, and will gather the wheat into his barn; but he will burn up the chaff with unquenchable fire."
030318 Then with many other exhortations he preached good news to the people,
030319 but Herod the tetrarch, being reproved by him for Herodias, his brother's wife, and for all the evil things which Herod had done,
030320 added this also to them all, that he shut up John in prison.
030321 Now it happened, when all the people were baptized, Jesus also had been baptized, and was praying. The sky was opened,
030322 and the Holy Spirit descended in a bodily form as a dove on him; and a voice came out of the sky, saying "You are my beloved Son. In you I am well pleased."
030323 Jesus himself, when he began to teach, was about thirty years old, being the son (as was supposed) of Joseph, the son of Heli,
030324 the son of Matthat, the son of Levi, the son of Melchi, the son of Jannai, the son of Joseph,
030325 the son of Mattathias, the son of Amos, the son of Nahum, the son of Esli, the son of Naggai,
030326 the son of Maath, the son of Mattathias, the son of Semein, the son of Joseph, the son of Judah,
030327 the son of Joanan, the son of Rhesa, the son of Zerubbabel, the son of Shealtiel, the son of Neri,
030328 the son of Melchi, the son of Addi, the son of Cosam, the son of Elmodam, the son of Er,
030329 the son of Jose, the son of Eliezer, the son of Jorim, the son of Matthat, the son of Levi,
030330 the son of Simeon, the son of Judah, the son of Joseph, the son of Jonan, the son of Eliakim,
030331 the son of Melea, the son of Menan, the son of Mattatha, the son of Nathan, the son of David,
030332 the son of Jesse, the son of Obed, the son of Boaz, the son of Salmon, the son of Nahshon,
030333 the son of Amminadab, the son of Aram, the son of Hezron, the son of Perez, the son of Judah,
030334 the son of Jacob, the son of Isaac, the son of Abraham, the son of Terah, the son of Nahor,
030335 the son of Serug, the son of Reu, the son of Peleg, the son of Eber, the son of Shelah,
030336 the son of Cainan, the son of Arphaxad, the son of Shem, the son of Noah, the son of Lamech,
030337 the son of Methuselah, the son of Enoch, the son of Jared, the son of Mahalaleel, the son of Cainan,
030338 the son of Enos, the son of Seth, the son of Adam, the son of God.
030401 Jesus, full of the Holy Spirit, returned from the Jordan, and was led by the Spirit into the wilderness
030402 for forty days, being tempted by the devil. He ate nothing in those days. Afterward, when they were completed, he was hungry.
030403 The devil said to him, "If you are the Son of God, command this stone to become bread."
030404 Jesus answered him, saying, "It is written, 'Man shall not live by bread alone, but by every word of God.'"
030405 The devil, leading him up on a high mountain, showed him all the kingdoms of the world in a moment of time.
030406 The devil said to him, "I will give you all this authority, and their glory, for it has been delivered to me; and I give it to whomever I want.
030407 If you therefore will worship before me, it will all be yours."
030408 Jesus answered him, "Get behind me Satan! For it is written, 'You shall worship the Lord your God, and you shall serve him only.'"
030409 He led him to Jerusalem, and set him on the pinnacle of the temple, and said to him, "If you are the Son of God, cast yourself down from here,
030410 for it is written, 'He will put his angels in charge of you, to guard you;'
030411 and, 'On their hands they will bear you up, lest perhaps you dash your foot against a stone.'"
030412 Jesus answering, said to him, "It has been said, 'You shall not tempt the Lord your God.'"
030413 When the devil had completed every temptation, he departed from him until another time.
030414 Jesus returned in the power of the Spirit into Galilee, and news about him spread through all the surrounding area.
030415 He taught in their synagogues, being glorified by all.
030416 He came to Nazareth, where he had been brought up. He entered, as was his custom, into the synagogue on the Sabbath day, and stood up to read.
030417 The book of the prophet Isaiah was handed to him. He opened the book, and found the place where it was written,
030418 "The Spirit of the Lord is on me, because he has anointed me to preach good news to the poor. He has sent me to heal the brokenhearted, to proclaim release to the captives, recovering of sight to the blind, to deliver those who are crushed,
030419 and to proclaim the acceptable year of the Lord."
030420 He closed the book, gave it back to the attendant, and sat down. The eyes of all in the synagogue were fastened on him.
030421 He began to tell them, "Today, this Scripture has been fulfilled in your hearing."
030422 All testified about him, and wondered at the gracious words which proceeded out of his mouth, and they said, "Isn't this Joseph's son?"
030423 He said to them, "Doubtless you will tell me this parable, 'Physician, heal yourself! Whatever we have heard done at Capernaum, do also here in your hometown.'"
030424 He said, "Most certainly I tell you, no prophet is acceptable in his hometown.
030425 But truly I tell you, there were many widows in Israel in the days of Elijah, when the sky was shut up three years and six months, when a great famine came over all the land.
030426 Elijah was sent to none of them, except to Zarephath, in the land of Sidon, to a woman who was a widow.
030427 There were many lepers in Israel in the time of Elisha the prophet, yet not one of them was cleansed, except Naaman, the Syrian."
030428 They were all filled with wrath in the synagogue, as they heard these things.
030429 They rose up, threw him out of the city, and led him to the brow of the hill that their city was built on, that they might throw him off the cliff.
030430 But he, passing through the midst of them, went his way.
030431 He came down to Capernaum, a city of Galilee. He was teaching them on the Sabbath day,
030432 and they were astonished at his teaching, for his word was with authority.
030433 In the synagogue there was a man who had a spirit of an unclean demon, and he cried out with a loud voice,
030434 saying, "Ah! what have we to do with you, Jesus of Nazareth? Have you come to destroy us? I know you who you are: the Holy One of God!"
030435 Jesus rebuked him, saying, "Be silent, and come out of him!" When the demon had thrown him down in their midst, he came out of him, having done him no harm.
030436 Amazement came on all, and they spoke together, one with another, saying, "What is this word? For with authority and power he commands the unclean spirits, and they come out!"
030437 News about him went out into every place of the surrounding region.
030438 He rose up from the synagogue, and entered into Simon's house. Simon's mother-in-law was afflicted with a great fever, and they begged him for her.
030439 He stood over her, and rebuked the fever; and it left her. Immediately she rose up and served them.
030440 When the sun was setting, all those who had any sick with various diseases brought them to him; and he laid his hands on every one of them, and healed them.
030441 Demons also came out from many, crying out, and saying, "You are the Christ, the Son of God!" Rebuking them, he didn't allow them to speak, because they knew that he was the Christ.
030442 When it was day, he departed and went into an uninhabited place, and the multitudes looked for him, and came to him, and held on to him, so that he wouldn't go away from them.
030443 But he said to them, "I must preach the good news of the Kingdom of God to the other cities also. For this reason I have been sent."
030444 He was preaching in the synagogues of Galilee.
030501 Now it happened, while the multitude pressed on him and heard the word of God, that he was standing by the lake of Gennesaret.
030502 He saw two boats standing by the lake, but the fishermen had gone out of them, and were washing their nets.
030503 He entered into one of the boats, which was Simon's, and asked him to put out a little from the land. He sat down and taught the multitudes from the boat.
030504 When he had finished speaking, he said to Simon, "Put out into the deep, and let down your nets for a catch."
030505 Simon answered him, "Master, we worked all night, and took nothing; but at your word I will let down the net."
030506 When they had done this, they caught a great multitude of fish, and their net was breaking.
030507 They beckoned to their partners in the other boat, that they should come and help them. They came, and filled both boats, so that they began to sink.
030508 But Simon Peter, when he saw it, fell down at Jesus' knees, saying, "Depart from me, for I am a sinful man, Lord."
030509 For he was amazed, and all who were with him, at the catch of fish which they had caught;
030510 and so also were James and John, sons of Zebedee, who were partners with Simon. Jesus said to Simon, "Don't be afraid. From now on you will be catching people alive."
030511 When they had brought their boats to land, they left everything, and followed him.
030512 It happened, while he was in one of the cities, behold, there was a man full of leprosy. When he saw Jesus, he fell on his face, and begged him, saying, "Lord, if you want to, you can make me clean."
030513 He stretched out his hand, and touched him, saying, "I want to. Be made clean." Immediately the leprosy left him.
030514 He commanded him to tell no one, "But go your way, and show yourself to the priest, and offer for your cleansing according to what Moses commanded, for a testimony to them."
030515 But the report concerning him spread much more, and great multitudes came together to hear, and to be healed by him of their infirmities.
030516 But he withdrew himself into the desert, and prayed.
030517 It happened on one of those days, that he was teaching; and there were Pharisees and teachers of the law sitting by, who had come out of every village of Galilee, Judea, and Jerusalem. The power of the Lord was with him to heal them.
030518 Behold, men brought a paralyzed man on a cot, and they sought to bring him in to lay before Jesus.
030519 Not finding a way to bring him in because of the multitude, they went up to the housetop, and let him down through the tiles with his cot into the midst before Jesus.
030520 Seeing their faith, he said to him, "Man, your sins are forgiven you."
030521 The scribes and the Pharisees began to reason, saying, "Who is this that speaks blasphemies? Who can forgive sins, but God alone?"
030522 But Jesus, perceiving their thoughts, answered them, "Why are you reasoning so in your hearts?
030523 Which is easier to say, 'Your sins are forgiven you;' or to say, 'Arise and walk?'
030524 But that you may know that the Son of Man has authority on earth to forgive sins" (he said to the paralyzed man), "I tell you, arise, and take up your cot, and go to your house."
030525 Immediately he rose up before them, and took up that which he was laying on, and departed to his house, glorifying God.
030526 Amazement took hold on all, and they glorified God. They were filled with fear, saying, "We have seen strange things today."
030527 After these things he went out, and saw a tax collector named Levi sitting at the tax office, and said to him, "Follow me!"
030528 He left everything, and rose up and followed him.
030529 Levi made a great feast for him in his house. There was a great crowd of tax collectors and others who were reclining with them.
030530 Their scribes and the Pharisees murmured against his disciples, saying, "Why do you eat and drink with the tax collectors and sinners?"
030531 Jesus answered them, "Those who are healthy have no need for a physician, but those who are sick do.
030532 I have not come to call the righteous, but sinners to repentance."
030533 They said to him, "Why do John's disciples often fast and pray, likewise also the disciples of the Pharisees, but yours eat and drink?"
030534 He said to them, "Can you make the friends of the bridegroom fast, while the bridegroom is with them?
030535 But the days will come when the bridegroom will be taken away from them. Then they will fast in those days."
030536 He also told a parable to them. "No one puts a piece from a new garment on an old garment, or else he will tear the new, and also the piece from the new will not match the old.
030537 No one puts new wine into old wineskins, or else the new wine will burst the skins, and it will be spilled, and the skins will be destroyed.
030538 But new wine must be put into fresh wineskins, and both are preserved.
030539 No man having drunk old wine immediately desires new, for he says, 'The old is better.'"
030601 Now it happened on the second Sabbath after the first, that he was going through the grain fields. His disciples plucked the heads of grain, and ate, rubbing them in their hands.
030602 But some of the Pharisees said to them, "Why do you do that which is not lawful to do on the Sabbath day?"
030603 Jesus, answering them, said, "Haven't you read what David did when he was hungry, he, and those who were with him;
030604 how he entered into the house of God, and took and ate the show bread, and gave also to those who were with him, which is not lawful to eat except for the priests alone?"
030605 He said to them, "The Son of Man is lord of the Sabbath."
030606 It also happened on another Sabbath that he entered into the synagogue and taught. There was a man there, and his right hand was withered.
