030607 The scribes and the Pharisees watched him, to see whether he would heal on the Sabbath, that they might find an accusation against him.
030608 But he knew their thoughts; and he said to the man who had the withered hand, "Rise up, and stand in the middle." He arose and stood.
030609 Then Jesus said to them, "I will ask you something: Is it lawful on the Sabbath to do good, or to do harm? To save a life, or to kill?"
030610 He looked around at them all, and said to the man, "Stretch out your hand." He did, and his hand was restored as sound as the other.
030611 But they were filled with rage, and talked with one another about what they might do to Jesus.
030612 It happened in these days, that he went out to the mountain to pray, and he continued all night in prayer to God.
030613 When it was day, he called his disciples, and from them he chose twelve, whom he also named apostles:
030614 Simon, whom he also named Peter; Andrew, his brother; James; John; Philip; Bartholomew;
030615 Matthew; Thomas; James, the son of Alphaeus; Simon, who was called the Zealot;
030616 Judas the son of James; and Judas Iscariot, who also became a traitor.
030617 He came down with them, and stood on a level place, with a crowd of his disciples, and a great number of the people from all Judea and Jerusalem, and the sea coast of Tyre and Sidon, who came to hear him and to be healed of their diseases;
030618 as well as those who were troubled by unclean spirits, and they were being healed.
030619 All the multitude sought to touch him, for power came out from him and healed them all.
030620 He lifted up his eyes to his disciples, and said, "Blessed are you who are poor, for yours is the Kingdom of God.
030621 Blessed are you who hunger now, for you will be filled. Blessed are you who weep now, for you will laugh.
030622 Blessed are you when men shall hate you, and when they shall exclude and mock you, and throw out your name as evil, for the Son of Man's sake.
030623 Rejoice in that day, and leap for joy, for behold, your reward is great in heaven, for their fathers did the same thing to the prophets.
030624 "But woe to you who are rich! For you have received your consolation.
030625 Woe to you, you who are full now, for you will be hungry. Woe to you who laugh now, for you will mourn and weep.
030626 Woe, when men speak well of you, for their fathers did the same thing to the false prophets.
030627 "But I tell you who hear: love your enemies, do good to those who hate you,
030628 bless those who curse you, and pray for those who mistreat you.
030629 To him who strikes you on the cheek, offer also the other; and from him who takes away your cloak, don't withhold your coat also.
030630 Give to everyone who asks you, and don't ask him who takes away your goods to give them back again.
030631 "As you would like people to do to you, do exactly so to them.
030632 If you love those who love you, what credit is that to you? For even sinners love those who love them.
030633 If you do good to those who do good to you, what credit is that to you? For even sinners do the same.
030634 If you lend to those from whom you hope to receive, what credit is that to you? Even sinners lend to sinners, to receive back as much.
030635 But love your enemies, and do good, and lend, expecting nothing back; and your reward will be great, and you will be children of the Most High; for he is kind toward the unthankful and evil.
030636 Therefore be merciful, even as your Father is also merciful.
030637 Don't judge, and you won't be judged. Don't condemn, and you won't be condemned. Set free, and you will be set free.
030638 "Give, and it will be given to you: good measure, pressed down, shaken together, and running over, will be given to you. For with the same measure you measure it will be measured back to you."
030639 He spoke a parable to them. "Can the blind guide the blind? Won't they both fall into a pit?
030640 A disciple is not above his teacher, but everyone when he is fully trained will be like his teacher.
030641 Why do you see the speck of chaff that is in your brother's eye, but don't consider the beam that is in your own eye?
030642 Or how can you tell your brother, 'Brother, let me remove the speck of chaff that is in your eye,' when you yourself don't see the beam that is in your own eye? You hypocrite! First remove the beam from your own eye, and then you can see clearly to remove the speck of chaff that is in your brother's eye.
030643 For there is no good tree that brings forth rotten fruit; nor again a rotten tree that brings forth good fruit.
030644 For each tree is known by its own fruit. For people don't gather figs from thorns, nor do they gather grapes from a bramble bush.
030645 The good man out of the good treasure of his heart brings out that which is good, and the evil man out of the evil treasure of his heart brings out that which is evil, for out of the abundance of the heart, his mouth speaks.
030646 "Why do you call me, 'Lord, Lord,' and don't do the things which I say?
030647 Everyone who comes to me, and hears my words, and does them, I will show you who he is like.
030648 He is like a man building a house, who dug and went deep, and laid a foundation on the rock. When a flood arose, the stream broke against that house, and could not shake it, because it was founded on the rock.
030649 But he who hears, and doesn't do, is like a man who built a house on the earth without a foundation, against which the stream broke, and immediately it fell, and the ruin of that house was great."
030701 After he had finished speaking in the hearing of the people, he entered into Capernaum.
030702 A certain centurion's servant, who was dear to him, was sick and at the point of death.
030703 When he heard about Jesus, he sent to him elders of the Jews, asking him to come and save his servant.
030704 When they came to Jesus, they begged him earnestly, saying, "He is worthy for you to do this for him,
030705 for he loves our nation, and he built our synagogue for us."
030706 Jesus went with them. When he was now not far from the house, the centurion sent friends to him, saying to him, "Lord, don't trouble yourself, for I am not worthy for you to come under my roof.
030707 Therefore I didn't even think myself worthy to come to you; but say the word, and my servant will be healed.
030708 For I also am a man placed under authority, having under myself soldiers. I tell this one, 'Go!' and he goes; and to another, 'Come!' and he comes; and to my servant, 'Do this,' and he does it."
030709 When Jesus heard these things, he marveled at him, and turned and said to the multitude who followed him, "I tell you, I have not found such great faith, no, not in Israel."
030710 Those who were sent, returning to the house, found that the servant who had been sick was well.
030711 It happened soon afterwards, that he went to a city called Nain. Many of his disciples, along with a great multitude, went with him.
030712 Now when he drew near to the gate of the city, behold, one who was dead was carried out, the only son of his mother, and she was a widow. Many people of the city were with her.
030713 When the Lord saw her, he had compassion on her, and said to her, "Don't cry."
030714 He came near and touched the coffin, and the bearers stood still. He said, "Young man, I tell you, arise!"
030715 He who was dead sat up, and began to speak. And he gave him to his mother.
030716 Fear took hold of all, and they glorified God, saying, "A great prophet has arisen among us!" and, "God has visited his people!"
030717 This report went out concerning him in the whole of Judea, and in all the surrounding region.
030718 The disciples of John told him about all these things.
030719 John, calling to himself two of his disciples, sent them to Jesus, saying, "Are you the one who is coming, or should we look for another?"
030720 When the men had come to him, they said, "John the Baptizer has sent us to you, saying, 'Are you he who comes, or should we look for another?'"
030721 In that hour he cured many of diseases and plagues and evil spirits; and to many who were blind he gave sight.
030722 Jesus answered them, "Go and tell John the things which you have seen and heard: that the blind receive their sight, the lame walk, the lepers are cleansed, the deaf hear, the dead are raised up, and the poor have good news preached to them.
030723 Blessed is he who is not offended by me."
030724 When John's messengers had departed, he began to tell the multitudes about John, "What did you go out into the wilderness to see? A reed shaken by the wind?
030725 But what did you go out to see? A man clothed in soft clothing? Behold, those who are gorgeously dressed, and live delicately, are in kings' courts.
030726 But what did you go out to see? A prophet? Yes, I tell you, and much more than a prophet.
030727 This is he of whom it is written, 'Behold, I send my messenger before your face, who will prepare your way before you.'
030728 "For I tell you, among those who are born of women there is not a greater prophet than John the Baptizer, yet he who is least in the Kingdom of God is greater than he."
030729 When all the people and the tax collectors heard this, they declared God to be just, having been baptized with John's baptism.
030730 But the Pharisees and the lawyers rejected the counsel of God, not being baptized by him themselves.
030731 "To what then will I liken the people of this generation? What are they like?
030732 They are like children who sit in the marketplace, and call one to another, saying, 'We piped to you, and you didn't dance. We mourned, and you didn't weep.'
030733 For John the Baptizer came neither eating bread nor drinking wine, and you say, 'He has a demon.'
030734 The Son of Man has come eating and drinking, and you say, 'Behold, a gluttonous man, and a drunkard; a friend of tax collectors and sinners!'
030735 Wisdom is justified by all her children."
030736 One of the Pharisees invited him to eat with him. He entered into the Pharisee's house, and sat at the table.
030737 Behold, a woman in the city who was a sinner, when she knew that he was reclining in the Pharisee's house, she brought an alabaster jar of ointment.
030738 Standing behind at his feet weeping, she began to wet his feet with her tears, and she wiped them with the hair of her head, kissed his feet, and anointed them with the ointment.
030739 Now when the Pharisee who had invited him saw it, he said to himself, "This man, if he were a prophet, would have perceived who and what kind of woman this is who touches him, that she is a sinner."
030740 Jesus answered him, "Simon, I have something to tell you." He said, "Teacher, say on."
030741 "A certain lender had two debtors. The one owed five hundred denarii, and the other fifty.
030742 When they couldn't pay, he forgave them both. Which of them therefore will love him most?"
030743 Simon answered, "He, I suppose, to whom he forgave the most." He said to him, "You have judged correctly."
030744 Turning to the woman, he said to Simon, "Do you see this woman? I entered into your house, and you gave me no water for my feet, but she has wet my feet with her tears, and wiped them with the hair of her head.
030745 You gave me no kiss, but she, since the time I came in, has not ceased to kiss my feet.
030746 You didn't anoint my head with oil, but she has anointed my feet with ointment.
030747 Therefore I tell you, her sins, which are many, are forgiven, for she loved much. But to whom little is forgiven, the same loves little."
030748 He said to her, "Your sins are forgiven."
030749 Those who sat at the table with him began to say to themselves, "Who is this who even forgives sins?"
030750 He said to the woman, "Your faith has saved you. Go in peace."
030801 It happened soon afterwards, that he went about through cities and villages, preaching and bringing the good news of the Kingdom of God. With him were the twelve,
030802 and certain women who had been healed of evil spirits and infirmities: Mary who was called Magdalene, from whom seven demons had gone out;
030803 and Joanna, the wife of Chuzas, Herod's steward; Susanna; and many others; who served them from their possessions.
030804 When a great multitude came together, and people from every city were coming to him, he spoke by a parable.
030805 "The farmer went out to sow his seed. As he sowed, some fell along the road, and it was trampled under foot, and the birds of the sky devoured it.
030806 Other seed fell on the rock, and as soon as it grew, it withered away, because it had no moisture.
030807 Other fell amid the thorns, and the thorns grew with it, and choked it.
030808 Other fell into the good ground, and grew, and brought forth fruit one hundred times." As he said these things, he called out, "He who has ears to hear, let him hear!"
030809 Then his disciples asked him, "What does this parable mean?"
030810 He said, "To you it is given to know the mysteries of the Kingdom of God, but to the rest in parables; that 'seeing they may not see, and hearing they may not understand.'
030811 Now the parable is this: The seed is the word of God.
030812 Those along the road are those who hear, then the devil comes, and takes away the word from their heart, that they may not believe and be saved.
030813 Those on the rock are they who, when they hear, receive the word with joy; but these have no root, who believe for a while, then fall away in time of temptation.
030814 That which fell among the thorns, these are those who have heard, and as they go on their way they are choked with cares, riches, and pleasures of life, and bring no fruit to maturity.
030815 That in the good ground, these are such as in an honest and good heart, having heard the word, hold it tightly, and bring forth fruit with patience.
030816 "No one, when he has lit a lamp, covers it with a container, or puts it under a bed; but puts it on a stand, that those who enter in may see the light.
030817 For nothing is hidden, that will not be revealed; nor anything secret, that will not be known and come to light.
030818 Be careful therefore how you hear. For whoever has, to him will be given; and whoever doesn't have, from him will be taken away even that which he thinks he has."
030819 His mother and brothers came to him, and they could not come near him for the crowd.
030820 It was told him by some saying, "Your mother and your brothers stand outside, desiring to see you."
030821 But he answered them, "My mother and my brothers are these who hear the word of God, and do it."
030822 Now it happened on one of those days, that he entered into a boat, himself and his disciples, and he said to them, "Let's go over to the other side of the lake." So they launched out.
030823 But as they sailed, he fell asleep. A wind storm came down on the lake, and they were taking on dangerous amounts of water.
030824 They came to him, and awoke him, saying, "Master, master, we are dying!" He awoke, and rebuked the wind and the raging of the water, and they ceased, and it was calm.
030825 He said to them, "Where is your faith?" Being afraid they marveled, saying one to another, "Who is this, then, that he commands even the winds and the water, and they obey him?"
030826 They arrived at the country of the Gadarenes, which is opposite Galilee.
030827 When Jesus stepped ashore, a certain man out of the city who had demons for a long time met him. He wore no clothes, and didn't live in a house, but in the tombs.
030828 When he saw Jesus, he cried out, and fell down before him, and with a loud voice said, "What do I have to do with you, Jesus, you Son of the Most High God? I beg you, don't torment me!"
030829 For Jesus was commanding the unclean spirit to come out of the man. For the unclean spirit had often seized the man. He was kept under guard, and bound with chains and fetters. Breaking the bands apart, he was driven by the demon into the desert.
030830 Jesus asked him, "What is your name?" He said, "Legion," for many demons had entered into him.
030831 They begged him that he would not command them to go into the abyss.
030832 Now there was there a herd of many pigs feeding on the mountain, and they begged him that he would allow them to enter into those. He allowed them.
030833 The demons came out from the man, and entered into the pigs, and the herd rushed down the steep bank into the lake, and were drowned.
030834 When those who fed them saw what had happened, they fled, and told it in the city and in the country.
030835 People went out to see what had happened. They came to Jesus, and found the man from whom the demons had gone out, sitting at Jesus' feet, clothed and in his right mind; and they were afraid.
030836 Those who saw it told them how he who had been possessed by demons was healed.
030837 All the people of the surrounding country of the Gadarenes asked him to depart from them, for they were very much afraid. He entered into the boat, and returned.
030838 But the man from whom the demons had gone out begged him that he might go with him, but Jesus sent him away, saying,
030839 "Return to your house, and declare what great things God has done for you." He went his way, proclaiming throughout the whole city what great things Jesus had done for him.
030840 It happened, when Jesus returned, that the multitude welcomed him, for they were all waiting for him.
030841 Behold, there came a man named Jairus, and he was a ruler of the synagogue. He fell down at Jesus' feet, and begged him to come into his house,
030842 for he had an only daughter, about twelve years of age, and she was dying. But as he went, the multitudes pressed against him.
030843 A woman who had a flow of blood for twelve years, who had spent all her living on physicians, and could not be healed by any,
030844 came behind him, and touched the fringe of his cloak, and immediately the flow of her blood stopped.
030845 Jesus said, "Who touched me?" When all denied it, Peter and those with him said, "Master, the multitudes press and jostle you, and you say, 'Who touched me?'"
030846 But Jesus said, "Someone did touch me, for I perceived that power has gone out of me."
030847 When the woman saw that she was not hidden, she came trembling, and falling down before him declared to him in the presence of all the people the reason why she had touched him, and how she was healed immediately.
030848 He said to her, "Daughter, cheer up. Your faith has made you well. Go in peace."
030849 While he still spoke, one from the ruler of the synagogue's house came, saying to him, "Your daughter is dead. Don't trouble the Teacher."
030850 But Jesus hearing it, answered him, "Don't be afraid. Only believe, and she will be healed."
030851 When he came to the house, he didn't allow anyone to enter in, except Peter, John, James, the father of the child, and her mother.
030852 All were weeping and mourning her, but he said, "Don't weep. She isn't dead, but sleeping."
030853 They were ridiculing him, knowing that she was dead.
030854 But he put them all outside, and taking her by the hand, he called, saying, "Child, arise!"
030855 Her spirit returned, and she rose up immediately. He commanded that something be given to her to eat.
030856 Her parents were amazed, but he commanded them to tell no one what had been done.
030901 He called the twelve together, and gave them power and authority over all demons, and to cure diseases.
030902 He sent them forth to preach the Kingdom of God, and to heal the sick.
030903 He said to them, "Take nothing for your journey--neither staffs, nor wallet, nor bread, nor money; neither have two coats apiece.
030904 Into whatever house you enter, stay there, and depart from there.
030905 As many as don't receive you, when you depart from that city, shake off even the dust from your feet for a testimony against them."
030906 They departed, and went throughout the villages, preaching the Good News, and healing everywhere.
030907 Now Herod the tetrarch heard of all that was done by him; and he was very perplexed, because it was said by some that John had risen from the dead,
030908 and by some that Elijah had appeared, and by others that one of the old prophets had risen again.
030909 Herod said, "John I beheaded, but who is this, about whom I hear such things?" He sought to see him.
030910 The apostles, when they had returned, told him what things they had done. He took them, and withdrew apart to a deserted place of a city called Bethsaida.
030911 But the multitudes, perceiving it, followed him. He welcomed them, and spoke to them of the Kingdom of God, and he cured those who needed healing.
030912 The day began to wear away; and the twelve came, and said to him, "Send the multitude away, that they may go into the surrounding villages and farms, and lodge, and get food, for we are here in a deserted place."
030913 But he said to them, "You give them something to eat." They said, "We have no more than five loaves and two fish, unless we should go and buy food for all these people."
030914 For they were about five thousand men. He said to his disciples, "Make them sit down in groups of about fifty each."
030915 They did so, and made them all sit down.
030916 He took the five loaves and the two fish, and looking up to the sky, he blessed them, and broke them, and gave them to the disciples to set before the multitude.
030917 They ate, and were all filled. They gathered up twelve baskets of broken pieces that were left over.
030918 It happened, as he was praying alone, that the disciples were with him, and he asked them, "Who do the multitudes say that I am?"
030919 They answered, "'John the Baptizer,' but others say, 'Elijah,' and others, that one of the old prophets is risen again."
030920 He said to them, "But who do you say that I am?" Peter answered, "The Christ of God."
030921 But he warned them, and commanded them to tell this to no one,
030922 saying, "The Son of Man must suffer many things, and be rejected by the elders, chief priests, and scribes, and be killed, and the third day be raised up."
030923 He said to all, "If anyone desires to come after me, let him deny himself, take up his cross, and follow me.
030924 For whoever desires to save his life will lose it, but whoever will lose his life for my sake, the same will save it.
030925 For what does it profit a man if he gains the whole world, and loses or forfeits his own self?
030926 For whoever will be ashamed of me and of my words, of him will the Son of Man be ashamed, when he comes in his glory, and the glory of the Father, and of the holy angels.
030927 But I tell you the truth: There are some of those who stand here, who will in no way taste of death, until they see the Kingdom of God."
030928 It happened about eight days after these sayings, that he took with him Peter, John, and James, and went up onto the mountain to pray.
030929 As he was praying, the appearance of his face was altered, and his clothing became white and dazzling.
030930 Behold, two men were talking with him, who were Moses and Elijah,
030931 who appeared in glory, and spoke of his departure, which he was about to accomplish at Jerusalem.
030932 Now Peter and those who were with him were heavy with sleep, but when they were fully awake, they saw his glory, and the two men who stood with him.
030933 It happened, as they were parting from him, that Peter said to Jesus, "Master, it is good for us to be here. Let's make three tents: one for you, and one for Moses, and one for Elijah," not knowing what he said.
030934 While he said these things, a cloud came and overshadowed them, and they were afraid as they entered into the cloud.
030935 A voice came out of the cloud, saying, "This is my beloved Son. Listen to him!"
030936 When the voice came, Jesus was found alone. They were silent, and told no one in those days any of the things which they had seen.
030937 It happened on the next day, when they had come down from the mountain, that a great multitude met him.
030938 Behold, a man from the crowd called out, saying, "Teacher, I beg you to look at my son, for he is my only child.
030939 Behold, a spirit takes him, he suddenly cries out, and it convulses him so that he foams, and it hardly departs from him, bruising him severely.
030940 I begged your disciples to cast it out, and they couldn't."
030941 Jesus answered, "Faithless and perverse generation, how long shall I be with you and bear with you? Bring your son here."
030942 While he was still coming, the demon threw him down and convulsed him violently. But Jesus rebuked the unclean spirit, and healed the boy, and gave him back to his father.
030943 They were all astonished at the majesty of God. But while all were marveling at all the things which Jesus did, he said to his disciples,
030944 "Let these words sink into your ears, for the Son of Man will be delivered up into the hands of men."
030945 But they didn't understand this saying. It was concealed from them, that they should not perceive it, and they were afraid to ask him about this saying.
030946 There arose an argument among them about which of them was the greatest.
030947 Jesus, perceiving the reasoning of their hearts, took a little child, and set him by his side,
030948 and said to them, "Whoever receives this little child in my name receives me. Whoever receives me receives him who sent me. For whoever is least among you all, this one will be great."
030949 John answered, "Master, we saw someone casting out demons in your name, and we forbade him, because he doesn't follow with us."
030950 Jesus said to him, "Don't forbid him, for he who is not against us is for us."
030951 It came to pass, when the days were near that he should be taken up, he intently set his face to go to Jerusalem,
030952 and sent messengers before his face. They went, and entered into a village of the Samaritans, so as to prepare for him.
030953 They didn't receive him, because he was traveling with his face set towards Jerusalem.
030954 When his disciples, James and John, saw this, they said, "Lord, do you want us to command fire to come down from the sky, and destroy them, just as Elijah did?"
030955 But he turned and rebuked them, "You don't know of what kind of spirit you are.
030956 For the Son of Man didn't come to destroy men's lives, but to save them." They went to another village.
030957 As they went on the way, a certain man said to him, "I want to follow you wherever you go, Lord."
030958 Jesus said to him, "The foxes have holes, and the birds of the sky have nests, but the Son of Man has no place to lay his head."
030959 He said to another, "Follow me!" But he said, "Lord, allow me first to go and bury my father."
030960 But Jesus said to him, "Leave the dead to bury their own dead, but you go and announce the Kingdom of God."
030961 Another also said, "I want to follow you, Lord, but first allow me to bid farewell to those who are at my house."
030962 But Jesus said to him, "No one, having put his hand to the plow, and looking back, is fit for the Kingdom of God."
031001 Now after these things, the Lord also appointed seventy others, and sent them two by two ahead of him into every city and place, where he was about to come.
031002 Then he said to them, "The harvest is indeed plentiful, but the laborers are few. Pray therefore to the Lord of the harvest, that he may send out laborers into his harvest.
031003 Go your ways. Behold, I send you out as lambs among wolves.
031004 Carry no purse, nor wallet, nor sandals. Greet no one on the way.
031005 Into whatever house you enter, first say, 'Peace be to this house.'
031006 If a son of peace is there, your peace will rest on him; but if not, it will return to you.
031007 Remain in that same house, eating and drinking the things they give, for the laborer is worthy of his wages. Don't go from house to house.
031008 Into whatever city you enter, and they receive you, eat the things that are set before you.
031009 Heal the sick who are therein, and tell them, 'The Kingdom of God has come near to you.'
031010 But into whatever city you enter, and they don't receive you, go out into its streets and say,
031011 'Even the dust from your city that clings to us, we wipe off against you. Nevertheless know this, that the Kingdom of God has come near to you.'
031012 I tell you, it will be more tolerable in that day for Sodom than for that city.
031013 "Woe to you, Chorazin! Woe to you, Bethsaida! For if the mighty works had been done in Tyre and Sidon which were done in you, they would have repented long ago, sitting in sackcloth and ashes.
031014 But it will be more tolerable for Tyre and Sidon in the judgment than for you.
031015 You, Capernaum, who are exalted to heaven, will be brought down to Hades.
031016 Whoever listens to you listens to me, and whoever rejects you rejects me. Whoever rejects me rejects him who sent me."
031017 The seventy returned with joy, saying, "Lord, even the demons are subject to us in your name!"
031018 He said to them, "I saw Satan having fallen like lightning from heaven.
031019 Behold, I give you authority to tread on serpents and scorpions, and over all the power of the enemy. Nothing will in any way hurt you.
031020 Nevertheless, don't rejoice in this, that the spirits are subject to you, but rejoice that your names are written in heaven."
031021 In that same hour Jesus rejoiced in the Holy Spirit, and said, "I thank you, O Father, Lord of heaven and earth, that you have hidden these things from the wise and understanding, and revealed them to little children. Yes, Father, for so it was well-pleasing in your sight."
031022 Turning to the disciples, he said, "All things have been delivered to me by my Father. No one knows who the Son is, except the Father, and who the Father is, except the Son, and he to whomever the Son desires to reveal him."
031023 Turning to the disciples, he said privately, "Blessed are the eyes which see the things that you see,
031024 for I tell you that many prophets and kings desired to see the things which you see, and didn't see them, and to hear the things which you hear, and didn't hear them."
031025 Behold, a certain lawyer stood up and tested him, saying, "Teacher, what shall I do to inherit eternal life?"
031026 He said to him, "What is written in the law? How do you read it?"
031027 He answered, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, with all your strength, and with all your mind; and your neighbor as yourself."
031028 He said to him, "You have answered correctly. Do this, and you will live."
031029 But he, desiring to justify himself, asked Jesus, "Who is my neighbor?"
031030 Jesus answered, "A certain man was going down from Jerusalem to Jericho, and he fell among robbers, who both stripped him and beat him, and departed, leaving him half dead.
031031 By chance a certain priest was going down that way. When he saw him, he passed by on the other side.
031032 In the same way a Levite also, when he came to the place, and saw him, passed by on the other side.
031033 But a certain Samaritan, as he traveled, came where he was. When he saw him, he was moved with compassion,
031034 came to him, and bound up his wounds, pouring on oil and wine. He set him on his own animal, and brought him to an inn, and took care of him.
031035 On the next day, when he departed, he took out two denarii, and gave them to the host, and said to him, 'Take care of him. Whatever you spend beyond that, I will repay you when I return.'
031036 Now which of these three do you think seemed to be a neighbor to him who fell among the robbers?"
031037 He said, "He who showed mercy on him." Then Jesus said to him, "Go and do likewise."
031038 It happened as they went on their way, he entered into a certain village, and a certain woman named Martha received him into her house.
031039 She had a sister called Mary, who also sat at Jesus' feet, and heard his word.
031040 But Martha was distracted with much serving, and she came up to him, and said, "Lord, don't you care that my sister left me to serve alone? Ask her therefore to help me."
031041 Jesus answered her, "Martha, Martha, you are anxious and troubled about many things,
031042 but one thing is needed. Mary has chosen the good part, which will not be taken away from her."
031101 It happened, that when he finished praying in a certain place, one of his disciples said to him, "Lord, teach us to pray, just as John also taught his disciples."
031102 He said to them, "When you pray, say, 'Our Father in heaven, may your name be kept holy. May your Kingdom come. May your will be done on Earth, as it is in heaven.
031103 Give us day by day our daily bread.
031104 Forgive us our sins, for we ourselves also forgive everyone who is indebted to us. Bring us not into temptation, but deliver us from the evil one.'"
031105 He said to them, "Which of you, if you go to a friend at midnight, and tell him, 'Friend, lend me three loaves of bread,
031106 for a friend of mine has come to me from a journey, and I have nothing to set before him,'
031107 and he from within will answer and say, 'Don't bother me. The door is now shut, and my children are with me in bed. I can't get up and give it to you'?
031108 I tell you, although he will not rise and give it to him because he is his friend, yet because of his persistence, he will get up and give him as many as he needs.
031109 "I tell you, keep asking, and it will be given you. Keep seeking, and you will find. Keep knocking, and it will be opened to you.
031110 For everyone who asks receives. He who seeks finds. To him who knocks it will be opened.
031111 "Which of you fathers, if your son asks for bread, will give him a stone? Or if he asks for a fish, he won't give him a snake instead of a fish, will he?
031112 Or if he asks for an egg, he won't give him a scorpion, will he?
031113 If you then, being evil, know how to give good gifts to your children, how much more will your heavenly Father give the Holy Spirit to those who ask him?"
031114 He was casting out a demon, and it was mute. It happened, when the demon had gone out, the mute man spoke; and the multitudes marveled.
031115 But some of them said, "He casts out demons by Beelzebul, the prince of the demons."
031116 Others, testing him, sought from him a sign from heaven.
031117 But he, knowing their thoughts, said to them, "Every kingdom divided against itself is brought to desolation. A house divided against itself falls.
031118 If Satan also is divided against himself, how will his kingdom stand? For you say that I cast out demons by Beelzebul.
031119 But if I cast out demons by Beelzebul, by whom do your children cast them out? Therefore will they be your judges.
031120 But if I by the finger of God cast out demons, then the Kingdom of God has come to you.
031121 "When the strong man, fully armed, guards his own dwelling, his goods are safe.
031122 But when someone stronger attacks him and overcomes him, he takes from him his whole armor in which he trusted, and divides his spoils.
031123 "He that is not with me is against me. He who doesn't gather with me scatters.
031124 The unclean spirit, when he has gone out of the man, passes through dry places, seeking rest, and finding none, he says, 'I will turn back to my house from which I came out.'
031125 When he returns, he finds it swept and put in order.
031126 Then he goes, and takes seven other spirits more evil than himself, and they enter in and dwell there. The last state of that man becomes worse than the first."
031127 It came to pass, as he said these things, a certain woman out of the multitude lifted up her voice, and said to him, "Blessed is the womb that bore you, and the breasts which nursed you!"
031128 But he said, "On the contrary, blessed are those who hear the word of God, and keep it."
031129 When the multitudes were gathering together to him, he began to say, "This is an evil generation. It seeks after a sign. No sign will be given to it but the sign of Jonah, the prophet.
031130 For even as Jonah became a sign to the Ninevites, so will also the Son of Man be to this generation.
031131 The Queen of the South will rise up in the judgment with the men of this generation, and will condemn them: for she came from the ends of the earth to hear the wisdom of Solomon; and behold, one greater than Solomon is here.
031132 The men of Nineveh will stand up in the judgment with this generation, and will condemn it: for they repented at the preaching of Jonah, and behold, one greater than Jonah is here.
031133 "No one, when he has lit a lamp, puts it in a cellar or under a basket, but on a stand, that those who come in may see the light.
031134 The lamp of the body is the eye. Therefore when your eye is good, your whole body is also full of light; but when it is evil, your body also is full of darkness.
031135 Therefore see whether the light that is in you isn't darkness.
031136 If therefore your whole body is full of light, having no part dark, it will be wholly full of light, as when the lamp with its bright shining gives you light."
031137 Now as he spoke, a certain Pharisee asked him to dine with him. He went in, and sat at the table.
031138 When the Pharisee saw it, he marveled that he had not first washed himself before dinner.
031139 The Lord said to him, "Now you Pharisees cleanse the outside of the cup and of the platter, but your inward part is full of extortion and wickedness.
031140 You foolish ones, didn't he who made the outside make the inside also?
031141 But give for gifts to the needy those things which are within, and behold, all things will be clean to you.
031142 But woe to you Pharisees! For you tithe mint and rue and every herb, but you bypass justice and the love of God. You ought to have done these, and not to have left the other undone.
031143 Woe to you Pharisees! For you love the best seats in the synagogues, and the greetings in the marketplaces.
031144 Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! For you are like hidden graves, and the men who walk over them don't know it."
031145 One of the lawyers answered him, "Teacher, in saying this you insult us also."
031146 He said, "Woe to you lawyers also! For you load men with burdens that are difficult to carry, and you yourselves won't even lift one finger to help carry those burdens.
031147 Woe to you! For you build the tombs of the prophets, and your fathers killed them.
031148 So you testify and consent to the works of your fathers. For they killed them, and you build their tombs.
031149 Therefore also the wisdom of God said, 'I will send to them prophets and apostles; and some of them they will kill and persecute,
031150 that the blood of all the prophets, which was shed from the foundation of the world, may be required of this generation;
031151 from the blood of Abel to the blood of Zachariah, who perished between the altar and the sanctuary.' Yes, I tell you, it will be required of this generation.
031152 Woe to you lawyers! For you took away the key of knowledge. You didn't enter in yourselves, and those who were entering in, you hindered."
031153 As he said these things to them, the scribes and the Pharisees began to be terribly angry, and to draw many things out of him;
031154 lying in wait for him, and seeking to catch him in something he might say, that they might accuse him.
031201 Meanwhile, when a multitude of many thousands had gathered together, so much so that they trampled on each other, he began to tell his disciples first of all, "Beware of the yeast of the Pharisees, which is hypocrisy.
031202 But there is nothing covered up, that will not be revealed, nor hidden, that will not be known.
031203 Therefore whatever you have said in the darkness will be heard in the light. What you have spoken in the ear in the inner chambers will be proclaimed on the housetops.
031204 "I tell you, my friends, don't be afraid of those who kill the body, and after that have no more that they can do.
031205 But I will warn you whom you should fear. Fear him, who after he has killed, has power to cast into Gehenna. Yes, I tell you, fear him.
031206 "Aren't five sparrows sold for two assaria coins? Not one of them is forgotten by God.
031207 But the very hairs of your head are all numbered. Therefore don't be afraid. You are of more value than many sparrows.
031208 "I tell you, everyone who confesses me before men, him will the Son of Man also confess before the angels of God;
031209 but he who denies me in the presence of men will be denied in the presence of the angels of God.
031210 Everyone who speaks a word against the Son of Man will be forgiven, but those who blaspheme against the Holy Spirit will not be forgiven.
031211 When they bring you before the synagogues, the rulers, and the authorities, don't be anxious how or what you will answer, or what you will say;
031212 for the Holy Spirit will teach you in that same hour what you must say."
031213 One of the multitude said to him, "Teacher, tell my brother to divide the inheritance with me."
031214 But he said to him, "Man, who made me a judge or an arbitrator over you?"
031215 He said to them, "Beware! Keep yourselves from covetousness, for a man's life doesn't consist of the abundance of the things which he possesses."
031216 He spoke a parable to them, saying, "The ground of a certain rich man brought forth abundantly.
031217 He reasoned within himself, saying, 'What will I do, because I don't have room to store my crops?'
031218 He said, 'This is what I will do. I will pull down my barns, and build bigger ones, and there I will store all my grain and my goods.
031219 I will tell my soul, "Soul, you have many goods laid up for many years. Take your ease, eat, drink, be merry."'
031220 "But God said to him, 'You foolish one, tonight your soul is required of you. The things which you have prepared--whose will they be?'
031221 So is he who lays up treasure for himself, and is not rich toward God."
031222 He said to his disciples, "Therefore I tell you, don't be anxious for your life, what you will eat, nor yet for your body, what you will wear.
031223 Life is more than food, and the body is more than clothing.
031224 Consider the ravens: they don't sow, they don't reap, they have no warehouse or barn, and God feeds them. How much more valuable are you than birds!
031225 Which of you by being anxious can add a cubit to his height?
031226 If then you aren't able to do even the least things, why are you anxious about the rest?
031227 Consider the lilies, how they grow. They don't toil, neither do they spin; yet I tell you, even Solomon in all his glory was not arrayed like one of these.
031228 But if this is how God clothes the grass in the field, which today exists, and tomorrow is cast into the oven, how much more will he clothe you, O you of little faith?
031229 Don't seek what you will eat or what you will drink; neither be anxious.
031230 For the nations of the world seek after all of these things, but your Father knows that you need these things.
031231 But seek God's Kingdom, and all these things will be added to you.
031232 Don't be afraid, little flock, for it is your Father's good pleasure to give you the Kingdom.
031233 Sell that which you have, and give gifts to the needy. Make for yourselves purses which don't grow old, a treasure in the heavens that doesn't fail, where no thief approaches, neither moth destroys.
031234 For where your treasure is, there will your heart be also.
031235 "Let your waist be girded and your lamps burning.
031236 Be like men watching for their lord, when he returns from the marriage feast; that, when he comes and knocks, they may immediately open to him.
031237 Blessed are those servants, whom the lord will find watching when he comes. Most certainly I tell you, that he will dress himself, and make them recline, and will come and serve them.
031238 They will be blessed if he comes in the second or third watch, and finds them so.
031239 But know this, that if the master of the house had known in what hour the thief was coming, he would have watched, and not allowed his house to be broken into.
031240 Therefore be ready also, for the Son of Man is coming in an hour that you don't expect him."
031241 Peter said to him, "Lord, are you telling this parable to us, or to everybody?"
031242 The Lord said, "Who then is the faithful and wise steward, whom his lord will set over his household, to give them their portion of food at the right times?
031243 Blessed is that servant whom his lord will find doing so when he comes.
031244 Truly I tell you, that he will set him over all that he has.
031245 But if that servant says in his heart, 'My lord delays his coming,' and begins to beat the menservants and the maidservants, and to eat and drink, and to be drunken,
031246 then the lord of that servant will come in a day when he isn't expecting him, and in an hour that he doesn't know, and will cut him in two, and place his portion with the unfaithful.
031247 That servant, who knew his lord's will, and didn't prepare, nor do what he wanted, will be beaten with many stripes,
031248 but he who didn't know, and did things worthy of stripes, will be beaten with few stripes. To whoever much is given, of him will much be required; and to whom much was entrusted, of him more will be asked.
031249 "I came to throw fire on the earth. I wish it were already kindled.
031250 But I have a baptism to be baptized with, and how distressed I am until it is accomplished!
031251 Do you think that I have come to give peace in the earth? I tell you, no, but rather division.
031252 For from now on, there will be five in one house divided, three against two, and two against three.
031253 They will be divided, father against son, and son against father; mother against daughter, and daughter against her mother; mother-in-law against her daughter-in-law, and daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law."
031254 He said to the multitudes also, "When you see a cloud rising from the west, immediately you say, 'A shower is coming,' and so it happens.
031255 When a south wind blows, you say, 'There will be a scorching heat,' and it happens.
031256 You hypocrites! You know how to interpret the appearance of the earth and the sky, but how is it that you don't interpret this time?
031257 Why don't you judge for yourselves what is right?
031258 For when you are going with your adversary before the magistrate, try diligently on the way to be released from him, lest perhaps he drag you to the judge, and the judge deliver you to the officer, and the officer throw you into prison.
031259 I tell you, you will by no means get out of there, until you have paid the very last penny."
031301 Now there were some present at the same time who told him about the Galileans, whose blood Pilate had mixed with their sacrifices.
031302 Jesus answered them, "Do you think that these Galileans were worse sinners than all the other Galileans, because they suffered such things?
031303 I tell you, no, but unless you repent, you will all perish in the same way.
031304 Or those eighteen, on whom the tower in Siloam fell, and killed them; do you think that they were worse offenders than all the men who dwell in Jerusalem?
031305 I tell you, no, but, unless you repent, you will all perish in the same way."
031306 He spoke this parable. "A certain man had a fig tree planted in his vineyard, and he came seeking fruit on it, and found none.
031307 He said to the vine dresser, 'Behold, these three years I have come looking for fruit on this fig tree, and found none. Cut it down. Why does it waste the soil?'
031308 He answered, 'Lord, leave it alone this year also, until I dig around it, and fertilize it.
031309 If it bears fruit, fine; but if not, after that, you can cut it down.'"
031310 He was teaching in one of the synagogues on the Sabbath day.
031311 Behold, there was a woman who had a spirit of infirmity eighteen years, and she was bent over, and could in no way straighten herself up.
031312 When Jesus saw her, he called her, and said to her, "Woman, you are freed from your infirmity."
031313 He laid his hands on her, and immediately she stood up straight, and glorified God.
031314 The ruler of the synagogue, being indignant because Jesus had healed on the Sabbath, said to the multitude, "There are six days in which men ought to work. Therefore come on those days and be healed, and not on the Sabbath day!"
031315 Therefore the Lord answered him, "You hypocrites! Doesn't each one of you free his ox or his donkey from the stall on the Sabbath, and lead him away to water?
031316 Ought not this woman, being a daughter of Abraham, whom Satan had bound eighteen long years, be freed from this bondage on the Sabbath day?"
031317 As he said these things, all his adversaries were disappointed, and all the multitude rejoiced for all the glorious things that were done by him.
031318 He said, "What is the Kingdom of God like? To what shall I compare it?
031319 It is like a grain of mustard seed, which a man took, and put in his own garden. It grew, and became a large tree, and the birds of the sky lodged in its branches."
031320 Again he said, "To what shall I compare the Kingdom of God?
031321 It is like yeast, which a woman took and hid in three measures of flour, until it was all leavened."
031322 He went on his way through cities and villages, teaching, and traveling on to Jerusalem.
031323 One said to him, "Lord, are they few who are saved?" He said to them,
031324 "Strive to enter in by the narrow door, for many, I tell you, will seek to enter in, and will not be able.
031325 When once the master of the house has risen up, and has shut the door, and you begin to stand outside, and to knock at the door, saying, 'Lord, Lord, open to us!' then he will answer and tell you, 'I don't know you or where you come from.'
031326 Then you will begin to say, 'We ate and drank in your presence, and you taught in our streets.'
031327 He will say, 'I tell you, I don't know where you come from. Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity.'
031328 There will be weeping and gnashing of teeth, when you see Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, and all the prophets, in the Kingdom of God, and yourselves being thrown outside.
031329 They will come from the east, west, north, and south, and will sit down in the Kingdom of God.
031330 Behold, there are some who are last who will be first, and there are some who are first who will be last."
031331 On that same day, some Pharisees came, saying to him, "Get out of here, and go away, for Herod wants to kill you."
031332 He said to them, "Go and tell that fox, 'Behold, I cast out demons and perform cures today and tomorrow, and the third day I complete my mission.
031333 Nevertheless I must go on my way today and tomorrow and the next day, for it can't be that a prophet perish outside of Jerusalem.'
031334 "Jerusalem, Jerusalem, that kills the prophets, and stones those who are sent to her! How often I wanted to gather your children together, like a hen gathers her own brood under her wings, and you refused!
031335 Behold, your house is left to you desolate. I tell you, you will not see me, until you say, 'Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord!'"
031401 It happened, when he went into the house of one of the rulers of the Pharisees on a Sabbath to eat bread, that they were watching him.
031402 Behold, a certain man who had dropsy was in front of him.
031403 Jesus, answering, spoke to the lawyers and Pharisees, saying, "Is it lawful to heal on the Sabbath?"
031404 But they were silent. He took him, and healed him, and let him go.
031405 He answered them, "Which of you, if your son or an ox fell into a well, wouldn't immediately pull him out on a Sabbath day?"
031406 They couldn't answer him regarding these things.
031407 He spoke a parable to those who were invited, when he noticed how they chose the best seats, and said to them,
031408 "When you are invited by anyone to a marriage feast, don't sit in the best seat, since perhaps someone more honorable than you might be invited by him,
031409 and he who invited both of you would come and tell you, 'Make room for this person.' Then you would begin, with shame, to take the lowest place.
031410 But when you are invited, go and sit in the lowest place, so that when he who invited you comes, he may tell you, 'Friend, move up higher.' Then you will be honored in the presence of all who sit at the table with you.
031411 For everyone who exalts himself will be humbled, and whoever humbles himself will be exalted."
031412 He also said to the one who had invited him, "When you make a dinner or a supper, don't call your friends, nor your brothers, nor your kinsmen, nor rich neighbors, or perhaps they might also return the favor, and pay you back.
031413 But when you make a feast, ask the poor, the maimed, the lame, or the blind;
031414 and you will be blessed, because they don't have the resources to repay you. For you will be repaid in the resurrection of the righteous."
031415 When one of those who sat at the table with him heard these things, he said to him, "Blessed is he who will feast in the Kingdom of God!"
031416 But he said to him, "A certain man made a great supper, and he invited many people.
031417 He sent out his servant at supper time to tell those who were invited, 'Come, for everything is ready now.'
031418 They all as one began to make excuses. "The first said to him, 'I have bought a field, and I must go and see it. Please have me excused.'
031419 "Another said, 'I have bought five yoke of oxen, and I must go try them out. Please have me excused.'
031420 "Another said, 'I have married a wife, and therefore I can't come.'
031421 "That servant came, and told his lord these things. Then the master of the house, being angry, said to his servant, 'Go out quickly into the streets and lanes of the city, and bring in the poor, maimed, blind, and lame.'
031422 "The servant said, 'Lord, it is done as you commanded, and there is still room.'
031423 "The lord said to the servant, 'Go out into the highways and hedges, and compel them to come in, that my house may be filled.
031424 For I tell you that none of those men who were invited will taste of my supper.'"
031425 Now great multitudes were going with him. He turned and said to them,
031426 "If anyone comes to me, and doesn't hate his own father, mother, wife, children, brothers, and sisters, yes, and his own life also, he can't be my disciple.
031427 Whoever doesn't bear his own cross, and come after me, can't be my disciple.
031428 For which of you, desiring to build a tower, doesn't first sit down and count the cost, to see if he has enough to complete it?
031429 Or perhaps, when he has laid a foundation, and is not able to finish, everyone who sees begins to mock him,
031430 saying, 'This man began to build, and wasn't able to finish.'
031431 Or what king, as he goes to encounter another king in war, will not sit down first and consider whether he is able with ten thousand to meet him who comes against him with twenty thousand?
031432 Or else, while the other is yet a great way off, he sends an envoy, and asks for conditions of peace.
031433 So therefore whoever of you who doesn't renounce all that he has, he can't be my disciple.
031434 Salt is good, but if the salt becomes flat and tasteless, with what do you season it?
031435 It is fit neither for the soil nor for the manure pile. It is thrown out. He who has ears to hear, let him hear."
031501 Now all the tax collectors and sinners were coming close to him to hear him.
031502 The Pharisees and the scribes murmured, saying, "This man welcomes sinners, and eats with them."
031503 He told them this parable.
031504 "Which of you men, if you had one hundred sheep, and lost one of them, wouldn't leave the ninety-nine in the wilderness, and go after the one that was lost, until he found it?
031505 When he has found it, he carries it on his shoulders, rejoicing.
031506 When he comes home, he calls together his friends and his neighbors, saying to them, 'Rejoice with me, for I have found my sheep which was lost!'
031507 I tell you that even so there will be more joy in heaven over one sinner who repents, than over ninety-nine righteous people who need no repentance.
031508 Or what woman, if she had ten drachma coins, if she lost one drachma coin, wouldn't light a lamp, sweep the house, and seek diligently until she found it?
031509 When she has found it, she calls together her friends and neighbors, saying, 'Rejoice with me, for I have found the drachma which I had lost.'
031510 Even so, I tell you, there is joy in the presence of the angels of God over one sinner repenting."
031511 He said, "A certain man had two sons.
031512 The younger of them said to his father, 'Father, give me my share of your property.' He divided his livelihood between them.
031513 Not many days after, the younger son gathered all of this together and traveled into a far country. There he wasted his property with riotous living.
031514 When he had spent all of it, there arose a severe famine in that country, and he began to be in need.
031515 He went and joined himself to one of the citizens of that country, and he sent him into his fields to feed pigs.
031516 He wanted to fill his belly with the husks that the pigs ate, but no one gave him any.
031517 But when he came to himself he said, 'How many hired servants of my father's have bread enough to spare, and I'm dying with hunger!
031518 I will get up and go to my father, and will tell him, "Father, I have sinned against heaven, and in your sight.
031519 I am no more worthy to be called your son. Make me as one of your hired servants."'
031520 "He arose, and came to his father. But while he was still far off, his father saw him, and was moved with compassion, and ran, and fell on his neck, and kissed him.
031521 The son said to him, 'Father, I have sinned against heaven, and in your sight. I am no longer worthy to be called your son.'
031522 "But the father said to his servants, 'Bring out the best robe, and put it on him. Put a ring on his hand, and shoes on his feet.
031523 Bring the fattened calf, kill it, and let us eat, and celebrate;
031524 for this, my son, was dead, and is alive again. He was lost, and is found.' They began to celebrate.
031525 "Now his elder son was in the field. As he came near to the house, he heard music and dancing.
031526 He called one of the servants to him, and asked what was going on.
031527 He said to him, 'Your brother has come, and your father has killed the fattened calf, because he has received him back safe and healthy.'
031528 But he was angry, and would not go in. Therefore his father came out, and begged him.
031529 But he answered his father, 'Behold, these many years I have served you, and I never disobeyed a commandment of yours, but you never gave me a goat, that I might celebrate with my friends.
031530 But when this, your son, came, who has devoured your living with prostitutes, you killed the fattened calf for him.'
031531 "He said to him, 'Son, you are always with me, and all that is mine is yours.
031532 But it was appropriate to celebrate and be glad, for this, your brother, was dead, and is alive again. He was lost, and is found.'"
031601 He also said to his disciples, "There was a certain rich man who had a manager. An accusation was made to him that this man was wasting his possessions.
031602 He called him, and said to him, 'What is this that I hear about you? Give an accounting of your management, for you can no longer be manager.'
031603 "The manager said within himself, 'What will I do, seeing that my lord is taking away the management position from me? I don't have strength to dig. I am ashamed to beg.
031604 I know what I will do, so that when I am removed from management, they may receive me into their houses.'
031605 Calling each one of his lord's debtors to him, he said to the first, 'How much do you owe to my lord?'
031606 He said, 'A hundred batos of oil.' He said to him, 'Take your bill, and sit down quickly and write fifty.'
031607 Then said he to another, 'How much do you owe?' He said, 'A hundred cors of wheat.' He said to him, 'Take your bill, and write eighty.'
031608 "His lord commended the dishonest manager because he had done wisely, for the children of this world are, in their own generation, wiser than the children of the light.
031609 I tell you, make for yourselves friends by means of unrighteous mammon, so that when you fail, they may receive you into the eternal tents.
031610 He who is faithful in a very little is faithful also in much. He who is dishonest in a very little is also dishonest in much.
031611 If therefore you have not been faithful in the unrighteous mammon, who will commit to your trust the true riches?
031612 If you have not been faithful in that which is another's, who will give you that which is your own?
031613 No servant can serve two masters, for either he will hate the one, and love the other; or else he will hold to one, and despise the other. You aren't able to serve God and mammon."
031614 The Pharisees, who were lovers of money, also heard all these things, and they scoffed at him.
031615 He said to them, "You are those who justify yourselves in the sight of men, but God knows your hearts. For that which is exalted among men is an abomination in the sight of God.
031616 The law and the prophets were until John. From that time the Good News of the Kingdom of God is preached, and everyone is forcing his way into it.
031617 But it is easier for heaven and earth to pass away, than for one tiny stroke of a pen in the law to fall.
031618 Everyone who divorces his wife, and marries another, commits adultery. He who marries one who is divorced from a husband commits adultery.
031619 "Now there was a certain rich man, and he was clothed in purple and fine linen, living in luxury every day.
031620 A certain beggar, named Lazarus, was laid at his gate, full of sores,
031621 and desiring to be fed with the crumbs that fell from the rich man's table. Yes, even the dogs came and licked his sores.
031622 It happened that the beggar died, and that he was carried away by the angels to Abraham's bosom. The rich man also died, and was buried.
031623 In Hades, he lifted up his eyes, being in torment, and saw Abraham far off, and Lazarus at his bosom.
031624 He cried and said, 'Father Abraham, have mercy on me, and send Lazarus, that he may dip the tip of his finger in water, and cool my tongue! For I am in anguish in this flame.'
031625 "But Abraham said, 'Son, remember that you, in your lifetime, received your good things, and Lazarus, in like manner, bad things. But now here he is comforted and you are in anguish.
031626 Besides all this, between us and you there is a great gulf fixed, that those who want to pass from here to you are not able, and that none may cross over from there to us.'
031627 "He said, 'I ask you therefore, father, that you would send him to my father's house;
031628 for I have five brothers, that he may testify to them, so they won't also come into this place of torment.'
031629 "But Abraham said to him, 'They have Moses and the prophets. Let them listen to them.'
031630 "He said, 'No, father Abraham, but if one goes to them from the dead, they will repent.'
031631 "He said to him, 'If they don't listen to Moses and the prophets, neither will they be persuaded if one rises from the dead.'"
031701 He said to the disciples, "It is impossible that no occasions of stumbling should come, but woe to him through whom they come!
031702 It would be better for him if a millstone were hung around his neck, and he were thrown into the sea, rather than that he should cause one of these little ones to stumble.
031703 Be careful. If your brother sins against you, rebuke him. If he repents, forgive him.
031704 If he sins against you seven times in the day, and seven times returns, saying, 'I repent,' you shall forgive him."
031705 The apostles said to the Lord, "Increase our faith."
031706 The Lord said, "If you had faith like a grain of mustard seed, you would tell this sycamore tree, 'Be uprooted, and be planted in the sea,' and it would obey you.
031707 But who is there among you, having a servant plowing or keeping sheep, that will say, when he comes in from the field, 'Come immediately and sit down at the table,'
031708 and will not rather tell him, 'Prepare my supper, clothe yourself properly, and serve me, while I eat and drink. Afterward you shall eat and drink'?
031709 Does he thank that servant because he did the things that were commanded? I think not.
031710 Even so you also, when you have done all the things that are commanded you, say, 'We are unworthy servants. We have done our duty.'"
031711 It happened as he was on his way to Jerusalem, that he was passing along the borders of Samaria and Galilee.
031712 As he entered into a certain village, ten men who were lepers met him, who stood at a distance.
031713 They lifted up their voices, saying, "Jesus, Master, have mercy on us!"
031714 When he saw them, he said to them, "Go and show yourselves to the priests." It happened that as they went, they were cleansed.
031715 One of them, when he saw that he was healed, turned back, glorifying God with a loud voice.
031716 He fell on his face at Jesus' feet, giving him thanks; and he was a Samaritan.
031717 Jesus answered, "Weren't the ten cleansed? But where are the nine?
031718 Were there none found who returned to give glory to God, except this stranger?"
031719 Then he said to him, "Get up, and go your way. Your faith has healed you."
031720 Being asked by the Pharisees when the Kingdom of God would come, he answered them, "The Kingdom of God doesn't come with observation;
031721 neither will they say, 'Look, here!' or, 'Look, there!' for behold, the Kingdom of God is within you."
031722 He said to the disciples, "The days will come, when you will desire to see one of the days of the Son of Man, and you will not see it.
031723 They will tell you, 'Look, here!' or 'Look, there!' Don't go away, nor follow after them,
031724 for as the lightning, when it flashes out of the one part under the sky, shines to the other part under the sky; so will the Son of Man be in his day.
031725 But first, he must suffer many things and be rejected by this generation.
031726 As it happened in the days of Noah, even so will it be also in the days of the Son of Man.
031727 They ate, they drank, they married, they were given in marriage, until the day that Noah entered into the ship, and the flood came, and destroyed them all.
031728 Likewise, even as it happened in the days of Lot: they ate, they drank, they bought, they sold, they planted, they built;
031729 but in the day that Lot went out from Sodom, it rained fire and sulfur from the sky, and destroyed them all.
031730 It will be the same way in the day that the Son of Man is revealed.
031731 In that day, he who will be on the housetop, and his goods in the house, let him not go down to take them away. Let him who is in the field likewise not turn back.
031732 Remember Lot's wife!
031733 Whoever seeks to save his life loses it, but whoever loses his life preserves it.
031734 I tell you, in that night there will be two people in one bed. The one will be taken, and the other will be left.
031735 There will be two grinding grain together. One will be taken, and the other will be left."
031736 
031737 They, answering, asked him, "Where, Lord?" He said to them, "Where the body is, there will the vultures also be gathered together."
031801 He also spoke a parable to them that they must always pray, and not give up,
031802 saying, "There was a judge in a certain city who didn't fear God, and didn't respect man.
031803 A widow was in that city, and she often came to him, saying, 'Defend me from my adversary!'
031804 He wouldn't for a while, but afterward he said to himself, 'Though I neither fear God, nor respect man,
031805 yet because this widow bothers me, I will defend her, or else she will wear me out by her continual coming.'"
031806 The Lord said, "Listen to what the unrighteous judge says.
031807 Won't God avenge his chosen ones, who are crying out to him day and night, and yet he exercises patience with them?
031808 I tell you that he will avenge them quickly. Nevertheless, when the Son of Man comes, will he find faith on the earth?"
031809 He spoke also this parable to certain people who were convinced of their own righteousness, and who despised all others.
031810 "Two men went up into the temple to pray; one was a Pharisee, and the other was a tax collector.
031811 The Pharisee stood and prayed to himself like this: 'God, I thank you, that I am not like the rest of men, extortioners, unrighteous, adulterers, or even like this tax collector.
031812 I fast twice a week. I give tithes of all that I get.'
031813 But the tax collector, standing far away, wouldn't even lift up his eyes to heaven, but beat his breast, saying, 'God, be merciful to me, a sinner!'
031814 I tell you, this man went down to his house justified rather than the other; for everyone who exalts himself will be humbled, but he who humbles himself will be exalted."
031815 They were also bringing their babies to him, that he might touch them. But when the disciples saw it, they rebuked them.
031816 Jesus summoned them, saying, "Allow the little children to come to me, and don't hinder them, for the Kingdom of God belongs to such as these.
031817 Most certainly, I tell you, whoever doesn't receive the Kingdom of God like a little child, he will in no way enter into it."
031818 A certain ruler asked him, saying, "Good Teacher, what shall I do to inherit eternal life?"
031819 Jesus asked him, "Why do you call me good? No one is good, except one--God.
031820 You know the commandments: 'Don't commit adultery,' 'Don't murder,' 'Don't steal,' 'Don't give false testimony,' 'Honor your father and your mother.'"
031821 He said, "I have observed all these things from my youth up."
031822 When Jesus heard these things, he said to him, "You still lack one thing. Sell all that you have, and distribute it to the poor. You will have treasure in heaven. Come, follow me."
031823 But when he heard these things, he became very sad, for he was very rich.
031824 Jesus, seeing that he became very sad, said, "How hard it is for those who have riches to enter into the Kingdom of God!
031825 For it is easier for a camel to enter in through a needle's eye, than for a rich man to enter into the Kingdom of God."
031826 Those who heard it said, "Then who can be saved?"
031827 But he said, "The things which are impossible with men are possible with God."
031828 Peter said, "Look, we have left everything, and followed you."
031829 He said to them, "Most certainly I tell you, there is no one who has left house, or wife, or brothers, or parents, or children, for the Kingdom of God's sake,
031830 who will not receive many times more in this time, and in the world to come, eternal life."
031831 He took the twelve aside, and said to them, "Behold, we are going up to Jerusalem, and all the things that are written through the prophets concerning the Son of Man will be completed.
031832 For he will be delivered up to the Gentiles, will be mocked, treated shamefully, and spit on.
031833 They will scourge and kill him. On the third day, he will rise again."
031834 They understood none of these things. This saying was hidden from them, and they didn't understand the things that were said.
031835 It happened, as he came near Jericho, a certain blind man sat by the road, begging.
031836 Hearing a multitude going by, he asked what this meant.
031837 They told him that Jesus of Nazareth was passing by.
031838 He cried out, "Jesus, you son of David, have mercy on me!"
031839 Those who led the way rebuked him, that he should be quiet; but he cried out all the more, "You son of David, have mercy on me!"
031840 Standing still, Jesus commanded him to be brought to him. When he had come near, he asked him,
031841 "What do you want me to do?" He said, "Lord, that I may see again."
031842 Jesus said to him, "Receive your sight. Your faith has healed you."
031843 Immediately he received his sight, and followed him, glorifying God. All the people, when they saw it, praised God.
031901 He entered and was passing through Jericho.
031902 There was a man named Zacchaeus. He was a chief tax collector, and he was rich.
031903 He was trying to see who Jesus was, and couldn't because of the crowd, because he was short.
031904 He ran on ahead, and climbed up into a sycamore tree to see him, for he was to pass that way.
031905 When Jesus came to the place, he looked up and saw him, and said to him, "Zacchaeus, hurry and come down, for today I must stay at your house."
031906 He hurried, came down, and received him joyfully.
031907 When they saw it, they all murmured, saying, "He has gone in to lodge with a man who is a sinner."
031908 Zacchaeus stood and said to the Lord, "Behold, Lord, half of my goods I give to the poor. If I have wrongfully exacted anything of anyone, I restore four times as much."
031909 Jesus said to him, "Today, salvation has come to this house, because he also is a son of Abraham.
031910 For the Son of Man came to seek and to save that which was lost."
031911 As they heard these things, he went on and told a parable, because he was near Jerusalem, and they supposed that the Kingdom of God would be revealed immediately.
031912 He said therefore, "A certain nobleman went into a far country to receive for himself a kingdom, and to return.
031913 He called ten servants of his, and gave them ten mina coins, and told them, 'Conduct business until I come.'
031914 But his citizens hated him, and sent an envoy after him, saying, 'We don't want this man to reign over us.'
031915 "It happened when he had come back again, having received the kingdom, that he commanded these servants, to whom he had given the money, to be called to him, that he might know what they had gained by conducting business.
031916 The first came before him, saying, 'Lord, your mina has made ten more minas.'
031917 "He said to him, 'Well done, you good servant! Because you were found faithful with very little, you shall have authority over ten cities.'
031918 "The second came, saying, 'Your mina, Lord, has made five minas.'
031919 "So he said to him, 'And you are to be over five cities.'
031920 Another came, saying, 'Lord, behold, your mina, which I kept laid away in a handkerchief,
031921 for I feared you, because you are an exacting man. You take up that which you didn't lay down, and reap that which you didn't sow.'
031922 "He said to him, 'Out of your own mouth will I judge you, you wicked servant! You knew that I am an exacting man, taking up that which I didn't lay down, and reaping that which I didn't sow.
031923 Then why didn't you deposit my money in the bank, and at my coming, I might have earned interest on it?'
031924 He said to those who stood by, 'Take the mina away from him, and give it to him who has the ten minas.'
031925 "They said to him, 'Lord, he has ten minas!'
031926 'For I tell you that to everyone who has, will more be given; but from him who doesn't have, even that which he has will be taken away from him.
031927 But bring those enemies of mine who didn't want me to reign over them here, and kill them before me.'"
031928 Having said these things, he went on ahead, going up to Jerusalem.
031929 It happened, when he drew near to Bethsphage and Bethany, at the mountain that is called Olivet, he sent two of his disciples,
031930 saying, "Go your way into the village on the other side, in which, as you enter, you will find a colt tied, whereon no man ever yet sat. Untie it, and bring it.
031931 If anyone asks you, 'Why are you untying it?' say to him: 'The Lord needs it.'"
031932 Those who were sent went away, and found things just as he had told them.
031933 As they were untying the colt, its owners said to them, "Why are you untying the colt?"
031934 They said, "The Lord needs it."
031935 They brought it to Jesus. They threw their cloaks on the colt, and set Jesus on them.
031936 As he went, they spread their cloaks in the way.
031937 As he was now getting near, at the descent of the Mount of Olives, the whole multitude of the disciples began to rejoice and praise God with a loud voice for all the mighty works which they had seen,
031938 saying, "Blessed is the King who comes in the name of the Lord! Peace in heaven, and glory in the highest!"
031939 Some of the Pharisees from the multitude said to him, "Teacher, rebuke your disciples!"
031940 He answered them, "I tell you that if these were silent, the stones would cry out."
031941 When he drew near, he saw the city and wept over it,
031942 saying, "If you, even you, had known today the things which belong to your peace! But now, they are hidden from your eyes.
031943 For the days will come on you, when your enemies will throw up a barricade against you, surround you, hem you in on every side,
031944 and will dash you and your children within you to the ground. They will not leave in you one stone on another, because you didn't know the time of your visitation."
031945 He entered into the temple, and began to drive out those who bought and sold in it,
031946 saying to them, "It is written, 'My house is a house of prayer,' but you have made it a 'den of robbers'!"
031947 He was teaching daily in the temple, but the chief priests and the scribes and the leading men among the people sought to destroy him.
031948 They couldn't find what they might do, for all the people hung on to every word that he said.
032001 It happened on one of those days, as he was teaching the people in the temple and preaching the Good News, that the priests and scribes came to him with the elders.
032002 They asked him, "Tell us: by what authority do you do these things? Or who is giving you this authority?"
032003 He answered them, "I also will ask you one question. Tell me:
032004 the baptism of John, was it from heaven, or from men?"
032005 They reasoned with themselves, saying, "If we say, 'From heaven,' he will say, 'Why didn't you believe him?'
032006 But if we say, 'From men,' all the people will stone us, for they are persuaded that John was a prophet."
032007 They answered that they didn't know where it was from.
032008 Jesus said to them, "Neither will I tell you by what authority I do these things."
032009 He began to tell the people this parable. "A man planted a vineyard, and rented it out to some farmers, and went into another country for a long time.
032010 At the proper season, he sent a servant to the farmers to collect his share of the fruit of the vineyard. But the farmers beat him, and sent him away empty.
032011 He sent yet another servant, and they also beat him, and treated him shamefully, and sent him away empty.
032012 He sent yet a third, and they also wounded him, and threw him out.
032013 The lord of the vineyard said, 'What shall I do? I will send my beloved son. It may be that seeing him, they will respect him.'
032014 "But when the farmers saw him, they reasoned among themselves, saying, 'This is the heir. Come, let's kill him, that the inheritance may be ours.'
032015 They threw him out of the vineyard, and killed him. What therefore will the lord of the vineyard do to them?
032016 He will come and destroy these farmers, and will give the vineyard to others." When they heard it, they said, "May it never be!"
032017 But he looked at them, and said, "Then what is this that is written, 'The stone which the builders rejected, the same was made the chief cornerstone?'
