032018 Everyone who falls on that stone will be broken to pieces, but it will crush whomever it falls on to dust."
032019 The chief priests and the scribes sought to lay hands on him that very hour, but they feared the people--for they knew he had spoken this parable against them.
032020 They watched him, and sent out spies, who pretended to be righteous, that they might trap him in something he said, so as to deliver him up to the power and authority of the governor.
032021 They asked him, "Teacher, we know that you say and teach what is right, and aren't partial to anyone, but truly teach the way of God.
032022 Is it lawful for us to pay taxes to Caesar, or not?"
032023 But he perceived their craftiness, and said to them, "Why do you test me?
032024 Show me a denarius. Whose image and inscription are on it?" They answered, "Caesar's."
032025 He said to them, "Then give to Caesar the things that are Caesar's, and to God the things that are God's."
032026 They weren't able to trap him in his words before the people. They marveled at his answer, and were silent.
032027 Some of the Sadducees came to him, those who deny that there is a resurrection.
032028 They asked him, "Teacher, Moses wrote to us that if a man's brother dies having a wife, and he is childless, his brother should take the wife, and raise up children for his brother.
032029 There were therefore seven brothers. The first took a wife, and died childless.
032030 The second took her as wife, and he died childless.
032031 The third took her, and likewise the seven all left no children, and died.
032032 Afterward the woman also died.
032033 Therefore in the resurrection whose wife of them will she be? For the seven had her as a wife."
032034 Jesus said to them, "The children of this age marry, and are given in marriage.
032035 But those who are considered worthy to attain to that age and the resurrection from the dead, neither marry, nor are given in marriage.
032036 For they can't die any more, for they are like the angels, and are children of God, being children of the resurrection.
032037 But that the dead are raised, even Moses showed at the bush, when he called the Lord 'The God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob.'
032038 Now he is not the God of the dead, but of the living, for all are alive to him."
032039 Some of the scribes answered, "Teacher, you speak well."
032040 They didn't dare to ask him any more questions.
032041 He said to them, "Why do they say that the Christ is David's son?
032042 David himself says in the book of Psalms, 'The Lord said to my Lord, "Sit at my right hand,
032043 until I make your enemies the footstool of your feet."'
032044 "David therefore calls him Lord, so how is he his son?"
032045 In the hearing of all the people, he said to his disciples,
032046 "Beware of the scribes, who like to walk in long robes, and love greetings in the marketplaces, the best seats in the synagogues, and the best places at feasts;
032047 who devour widows' houses, and for a pretense make long prayers: these will receive greater condemnation."
032101 He looked up, and saw the rich people who were putting their gifts into the treasury.
032102 He saw a certain poor widow casting in two small brass coins.
032103 He said, "Truly I tell you, this poor widow put in more than all of them,
032104 for all these put in gifts for God from their abundance, but she, out of her poverty, put in all that she had to live on."
032105 As some were talking about the temple and how it was decorated with beautiful stones and gifts, he said,
032106 "As for these things which you see, the days will come, in which there will not be left here one stone on another that will not be thrown down."
032107 They asked him, "Teacher, so when will these things be? What is the sign that these things are about to happen?"
032108 He said, "Watch out that you don't get led astray, for many will come in my name, saying, 'I am he,' and, 'The time is at hand.' Therefore don't follow them.
032109 When you hear of wars and disturbances, don't be terrified, for these things must happen first, but the end won't come immediately."
032110 Then he said to them, "Nation will rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom.
032111 There will be great earthquakes, famines, and plagues in various places. There will be terrors and great signs from heaven.
032112 But before all these things, they will lay their hands on you and will persecute you, delivering you up to synagogues and prisons, bringing you before kings and governors for my name's sake.
032113 It will turn out as a testimony for you.
032114 Settle it therefore in your hearts not to meditate beforehand how to answer,
032115 for I will give you a mouth and wisdom which all your adversaries will not be able to withstand or to contradict.
032116 You will be handed over even by parents, brothers, relatives, and friends. They will cause some of you to be put to death.
032117 You will be hated by all men for my name's sake.
032118 And not a hair of your head will perish.
032119 "By your endurance you will win your lives.
032120 "But when you see Jerusalem surrounded by armies, then know that its desolation is at hand.
032121 Then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains. Let those who are in the midst of her depart. Let those who are in the country not enter therein.
032122 For these are days of vengeance, that all things which are written may be fulfilled.
032123 Woe to those who are pregnant and to those who nurse infants in those days! For there will be great distress in the land, and wrath to this people.
032124 They will fall by the edge of the sword, and will be led captive into all the nations. Jerusalem will be trampled down by the Gentiles, until the times of the Gentiles are fulfilled.
032125 There will be signs in the sun, moon, and stars; and on the earth anxiety of nations, in perplexity for the roaring of the sea and the waves;
032126 men fainting for fear, and for expectation of the things which are coming on the world: for the powers of the heavens will be shaken.
032127 Then they will see the Son of Man coming in a cloud with power and great glory.
032128 But when these things begin to happen, look up, and lift up your heads, because your redemption is near."
032129 He told them a parable. "See the fig tree, and all the trees.
032130 When they are already budding, you see it and know by your own selves that the summer is already near.
032131 Even so you also, when you see these things happening, know that the Kingdom of God is near.
032132 Most certainly I tell you, this generation will not pass away until all things are accomplished.
032133 Heaven and earth will pass away, but my words will by no means pass away.
032134 "So be careful, or your hearts will be loaded down with carousing, drunkenness, and cares of this life, and that day will come on you suddenly.
032135 For it will come like a snare on all those who dwell on the surface of all the earth.
032136 Therefore be watchful all the time, praying that you may be counted worthy to escape all these things that will happen, and to stand before the Son of Man."
032137 Every day Jesus was teaching in the temple, and every night he would go out and spend the night on the mountain that is called Olivet.
032138 All the people came early in the morning to him in the temple to hear him.
032201 Now the feast of unleavened bread, which is called the Passover, drew near.
032202 The chief priests and the scribes sought how they might put him to death, for they feared the people.
032203 Satan entered into Judas, who was surnamed Iscariot, who was numbered with the twelve.
032204 He went away, and talked with the chief priests and captains about how he might deliver him to them.
032205 They were glad, and agreed to give him money.
032206 He consented, and sought an opportunity to deliver him to them in the absence of the multitude.
032207 The day of unleavened bread came, on which the Passover must be sacrificed.
032208 He sent Peter and John, saying, "Go and prepare the Passover for us, that we may eat."
032209 They said to him, "Where do you want us to prepare?"
032210 He said to them, "Behold, when you have entered into the city, a man carrying a pitcher of water will meet you. Follow him into the house which he enters.
032211 Tell the master of the house, 'The Teacher says to you, "Where is the guest room, where I may eat the Passover with my disciples?"'
032212 He will show you a large, furnished upper room. Make preparations there."
032213 They went, found things as he had told them, and they prepared the Passover.
032214 When the hour had come, he sat down with the twelve apostles.
032215 He said to them, "I have earnestly desired to eat this Passover with you before I suffer,
032216 for I tell you, I will no longer by any means eat of it until it is fulfilled in the Kingdom of God."
032217 He received a cup, and when he had given thanks, he said, "Take this, and share it among yourselves,
032218 for I tell you, I will not drink at all again from the fruit of the vine, until the Kingdom of God comes."
032219 He took bread, and when he had given thanks, he broke it, and gave to them, saying, "This is my body which is given for you. Do this in memory of me."
032220 Likewise, he took the cup after supper, saying, "This cup is the new covenant in my blood, which is poured out for you.
032221 But behold, the hand of him who betrays me is with me on the table.
032222 The Son of Man indeed goes, as it has been determined, but woe to that man through whom he is betrayed!"
032223 They began to question among themselves, which of them it was who would do this thing.
032224 There arose also a contention among them, which of them was considered to be greatest.
032225 He said to them, "The kings of the nations lord it over them, and those who have authority over them are called 'benefactors.'
032226 But not so with you. But one who is the greater among you, let him become as the younger, and one who is governing, as one who serves.
032227 For who is greater, one who sits at the table, or one who serves? Isn't it he who sits at the table? But I am in the midst of you as one who serves.
032228 But you are those who have continued with me in my trials.
032229 I confer on you a kingdom, even as my Father conferred on me,
032230 that you may eat and drink at my table in my Kingdom. You will sit on thrones, judging the twelve tribes of Israel."
032231 The Lord said, "Simon, Simon, behold, Satan asked to have you, that he might sift you as wheat,
032232 but I prayed for you, that your faith wouldn't fail. You, when once you have turned again, establish your brothers."
032233 He said to him, "Lord, I am ready to go with you both to prison and to death!"
032234 He said, "I tell you, Peter, the rooster will by no means crow today until you deny that you know me three times."
032235 He said to them, "When I sent you out without purse, and wallet, and shoes, did you lack anything?" They said, "Nothing."
032236 Then he said to them, "But now, whoever has a purse, let him take it, and likewise a wallet. Whoever has none, let him sell his cloak, and buy a sword.
032237 For I tell you that this which is written must still be fulfilled in me: 'He was counted with transgressors.' For that which concerns me has an end."
032238 They said, "Lord, behold, here are two swords." He said to them, "That is enough."
032239 He came out, and went, as his custom was, to the Mount of Olives. His disciples also followed him.
032240 When he was at the place, he said to them, "Pray that you don't enter into temptation."
032241 He was withdrawn from them about a stone's throw, and he knelt down and prayed,
032242 saying, "Father, if you are willing, remove this cup from me. Nevertheless, not my will, but yours, be done."
032243 An angel from heaven appeared to him, strengthening him.
032244 Being in agony he prayed more earnestly. His sweat became like great drops of blood falling down on the ground.
032245 When he rose up from his prayer, he came to the disciples, and found them sleeping because of grief,
032246 and said to them, "Why do you sleep? Rise and pray that you may not enter into temptation."
032247 While he was still speaking, behold, a multitude, and he who was called Judas, one of the twelve, was leading them. He came near to Jesus to kiss him.
032248 But Jesus said to him, "Judas, do you betray the Son of Man with a kiss?"
032249 When those who were around him saw what was about to happen, they said to him, "Lord, shall we strike with the sword?"
032250 A certain one of them struck the servant of the high priest, and cut off his right ear.
032251 But Jesus answered, "Let me at least do this"--and he touched his ear, and healed him.
032252 Jesus said to the chief priests, captains of the temple, and elders, who had come against him, "Have you come out as against a robber, with swords and clubs?
032253 When I was with you in the temple daily, you didn't stretch out your hands against me. But this is your hour, and the power of darkness."
032254 They seized him, and led him away, and brought him into the high priest's house. But Peter followed from a distance.
032255 When they had kindled a fire in the middle of the courtyard, and had sat down together, Peter sat among them.
032256 A certain servant girl saw him as he sat in the light, and looking intently at him, said, "This man also was with him."
032257 He denied Jesus, saying, "Woman, I don't know him."
032258 After a little while someone else saw him, and said, "You also are one of them!" But Peter answered, "Man, I am not!"
032259 After about one hour passed, another confidently affirmed, saying, "Truly this man also was with him, for he is a Galilean!"
032260 But Peter said, "Man, I don't know what you are talking about!" Immediately, while he was still speaking, a rooster crowed.
032261 The Lord turned, and looked at Peter. Then Peter remembered the Lord's word, how he said to him, "Before the rooster crows you will deny me three times."
032262 He went out, and wept bitterly.
032263 The men who held Jesus mocked him and beat him.
032264 Having blindfolded him, they struck him on the face and asked him, "Prophesy! Who is the one who struck you?"
032265 They spoke many other things against him, insulting him.
032266 As soon as it was day, the assembly of the elders of the people was gathered together, both chief priests and scribes, and they led him away into their council, saying,
032267 "If you are the Christ, tell us." But he said to them, "If I tell you, you won't believe,
032268 and if I ask, you will in no way answer me or let me go.
032269 From now on, the Son of Man will be seated at the right hand of the power of God."
032270 They all said, "Are you then the Son of God?" He said to them, "You say it, because I am."
032271 They said, "Why do we need any more witness? For we ourselves have heard from his own mouth!"
032301 The whole company of them rose up and brought him before Pilate.
032302 They began to accuse him, saying, "We found this man perverting the nation, forbidding paying taxes to Caesar, and saying that he himself is Christ, a king."
032303 Pilate asked him, "Are you the King of the Jews?" He answered him, "So you say."
032304 Pilate said to the chief priests and the multitudes, "I find no basis for a charge against this man."
032305 But they insisted, saying, "He stirs up the people, teaching throughout all Judea, beginning from Galilee even to this place."
032306 But when Pilate heard Galilee mentioned, he asked if the man was a Galilean.
032307 When he found out that he was in Herod's jurisdiction, he sent him to Herod, who was also in Jerusalem during those days.
032308 Now when Herod saw Jesus, he was exceedingly glad, for he had wanted to see him for a long time, because he had heard many things about him. He hoped to see some miracle done by him.
032309 He questioned him with many words, but he gave no answers.
032310 The chief priests and the scribes stood, vehemently accusing him.
032311 Herod with his soldiers humiliated him and mocked him. Dressing him in luxurious clothing, they sent him back to Pilate.
032312 Herod and Pilate became friends with each other that very day, for before that they were enemies with each other.
032313 Pilate called together the chief priests and the rulers and the people,
032314 and said to them, "You brought this man to me as one that perverts the people, and see, I have examined him before you, and found no basis for a charge against this man concerning those things of which you accuse him.
032315 Neither has Herod, for I sent you to him, and see, nothing worthy of death has been done by him.
032316 I will therefore chastise him and release him."
032317 Now he had to release one prisoner to them at the feast.
032318 But they all cried out together, saying, "Away with this man! Release to us Barabbas!"--
032319 one who was thrown into prison for a certain revolt in the city, and for murder.
032320 Then Pilate spoke to them again, wanting to release Jesus,
032321 but they shouted, saying, "Crucify! Crucify him!"
032322 He said to them the third time, "Why? What evil has this man done? I have found no capital crime in him. I will therefore chastise him and release him."
032323 But they were urgent with loud voices, asking that he might be crucified. Their voices and the voices of the chief priests prevailed.
032324 Pilate decreed that what they asked for should be done.
032325 He released him who had been thrown into prison for insurrection and murder, for whom they asked, but he delivered Jesus up to their will.
032326 When they led him away, they grabbed one Simon of Cyrene, coming from the country, and laid on him the cross, to carry it after Jesus.
032327 A great multitude of the people followed him, including women who also mourned and lamented him.
032328 But Jesus, turning to them, said, "Daughters of Jerusalem, don't weep for me, but weep for yourselves and for your children.
032329 For behold, the days are coming in which they will say, 'Blessed are the barren, the wombs that never bore, and the breasts that never nursed.'
032330 Then they will begin to tell the mountains, 'Fall on us!' and tell the hills, 'Cover us.'
032331 For if they do these things in the green tree, what will be done in the dry?"
032332 There were also others, two criminals, led with him to be put to death.
032333 When they came to the place that is called The Skull, they crucified him there with the criminals, one on the right and the other on the left.
032334 Jesus said, "Father, forgive them, for they don't know what they are doing." Dividing his garments among them, they cast lots.
032335 The people stood watching. The rulers with them also scoffed at him, saying, "He saved others. Let him save himself, if this is the Christ of God, his chosen one!"
032336 The soldiers also mocked him, coming to him and offering him vinegar,
032337 and saying, "If you are the King of the Jews, save yourself!"
032338 An inscription was also written over him in letters of Greek, Latin, and Hebrew: "THIS IS THE KING OF THE JEWS."
032339 One of the criminals who was hanged insulted him, saying, "If you are the Christ, save yourself and us!"
032340 But the other answered, and rebuking him said, "Don't you even fear God, seeing you are under the same condemnation?
032341 And we indeed justly, for we receive the due reward for our deeds, but this man has done nothing wrong."
032342 He said to Jesus, "Lord, remember me when you come into your Kingdom."
032343 Jesus said to him, "Assuredly I tell you, today you will be with me in Paradise."
032344 It was now about the sixth hour, and darkness came over the whole land until the ninth hour.
032345 The sun was darkened, and the veil of the temple was torn in two.
032346 Jesus, crying with a loud voice, said, "Father, into your hands I commit my spirit!" Having said this, he breathed his last.
032347 When the centurion saw what was done, he glorified God, saying, "Certainly this was a righteous man."
032348 All the multitudes that came together to see this, when they saw the things that were done, returned home beating their breasts.
032349 All his acquaintances, and the women who followed with him from Galilee, stood at a distance, watching these things.
032350 Behold, a man named Joseph, who was a member of the council, a good and righteous man
032351 (he had not consented to their counsel and deed), from Arimathaea, a city of the Jews, who was also waiting for the Kingdom of God:
032352 this man went to Pilate, and asked for Jesus' body.
032353 He took it down, and wrapped it in a linen cloth, and laid him in a tomb that was cut in stone, where no one had ever been laid.
032354 It was the day of the Preparation, and the Sabbath was drawing near.
032355 The women, who had come with him out of Galilee, followed after, and saw the tomb, and how his body was laid.
032356 They returned, and prepared spices and ointments. On the Sabbath they rested according to the commandment.
032401 But on the first day of the week, at early dawn, they and some others came to the tomb, bringing the spices which they had prepared.
032402 They found the stone rolled away from the tomb.
032403 They entered in, and didn't find the Lord Jesus' body.
032404 It happened, while they were greatly perplexed about this, behold, two men stood by them in dazzling clothing.
032405 Becoming terrified, they bowed their faces down to the earth. They said to them, "Why do you seek the living among the dead?
032406 He isn't here, but is risen. Remember what he told you when he was still in Galilee,
032407 saying that the Son of Man must be delivered up into the hands of sinful men, and be crucified, and the third day rise again?"
032408 They remembered his words,
032409 returned from the tomb, and told all these things to the eleven, and to all the rest.
032410 Now they were Mary Magdalene, Joanna, and Mary the mother of James. The other women with them told these things to the apostles.
032411 These words seemed to them to be nonsense, and they didn't believe them.
032412 But Peter got up and ran to the tomb. Stooping and looking in, he saw the strips of linen lying by themselves, and he departed to his home, wondering what had happened.
032413 Behold, two of them were going that very day to a village named Emmaus, which was sixty stadia from Jerusalem.
032414 They talked with each other about all of these things which had happened.
032415 It happened, while they talked and questioned together, that Jesus himself came near, and went with them.
032416 But their eyes were kept from recognizing him.
032417 He said to them, "What are you talking about as you walk, and are sad?"
032418 One of them, named Cleopas, answered him, "Are you the only stranger in Jerusalem who doesn't know the things which have happened there in these days?"
032419 He said to them, "What things?" They said to him, "The things concerning Jesus, the Nazarene, who was a prophet mighty in deed and word before God and all the people;
032420 and how the chief priests and our rulers delivered him up to be condemned to death, and crucified him.
032421 But we were hoping that it was he who would redeem Israel. Yes, and besides all this, it is now the third day since these things happened.
032422 Also, certain women of our company amazed us, having arrived early at the tomb;
032423 and when they didn't find his body, they came saying that they had also seen a vision of angels, who said that he was alive.
032424 Some of us went to the tomb, and found it just like the women had said, but they didn't see him."
032425 He said to them, "Foolish men, and slow of heart to believe in all that the prophets have spoken!
032426 Didn't the Christ have to suffer these things and to enter into his glory?"
032427 Beginning from Moses and from all the prophets, he explained to them in all the Scriptures the things concerning himself.
032428 They drew near to the village, where they were going, and he acted like he would go further.
032429 They urged him, saying, "Stay with us, for it is almost evening, and the day is almost over." He went in to stay with them.
032430 It happened, that when he had sat down at the table with them, he took the bread and gave thanks. Breaking it, he gave to them.
032431 Their eyes were opened, and they recognized him, and he vanished out of their sight.
032432 They said one to another, "Weren't our hearts burning within us, while he spoke to us along the way, and while he opened the Scriptures to us?"
032433 They rose up that very hour, returned to Jerusalem, and found the eleven gathered together, and those who were with them,
032434 saying, "The Lord is risen indeed, and has appeared to Simon!"
032435 They related the things that happened along the way, and how he was recognized by them in the breaking of the bread.
032436 As they said these things, Jesus himself stood among them, and said to them, "Peace be to you."
032437 But they were terrified and filled with fear, and supposed that they had seen a spirit.
032438 He said to them, "Why are you troubled? Why do doubts arise in your hearts?
032439 See my hands and my feet, that it is truly me. Touch me and see, for a spirit doesn't have flesh and bones, as you see that I have."
032440 When he had said this, he showed them his hands and his feet.
032441 While they still didn't believe for joy, and wondered, he said to them, "Do you have anything here to eat?"
032442 They gave him a piece of a broiled fish and some honeycomb.
032443 He took them, and ate in front of them.
032444 He said to them, "This is what I told you, while I was still with you, that all things which are written in the law of Moses, the prophets, and the psalms, concerning me must be fulfilled."
032445 Then he opened their minds, that they might understand the Scriptures.
032446 He said to them, "Thus it is written, and thus it was necessary for the Christ to suffer and to rise from the dead the third day,
032447 and that repentance and remission of sins should be preached in his name to all the nations, beginning at Jerusalem.
032448 You are witnesses of these things.
032449 Behold, I send forth the promise of my Father on you. But wait in the city of Jerusalem until you are clothed with power from on high."
032450 He led them out as far as Bethany, and he lifted up his hands, and blessed them.
032451 It happened, while he blessed them, that he withdrew from them, and was carried up into heaven.
032452 They worshiped him, and returned to Jerusalem with great joy,
032453 and were continually in the temple, praising and blessing God. Amen.
040101 In the beginning was the Word, and the Word was with God, and the Word was God.
040102 The same was in the beginning with God.
040103 All things were made through him. Without him was not anything made that has been made.
040104 In him was life, and the life was the light of men.
040105 The light shines in the darkness, and the darkness hasn't overcome it.
040106 There came a man, sent from God, whose name was John.
040107 The same came as a witness, that he might testify about the light, that all might believe through him.
040108 He was not the light, but was sent that he might testify about the light.
040109 The true light that enlightens everyone was coming into the world.
040110 He was in the world, and the world was made through him, and the world didn't recognize him.
040111 He came to his own, and those who were his own didn't receive him.
040112 But as many as received him, to them he gave the right to become God's children, to those who believe in his name:
040113 who were born not of blood, nor of the will of the flesh, nor of the will of man, but of God.
040114 The Word became flesh, and lived among us. We saw his glory, such glory as of the one and only Son of the Father, full of grace and truth.
040115 John testified about him. He cried out, saying, "This was he of whom I said, 'He who comes after me has surpassed me, for he was before me.'"
040116 From his fullness we all received grace upon grace.
040117 For the law was given through Moses. Grace and truth were realized through Jesus Christ.
040118 No one has seen God at any time. The one and only Son, who is in the bosom of the Father, he has declared him.
040119 This is John's testimony, when the Jews sent priests and Levites from Jerusalem to ask him, "Who are you?"
040120 He declared, and didn't deny, but he declared, "I am not the Christ."
040121 They asked him, "What then? Are you Elijah?" He said, "I am not." "Are you the prophet?" He answered, "No."
040122 They said therefore to him, "Who are you? Give us an answer to take back to those who sent us. What do you say about yourself?"
040123 He said, "I am the voice of one crying in the wilderness, 'Make straight the way of the Lord,' as Isaiah the prophet said."
040124 The ones who had been sent were from the Pharisees.
040125 They asked him, "Why then do you baptize, if you are not the Christ, nor Elijah, nor the prophet?"
040126 John answered them, "I baptize in water, but among you stands one whom you don't know.
040127 He is the one who comes after me, who is preferred before me, whose sandal strap I'm not worthy to loosen."
040128 These things were done in Bethany beyond the Jordan, where John was baptizing.
040129 The next day, he saw Jesus coming to him, and said, "Behold, the Lamb of God, who takes away the sin of the world!
040130 This is he of whom I said, 'After me comes a man who is preferred before me, for he was before me.'
040131 I didn't know him, but for this reason I came baptizing in water: that he would be revealed to Israel."
040132 John testified, saying, "I have seen the Spirit descending like a dove out of heaven, and it remained on him.
040133 I didn't recognize him, but he who sent me to baptize in water, he said to me, 'On whomever you will see the Spirit descending, and remaining on him, the same is he who baptizes in the Holy Spirit.'
040134 I have seen, and have testified that this is the Son of God."
040135 Again, the next day, John was standing with two of his disciples,
040136 and he looked at Jesus as he walked, and said, "Behold, the Lamb of God!"
040137 The two disciples heard him speak, and they followed Jesus.
040138 Jesus turned, and saw them following, and said to them, "What are you looking for?" They said to him, "Rabbi" (which is to say, being interpreted, Teacher), "where are you staying?"
040139 He said to them, "Come, and see." They came and saw where he was staying, and they stayed with him that day. It was about the tenth hour.
040140 One of the two who heard John, and followed him, was Andrew, Simon Peter's brother.
040141 He first found his own brother, Simon, and said to him, "We have found the Messiah!" (which is, being interpreted, Christ).
040142 He brought him to Jesus. Jesus looked at him, and said, "You are Simon the son of Jonah. You shall be called Cephas" (which is by interpretation, Peter).
040143 On the next day, he was determined to go out into Galilee, and he found Philip. Jesus said to him, "Follow me."
040144 Now Philip was from Bethsaida, of the city of Andrew and Peter.
040145 Philip found Nathanael, and said to him, "We have found him, of whom Moses in the law, and the prophets, wrote: Jesus of Nazareth, the son of Joseph."
040146 Nathanael said to him, "Can any good thing come out of Nazareth?" Philip said to him, "Come and see."
040147 Jesus saw Nathanael coming to him, and said about him, "Behold, an Israelite indeed, in whom is no deceit!"
040148 Nathanael said to him, "How do you know me?" Jesus answered him, "Before Philip called you, when you were under the fig tree, I saw you."
040149 Nathanael answered him, "Rabbi, you are the Son of God! You are King of Israel!"
040150 Jesus answered him, "Because I told you, 'I saw you underneath the fig tree,' do you believe? You will see greater things than these!"
040151 He said to him, "Most certainly, I tell you, hereafter you will see heaven opened, and the angels of God ascending and descending on the Son of Man."
040201 The third day, there was a marriage in Cana of Galilee. Jesus' mother was there.
040202 Jesus also was invited, with his disciples, to the marriage.
040203 When the wine ran out, Jesus' mother said to him, "They have no wine."
040204 Jesus said to her, "Woman, what does that have to do with you and me? My hour has not yet come."
040205 His mother said to the servants, "Whatever he says to you, do it."
040206 Now there were six water pots of stone set there after the Jews' manner of purifying, containing two or three metretes apiece.
040207 Jesus said to them, "Fill the water pots with water." They filled them up to the brim.
040208 He said to them, "Now draw some out, and take it to the ruler of the feast." So they took it.
040209 When the ruler of the feast tasted the water now become wine, and didn't know where it came from (but the servants who had drawn the water knew), the ruler of the feast called the bridegroom,
040210 and said to him, "Everyone serves the good wine first, and when the guests have drunk freely, then that which is worse. You have kept the good wine until now!"
040211 This beginning of his signs Jesus did in Cana of Galilee, and revealed his glory; and his disciples believed in him.
040212 After this, he went down to Capernaum, he, and his mother, his brothers, and his disciples; and they stayed there a few days.
040213 The Passover of the Jews was at hand, and Jesus went up to Jerusalem.
040214 He found in the temple those who sold oxen, sheep, and doves, and the changers of money sitting.
040215 He made a whip of cords, and threw all out of the temple, both the sheep and the oxen; and he poured out the changers' money, and overthrew their tables.
040216 To those who sold the doves, he said, "Take these things out of here! Don't make my Father's house a marketplace!"
040217 His disciples remembered that it was written, "Zeal for your house will eat me up."
040218 The Jews therefore answered him, "What sign do you show us, seeing that you do these things?"
040219 Jesus answered them, "Destroy this temple, and in three days I will raise it up."
040220 The Jews therefore said, "Forty-six years was this temple in building, and will you raise it up in three days?"
040221 But he spoke of the temple of his body.
040222 When therefore he was raised from the dead, his disciples remembered that he said this, and they believed the Scripture, and the word which Jesus had said.
040223 Now when he was in Jerusalem at the Passover, during the feast, many believed in his name, observing his signs which he did.
040224 But Jesus didn't trust himself to them, because he knew everyone,
040225 and because he didn't need for anyone to testify concerning man; for he himself knew what was in man.
040301 Now there was a man of the Pharisees named Nicodemus, a ruler of the Jews.
040302 The same came to him by night, and said to him, "Rabbi, we know that you are a teacher come from God, for no one can do these signs that you do, unless God is with him."
040303 Jesus answered him, "Most certainly, I tell you, unless one is born anew, he can't see the Kingdom of God."
040304 Nicodemus said to him, "How can a man be born when he is old? Can he enter a second time into his mother's womb, and be born?"
040305 Jesus answered, "Most certainly I tell you, unless one is born of water and spirit, he can't enter into the Kingdom of God!
040306 That which is born of the flesh is flesh. That which is born of the Spirit is spirit.
040307 Don't marvel that I said to you, 'You must be born anew.'
040308 The wind blows where it wants to, and you hear its sound, but don't know where it comes from and where it is going. So is everyone who is born of the Spirit."
040309 Nicodemus answered him, "How can these things be?"
040310 Jesus answered him, "Are you the teacher of Israel, and don't understand these things?
040311 Most certainly I tell you, we speak that which we know, and testify of that which we have seen, and you don't receive our witness.
040312 If I told you earthly things and you don't believe, how will you believe if I tell you heavenly things?
040313 No one has ascended into heaven, but he who descended out of heaven, the Son of Man, who is in heaven.
040314 As Moses lifted up the serpent in the wilderness, even so must the Son of Man be lifted up,
040315 that whoever believes in him should not perish, but have eternal life.
040316 For God so loved the world, that he gave his one and only Son, that whoever believes in him should not perish, but have eternal life.
040317 For God didn't send his Son into the world to judge the world, but that the world should be saved through him.
040318 He who believes in him is not judged. He who doesn't believe has been judged already, because he has not believed in the name of the one and only Son of God.
040319 This is the judgment, that the light has come into the world, and men loved the darkness rather than the light; for their works were evil.
040320 For everyone who does evil hates the light, and doesn't come to the light, lest his works would be exposed.
040321 But he who does the truth comes to the light, that his works may be revealed, that they have been done in God."
040322 After these things, Jesus came with his disciples into the land of Judea. He stayed there with them, and baptized.
040323 John also was baptizing in Enon near Salim, because there was much water there. They came, and were baptized.
040324 For John was not yet thrown into prison.
040325 There arose therefore a questioning on the part of John's disciples with some Jews about purification.
040326 They came to John, and said to him, "Rabbi, he who was with you beyond the Jordan, to whom you have testified, behold, the same baptizes, and everyone is coming to him."
040327 John answered, "A man can receive nothing, unless it has been given him from heaven.
040328 You yourselves testify that I said, 'I am not the Christ,' but, 'I have been sent before him.'
040329 He who has the bride is the bridegroom; but the friend of the bridegroom, who stands and hears him, rejoices greatly because of the bridegroom's voice. This, my joy, therefore is made full.
040330 He must increase, but I must decrease.
040331 He who comes from above is above all. He who is from the Earth belongs to the Earth, and speaks of the Earth. He who comes from heaven is above all.
040332 What he has seen and heard, of that he testifies; and no one receives his witness.
040333 He who has received his witness has set his seal to this, that God is true.
040334 For he whom God has sent speaks the words of God; for God gives the Spirit without measure.
040335 The Father loves the Son, and has given all things into his hand.
040336 One who believes in the Son has eternal life, but one who disobeys the Son won't see life, but the wrath of God remains on him."
040401 Therefore when the Lord knew that the Pharisees had heard that Jesus was making and baptizing more disciples than John
040402 (although Jesus himself didn't baptize, but his disciples),
040403 he left Judea, and departed into Galilee.
040404 He needed to pass through Samaria.
040405 So he came to a city of Samaria, called Sychar, near the parcel of ground that Jacob gave to his son, Joseph.
040406 Jacob's well was there. Jesus therefore, being tired from his journey, sat down by the well. It was about the sixth hour.
040407 A woman of Samaria came to draw water. Jesus said to her, "Give me a drink."
040408 For his disciples had gone away into the city to buy food.
040409 The Samaritan woman therefore said to him, "How is it that you, being a Jew, ask for a drink from me, a Samaritan woman?" (For Jews have no dealings with Samaritans.)
040410 Jesus answered her, "If you knew the gift of God, and who it is who says to you, 'Give me a drink,' you would have asked him, and he would have given you living water."
040411 The woman said to him, "Sir, you have nothing to draw with, and the well is deep. From where then have you that living water?
040412 Are you greater than our father, Jacob, who gave us the well, and drank of it himself, as did his children, and his livestock?"
040413 Jesus answered her, "Everyone who drinks of this water will thirst again,
040414 but whoever drinks of the water that I will give him will never thirst again; but the water that I will give him will become in him a well of water springing up to eternal life."
040415 The woman said to him, "Sir, give me this water, so that I don't get thirsty, neither come all the way here to draw."
040416 Jesus said to her, "Go, call your husband, and come here."
040417 The woman answered, "I have no husband." Jesus said to her, "You said well, 'I have no husband,'
040418 for you have had five husbands; and he whom you now have is not your husband. This you have said truly."
040419 The woman said to him, "Sir, I perceive that you are a prophet.
040420 Our fathers worshiped in this mountain, and you Jews say that in Jerusalem is the place where people ought to worship."
040421 Jesus said to her, "Woman, believe me, the hour comes, when neither in this mountain, nor in Jerusalem, will you worship the Father.
040422 You worship that which you don't know. We worship that which we know; for salvation is from the Jews.
040423 But the hour comes, and now is, when the true worshippers will worship the Father in spirit and truth, for the Father seeks such to be his worshippers.
040424 God is spirit, and those who worship him must worship in spirit and truth."
040425 The woman said to him, "I know that Messiah comes," (he who is called Christ). "When he has come, he will declare to us all things."
040426 Jesus said to her, "I am he, the one who speaks to you."
040427 At this, his disciples came. They marveled that he was speaking with a woman; yet no one said, "What are you looking for?" or, "Why do you speak with her?"
040428 So the woman left her water pot, and went away into the city, and said to the people,
040429 "Come, see a man who told me everything that I did. Can this be the Christ?"
040430 They went out of the city, and were coming to him.
040431 In the meanwhile, the disciples urged him, saying, "Rabbi, eat."
040432 But he said to them, "I have food to eat that you don't know about."
040433 The disciples therefore said one to another, "Has anyone brought him something to eat?"
040434 Jesus said to them, "My food is to do the will of him who sent me, and to accomplish his work.
040435 Don't you say, 'There are yet four months until the harvest?' Behold, I tell you, lift up your eyes, and look at the fields, that they are white for harvest already.
040436 He who reaps receives wages, and gathers fruit to eternal life; that both he who sows and he who reaps may rejoice together.
040437 For in this the saying is true, 'One sows, and another reaps.'
040438 I sent you to reap that for which you haven't labored. Others have labored, and you have entered into their labor."
040439 From that city many of the Samaritans believed in him because of the word of the woman, who testified, "He told me everything that I did."
040440 So when the Samaritans came to him, they begged him to stay with them. He stayed there two days.
040441 Many more believed because of his word.
040442 They said to the woman, "Now we believe, not because of your speaking; for we have heard for ourselves, and know that this is indeed the Christ, the Savior of the world."
040443 After the two days he went out from there and went into Galilee.
040444 For Jesus himself testified that a prophet has no honor in his own country.
040445 So when he came into Galilee, the Galileans received him, having seen all the things that he did in Jerusalem at the feast, for they also went to the feast.
040446 Jesus came therefore again to Cana of Galilee, where he made the water into wine. There was a certain nobleman whose son was sick at Capernaum.
040447 When he heard that Jesus had come out of Judea into Galilee, he went to him, and begged him that he would come down and heal his son, for he was at the point of death.
040448 Jesus therefore said to him, "Unless you see signs and wonders, you will in no way believe."
040449 The nobleman said to him, "Sir, come down before my child dies."
040450 Jesus said to him, "Go your way. Your son lives." The man believed the word that Jesus spoke to him, and he went his way.
040451 As he was now going down, his servants met him and reported, saying "Your child lives!"
040452 So he inquired of them the hour when he began to get better. They said therefore to him, "Yesterday at the seventh hour, the fever left him."
040453 So the father knew that it was at that hour in which Jesus said to him, "Your son lives." He believed, as did his whole house.
040454 This is again the second sign that Jesus did, having come out of Judea into Galilee.
040501 After these things, there was a feast of the Jews, and Jesus went up to Jerusalem.
040502 Now in Jerusalem by the sheep gate, there is a pool, which is called in Hebrew, "Bethesda," having five porches.
040503 In these lay a great multitude of those who were sick, blind, lame, or paralyzed, waiting for the moving of the water;
040504 for an angel of the Lord went down at certain times into the pool, and stirred up the water. Whoever stepped in first after the stirring of the water was made whole of whatever disease he had.
040505 A certain man was there, who had been sick for thirty-eight years.
040506 When Jesus saw him lying there, and knew that he had been sick for a long time, he asked him, "Do you want to be made well?"
040507 The sick man answered him, "Sir, I have no one to put me into the pool when the water is stirred up, but while I'm coming, another steps down before me."
040508 Jesus said to him, "Arise, take up your mat, and walk."
040509 Immediately, the man was made well, and took up his mat and walked. Now it was the Sabbath on that day.
040510 So the Jews said to him who was cured, "It is the Sabbath. It is not lawful for you to carry the mat."
040511 He answered them, "He who made me well, the same said to me, 'Take up your mat, and walk.'"
040512 Then they asked him, "Who is the man who said to you, 'Take up your mat, and walk'?"
040513 But he who was healed didn't know who it was, for Jesus had withdrawn, a crowd being in the place.
040514 Afterward Jesus found him in the temple, and said to him, "Behold, you are made well. Sin no more, so that nothing worse happens to you."
040515 The man went away, and told the Jews that it was Jesus who had made him well.
040516 For this cause the Jews persecuted Jesus, and sought to kill him, because he did these things on the Sabbath.
040517 But Jesus answered them, "My Father is still working, so I am working, too."
040518 For this cause therefore the Jews sought all the more to kill him, because he not only broke the Sabbath, but also called God his own Father, making himself equal with God.
040519 Jesus therefore answered them, "Most certainly, I tell you, the Son can do nothing of himself, but what he sees the Father doing. For whatever things he does, these the Son also does likewise.
040520 For the Father has affection for the Son, and shows him all things that he himself does. He will show him greater works than these, that you may marvel.
040521 For as the Father raises the dead and gives them life, even so the Son also gives life to whom he desires.
040522 For the Father judges no one, but he has given all judgment to the Son,
040523 that all may honor the Son, even as they honor the Father. He who doesn't honor the Son doesn't honor the Father who sent him.
040524 "Most certainly I tell you, he who hears my word, and believes him who sent me, has eternal life, and doesn't come into judgment, but has passed out of death into life.
040525 Most certainly, I tell you, the hour comes, and now is, when the dead will hear the Son of God's voice; and those who hear will live.
040526 For as the Father has life in himself, even so he gave to the Son also to have life in himself.
040527 He also gave him authority to execute judgment, because he is a son of man.
040528 Don't marvel at this, for the hour comes, in which all that are in the tombs will hear his voice,
040529 and will come out; those who have done good, to the resurrection of life; and those who have done evil, to the resurrection of judgment.
040530 I can of myself do nothing. As I hear, I judge, and my judgment is righteous; because I don't seek my own will, but the will of my Father who sent me.
040531 "If I testify about myself, my witness is not valid.
040532 It is another who testifies about me. I know that the testimony which he testifies about me is true.
040533 You have sent to John, and he has testified to the truth.
040534 But the testimony which I receive is not from man. However, I say these things that you may be saved.
040535 He was the burning and shining lamp, and you were willing to rejoice for a while in his light.
040536 But the testimony which I have is greater than that of John, for the works which the Father gave me to accomplish, the very works that I do, testify about me, that the Father has sent me.
040537 The Father himself, who sent me, has testified about me. You have neither heard his voice at any time, nor seen his form.
040538 You don't have his word living in you; because you don't believe him whom he sent.
040539 "You search the Scriptures, because you think that in them you have eternal life; and these are they which testify about me.
040540 Yet you will not come to me, that you may have life.
040541 I don't receive glory from men.
040542 But I know you, that you don't have God's love in yourselves.
040543 I have come in my Father's name, and you don't receive me. If another comes in his own name, you will receive him.
040544 How can you believe, who receive glory from one another, and you don't seek the glory that comes from the only God?
040545 "Don't think that I will accuse you to the Father. There is one who accuses you, even Moses, on whom you have set your hope.
040546 For if you believed Moses, you would believe me; for he wrote about me.
040547 But if you don't believe his writings, how will you believe my words?"
040601 After these things, Jesus went away to the other side of the sea of Galilee, which is also called the Sea of Tiberias.
040602 A great multitude followed him, because they saw his signs which he did on those who were sick.
040603 Jesus went up into the mountain, and he sat there with his disciples.
040604 Now the Passover, the feast of the Jews, was at hand.
040605 Jesus therefore lifting up his eyes, and seeing that a great multitude was coming to him, said to Philip, "Where are we to buy bread, that these may eat?"
040606 This he said to test him, for he himself knew what he would do.
040607 Philip answered him, "Two hundred denarii worth of bread is not sufficient for them, that everyone of them may receive a little."
040608 One of his disciples, Andrew, Simon Peter's brother, said to him,
040609 "There is a boy here who has five barley loaves and two fish, but what are these among so many?"
040610 Jesus said, "Have the people sit down." Now there was much grass in that place. So the men sat down, in number about five thousand.
040611 Jesus took the loaves; and having given thanks, he distributed to the disciples, and the disciples to those who were sitting down; likewise also of the fish as much as they desired.
040612 When they were filled, he said to his disciples, "Gather up the broken pieces which are left over, that nothing be lost."
040613 So they gathered them up, and filled twelve baskets with broken pieces from the five barley loaves, which were left over by those who had eaten.
040614 When therefore the people saw the sign which Jesus did, they said, "This is truly the prophet who comes into the world."
040615 Jesus therefore, perceiving that they were about to come and take him by force, to make him king, withdrew again to the mountain by himself.
040616 When evening came, his disciples went down to the sea,
040617 and they entered into the boat, and were going over the sea to Capernaum. It was now dark, and Jesus had not come to them.
040618 The sea was tossed by a great wind blowing.
040619 When therefore they had rowed about twenty-five or thirty stadia, they saw Jesus walking on the sea, and drawing near to the boat; and they were afraid.
040620 But he said to them, "It is I. Don't be afraid."
040621 They were willing therefore to receive him into the boat. Immediately the boat was at the land where they were going.
040622 On the next day, the multitude that stood on the other side of the sea saw that there was no other boat there, except the one in which his disciples had embarked, and that Jesus hadn't entered with his disciples into the boat, but his disciples had gone away alone.
040623 However boats from Tiberias came near to the place where they ate the bread after the Lord had given thanks.
040624 When the multitude therefore saw that Jesus wasn't there, nor his disciples, they themselves got into the boats, and came to Capernaum, seeking Jesus.
040625 When they found him on the other side of the sea, they asked him, "Rabbi, when did you come here?"
040626 Jesus answered them, "Most certainly I tell you, you seek me, not because you saw signs, but because you ate of the loaves, and were filled.
040627 Don't work for the food which perishes, but for the food which remains to eternal life, which the Son of Man will give to you. For God the Father has sealed him."
040628 They said therefore to him, "What must we do, that we may work the works of God?"
040629 Jesus answered them, "This is the work of God, that you believe in him whom he has sent."
040630 They said therefore to him, "What then do you do for a sign, that we may see, and believe you? What work do you do?
040631 Our fathers ate the manna in the wilderness. As it is written, 'He gave them bread out of heaven to eat.'"
040632 Jesus therefore said to them, "Most certainly, I tell you, it wasn't Moses who gave you the bread out of heaven, but my Father gives you the true bread out of heaven.
040633 For the bread of God is that which comes down out of heaven, and gives life to the world."
040634 They said therefore to him, "Lord, always give us this bread."
040635 Jesus said to them, "I am the bread of life. He who comes to me will not be hungry, and he who believes in me will never be thirsty.
040636 But I told you that you have seen me, and yet you don't believe.
040637 All those who the Father gives me will come to me. Him who comes to me I will in no way throw out.
040638 For I have come down from heaven, not to do my own will, but the will of him who sent me.
040639 This is the will of my Father who sent me, that of all he has given to me I should lose nothing, but should raise him up at the last day.
040640 This is the will of the one who sent me, that everyone who sees the Son, and believes in him, should have eternal life; and I will raise him up at the last day."
040641 The Jews therefore murmured concerning him, because he said, "I am the bread which came down out of heaven."
040642 They said, "Isn't this Jesus, the son of Joseph, whose father and mother we know? How then does he say, 'I have come down out of heaven?'"
040643 Therefore Jesus answered them, "Don't murmur among yourselves.
040644 No one can come to me unless the Father who sent me draws him, and I will raise him up in the last day.
040645 It is written in the prophets, 'They will all be taught by God.' Therefore everyone who hears from the Father, and has learned, comes to me.
040646 Not that anyone has seen the Father, except he who is from God. He has seen the Father.
040647 Most certainly, I tell you, he who believes in me has eternal life.
040648 I am the bread of life.
040649 Your fathers ate the manna in the wilderness, and they died.
040650 This is the bread which comes down out of heaven, that anyone may eat of it and not die.
040651 I am the living bread which came down out of heaven. If anyone eats of this bread, he will live forever. Yes, the bread which I will give for the life of the world is my flesh."
040652 The Jews therefore contended with one another, saying, "How can this man give us his flesh to eat?"
040653 Jesus therefore said to them, "Most certainly I tell you, unless you eat the flesh of the Son of Man and drink his blood, you don't have life in yourselves.
040654 He who eats my flesh and drinks my blood has eternal life, and I will raise him up at the last day.
040655 For my flesh is food indeed, and my blood is drink indeed.
040656 He who eats my flesh and drinks my blood lives in me, and I in him.
040657 As the living Father sent me, and I live because of the Father; so he who feeds on me, he will also live because of me.
040658 This is the bread which came down out of heaven--not as our fathers ate the manna, and died. He who eats this bread will live forever."
040659 He said these things in the synagogue, as he taught in Capernaum.
040660 Therefore many of his disciples, when they heard this, said, "This is a hard saying! Who can listen to it?"
040661 But Jesus knowing in himself that his disciples murmured at this, said to them, "Does this cause you to stumble?
040662 Then what if you would see the Son of Man ascending to where he was before?
040663 It is the spirit who gives life. The flesh profits nothing. The words that I speak to you are spirit, and are life.
040664 But there are some of you who don't believe." For Jesus knew from the beginning who they were who didn't believe, and who it was who would betray him.
040665 He said, "For this cause have I said to you that no one can come to me, unless it is given to him by my Father."
040666 At this, many of his disciples went back, and walked no more with him.
040667 Jesus said therefore to the twelve, "You don't also want to go away, do you?"
040668 Simon Peter answered him, "Lord, to whom would we go? You have the words of eternal life.
040669 We have come to believe and know that you are the Christ, the Son of the living God."
040670 Jesus answered them, "Didn't I choose you, the twelve, and one of you is a devil?"
040671 Now he spoke of Judas, the son of Simon Iscariot, for it was he who would betray him, being one of the twelve.
040701 After these things, Jesus was walking in Galilee, for he wouldn't walk in Judea, because the Jews sought to kill him.
040702 Now the feast of the Jews, the Feast of Booths, was at hand.
040703 His brothers therefore said to him, "Depart from here, and go into Judea, that your disciples also may see your works which you do.
040704 For no one does anything in secret, and himself seeks to be known openly. If you do these things, reveal yourself to the world."
040705 For even his brothers didn't believe in him.
040706 Jesus therefore said to them, "My time has not yet come, but your time is always ready.
040707 The world can't hate you, but it hates me, because I testify about it, that its works are evil.
040708 You go up to the feast. I am not yet going up to this feast, because my time is not yet fulfilled."
040709 Having said these things to them, he stayed in Galilee.
040710 But when his brothers had gone up to the feast, then he also went up, not publicly, but as it were in secret.
040711 The Jews therefore sought him at the feast, and said, "Where is he?"
040712 There was much murmuring among the multitudes concerning him. Some said, "He is a good man." Others said, "Not so, but he leads the multitude astray."
040713 Yet no one spoke openly of him for fear of the Jews.
040714 But when it was now the midst of the feast, Jesus went up into the temple and taught.
040715 The Jews therefore marveled, saying, "How does this man know letters, having never been educated?"
040716 Jesus therefore answered them, "My teaching is not mine, but his who sent me.
040717 If anyone desires to do his will, he will know about the teaching, whether it is from God, or if I am speaking from myself.
040718 He who speaks from himself seeks his own glory, but he who seeks the glory of him who sent him is true, and no unrighteousness is in him.
040719 Didn't Moses give you the law, and yet none of you keeps the law? Why do you seek to kill me?"
040720 The multitude answered, "You have a demon! Who seeks to kill you?"
040721 Jesus answered them, "I did one work, and you all marvel because of it.
040722 Moses has given you circumcision (not that it is of Moses, but of the fathers), and on the Sabbath you circumcise a boy.
040723 If a boy receives circumcision on the Sabbath, that the law of Moses may not be broken, are you angry with me, because I made a man completely healthy on the Sabbath?
040724 Don't judge according to appearance, but judge righteous judgment."
040725 Therefore some of them of Jerusalem said, "Isn't this he whom they seek to kill?
040726 Behold, he speaks openly, and they say nothing to him. Can it be that the rulers indeed know that this is truly the Christ?
040727 However we know where this man comes from, but when the Christ comes, no one will know where he comes from."
040728 Jesus therefore cried out in the temple, teaching and saying, "You both know me, and know where I am from. I have not come of myself, but he who sent me is true, whom you don't know.
040729 I know him, because I am from him, and he sent me."
040730 They sought therefore to take him; but no one laid a hand on him, because his hour had not yet come.
040731 But of the multitude, many believed in him. They said, "When the Christ comes, he won't do more signs than those which this man has done, will he?"
040732 The Pharisees heard the multitude murmuring these things concerning him, and the chief priests and the Pharisees sent officers to arrest him.
040733 Then Jesus said, "I will be with you a little while longer, then I go to him who sent me.
040734 You will seek me, and won't find me; and where I am, you can't come."
040735 The Jews therefore said among themselves, "Where will this man go that we won't find him? Will he go to the Dispersion among the Greeks, and teach the Greeks?
040736 What is this word that he said, 'You will seek me, and won't find me; and where I am, you can't come'?"
040737 Now on the last and greatest day of the feast, Jesus stood and cried out, "If anyone is thirsty, let him come to me and drink!
040738 He who believes in me, as the Scripture has said, from within him will flow rivers of living water."
040739 But he said this about the Spirit, which those believing in him were to receive. For the Holy Spirit was not yet given, because Jesus wasn't yet glorified.
040740 Many of the multitude therefore, when they heard these words, said, "This is truly the prophet."
040741 Others said, "This is the Christ." But some said, "What, does the Christ come out of Galilee?
040742 Hasn't the Scripture said that the Christ comes of the seed of David, and from Bethlehem, the village where David was?"
040743 So there arose a division in the multitude because of him.
040744 Some of them would have arrested him, but no one laid hands on him.
040745 The officers therefore came to the chief priests and Pharisees, and they said to them, "Why didn't you bring him?"
040746 The officers answered, "No man ever spoke like this man!"
040747 The Pharisees therefore answered them, "You aren't also led astray, are you?
040748 Have any of the rulers believed in him, or of the Pharisees?
040749 But this multitude that doesn't know the law is accursed."
040750 Nicodemus (he who came to him by night, being one of them) said to them,
040751 "Does our law judge a man, unless it first hears from him personally and knows what he does?"
040752 They answered him, "Are you also from Galilee? Search, and see that no prophet has arisen out of Galilee."
040753 Everyone went to his own house,
040801 but Jesus went to the Mount of Olives.
040802 Now very early in the morning, he came again into the temple, and all the people came to him. He sat down, and taught them.
040803 The scribes and the Pharisees brought a woman taken in adultery. Having set her in the midst,
040804 they told him, "Teacher, we found this woman in adultery, in the very act.
040805 Now in our law, Moses commanded us to stone such. What then do you say about her?"
040806 They said this testing him, that they might have something to accuse him of. But Jesus stooped down, and wrote on the ground with his finger.
040807 But when they continued asking him, he looked up and said to them, "He who is without sin among you, let him throw the first stone at her."
040808 Again he stooped down, and with his finger wrote on the ground.
040809 They, when they heard it, being convicted by their conscience, went out one by one, beginning from the oldest, even to the last. Jesus was left alone with the woman where she was, in the middle.
040810 Jesus, standing up, saw her and said, "Woman, where are your accusers? Did no one condemn you?"
040811 She said, "No one, Lord." Jesus said, "Neither do I condemn you. Go your way. From now on, sin no more."
040812 Again, therefore, Jesus spoke to them, saying, "I am the light of the world. He who follows me will not walk in the darkness, but will have the light of life."
040813 The Pharisees therefore said to him, "You testify about yourself. Your testimony is not valid."
040814 Jesus answered them, "Even if I testify about myself, my testimony is true, for I know where I came from, and where I am going; but you don't know where I came from, or where I am going.
040815 You judge according to the flesh. I judge no one.
040816 Even if I do judge, my judgment is true, for I am not alone, but I am with the Father who sent me.
040817 It's also written in your law that the testimony of two people is valid.
040818 I am one who testifies about myself, and the Father who sent me testifies about me."
040819 They said therefore to him, "Where is your Father?" Jesus answered, "You know neither me, nor my Father. If you knew me, you would know my Father also."
040820 Jesus spoke these words in the treasury, as he taught in the temple. Yet no one arrested him, because his hour had not yet come.
040821 Jesus said therefore again to them, "I am going away, and you will seek me, and you will die in your sins. Where I go, you can't come."
040822 The Jews therefore said, "Will he kill himself, that he says, 'Where I am going, you can't come?'"
040823 He said to them, "You are from beneath. I am from above. You are of this world. I am not of this world.
040824 I said therefore to you that you will die in your sins; for unless you believe that I am he, you will die in your sins."
040825 They said therefore to him, "Who are you?" Jesus said to them, "Just what I have been saying to you from the beginning.
040826 I have many things to speak and to judge concerning you. However he who sent me is true; and the things which I heard from him, these I say to the world."
040827 They didn't understand that he spoke to them about the Father.
040828 Jesus therefore said to them, "When you have lifted up the Son of Man, then you will know that I am he, and I do nothing of myself, but as my Father taught me, I say these things.
040829 He who sent me is with me. The Father hasn't left me alone, for I always do the things that are pleasing to him."
040830 As he spoke these things, many believed in him.
040831 Jesus therefore said to those Jews who had believed him, "If you remain in my word, then you are truly my disciples.
040832 You will know the truth, and the truth will make you free."
040833 They answered him, "We are Abraham's seed, and have never been in bondage to anyone. How do you say, 'You will be made free?'"
040834 Jesus answered them, "Most certainly I tell you, everyone who commits sin is the bondservant of sin.
040835 A bondservant doesn't live in the house forever. A son remains forever.
040836 If therefore the Son makes you free, you will be free indeed.
040837 I know that you are Abraham's seed, yet you seek to kill me, because my word finds no place in you.
040838 I say the things which I have seen with my Father; and you also do the things which you have seen with your father."
040839 They answered him, "Our father is Abraham." Jesus said to them, "If you were Abraham's children, you would do the works of Abraham.
040840 But now you seek to kill me, a man who has told you the truth, which I heard from God. Abraham didn't do this.
040841 You do the works of your father." They said to him, "We were not born of sexual immorality. We have one Father, God."
040842 Therefore Jesus said to them, "If God were your father, you would love me, for I came out and have come from God. For I haven't come of myself, but he sent me.
040843 Why don't you understand my speech? Because you can't hear my word.
040844 You are of your father, the devil, and you want to do the desires of your father. He was a murderer from the beginning, and doesn't stand in the truth, because there is no truth in him. When he speaks a lie, he speaks on his own; for he is a liar, and its father.
040845 But because I tell the truth, you don't believe me.
040846 Which of you convicts me of sin? If I tell the truth, why do you not believe me?
040847 He who is of God hears the words of God. For this cause you don't hear, because you are not of God."
040848 Then the Jews answered him, "Don't we say well that you are a Samaritan, and have a demon?"
040849 Jesus answered, "I don't have a demon, but I honor my Father, and you dishonor me.
040850 But I don't seek my own glory. There is one who seeks and judges.
040851 Most certainly, I tell you, if a person keeps my word, he will never see death."
040852 Then the Jews said to him, "Now we know that you have a demon. Abraham died, and the prophets; and you say, 'If a man keeps my word, he will never taste of death.'
040853 Are you greater than our father, Abraham, who died? The prophets died. Who do you make yourself out to be?"
040854 Jesus answered, "If I glorify myself, my glory is nothing. It is my Father who glorifies me, of whom you say that he is our God.
040855 You have not known him, but I know him. If I said, 'I don't know him,' I would be like you, a liar. But I know him, and keep his word.
040856 Your father Abraham rejoiced to see my day. He saw it, and was glad."
040857 The Jews therefore said to him, "You are not yet fifty years old, and have you seen Abraham?"
040858 Jesus said to them, "Most certainly, I tell you, before Abraham came into existence, I AM."
040859 Therefore they took up stones to throw at him, but Jesus was hidden, and went out of the temple, having gone through the midst of them, and so passed by.
040901 As he passed by, he saw a man blind from birth.
040902 His disciples asked him, "Rabbi, who sinned, this man or his parents, that he was born blind?"
040903 Jesus answered, "Neither did this man sin, nor his parents; but, that the works of God might be revealed in him.
040904 I must work the works of him who sent me, while it is day. The night is coming, when no one can work.
040905 While I am in the world, I am the light of the world."
040906 When he had said this, he spat on the ground, made mud with the saliva, anointed the blind man's eyes with the mud,
040907 and said to him, "Go, wash in the pool of Siloam" (which means "Sent"). So he went away, washed, and came back seeing.
040908 The neighbors therefore, and those who saw that he was blind before, said, "Isn't this he who sat and begged?"
040909 Others were saying, "It is he." Still others were saying, "He looks like him." He said, "I am he."
040910 They therefore were asking him, "How were your eyes opened?"
040911 He answered, "A man called Jesus made mud, anointed my eyes, and said to me, 'Go to the pool of Siloam, and wash.' So I went away and washed, and I received sight."
040912 Then they asked him, "Where is he?" He said, "I don't know."
040913 They brought him who had been blind to the Pharisees.
040914 It was a Sabbath when Jesus made the mud and opened his eyes.
040915 Again therefore the Pharisees also asked him how he received his sight. He said to them, "He put mud on my eyes, I washed, and I see."
040916 Some therefore of the Pharisees said, "This man is not from God, because he doesn't keep the Sabbath." Others said, "How can a man who is a sinner do such signs?" There was division among them.
040917 Therefore they asked the blind man again, "What do you say about him, because he opened your eyes?" He said, "He is a prophet."
040918 The Jews therefore did not believe concerning him, that he had been blind, and had received his sight, until they called the parents of him who had received his sight,
040919 and asked them, "Is this your son, who you say was born blind? How then does he now see?"
040920 His parents answered them, "We know that this is our son, and that he was born blind;
040921 but how he now sees, we don't know; or who opened his eyes, we don't know. He is of age. Ask him. He will speak for himself."
040922 His parents said these things because they feared the Jews; for the Jews had already agreed that if any man would confess him as Christ, he would be put out of the synagogue.
040923 Therefore his parents said, "He is of age. Ask him."
040924 So they called the man who was blind a second time, and said to him, "Give glory to God. We know that this man is a sinner."
040925 He therefore answered, "I don't know if he is a sinner. One thing I do know: that though I was blind, now I see."
040926 They said to him again, "What did he do to you? How did he open your eyes?"
040927 He answered them, "I told you already, and you didn't listen. Why do you want to hear it again? You don't also want to become his disciples, do you?"
040928 They insulted him and said, "You are his disciple, but we are disciples of Moses.
040929 We know that God has spoken to Moses. But as for this man, we don't know where he comes from."
040930 The man answered them, "How amazing! You don't know where he comes from, yet he opened my eyes.
040931 We know that God doesn't listen to sinners, but if anyone is a worshipper of God, and does his will, he listens to him.
040932 Since the world began it has never been heard of that anyone opened the eyes of someone born blind.
040933 If this man were not from God, he could do nothing."
040934 They answered him, "You were altogether born in sins, and do you teach us?" They threw him out.
040935 Jesus heard that they had thrown him out, and finding him, he said, "Do you believe in the Son of God?"
040936 He answered, "Who is he, Lord, that I may believe in him?"
040937 Jesus said to him, "You have both seen him, and it is he who speaks with you."
040938 He said, "Lord, I believe!" and he worshiped him.
040939 Jesus said, "I came into this world for judgment, that those who don't see may see; and that those who see may become blind."
040940 Those of the Pharisees who were with him heard these things, and said to him, "Are we also blind?"
040941 Jesus said to them, "If you were blind, you would have no sin; but now you say, 'We see.' Therefore your sin remains.
041001 "Most certainly, I tell you, one who doesn't enter by the door into the sheep fold, but climbs up some other way, the same is a thief and a robber.
041002 But one who enters in by the door is the shepherd of the sheep.
041003 The gatekeeper opens the gate for him, and the sheep listen to his voice. He calls his own sheep by name, and leads them out.
041004 Whenever he brings out his own sheep, he goes before them, and the sheep follow him, for they know his voice.
041005 They will by no means follow a stranger, but will flee from him; for they don't know the voice of strangers."
041006 Jesus spoke this parable to them, but they didn't understand what he was telling them.
041007 Jesus therefore said to them again, "Most certainly, I tell you, I am the sheep's door.
041008 All who came before me are thieves and robbers, but the sheep didn't listen to them.
041009 I am the door. If anyone enters in by me, he will be saved, and will go in and go out, and will find pasture.
041010 The thief only comes to steal, kill, and destroy. I came that they may have life, and may have it abundantly.
041011 I am the good shepherd. The good shepherd lays down his life for the sheep.
041012 He who is a hired hand, and not a shepherd, who doesn't own the sheep, sees the wolf coming, leaves the sheep, and flees. The wolf snatches the sheep, and scatters them.
041013 The hired hand flees because he is a hired hand, and doesn't care for the sheep.
041014 I am the good shepherd. I know my own, and I'm known by my own;
041015 even as the Father knows me, and I know the Father. I lay down my life for the sheep.
041016 I have other sheep, which are not of this fold. I must bring them also, and they will hear my voice. They will become one flock with one shepherd.
041017 Therefore the Father loves me, because I lay down my life, that I may take it again.
041018 No one takes it away from me, but I lay it down by myself. I have power to lay it down, and I have power to take it again. I received this commandment from my Father."
041019 Therefore a division arose again among the Jews because of these words.
041020 Many of them said, "He has a demon, and is insane! Why do you listen to him?"
041021 Others said, "These are not the sayings of one possessed by a demon. It isn't possible for a demon to open the eyes of the blind, is it?"
041022 It was the Feast of the Dedication at Jerusalem.
041023 It was winter, and Jesus was walking in the temple, in Solomon's porch.
041024 The Jews therefore came around him and said to him, "How long will you hold us in suspense? If you are the Christ, tell us plainly."
041025 Jesus answered them, "I told you, and you don't believe. The works that I do in my Father's name, these testify about me.
041026 But you don't believe, because you are not of my sheep, as I told you.
041027 My sheep hear my voice, and I know them, and they follow me.
041028 I give eternal life to them. They will never perish, and no one will snatch them out of my hand.
041029 My Father, who has given them to me, is greater than all. No one is able to snatch them out of my Father's hand.
041030 I and the Father are one."
041031 Therefore Jews took up stones again to stone him.
041032 Jesus answered them, "I have shown you many good works from my Father. For which of those works do you stone me?"
041033 The Jews answered him, "We don't stone you for a good work, but for blasphemy: because you, being a man, make yourself God."
041034 Jesus answered them, "Isn't it written in your law, 'I said, you are gods?'
041035 If he called them gods, to whom the word of God came (and the Scripture can't be broken),
041036 do you say of him whom the Father sanctified and sent into the world, 'You blaspheme,' because I said, 'I am the Son of God?'
041037 If I don't do the works of my Father, don't believe me.
041038 But if I do them, though you don't believe me, believe the works; that you may know and believe that the Father is in me, and I in the Father."
041039 They sought again to seize him, and he went out of their hand.
041040 He went away again beyond the Jordan into the place where John was baptizing at first, and there he stayed.
041041 Many came to him. They said, "John indeed did no sign, but everything that John said about this man is true."
041042 Many believed in him there.
041101 Now a certain man was sick, Lazarus from Bethany, of the village of Mary and her sister, Martha.
