041102 It was that Mary who had anointed the Lord with ointment, and wiped his feet with her hair, whose brother, Lazarus, was sick.
041103 The sisters therefore sent to him, saying, "Lord, behold, he for whom you have great affection is sick."
041104 But when Jesus heard it, he said, "This sickness is not to death, but for the glory of God, that God's Son may be glorified by it."
041105 Now Jesus loved Martha, and her sister, and Lazarus.
041106 When therefore he heard that he was sick, he stayed two days in the place where he was.
041107 Then after this he said to the disciples, "Let's go into Judea again."
041108 The disciples told him, "Rabbi, the Jews were just trying to stone you, and are you going there again?"
041109 Jesus answered, "Aren't there twelve hours of daylight? If a man walks in the day, he doesn't stumble, because he sees the light of this world.
041110 But if a man walks in the night, he stumbles, because the light isn't in him."
041111 He said these things, and after that, he said to them, "Our friend, Lazarus, has fallen asleep, but I am going so that I may awake him out of sleep."
041112 The disciples therefore said, "Lord, if he has fallen asleep, he will recover."
041113 Now Jesus had spoken of his death, but they thought that he spoke of taking rest in sleep.
041114 So Jesus said to them plainly then, "Lazarus is dead.
041115 I am glad for your sakes that I was not there, so that you may believe. Nevertheless, let's go to him."
041116 Thomas therefore, who is called Didymus, said to his fellow disciples, "Let's go also, that we may die with him."
041117 So when Jesus came, he found that he had been in the tomb four days already.
041118 Now Bethany was near Jerusalem, about fifteen stadia away.
041119 Many of the Jews had joined the women around Martha and Mary, to console them concerning their brother.
041120 Then when Martha heard that Jesus was coming, she went and met him, but Mary stayed in the house.
041121 Therefore Martha said to Jesus, "Lord, if you would have been here, my brother wouldn't have died.
041122 Even now I know that, whatever you ask of God, God will give you."
041123 Jesus said to her, "Your brother will rise again."
041124 Martha said to him, "I know that he will rise again in the resurrection at the last day."
041125 Jesus said to her, "I am the resurrection and the life. He who believes in me will still live, even if he dies.
041126 Whoever lives and believes in me will never die. Do you believe this?"
041127 She said to him, "Yes, Lord. I have come to believe that you are the Christ, God's Son, he who comes into the world."
041128 When she had said this, she went away, and called Mary, her sister, secretly, saying, "The Teacher is here, and is calling you."
041129 When she heard this, she arose quickly, and went to him.
041130 Now Jesus had not yet come into the village, but was in the place where Martha met him.
041131 Then the Jews who were with her in the house, and were consoling her, when they saw Mary, that she rose up quickly and went out, followed her, saying, "She is going to the tomb to weep there."
041132 Therefore when Mary came to where Jesus was, and saw him, she fell down at his feet, saying to him, "Lord, if you would have been here, my brother wouldn't have died."
041133 When Jesus therefore saw her weeping, and the Jews weeping who came with her, he groaned in the spirit, and was troubled,
041134 and said, "Where have you laid him?" They told him, "Lord, come and see."
041135 Jesus wept.
041136 The Jews therefore said, "See how much affection he had for him!"
041137 Some of them said, "Couldn't this man, who opened the eyes of him who was blind, have also kept this man from dying?"
041138 Jesus therefore, again groaning in himself, came to the tomb. Now it was a cave, and a stone lay against it.
041139 Jesus said, "Take away the stone." Martha, the sister of him who was dead, said to him, "Lord, by this time there is a stench, for he has been dead four days."
041140 Jesus said to her, "Didn't I tell you that if you believed, you would see God's glory?"
041141 So they took away the stone from the place where the dead man was lying. Jesus lifted up his eyes, and said, "Father, I thank you that you listened to me.
041142 I know that you always listen to me, but because of the multitude that stands around I said this, that they may believe that you sent me."
041143 When he had said this, he cried with a loud voice, "Lazarus, come out!"
041144 He who was dead came out, bound hand and foot with wrappings, and his face was wrapped around with a cloth. Jesus said to them, "Free him, and let him go."
041145 Therefore many of the Jews, who came to Mary and saw what Jesus did, believed in him.
041146 But some of them went away to the Pharisees, and told them the things which Jesus had done.
041147 The chief priests therefore and the Pharisees gathered a council, and said, "What are we doing? For this man does many signs.
041148 If we leave him alone like this, everyone will believe in him, and the Romans will come and take away both our place and our nation."
041149 But a certain one of them, Caiaphas, being high priest that year, said to them, "You know nothing at all,
041150 nor do you consider that it is advantageous for us that one man should die for the people, and that the whole nation not perish."
041151 Now he didn't say this of himself, but being high priest that year, he prophesied that Jesus would die for the nation,
041152 and not for the nation only, but that he might also gather together into one the children of God who are scattered abroad.
041153 So from that day forward they took counsel that they might put him to death.
041154 Jesus therefore walked no more openly among the Jews, but departed from there into the country near the wilderness, to a city called Ephraim. He stayed there with his disciples.
041155 Now the Passover of the Jews was at hand. Many went up from the country to Jerusalem before the Passover, to purify themselves.
041156 Then they sought for Jesus and spoke one with another, as they stood in the temple, "What do you think--that he isn't coming to the feast at all?"
041157 Now the chief priests and the Pharisees had commanded that if anyone knew where he was, he should report it, that they might seize him.
041201 Then six days before the Passover, Jesus came to Bethany, where Lazarus was, who had been dead, whom he raised from the dead.
041202 So they made him a supper there. Martha served, but Lazarus was one of those who sat at the table with him.
041203 Mary, therefore, took a pound of ointment of pure nard, very precious, and anointed the feet of Jesus, and wiped his feet with her hair. The house was filled with the fragrance of the ointment.
041204 Then Judas Iscariot, Simon's son, one of his disciples, who would betray him, said,
041205 "Why wasn't this ointment sold for three hundred denarii, and given to the poor?"
041206 Now he said this, not because he cared for the poor, but because he was a thief, and having the money box, used to steal what was put into it.
041207 But Jesus said, "Leave her alone. She has kept this for the day of my burial.
041208 For you always have the poor with you, but you don't always have me."
041209 A large crowd therefore of the Jews learned that he was there, and they came, not for Jesus' sake only, but that they might see Lazarus also, whom he had raised from the dead.
041210 But the chief priests conspired to put Lazarus to death also,
041211 because on account of him many of the Jews went away and believed in Jesus.
041212 On the next day a great multitude had come to the feast. When they heard that Jesus was coming to Jerusalem,
041213 they took the branches of the palm trees, and went out to meet him, and cried out, "Hosanna! Blessed is he who comes in the name of the Lord, the King of Israel!"
041214 Jesus, having found a young donkey, sat on it. As it is written,
041215 "Don't be afraid, daughter of Zion. Behold, your King comes, sitting on a donkey's colt."
041216 His disciples didn't understand these things at first, but when Jesus was glorified, then they remembered that these things were written about him, and that they had done these things to him.
041217 The multitude therefore that was with him when he called Lazarus out of the tomb, and raised him from the dead, was testifying about it.
041218 For this cause also the multitude went and met him, because they heard that he had done this sign.
041219 The Pharisees therefore said among themselves, "See how you accomplish nothing. Behold, the world has gone after him."
041220 Now there were certain Greeks among those that went up to worship at the feast.
041221 These, therefore, came to Philip, who was from Bethsaida of Galilee, and asked him, saying, "Sir, we want to see Jesus."
041222 Philip came and told Andrew, and in turn, Andrew came with Philip, and they told Jesus.
041223 Jesus answered them, "The time has come for the Son of Man to be glorified.
041224 Most certainly I tell you, unless a grain of wheat falls into the earth and dies, it remains by itself alone. But if it dies, it bears much fruit.
041225 He who loves his life will lose it. He who hates his life in this world will keep it to eternal life.
041226 If anyone serves me, let him follow me. Where I am, there will my servant also be. If anyone serves me, the Father will honor him.
041227 "Now my soul is troubled. What shall I say? 'Father, save me from this time?' But for this cause I came to this time.
041228 Father, glorify your name!" Then there came a voice out of the sky, saying, "I have both glorified it, and will glorify it again."
041229 The multitude therefore, who stood by and heard it, said that it had thundered. Others said, "An angel has spoken to him."
041230 Jesus answered, "This voice hasn't come for my sake, but for your sakes.
041231 Now is the judgment of this world. Now the prince of this world will be cast out.
041232 And I, if I am lifted up from the earth, will draw all people to myself."
041233 But he said this, signifying by what kind of death he should die.
041234 The multitude answered him, "We have heard out of the law that the Christ remains forever. How do you say, 'The Son of Man must be lifted up?' Who is this Son of Man?"
041235 Jesus therefore said to them, "Yet a little while the light is with you. Walk while you have the light, that darkness doesn't overtake you. He who walks in the darkness doesn't know where he is going.
041236 While you have the light, believe in the light, that you may become children of light." Jesus said these things, and he departed and hid himself from them.
041237 But though he had done so many signs before them, yet they didn't believe in him,
041238 that the word of Isaiah the prophet might be fulfilled, which he spoke, "Lord, who has believed our report? To whom has the arm of the Lord been revealed?"
041239 For this cause they couldn't believe, for Isaiah said again,
041240 "He has blinded their eyes and he hardened their heart, lest they should see with their eyes, and perceive with their heart, and would turn, and I would heal them."
041241 Isaiah said these things when he saw his glory, and spoke of him.
041242 Nevertheless even of the rulers many believed in him, but because of the Pharisees they didn't confess it, so that they wouldn't be put out of the synagogue,
041243 for they loved men's praise more than God's praise.
041244 Jesus cried out and said, "Whoever believes in me, believes not in me, but in him who sent me.
041245 He who sees me sees him who sent me.
041246 I have come as a light into the world, that whoever believes in me may not remain in the darkness.
041247 If anyone listens to my sayings, and doesn't believe, I don't judge him. For I came not to judge the world, but to save the world.
041248 He who rejects me, and doesn't receive my sayings, has one who judges him. The word that I spoke, the same will judge him in the last day.
041249 For I spoke not from myself, but the Father who sent me, he gave me a commandment, what I should say, and what I should speak.
041250 I know that his commandment is eternal life. The things therefore which I speak, even as the Father has said to me, so I speak."
041301 Now before the feast of the Passover, Jesus, knowing that his time had come that he would depart from this world to the Father, having loved his own who were in the world, he loved them to the end.
041302 During supper, the devil having already put into the heart of Judas Iscariot, Simon's son, to betray him,
041303 Jesus, knowing that the Father had given all things into his hands, and that he came forth from God, and was going to God,
041304 arose from supper, and laid aside his outer garments. He took a towel, and wrapped a towel around his waist.
041305 Then he poured water into the basin, and began to wash the disciples' feet, and to wipe them with the towel that was wrapped around him.
041306 Then he came to Simon Peter. He said to him, "Lord, do you wash my feet?"
041307 Jesus answered him, "You don't know what I am doing now, but you will understand later."
041308 Peter said to him, "You will never wash my feet!" Jesus answered him, "If I don't wash you, you have no part with me."
041309 Simon Peter said to him, "Lord, not my feet only, but also my hands and my head!"
041310 Jesus said to him, "Someone who has bathed only needs to have his feet washed, but is completely clean. You are clean, but not all of you."
041311 For he knew him who would betray him, therefore he said, "You are not all clean."
041312 So when he had washed their feet, put his outer garment back on, and sat down again, he said to them, "Do you know what I have done to you?
041313 You call me, 'Teacher' and 'Lord.' You say so correctly, for so I am.
041314 If I then, the Lord and the Teacher, have washed your feet, you also ought to wash one another's feet.
041315 For I have given you an example, that you also should do as I have done to you.
041316 Most certainly I tell you, a servant is not greater than his lord, neither one who is sent greater than he who sent him.
041317 If you know these things, blessed are you if you do them.
041318 I don't speak concerning all of you. I know whom I have chosen. But that the Scripture may be fulfilled, 'He who eats bread with me has lifted up his heel against me.'
041319 From now on, I tell you before it happens, that when it happens, you may believe that I am he.
041320 Most certainly I tell you, he who receives whomever I send, receives me; and he who receives me, receives him who sent me."
041321 When Jesus had said this, he was troubled in spirit, and testified, "Most certainly I tell you that one of you will betray me."
041322 The disciples looked at one another, perplexed about whom he spoke.
041323 One of his disciples, whom Jesus loved, was at the table, leaning against Jesus' breast.
041324 Simon Peter therefore beckoned to him, and said to him, "Tell us who it is of whom he speaks."
041325 He, leaning back, as he was, on Jesus' breast, asked him, "Lord, who is it?"
041326 Jesus therefore answered, "It is he to whom I will give this piece of bread when I have dipped it." So when he had dipped the piece of bread, he gave it to Judas, the son of Simon Iscariot.
041327 After the piece of bread, then Satan entered into him. Then Jesus said to him, "What you do, do quickly."
041328 Now no man at the table knew why he said this to him.
041329 For some thought, because Judas had the money box, that Jesus said to him, "Buy what things we need for the feast," or that he should give something to the poor.
041330 Therefore, having received that morsel, he went out immediately. It was night.
041331 When he had gone out, Jesus said, "Now the Son of Man has been glorified, and God has been glorified in him.
041332 If God has been glorified in him, God will also glorify him in himself, and he will glorify him immediately.
041333 Little children, I will be with you a little while longer. You will seek me, and as I said to the Jews, 'Where I am going, you can't come,' so now I tell you.
041334 A new commandment I give to you, that you love one another, just like I have loved you; that you also love one another.
041335 By this everyone will know that you are my disciples, if you have love for one another."
041336 Simon Peter said to him, "Lord, where are you going?" Jesus answered, "Where I am going, you can't follow now, but you will follow afterwards."
041337 Peter said to him, "Lord, why can't I follow you now? I will lay down my life for you."
041338 Jesus answered him, "Will you lay down your life for me? Most certainly I tell you, the rooster won't crow until you have denied me three times.
041401 "Don't let your heart be troubled. Believe in God. Believe also in me.
041402 In my Father's house are many homes. If it weren't so, I would have told you. I am going to prepare a place for you.
041403 If I go and prepare a place for you, I will come again, and will receive you to myself; that where I am, you may be there also.
041404 Where I go, you know, and you know the way."
041405 Thomas said to him, "Lord, we don't know where you are going. How can we know the way?"
041406 Jesus said to him, "I am the way, the truth, and the life. No one comes to the Father, except through me.
041407 If you had known me, you would have known my Father also. From now on, you know him, and have seen him."
041408 Philip said to him, "Lord, show us the Father, and that will be enough for us."
041409 Jesus said to him, "Have I been with you such a long time, and do you not know me, Philip? He who has seen me has seen the Father. How do you say, 'Show us the Father?'
041410 Don't you believe that I am in the Father, and the Father in me? The words that I tell you, I speak not from myself; but the Father who lives in me does his works.
041411 Believe me that I am in the Father, and the Father in me; or else believe me for the very works' sake.
041412 Most certainly I tell you, he who believes in me, the works that I do, he will do also; and he will do greater works than these, because I am going to my Father.
041413 Whatever you will ask in my name, that will I do, that the Father may be glorified in the Son.
041414 If you will ask anything in my name, I will do it.
041415 If you love me, keep my commandments.
041416 I will pray to the Father, and he will give you another Counselor, that he may be with you forever,--
041417 the Spirit of truth, whom the world can't receive; for it doesn't see him, neither knows him. You know him, for he lives with you, and will be in you.
041418 I will not leave you orphans. I will come to you.
041419 Yet a little while, and the world will see me no more; but you will see me. Because I live, you will live also.
041420 In that day you will know that I am in my Father, and you in me, and I in you.
041421 One who has my commandments, and keeps them, that person is one who loves me. One who loves me will be loved by my Father, and I will love him, and will reveal myself to him."
041422 Judas (not Iscariot) said to him, "Lord, what has happened that you are about to reveal yourself to us, and not to the world?"
041423 Jesus answered him, "If a man loves me, he will keep my word. My Father will love him, and we will come to him, and make our home with him.
041424 He who doesn't love me doesn't keep my words. The word which you hear isn't mine, but the Father's who sent me.
041425 I have said these things to you, while still living with you.
041426 But the Counselor, the Holy Spirit, whom the Father will send in my name, he will teach you all things, and will remind you of all that I said to you.
041427 Peace I leave with you. My peace I give to you; not as the world gives, give I to you. Don't let your heart be troubled, neither let it be fearful.
041428 You heard how I told you, 'I go away, and I come to you.' If you loved me, you would have rejoiced, because I said 'I am going to my Father;' for the Father is greater than I.
041429 Now I have told you before it happens so that, when it happens, you may believe.
041430 I will no more speak much with you, for the prince of the world comes, and he has nothing in me.
041431 But that the world may know that I love the Father, and as the Father commanded me, even so I do. Arise, let us go from here.
041501 "I am the true vine, and my Father is the farmer.
041502 Every branch in me that doesn't bear fruit, he takes away. Every branch that bears fruit, he prunes, that it may bear more fruit.
041503 You are already pruned clean because of the word which I have spoken to you.
041504 Remain in me, and I in you. As the branch can't bear fruit by itself, unless it remains in the vine, so neither can you, unless you remain in me.
041505 I am the vine. You are the branches. He who remains in me, and I in him, the same bears much fruit, for apart from me you can do nothing.
041506 If a man doesn't remain in me, he is thrown out as a branch, and is withered; and they gather them, throw them into the fire, and they are burned.
041507 If you remain in me, and my words remain in you, you will ask whatever you desire, and it will be done for you.
041508 "In this is my Father glorified, that you bear much fruit; and so you will be my disciples.
041509 Even as the Father has loved me, I also have loved you. Remain in my love.
041510 If you keep my commandments, you will remain in my love; even as I have kept my Father's commandments, and remain in his love.
041511 I have spoken these things to you, that my joy may remain in you, and that your joy may be made full.
041512 "This is my commandment, that you love one another, even as I have loved you.
041513 Greater love has no one than this, that someone lay down his life for his friends.
041514 You are my friends, if you do whatever I command you.
041515 No longer do I call you servants, for the servant doesn't know what his lord does. But I have called you friends, for everything that I heard from my Father, I have made known to you.
041516 You didn't choose me, but I chose you, and appointed you, that you should go and bear fruit, and that your fruit should remain; that whatever you will ask of the Father in my name, he may give it to you.
041517 "I command these things to you, that you may love one another.
041518 If the world hates you, you know that it has hated me before it hated you.
041519 If you were of the world, the world would love its own. But because you are not of the world, since I chose you out of the world, therefore the world hates you.
041520 Remember the word that I said to you: 'A servant is not greater than his lord.' If they persecuted me, they will also persecute you. If they kept my word, they will keep yours also.
041521 But all these things will they do to you for my name's sake, because they don't know him who sent me.
041522 If I had not come and spoken to them, they would not have had sin; but now they have no excuse for their sin.
041523 He who hates me, hates my Father also.
041524 If I hadn't done among them the works which no one else did, they wouldn't have had sin. But now have they seen and also hated both me and my Father.
041525 But this happened so that the word may be fulfilled which was written in their law, 'They hated me without a cause.'
041526 "When the Counselor has come, whom I will send to you from the Father, the Spirit of truth, who proceeds from the Father, he will testify about me.
041527 You will also testify, because you have been with me from the beginning.
041601 "These things have I spoken to you, so that you wouldn't be caused to stumble.
041602 They will put you out of the synagogues. Yes, the time comes that whoever kills you will think that he offers service to God.
041603 They will do these things because they have not known the Father, nor me.
041604 But I have told you these things, so that when the time comes, you may remember that I told you about them. I didn't tell you these things from the beginning, because I was with you.
041605 But now I am going to him who sent me, and none of you asks me, 'Where are you going?'
041606 But because I have told you these things, sorrow has filled your heart.
041607 Nevertheless I tell you the truth: It is to your advantage that I go away, for if I don't go away, the Counselor won't come to you. But if I go, I will send him to you.
041608 When he has come, he will convict the world about sin, about righteousness, and about judgment;
041609 about sin, because they don't believe in me;
041610 about righteousness, because I am going to my Father, and you won't see me any more;
041611 about judgment, because the prince of this world has been judged.
041612 "I have yet many things to tell you, but you can't bear them now.
041613 However when he, the Spirit of truth, has come, he will guide you into all truth, for he will not speak from himself; but whatever he hears, he will speak. He will declare to you things that are coming.
041614 He will glorify me, for he will take from what is mine, and will declare it to you.
041615 All things whatever the Father has are mine; therefore I said that he takes of mine, and will declare it to you.
041616 A little while, and you will not see me. Again a little while, and you will see me."
041617 Some of his disciples therefore said to one another, "What is this that he says to us, 'A little while, and you won't see me, and again a little while, and you will see me;' and, 'Because I go to the Father?'"
041618 They said therefore, "What is this that he says, 'A little while?' We don't know what he is saying."
041619 Therefore Jesus perceived that they wanted to ask him, and he said to them, "Do you inquire among yourselves concerning this, that I said, 'A little while, and you won't see me, and again a little while, and you will see me?'
041620 Most certainly I tell you, that you will weep and lament, but the world will rejoice. You will be sorrowful, but your sorrow will be turned into joy.
041621 A woman, when she gives birth, has sorrow, because her time has come. But when she has delivered the child, she doesn't remember the anguish any more, for the joy that a human being is born into the world.
041622 Therefore you now have sorrow, but I will see you again, and your heart will rejoice, and no one will take your joy away from you.
041623 "In that day you will ask me no questions. Most certainly I tell you, whatever you may ask of the Father in my name, he will give it to you.
041624 Until now, you have asked nothing in my name. Ask, and you will receive, that your joy may be made full.
041625 I have spoken these things to you in figures of speech. But the time is coming when I will no more speak to you in figures of speech, but will tell you plainly about the Father.
041626 In that day you will ask in my name; and I don't say to you, that I will pray to the Father for you,
041627 for the Father himself loves you, because you have loved me, and have believed that I came forth from God.
041628 I came out from the Father, and have come into the world. Again, I leave the world, and go to the Father."
041629 His disciples said to him, "Behold, now you speak plainly, and speak no figures of speech.
041630 Now we know that you know all things, and don't need for anyone to question you. By this we believe that you came forth from God."
041631 Jesus answered them, "Do you now believe?
041632 Behold, the time is coming, yes, and has now come, that you will be scattered, everyone to his own place, and you will leave me alone. Yet I am not alone, because the Father is with me.
041633 I have told you these things, that in me you may have peace. In the world you have oppression; but cheer up! I have overcome the world."
041701 Jesus said these things, and lifting up his eyes to heaven, he said, "Father, the time has come. Glorify your Son, that your Son may also glorify you;
041702 even as you gave him authority over all flesh, he will give eternal life to all whom you have given him.
041703 This is eternal life, that they should know you, the only true God, and him whom you sent, Jesus Christ.
041704 I glorified you on the earth. I have accomplished the work which you have given me to do.
041705 Now, Father, glorify me with your own self with the glory which I had with you before the world existed.
041706 I revealed your name to the people whom you have given me out of the world. They were yours, and you have given them to me. They have kept your word.
041707 Now they have known that all things whatever you have given me are from you,
041708 for the words which you have given me I have given to them, and they received them, and knew for sure that I came forth from you, and they have believed that you sent me.
041709 I pray for them. I don't pray for the world, but for those whom you have given me, for they are yours.
041710 All things that are mine are yours, and yours are mine, and I am glorified in them.
041711 I am no more in the world, but these are in the world, and I am coming to you. Holy Father, keep them through your name which you have given me, that they may be one, even as we are.
041712 While I was with them in the world, I kept them in your name. Those whom you have given me I have kept. None of them is lost, except the son of destruction, that the Scripture might be fulfilled.
041713 But now I come to you, and I say these things in the world, that they may have my joy made full in themselves.
041714 I have given them your word. The world hated them, because they are not of the world, even as I am not of the world.
041715 I pray not that you would take them from the world, but that you would keep them from the evil one.
041716 They are not of the world even as I am not of the world.
041717 Sanctify them in your truth. Your word is truth.
041718 As you sent me into the world, even so I have sent them into the world.
041719 For their sakes I sanctify myself, that they themselves also may be sanctified in truth.
041720 Not for these only do I pray, but for those also who believe in me through their word,
041721 that they may all be one; even as you, Father, are in me, and I in you, that they also may be one in us; that the world may believe that you sent me.
041722 The glory which you have given me, I have given to them; that they may be one, even as we are one;
041723 I in them, and you in me, that they may be perfected into one; that the world may know that you sent me, and loved them, even as you loved me.
041724 Father, I desire that they also whom you have given me be with me where I am, that they may see my glory, which you have given me, for you loved me before the foundation of the world.
041725 Righteous Father, the world hasn't known you, but I knew you; and these knew that you sent me.
041726 I made known to them your name, and will make it known; that the love with which you loved me may be in them, and I in them."
041801 When Jesus had spoken these words, he went out with his disciples over the brook Kidron, where there was a garden, into which he and his disciples entered.
041802 Now Judas, who betrayed him, also knew the place, for Jesus often met there with his disciples.
041803 Judas then, having taken a detachment of soldiers and officers from the chief priests and the Pharisees, came there with lanterns, torches, and weapons.
041804 Jesus therefore, knowing all the things that were happening to him, went forth, and said to them, "Who are you looking for?"
041805 They answered him, "Jesus of Nazareth." Jesus said to them, "I am he." Judas also, who betrayed him, was standing with them.
041806 When therefore he said to them, "I am he," they went backward, and fell to the ground.
041807 Again therefore he asked them, "Who are you looking for?" They said, "Jesus of Nazareth."
041808 Jesus answered, "I told you that I am he. If therefore you seek me, let these go their way,"
041809 that the word might be fulfilled which he spoke, "Of those whom you have given me, I have lost none."
041810 Simon Peter therefore, having a sword, drew it, and struck the high priest's servant, and cut off his right ear. The servant's name was Malchus.
041811 Jesus therefore said to Peter, "Put the sword into its sheath. The cup which the Father has given me, shall I not surely drink it?"
041812 So the detachment, the commanding officer, and the officers of the Jews, seized Jesus and bound him,
041813 and led him to Annas first, for he was father-in-law to Caiaphas, who was high priest that year.
041814 Now it was Caiaphas who advised the Jews that it was expedient that one man should perish for the people.
041815 Simon Peter followed Jesus, as did another disciple. Now that disciple was known to the high priest, and entered in with Jesus into the court of the high priest;
041816 but Peter was standing at the door outside. So the other disciple, who was known to the high priest, went out and spoke to her who kept the door, and brought in Peter.
041817 Then the maid who kept the door said to Peter, "Are you also one of this man's disciples?" He said, "I am not."
041818 Now the servants and the officers were standing there, having made a fire of coals, for it was cold. They were warming themselves. Peter was with them, standing and warming himself.
041819 The high priest therefore asked Jesus about his disciples, and about his teaching.
041820 Jesus answered him, "I spoke openly to the world. I always taught in synagogues, and in the temple, where the Jews always meet. I said nothing in secret.
041821 Why do you ask me? Ask those who have heard me what I said to them. Behold, these know the things which I said."
041822 When he had said this, one of the officers standing by slapped Jesus with his hand, saying, "Do you answer the high priest like that?"
041823 Jesus answered him, "If I have spoken evil, testify of the evil; but if well, why do you beat me?"
041824 Annas sent him bound to Caiaphas, the high priest.
041825 Now Simon Peter was standing and warming himself. They said therefore to him, "You aren't also one of his disciples, are you?" He denied it, and said, "I am not."
041826 One of the servants of the high priest, being a relative of him whose ear Peter had cut off, said, "Didn't I see you in the garden with him?"
041827 Peter therefore denied it again, and immediately the rooster crowed.
041828 They led Jesus therefore from Caiaphas into the Praetorium. It was early, and they themselves didn't enter into the Praetorium, that they might not be defiled, but might eat the Passover.
041829 Pilate therefore went out to them, and said, "What accusation do you bring against this man?"
041830 They answered him, "If this man weren't an evildoer, we wouldn't have delivered him up to you."
041831 Pilate therefore said to them, "Take him yourselves, and judge him according to your law." Therefore the Jews said to him, "It is not lawful for us to put anyone to death,"
041832 that the word of Jesus might be fulfilled, which he spoke, signifying by what kind of death he should die.
041833 Pilate therefore entered again into the Praetorium, called Jesus, and said to him, "Are you the King of the Jews?"
041834 Jesus answered him, "Do you say this by yourself, or did others tell you about me?"
041835 Pilate answered, "I'm not a Jew, am I? Your own nation and the chief priests delivered you to me. What have you done?"
041836 Jesus answered, "My Kingdom is not of this world. If my Kingdom were of this world, then my servants would fight, that I wouldn't be delivered to the Jews. But now my Kingdom is not from here."
041837 Pilate therefore said to him, "Are you a king then?" Jesus answered, "You say that I am a king. For this reason I have been born, and for this reason I have come into the world, that I should testify to the truth. Everyone who is of the truth listens to my voice."
041838 Pilate said to him, "What is truth?" When he had said this, he went out again to the Jews, and said to them, "I find no basis for a charge against him.
041839 But you have a custom, that I should release someone to you at the Passover. Therefore do you want me to release to you the King of the Jews?"
041840 Then they all shouted again, saying, "Not this man, but Barabbas!" Now Barabbas was a robber.
041901 So Pilate then took Jesus, and flogged him.
041902 The soldiers twisted thorns into a crown, and put it on his head, and dressed him in a purple garment.
041903 They kept saying, "Hail, King of the Jews!" and they kept slapping him.
041904 Then Pilate went out again, and said to them, "Behold, I bring him out to you, that you may know that I find no basis for a charge against him."
041905 Jesus therefore came out, wearing the crown of thorns and the purple garment. Pilate said to them, "Behold, the man!"
041906 When therefore the chief priests and the officers saw him, they shouted, saying, "Crucify! Crucify!" Pilate said to them, "Take him yourselves, and crucify him, for I find no basis for a charge against him."
041907 The Jews answered him, "We have a law, and by our law he ought to die, because he made himself the Son of God."
041908 When therefore Pilate heard this saying, he was more afraid.
041909 He entered into the Praetorium again, and said to Jesus, "Where are you from?" But Jesus gave him no answer.
041910 Pilate therefore said to him, "Aren't you speaking to me? Don't you know that I have power to release you, and have power to crucify you?"
041911 Jesus answered, "You would have no power at all against me, unless it were given to you from above. Therefore he who delivered me to you has greater sin."
041912 At this, Pilate was seeking to release him, but the Jews cried out, saying, "If you release this man, you aren't Caesar's friend! Everyone who makes himself a king speaks against Caesar!"
041913 When Pilate therefore heard these words, he brought Jesus out, and sat down on the judgment seat at a place called "The Pavement," but in Hebrew, "Gabbatha."
041914 Now it was the Preparation Day of the Passover, at about the sixth hour. He said to the Jews, "Behold, your King!"
041915 They cried out, "Away with him! Away with him! Crucify him!" Pilate said to them, "Shall I crucify your King?" The chief priests answered, "We have no king but Caesar!"
041916 So then he delivered him to them to be crucified. So they took Jesus and led him away.
041917 He went out, bearing his cross, to the place called "The Place of a Skull," which is called in Hebrew, "Golgotha,"
041918 where they crucified him, and with him two others, on either side one, and Jesus in the middle.
041919 Pilate wrote a title also, and put it on the cross. There was written, "JESUS OF NAZARETH, THE KING OF THE JEWS."
041920 Therefore many of the Jews read this title, for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city; and it was written in Hebrew, in Latin, and in Greek.
041921 The chief priests of the Jews therefore said to Pilate, "Don't write, 'The King of the Jews,' but, 'he said, I am King of the Jews.'"
041922 Pilate answered, "What I have written, I have written."
041923 Then the soldiers, when they had crucified Jesus, took his garments and made four parts, to every soldier a part; and also the coat. Now the coat was without seam, woven from the top throughout.
041924 Then they said to one another, "Let's not tear it, but cast lots for it to decide whose it will be," that the Scripture might be fulfilled, which says, "They parted my garments among them. For my cloak they cast lots." Therefore the soldiers did these things.
041925 But there were standing by the cross of Jesus his mother, and his mother's sister, Mary the wife of Clopas, and Mary Magdalene.
041926 Therefore when Jesus saw his mother, and the disciple whom he loved standing there, he said to his mother, "Woman, behold your son!"
041927 Then he said to the disciple, "Behold, your mother!" From that hour, the disciple took her to his own home.
041928 After this, Jesus, seeing that all things were now finished, that the Scripture might be fulfilled, said, "I am thirsty."
041929 Now a vessel full of vinegar was set there; so they put a sponge full of the vinegar on hyssop, and held it at his mouth.
041930 When Jesus therefore had received the vinegar, he said, "It is finished." He bowed his head, and gave up his spirit.
041931 Therefore the Jews, because it was the Preparation Day, so that the bodies wouldn't remain on the cross on the Sabbath (for that Sabbath was a special one), asked of Pilate that their legs might be broken, and that they might be taken away.
041932 Therefore the soldiers came, and broke the legs of the first, and of the other who was crucified with him;
041933 but when they came to Jesus, and saw that he was already dead, they didn't break his legs.
041934 However one of the soldiers pierced his side with a spear, and immediately blood and water came out.
041935 He who has seen has testified, and his testimony is true. He knows that he tells the truth, that you may believe.
041936 For these things happened, that the Scripture might be fulfilled, "A bone of him will not be broken."
041937 Again another Scripture says, "They will look on him whom they pierced."
041938 After these things, Joseph of Arimathaea, being a disciple of Jesus, but secretly for fear of the Jews, asked of Pilate that he might take away Jesus' body. Pilate gave him permission. He came therefore and took away his body.
041939 Nicodemus, who at first came to Jesus by night, also came bringing a mixture of myrrh and aloes, about a hundred Roman pounds.
041940 So they took Jesus' body, and bound it in linen cloths with the spices, as the custom of the Jews is to bury.
041941 Now in the place where he was crucified there was a garden. In the garden was a new tomb in which no man had ever yet been laid.
041942 Then because of the Jews' Preparation Day (for the tomb was near at hand) they laid Jesus there.
042001 Now on the first day of the week, Mary Magdalene went early, while it was still dark, to the tomb, and saw the stone taken away from the tomb.
042002 Therefore she ran and came to Simon Peter, and to the other disciple whom Jesus loved, and said to them, "They have taken away the Lord out of the tomb, and we don't know where they have laid him!"
042003 Therefore Peter and the other disciple went out, and they went toward the tomb.
042004 They both ran together. The other disciple outran Peter, and came to the tomb first.
042005 Stooping and looking in, he saw the linen cloths lying, yet he didn't enter in.
042006 Then Simon Peter came, following him, and entered into the tomb. He saw the linen cloths lying,
042007 and the cloth that had been on his head, not lying with the linen cloths, but rolled up in a place by itself.
042008 So then the other disciple who came first to the tomb also entered in, and he saw and believed.
042009 For as yet they didn't know the Scripture, that he must rise from the dead.
042010 So the disciples went away again to their own homes.
042011 But Mary was standing outside at the tomb weeping. So, as she wept, she stooped and looked into the tomb,
042012 and she saw two angels in white sitting, one at the head, and one at the feet, where the body of Jesus had lain.
042013 They told her, "Woman, why are you weeping?" She said to them, "Because they have taken away my Lord, and I don't know where they have laid him."
042014 When she had said this, she turned around and saw Jesus standing, and didn't know that it was Jesus.
042015 Jesus said to her, "Woman, why are you weeping? Who are you looking for?" She, supposing him to be the gardener, said to him, "Sir, if you have carried him away, tell me where you have laid him, and I will take him away."
042016 Jesus said to her, "Mary." She turned and said to him, "Rabboni!" which is to say, "Teacher!"
042017 Jesus said to her, "Don't hold me, for I haven't yet ascended to my Father; but go to my brothers, and tell them, 'I am ascending to my Father and your Father, to my God and your God.'"
042018 Mary Magdalene came and told the disciples that she had seen the Lord, and that he had said these things to her.
042019 When therefore it was evening, on that day, the first day of the week, and when the doors were locked where the disciples were assembled, for fear of the Jews, Jesus came and stood in the midst, and said to them, "Peace be to you."
042020 When he had said this, he showed them his hands and his side. The disciples therefore were glad when they saw the Lord.
042021 Jesus therefore said to them again, "Peace be to you. As the Father has sent me, even so I send you."
042022 When he had said this, he breathed on them, and said to them, "Receive the Holy Spirit!
042023 Whoever's sins you forgive, they are forgiven them. Whoever's sins you retain, they have been retained."
042024 But Thomas, one of the twelve, called Didymus, wasn't with them when Jesus came.
042025 The other disciples therefore said to him, "We have seen the Lord!" But he said to them, "Unless I see in his hands the print of the nails, and put my hand into his side, I will not believe."
042026 After eight days again his disciples were inside, and Thomas was with them. Jesus came, the doors being locked, and stood in the midst, and said, "Peace be to you."
042027 Then he said to Thomas, "Reach here your finger, and see my hands. Reach here your hand, and put it into my side. Don't be unbelieving, but believing."
042028 Thomas answered him, "My Lord and my God!"
042029 Jesus said to him, "Because you have seen me, you have believed. Blessed are those who have not seen, and have believed."
042030 Therefore Jesus did many other signs in the presence of his disciples, which are not written in this book;
042031 but these are written, that you may believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God, and that believing you may have life in his name.
042101 After these things, Jesus revealed himself again to the disciples at the sea of Tiberias. He revealed himself this way.
042102 Simon Peter, Thomas called Didymus, Nathanael of Cana in Galilee, and the sons of Zebedee, and two others of his disciples were together.
042103 Simon Peter said to them, "I'm going fishing." They told him, "We are also coming with you." They immediately went out, and entered into the boat. That night, they caught nothing.
042104 But when day had already come, Jesus stood on the beach, yet the disciples didn't know that it was Jesus.
042105 Jesus therefore said to them, "Children, have you anything to eat?" They answered him, "No."
042106 He said to them, "Cast the net on the right side of the boat, and you will find some." They cast it therefore, and now they weren't able to draw it in for the multitude of fish.
042107 That disciple therefore whom Jesus loved said to Peter, "It's the Lord!" So when Simon Peter heard that it was the Lord, he wrapped his coat around him (for he was naked), and threw himself into the sea.
042108 But the other disciples came in the little boat (for they were not far from the land, but about two hundred cubits away), dragging the net full of fish.
042109 So when they got out on the land, they saw a fire of coals there, and fish laid on it, and bread.
042110 Jesus said to them, "Bring some of the fish which you have just caught."
042111 Simon Peter went up, and drew the net to land, full of great fish, one hundred fifty-three; and even though there were so many, the net wasn't torn.
042112 Jesus said to them, "Come and eat breakfast." None of the disciples dared inquire of him, "Who are you?" knowing that it was the Lord.
042113 Then Jesus came and took the bread, gave it to them, and the fish likewise.
042114 This is now the third time that Jesus was revealed to his disciples, after he had risen from the dead.
042115 So when they had eaten their breakfast, Jesus said to Simon Peter, "Simon, son of Jonah, do you love me more than these?" He said to him, "Yes, Lord; you know that I have affection for you." He said to him, "Feed my lambs."
042116 He said to him again a second time, "Simon, son of Jonah, do you love me?" He said to him, "Yes, Lord; you know that I have affection for you." He said to him, "Tend my sheep."
042117 He said to him the third time, "Simon, son of Jonah, do you have affection for me?" Peter was grieved because he asked him the third time, "Do you have affection for me?" He said to him, "Lord, you know everything. You know that I have affection for you." Jesus said to him, "Feed my sheep.
042118 Most certainly I tell you, when you were young, you dressed yourself, and walked where you wanted to. But when you are old, you will stretch out your hands, and another will dress you, and carry you where you don't want to go."
042119 Now he said this, signifying by what kind of death he would glorify God. When he had said this, he said to him, "Follow me."
042120 Then Peter, turning around, saw a disciple following. This was the disciple whom Jesus sincerely loved, the one who had also leaned on Jesus' breast at the supper and asked, "Lord, who is going to betray You?"
042121 Peter seeing him, said to Jesus, "Lord, what about this man?"
042122 Jesus said to him, "If I desire that he stay until I come, what is that to you? You follow me."
042123 This saying therefore went out among the brothers, that this disciple wouldn't die. Yet Jesus didn't say to him that he wouldn't die, but, "If I desire that he stay until I come, what is that to you?"
042124 This is the disciple who testifies about these things, and wrote these things. We know that his witness is true.
042125 There are also many other things which Jesus did, which if they would all be written, I suppose that even the world itself wouldn't have room for the books that would be written.
050101 The first book I wrote, Theophilus, concerned all that Jesus began both to do and to teach,
050102 until the day in which he was received up, after he had given commandment through the Holy Spirit to the apostles whom he had chosen.
050103 To these he also showed himself alive after he suffered, by many proofs, appearing to them over a period of forty days, and speaking about God's Kingdom.
050104 Being assembled together with them, he commanded them, "Don't depart from Jerusalem, but wait for the promise of the Father, which you heard from me.
050105 For John indeed baptized in water, but you will be baptized in the Holy Spirit not many days from now."
050106 Therefore, when they had come together, they asked him, "Lord, are you now restoring the kingdom to Israel?"
050107 He said to them, "It isn't for you to know times or seasons which the Father has set within his own authority.
050108 But you will receive power when the Holy Spirit has come upon you. You will be witnesses to me in Jerusalem, in all Judea and Samaria, and to the uttermost parts of the earth."
050109 When he had said these things, as they were looking, he was taken up, and a cloud received him out of their sight.
050110 While they were looking steadfastly into the sky as he went, behold, two men stood by them in white clothing,
050111 who also said, "You men of Galilee, why do you stand looking into the sky? This Jesus, who was received up from you into the sky will come back in the same way as you saw him going into the sky."
050112 Then they returned to Jerusalem from the mountain called Olivet, which is near Jerusalem, a Sabbath day's journey away.
050113 When they had come in, they went up into the upper room, where they were staying; that is Peter, John, James, Andrew, Philip, Thomas, Bartholomew, Matthew, James the son of Alphaeus, Simon the Zealot, and Judas the son of James.
050114 All these with one accord continued steadfastly in prayer and supplication, along with the women, and Mary the mother of Jesus, and with his brothers.
050115 In these days, Peter stood up in the midst of the disciples (and the number of names was about one hundred twenty), and said,
050116 "Brothers, it was necessary that this Scripture should be fulfilled, which the Holy Spirit spoke before by the mouth of David concerning Judas, who was guide to those who took Jesus.
050117 For he was numbered with us, and received his portion in this ministry.
050118 Now this man obtained a field with the reward for his wickedness, and falling headlong, his body burst open, and all his intestines gushed out.
050119 It became known to everyone who lived in Jerusalem that in their language that field was called 'Akeldama,' that is, 'The field of blood.'
050120 For it is written in the book of Psalms, 'Let his habitation be made desolate. Let no one dwell therein;' and, 'Let another take his office.'
050121 "Of the men therefore who have accompanied us all the time that the Lord Jesus went in and out among us,
050122 beginning from the baptism of John, to the day that he was received up from us, of these one must become a witness with us of his resurrection."
050123 They put forward two, Joseph called Barsabbas, who was surnamed Justus, and Matthias.
050124 They prayed, and said, "You, Lord, who know the hearts of all men, show which one of these two you have chosen
050125 to take part in this ministry and apostleship from which Judas fell away, that he might go to his own place."
050126 They drew lots for them, and the lot fell on Matthias, and he was numbered with the eleven apostles.
050201 Now when the day of Pentecost had come, they were all with one accord in one place.
050202 Suddenly there came from the sky a sound like the rushing of a mighty wind, and it filled all the house where they were sitting.
050203 Tongues like fire appeared and were distributed to them, and one sat on each of them.
050204 They were all filled with the Holy Spirit, and began to speak with other languages, as the Spirit gave them the ability to speak.
050205 Now there were dwelling in Jerusalem Jews, devout men, from every nation under the sky.
050206 When this sound was heard, the multitude came together, and were bewildered, because everyone heard them speaking in his own language.
050207 They were all amazed and marveled, saying to one another, "Behold, aren't all these who speak Galileans?
050208 How do we hear, everyone in our own native language?
050209 Parthians, Medes, Elamites, and people from Mesopotamia, Judea, Cappadocia, Pontus, Asia,
050210 Phrygia, Pamphylia, Egypt, the parts of Libya around Cyrene, visitors from Rome, both Jews and proselytes,
050211 Cretans and Arabians: we hear them speaking in our languages the mighty works of God!"
050212 They were all amazed, and were perplexed, saying one to another, "What does this mean?"
050213 Others, mocking, said, "They are filled with new wine."
050214 But Peter, standing up with the eleven, lifted up his voice, and spoke out to them, "You men of Judea, and all you who dwell at Jerusalem, let this be known to you, and listen to my words.
050215 For these aren't drunken, as you suppose, seeing it is only the third hour of the day.
050216 But this is what has been spoken through the prophet Joel:
050217 'It will be in the last days, says God, that I will pour out my Spirit on all flesh. Your sons and your daughters will prophesy. Your young men will see visions. Your old men will dream dreams.
050218 Yes, and on my servants and on my handmaidens in those days, I will pour out my Spirit, and they will prophesy.
050219 I will show wonders in the sky above, and signs on the earth beneath; blood, and fire, and billows of smoke.
050220 The sun will be turned into darkness, and the moon into blood, before the great and glorious day of the Lord comes.
050221 It will be, that whoever will call on the name of the Lord will be saved.'
050222 "Men of Israel, hear these words! Jesus of Nazareth, a man approved by God to you by mighty works and wonders and signs which God did by him in the midst of you, even as you yourselves know,
050223 him, being delivered up by the determined counsel and foreknowledge of God, you have taken by the hand of lawless men, crucified and killed;
050224 whom God raised up, having freed him from the agony of death, because it was not possible that he should be held by it.
050225 For David says concerning him, 'I saw the Lord always before my face, For he is on my right hand, that I should not be moved.
050226 Therefore my heart was glad, and my tongue rejoiced. Moreover my flesh also will dwell in hope;
050227 because you will not leave my soul in Hades, neither will you allow your Holy One to see decay.
050228 You made known to me the ways of life. You will make me full of gladness with your presence.'
050229 "Brothers, I may tell you freely of the patriarch David, that he both died and was buried, and his tomb is with us to this day.
050230 Therefore, being a prophet, and knowing that God had sworn with an oath to him that of the fruit of his body, according to the flesh, he would raise up the Christ to sit on his throne,
050231 he foreseeing this spoke about the resurrection of the Christ, that neither was his soul left in Hades, nor did his flesh see decay.
050232 This Jesus God raised up, to which we all are witnesses.
050233 Being therefore exalted by the right hand of God, and having received from the Father the promise of the Holy Spirit, he has poured out this, which you now see and hear.
050234 For David didn't ascend into the heavens, but he says himself, 'The Lord said to my Lord, "Sit by my right hand,
050235 until I make your enemies a footstool for your feet."'
050236 "Let all the house of Israel therefore know certainly that God has made him both Lord and Christ, this Jesus whom you crucified."
050237 Now when they heard this, they were cut to the heart, and said to Peter and the rest of the apostles, "Brothers, what shall we do?"
050238 Peter said to them, "Repent, and be baptized, every one of you, in the name of Jesus Christ for the forgiveness of sins, and you will receive the gift of the Holy Spirit.
050239 For the promise is to you, and to your children, and to all who are far off, even as many as the Lord our God will call to himself."
050240 With many other words he testified, and exhorted them, saying, "Save yourselves from this crooked generation!"
050241 Then those who gladly received his word were baptized. There were added that day about three thousand souls.
050242 They continued steadfastly in the apostles' teaching and fellowship, in the breaking of bread, and prayer.
050243 Fear came on every soul, and many wonders and signs were done through the apostles.
050244 All who believed were together, and had all things in common.
050245 They sold their possessions and goods, and distributed them to all, according as anyone had need.
050246 Day by day, continuing steadfastly with one accord in the temple, and breaking bread at home, they took their food with gladness and singleness of heart,
050247 praising God, and having favor with all the people. The Lord added to the assembly day by day those who were being saved.
050301 Peter and John were going up into the temple at the hour of prayer, the ninth hour.
050302 A certain man who was lame from his mother's womb was being carried, whom they laid daily at the door of the temple which is called Beautiful, to ask gifts for the needy of those who entered into the temple.
050303 Seeing Peter and John about to go into the temple, he asked to receive gifts for the needy.
050304 Peter, fastening his eyes on him, with John, said, "Look at us."
050305 He listened to them, expecting to receive something from them.
050306 But Peter said, "Silver and gold have I none, but what I have, that I give you. In the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, get up and walk!"
050307 He took him by the right hand, and raised him up. Immediately his feet and his ankle bones received strength.
050308 Leaping up, he stood, and began to walk. He entered with them into the temple, walking, leaping, and praising God.
050309 All the people saw him walking and praising God.
050310 They recognized him, that it was he who used to sit begging for gifts for the needy at the Beautiful Gate of the temple. They were filled with wonder and amazement at what had happened to him.
050311 As the lame man who was healed held on to Peter and John, all the people ran together to them in the porch that is called Solomon's, greatly wondering.
050312 When Peter saw it, he responded to the people, "You men of Israel, why do you marvel at this man? Why do you fasten your eyes on us, as though by our own power or godliness we had made him walk?
050313 The God of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, the God of our fathers, has glorified his Servant Jesus, whom you delivered up, and denied in the presence of Pilate, when he had determined to release him.
050314 But you denied the Holy and Righteous One, and asked for a murderer to be granted to you,
050315 and killed the Prince of life, whom God raised from the dead, to which we are witnesses.
050316 By faith in his name, his name has made this man strong, whom you see and know. Yes, the faith which is through him has given him this perfect soundness in the presence of you all.
050317 "Now, brothers, I know that you did this in ignorance, as did also your rulers.
050318 But the things which God announced by the mouth of all his prophets, that Christ should suffer, he thus fulfilled.
050319 "Repent therefore, and turn again, that your sins may be blotted out, so that there may come times of refreshing from the presence of the Lord,
050320 and that he may send Christ Jesus, who was ordained for you before,
050321 whom heaven must receive until the times of restoration of all things, which God spoke long ago by the mouth of his holy prophets.
050322 For Moses indeed said to the fathers, 'The Lord God will raise up a prophet for you from among your brothers, like me. You shall listen to him in all things whatever he says to you.
050323 It will be, that every soul that will not listen to that prophet will be utterly destroyed from among the people.'
050324 Yes, and all the prophets from Samuel and those who followed after, as many as have spoken, they also told of these days.
050325 You are the children of the prophets, and of the covenant which God made with our fathers, saying to Abraham, 'In your seed will all the families of the earth be blessed.'
050326 God, having raised up his servant, Jesus, sent him to you first, to bless you, in turning away everyone of you from your wickedness."
050401 As they spoke to the people, the priests and the captain of the temple and the Sadducees came to them,
050402 being upset because they taught the people and proclaimed in Jesus the resurrection from the dead.
050403 They laid hands on them, and put them in custody until the next day, for it was now evening.
050404 But many of those who heard the word believed, and the number of the men came to be about five thousand.
050405 It happened in the morning, that their rulers, elders, and scribes were gathered together in Jerusalem.
050406 Annas the high priest was there, with Caiaphas, John, Alexander, and as many as were relatives of the high priest.
050407 When they had stood them in the middle of them, they inquired, "By what power, or in what name, have you done this?"
050408 Then Peter, filled with the Holy Spirit, said to them, "You rulers of the people, and elders of Israel,
050409 if we are examined today concerning a good deed done to a crippled man, by what means this man has been healed,
050410 be it known to you all, and to all the people of Israel, that in the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, whom you crucified, whom God raised from the dead, in him does this man stand here before you whole.
050411 He is 'the stone which was regarded as worthless by you, the builders, which has become the head of the corner.'
050412 There is salvation in none other, for neither is there any other name under heaven, that is given among men, by which we must be saved!"
050413 Now when they saw the boldness of Peter and John, and had perceived that they were unlearned and ignorant men, they marveled. They recognized that they had been with Jesus.
050414 Seeing the man who was healed standing with them, they could say nothing against it.
050415 But when they had commanded them to go aside out of the council, they conferred among themselves,
050416 saying, "What shall we do to these men? Because indeed a notable miracle has been done through them, as can be plainly seen by all who dwell in Jerusalem, and we can't deny it.
050417 But so that this spreads no further among the people, let's threaten them, that from now on they don't speak to anyone in this name."
050418 They called them, and commanded them not to speak at all nor teach in the name of Jesus.
050419 But Peter and John answered them, "Whether it is right in the sight of God to listen to you rather than to God, judge for yourselves,
050420 for we can't help telling the things which we saw and heard."
050421 When they had further threatened them, they let them go, finding no way to punish them, because of the people; for everyone glorified God for that which was done.
050422 For the man on whom this miracle of healing was performed was more than forty years old.
050423 Being let go, they came to their own company, and reported all that the chief priests and the elders had said to them.
050424 When they heard it, they lifted up their voice to God with one accord, and said, "O Lord, you are God, who made the heaven, the earth, the sea, and all that is in them;
050425 who by the mouth of your servant, David, said, 'Why do the nations rage, and the peoples plot a vain thing?
050426 The kings of the earth take a stand, and the rulers take council together, against the Lord, and against his Christ.'
050427 "For truly, in this city against your holy servant, Jesus, whom you anointed, both Herod and Pontius Pilate, with the Gentiles and the people of Israel, were gathered together
050428 to do whatever your hand and your council foreordained to happen.
050429 Now, Lord, look at their threats, and grant to your servants to speak your word with all boldness,
050430 while you stretch out your hand to heal; and that signs and wonders may be done through the name of your holy Servant Jesus."
050431 When they had prayed, the place was shaken where they were gathered together. They were all filled with the Holy Spirit, and they spoke the word of God with boldness.
050432 The multitude of those who believed were of one heart and soul. Not one of them claimed that anything of the things which he possessed was his own, but they had all things in common.
050433 With great power, the apostles gave their testimony of the resurrection of the Lord Jesus. Great grace was on them all.
050434 For neither was there among them any who lacked, for as many as were owners of lands or houses sold them, and brought the proceeds of the things that were sold,
050435 and laid them at the apostles' feet, and distribution was made to each, according as anyone had need.
050436 Joses, who by the apostles was surnamed Barnabas (which is, being interpreted, Son of Encouragement), a Levite, a man of Cyprus by race,
050437 having a field, sold it, and brought the money and laid it at the apostles' feet.
050501 But a certain man named Ananias, with Sapphira, his wife, sold a possession,
050502 and kept back part of the price, his wife also being aware of it, and brought a certain part, and laid it at the apostles' feet.
050503 But Peter said, "Ananias, why has Satan filled your heart to lie to the Holy Spirit, and to keep back part of the price of the land?
050504 While you kept it, didn't it remain your own? After it was sold, wasn't it in your power? How is it that you have conceived this thing in your heart? You haven't lied to men, but to God."
050505 Ananias, hearing these words, fell down and died. Great fear came on all who heard these things.
050506 The young men arose and wrapped him up, and they carried him out and buried him.
050507 About three hours later, his wife, not knowing what had happened, came in.
050508 Peter answered her, "Tell me whether you sold the land for so much." She said, "Yes, for so much."
050509 But Peter asked her, "How is it that you have agreed together to tempt the Spirit of the Lord? Behold, the feet of those who have buried your husband are at the door, and they will carry you out."
050510 She fell down immediately at his feet, and died. The young men came in and found her dead, and they carried her out and buried her by her husband.
050511 Great fear came on the whole assembly, and on all who heard these things.
050512 By the hands of the apostles many signs and wonders were done among the people. They were all with one accord in Solomon's porch.
050513 None of the rest dared to join them, however the people honored them.
050514 More believers were added to the Lord, multitudes of both men and women.
050515 They even carried out the sick into the streets, and laid them on cots and mattresses, so that as Peter came by, at the least his shadow might overshadow some of them.
050516 Multitudes also came together from the cities around Jerusalem, bringing sick people, and those who were tormented by unclean spirits: and they were all healed.
050517 But the high priest rose up, and all those who were with him (which is the sect of the Sadducees), and they were filled with jealousy,
050518 and laid hands on the apostles, and put them in public custody.
050519 But an angel of the Lord opened the prison doors by night, and brought them out, and said,
050520 "Go stand and speak in the temple to the people all the words of this life."
050521 When they heard this, they entered into the temple about daybreak, and taught. But the high priest came, and those who were with him, and called the council together, and all the senate of the children of Israel, and sent to the prison to have them brought.
050522 But the officers who came didn't find them in the prison. They returned and reported,
050523 "We found the prison shut and locked, and the guards standing before the doors, but when we opened them, we found no one inside!"
050524 Now when the high priest, the captain of the temple, and the chief priests heard these words, they were very perplexed about them and what might become of this.
050525 One came and told them, "Behold, the men whom you put in prison are in the temple, standing and teaching the people."
050526 Then the captain went with the officers, and brought them without violence, for they were afraid that the people might stone them.
050527 When they had brought them, they set them before the council. The high priest questioned them,
050528 saying, "Didn't we strictly command you not to teach in this name? Behold, you have filled Jerusalem with your teaching, and intend to bring this man's blood on us."
050529 But Peter and the apostles answered, "We must obey God rather than men.
050530 The God of our fathers raised up Jesus, whom you killed, hanging him on a tree.
050531 God exalted him with his right hand to be a Prince and a Savior, to give repentance to Israel, and remission of sins.
050532 We are His witnesses of these things; and so also is the Holy Spirit, whom God has given to those who obey him."
050533 But they, when they heard this, were cut to the heart, and determined to kill them.
050534 But one stood up in the council, a Pharisee named Gamaliel, a teacher of the law, honored by all the people, and commanded to put the apostles out for a little while.
050535 He said to them, "You men of Israel, be careful concerning these men, what you are about to do.
050536 For before these days Theudas rose up, making himself out to be somebody; to whom a number of men, about four hundred, joined themselves: who was slain; and all, as many as obeyed him, were dispersed, and came to nothing.
050537 After this man, Judas of Galilee rose up in the days of the enrollment, and drew away some people after him. He also perished, and all, as many as obeyed him, were scattered abroad.
050538 Now I tell you, withdraw from these men, and leave them alone. For if this counsel or this work is of men, it will be overthrown.
050539 But if it is of God, you will not be able to overthrow it, and you would be found even to be fighting against God!"
050540 They agreed with him. Summoning the apostles, they beat them and commanded them not to speak in the name of Jesus, and let them go.
050541 They therefore departed from the presence of the council, rejoicing that they were counted worthy to suffer dishonor for Jesus' name.
050542 Every day, in the temple and at home, they never stopped teaching and preaching Jesus, the Christ.
050601 Now in those days, when the number of the disciples was multiplying, a complaint arose from the Hellenists against the Hebrews, because their widows were neglected in the daily service.
050602 The twelve summoned the multitude of the disciples and said, "It is not appropriate for us to forsake the word of God and serve tables.
050603 Therefore select from among you, brothers, seven men of good report, full of the Holy Spirit and of wisdom, whom we may appoint over this business.
050604 But we will continue steadfastly in prayer and in the ministry of the word."
050605 These words pleased the whole multitude. They chose Stephen, a man full of faith and of the Holy Spirit, Philip, Prochorus, Nicanor, Timon, Parmenas, and Nicolaus, a proselyte of Antioch;
050606 whom they set before the apostles. When they had prayed, they laid their hands on them.
050607 The word of God increased and the number of the disciples multiplied in Jerusalem exceedingly. A great company of the priests were obedient to the faith.
050608 Stephen, full of faith and power, performed great wonders and signs among the people.
050609 But some of those who were of the synagogue called "The Libertines," and of the Cyrenians, of the Alexandrians, and of those of Cilicia and Asia arose, disputing with Stephen.
050610 They weren't able to withstand the wisdom and the Spirit by which he spoke.
050611 Then they secretly induced men to say, "We have heard him speak blasphemous words against Moses and God."
050612 They stirred up the people, the elders, and the scribes, and came against him and seized him, and brought him in to the council,
050613 and set up false witnesses who said, "This man never stops speaking blasphemous words against this holy place and the law.
050614 For we have heard him say that this Jesus of Nazareth will destroy this place, and will change the customs which Moses delivered to us."
050615 All who sat in the council, fastening their eyes on him, saw his face like it was the face of an angel.
050701 The high priest said, "Are these things so?"
050702 He said, "Brothers and fathers, listen. The God of glory appeared to our father Abraham, when he was in Mesopotamia, before he lived in Haran,
050703 and said to him, 'Get out of your land, and from your relatives, and come into a land which I will show you.'
050704 Then he came out of the land of the Chaldaeans, and lived in Haran. From there, when his father was dead, God moved him into this land, where you are now living.
050705 He gave him no inheritance in it, no, not so much as to set his foot on. He promised that he would give it to him for a possession, and to his seed after him, when he still had no child.
050706 God spoke in this way: that his seed would live as aliens in a strange land, and that they would be enslaved and mistreated for four hundred years.
050707 'I will judge the nation to which they will be in bondage,' said God, 'and after that will they come out, and serve me in this place.'
050708 He gave him the covenant of circumcision. So Abraham became the father of Isaac, and circumcised him the eighth day. Isaac became the father of Jacob, and Jacob became the father of the twelve patriarchs.
050709 "The patriarchs, moved with jealousy against Joseph, sold him into Egypt. God was with him,
050710 and delivered him out of all his afflictions, and gave him favor and wisdom before Pharaoh, king of Egypt. He made him governor over Egypt and all his house.
050711 Now a famine came over all the land of Egypt and Canaan, and great affliction. Our fathers found no food.
050712 But when Jacob heard that there was grain in Egypt, he sent out our fathers the first time.
050713 On the second time Joseph was made known to his brothers, and Joseph's race was revealed to Pharaoh.
050714 Joseph sent, and summoned Jacob, his father, and all his relatives, seventy-five souls.
050715 Jacob went down into Egypt, and he died, himself and our fathers,
050716 and they were brought back to Shechem, and laid in the tomb that Abraham bought for a price in silver from the children of Hamor of Shechem.
050717 "But as the time of the promise came close which God had sworn to Abraham, the people grew and multiplied in Egypt,
050718 until there arose a different king, who didn't know Joseph.
050719 The same took advantage of our race, and mistreated our fathers, and forced them to throw out their babies, so that they wouldn't stay alive.
050720 At that time Moses was born, and was exceedingly handsome. He was nourished three months in his father's house.
050721 When he was thrown out, Pharaoh's daughter took him up, and reared him as her own son.
050722 Moses was instructed in all the wisdom of the Egyptians. He was mighty in his words and works.
050723 But when he was forty years old, it came into his heart to visit his brothers, the children of Israel.
050724 Seeing one of them suffer wrong, he defended him, and avenged him who was oppressed, striking the Egyptian.
050725 He supposed that his brothers understood that God, by his hand, was giving them deliverance; but they didn't understand.
050726 "The day following, he appeared to them as they fought, and urged them to be at peace again, saying, 'Sirs, you are brothers. Why do you wrong one another?'
050727 But he who did his neighbor wrong pushed him away, saying, 'Who made you a ruler and a judge over us?
050728 Do you want to kill me, as you killed the Egyptian yesterday?'
050729 Moses fled at this saying, and became a stranger in the land of Midian, where he became the father of two sons.
050730 "When forty years were fulfilled, an angel of the Lord appeared to him in the wilderness of Mount Sinai, in a flame of fire in a bush.
050731 When Moses saw it, he wondered at the sight. As he came close to see, a voice of the Lord came to him,
050732 'I am the God of your fathers, the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob.' Moses trembled, and dared not look.
050733 The Lord said to him, 'Take your sandals off of your feet, for the place where you stand is holy ground.
050734 I have surely seen the affliction of my people that is in Egypt, and have heard their groaning. I have come down to deliver them. Now come, I will send you into Egypt.'
050735 "This Moses, whom they refused, saying, 'Who made you a ruler and a judge?'--God has sent him as both a ruler and a deliverer by the hand of the angel who appeared to him in the bush.
050736 This man led them out, having worked wonders and signs in Egypt, in the Red Sea, and in the wilderness for forty years.
050737 This is that Moses, who said to the children of Israel, 'The Lord our God will raise up a prophet for you from among your brothers, like me.'
050738 This is he who was in the assembly in the wilderness with the angel that spoke to him on Mount Sinai, and with our fathers, who received living oracles to give to us,
050739 to whom our fathers wouldn't be obedient, but rejected him, and turned back in their hearts to Egypt,
050740 saying to Aaron, 'Make us gods that will go before us, for as for this Moses, who led us out of the land of Egypt, we don't know what has become of him.'
