050741 They made a calf in those days, and brought a sacrifice to the idol, and rejoiced in the works of their hands.
050742 But God turned, and gave them up to serve the army of the sky, as it is written in the book of the prophets, 'Did you offer to me slain animals and sacrifices forty years in the wilderness, O house of Israel?
050743 You took up the tabernacle of Moloch, the star of your god Rephan, the figures which you made to worship. I will carry you away beyond Babylon.'
050744 "Our fathers had the tabernacle of the testimony in the wilderness, even as he who spoke to Moses commanded him to make it according to the pattern that he had seen;
050745 which also our fathers, in their turn, brought in with Joshua when they entered into the possession of the nations, whom God drove out before the face of our fathers, to the days of David,
050746 who found favor in the sight of God, and asked to find a habitation for the God of Jacob.
050747 But Solomon built him a house.
050748 However, the Most High doesn't dwell in temples made with hands, as the prophet says,
050749 'heaven is my throne, and the earth a footstool for my feet. What kind of house will you build me?' says the Lord; 'or what is the place of my rest?
050750 Didn't my hand make all these things?'
050751 "You stiff-necked and uncircumcised in heart and ears, you always resist the Holy Spirit! As your fathers did, so you do.
050752 Which of the prophets didn't your fathers persecute? They killed those who foretold the coming of the Righteous One, of whom you have now become betrayers and murderers.
050753 You received the law as it was ordained by angels, and didn't keep it!"
050754 Now when they heard these things, they were cut to the heart, and they gnashed at him with their teeth.
050755 But he, being full of the Holy Spirit, looked up steadfastly into heaven, and saw the glory of God, and Jesus standing on the right hand of God,
050756 and said, "Behold, I see the heavens opened, and the Son of Man standing at the right hand of God!"
050757 But they cried out with a loud voice, and stopped their ears, and rushed at him with one accord.
050758 They threw him out of the city, and stoned him. The witnesses placed their garments at the feet of a young man named Saul.
050759 They stoned Stephen as he called out, saying, "Lord Jesus, receive my spirit!"
050760 He kneeled down, and cried with a loud voice, "Lord, don't hold this sin against them!" When he had said this, he fell asleep.
050801 Saul was consenting to his death. A great persecution arose against the assembly which was in Jerusalem in that day. They were all scattered abroad throughout the regions of Judea and Samaria, except for the apostles.
050802 Devout men buried Stephen, and lamented greatly over him.
050803 But Saul ravaged the assembly, entering into every house, and dragged both men and women off to prison.
050804 Therefore those who were scattered abroad went around preaching the word.
050805 Philip went down to the city of Samaria, and proclaimed to them the Christ.
050806 The multitudes listened with one accord to the things that were spoken by Philip, when they heard and saw the signs which he did.
050807 For unclean spirits came out of many of those who had them. They came out, crying with a loud voice. Many who had been paralyzed and lame were healed.
050808 There was great joy in that city.
050809 But there was a certain man, Simon by name, who used to practice sorcery in the city, and amazed the people of Samaria, making himself out to be some great one,
050810 to whom they all listened, from the least to the greatest, saying, "This man is that great power of God."
050811 They listened to him, because for a long time he had amazed them with his sorceries.
050812 But when they believed Philip preaching good news concerning the Kingdom of God and the name of Jesus Christ, they were baptized, both men and women.
050813 Simon himself also believed. Being baptized, he continued with Philip. Seeing signs and great miracles occurring, he was amazed.
050814 Now when the apostles who were at Jerusalem heard that Samaria had received the word of God, they sent Peter and John to them,
050815 who, when they had come down, prayed for them, that they might receive the Holy Spirit;
050816 for as yet he had fallen on none of them. They had only been baptized in the name of Christ Jesus.
050817 Then they laid their hands on them, and they received the Holy Spirit.
050818 Now when Simon saw that the Holy Spirit was given through the laying on of the apostles' hands, he offered them money,
050819 saying, "Give me also this power, that whoever I lay my hands on may receive the Holy Spirit."
050820 But Peter said to him, "May your silver perish with you, because you thought you could obtain the gift of God with money!
050821 You have neither part nor lot in this matter, for your heart isn't right before God.
050822 Repent therefore of this, your wickedness, and ask God if perhaps the thought of your heart may be forgiven you.
050823 For I see that you are in the gall of bitterness and in the bondage of iniquity."
050824 Simon answered, "Pray for me to the Lord, that none of the things which you have spoken happen to me."
050825 They therefore, when they had testified and spoken the word of the Lord, returned to Jerusalem, and preached the Good News to many villages of the Samaritans.
050826 But an angel of the Lord spoke to Philip, saying, "Arise, and go toward the south to the way that goes down from Jerusalem to Gaza. This is a desert."
050827 He arose and went; and behold, there was a man of Ethiopia, a eunuch of great authority under Candace, queen of the Ethiopians, who was over all her treasure, who had come to Jerusalem to worship.
050828 He was returning and sitting in his chariot, and was reading the prophet Isaiah.
050829 The Spirit said to Philip, "Go near, and join yourself to this chariot."
050830 Philip ran to him, and heard him reading Isaiah the prophet, and said, "Do you understand what you are reading?"
050831 He said, "How can I, unless someone explains it to me?" He begged Philip to come up and sit with him.
050832 Now the passage of the Scripture which he was reading was this, "He was led as a sheep to the slaughter. As a lamb before his shearer is silent, so he doesn't open his mouth.
050833 In his humiliation, his judgment was taken away. Who will declare His generation? For his life is taken from the earth."
050834 The eunuch answered Philip, "Who is the prophet talking about? About himself, or about someone else?"
050835 Philip opened his mouth, and beginning from this Scripture, preached to him Jesus.
050836 As they went on the way, they came to some water, and the eunuch said, "Behold, here is water. What is keeping me from being baptized?"
050837 
050838 He commanded the chariot to stand still, and they both went down into the water, both Philip and the eunuch, and he baptized him.
050839 When they came up out of the water, the Spirit of the Lord caught Philip away, and the eunuch didn't see him any more, for he went on his way rejoicing.
050840 But Philip was found at Azotus. Passing through, he preached the Good News to all the cities, until he came to Caesarea.
050901 But Saul, still breathing threats and slaughter against the disciples of the Lord, went to the high priest,
050902 and asked for letters from him to the synagogues of Damascus, that if he found any who were of the Way, whether men or women, he might bring them bound to Jerusalem.
050903 As he traveled, it happened that he got close to Damascus, and suddenly a light from the sky shone around him.
050904 He fell on the earth, and heard a voice saying to him, "Saul, Saul, why do you persecute me?"
050905 He said, "Who are you, Lord?" The Lord said, "I am Jesus, whom you are persecuting.
050906 But rise up, and enter into the city, and you will be told what you must do."
050907 The men who traveled with him stood speechless, hearing the sound, but seeing no one.
050908 Saul arose from the ground, and when his eyes were opened, he saw no one. They led him by the hand, and brought him into Damascus.
050909 He was without sight for three days, and neither ate nor drank.
050910 Now there was a certain disciple at Damascus named Ananias. The Lord said to him in a vision, "Ananias!" He said, "Behold, it's me, Lord."
050911 The Lord said to him, "Arise, and go to the street which is called Straight, and inquire in the house of Judah for one named Saul, a man of Tarsus. For behold, he is praying,
050912 and in a vision he has seen a man named Ananias coming in, and laying his hands on him, that he might receive his sight."
050913 But Ananias answered, "Lord, I have heard from many about this man, how much evil he did to your saints at Jerusalem.
050914 Here he has authority from the chief priests to bind all who call on your name."
050915 But the Lord said to him, "Go your way, for he is my chosen vessel to bear my name before the nations and kings, and the children of Israel.
050916 For I will show him how many things he must suffer for my name's sake."
050917 Ananias departed, and entered into the house. Laying his hands on him, he said, "Brother Saul, the Lord, who appeared to you on the road by which you came, has sent me, that you may receive your sight, and be filled with the Holy Spirit."
050918 Immediately something like scales fell from his eyes, and he received his sight. He arose and was baptized.
050919 He took food and was strengthened. Saul stayed several days with the disciples who were at Damascus.
050920 Immediately in the synagogues he proclaimed the Christ, that he is the Son of God.
050921 All who heard him were amazed, and said, "Isn't this he who in Jerusalem made havoc of those who called on this name? And he had come here intending to bring them bound before the chief priests!"
050922 But Saul increased more in strength, and confounded the Jews who lived at Damascus, proving that this is the Christ.
050923 When many days were fulfilled, the Jews conspired together to kill him,
050924 but their plot became known to Saul. They watched the gates both day and night that they might kill him,
050925 but his disciples took him by night, and let him down through the wall, lowering him in a basket.
050926 When Saul had come to Jerusalem, he tried to join himself to the disciples; but they were all afraid of him, not believing that he was a disciple.
050927 But Barnabas took him, and brought him to the apostles, and declared to them how he had seen the Lord in the way, and that he had spoken to him, and how at Damascus he had preached boldly in the name of Jesus.
050928 He was with them entering into Jerusalem,
050929 preaching boldly in the name of the Lord Jesus. He spoke and disputed against the Hellenists, but they were seeking to kill him.
050930 When the brothers knew it, they brought him down to Caesarea, and sent him off to Tarsus.
050931 So the assemblies throughout all Judea and Galilee and Samaria had peace, and were built up. They were multiplied, walking in the fear of the Lord and in the comfort of the Holy Spirit.
050932 It happened, as Peter went throughout all those parts, he came down also to the saints who lived at Lydda.
050933 There he found a certain man named Aeneas, who had been bedridden for eight years, because he was paralyzed.
050934 Peter said to him, "Aeneas, Jesus Christ heals you. Get up and make your bed!" Immediately he arose.
050935 All who lived at Lydda and in Sharon saw him, and they turned to the Lord.
050936 Now there was at Joppa a certain disciple named Tabitha, which when translated, means Dorcas. This woman was full of good works and acts of mercy which she did.
050937 It happened in those days that she fell sick, and died. When they had washed her, they laid her in an upper chamber.
050938 As Lydda was near Joppa, the disciples, hearing that Peter was there, sent two men to him, imploring him not to delay in coming to them.
050939 Peter got up and went with them. When he had come, they brought him into the upper chamber. All the widows stood by him weeping, and showing the coats and garments which Dorcas had made while she was with them.
050940 Peter put them all out, and kneeled down and prayed. Turning to the body, he said, "Tabitha, get up!" She opened her eyes, and when she saw Peter, she sat up.
050941 He gave her his hand, and raised her up. Calling the saints and widows, he presented her alive.
050942 And it became known throughout all Joppa, and many believed in the Lord.
050943 It happened, that he stayed many days in Joppa with one Simon, a tanner.
051001 Now there was a certain man in Caesarea, Cornelius by name, a centurion of what was called the Italian Regiment,
051002 a devout man, and one who feared God with all his house, who gave gifts for the needy generously to the people, and always prayed to God.
051003 At about the ninth hour of the day, he clearly saw in a vision an angel of God coming to him, and saying to him, "Cornelius!"
051004 He, fastening his eyes on him, and being frightened, said, "What is it, Lord?" He said to him, "Your prayers and your gifts to the needy have gone up for a memorial before God.
051005 Now send men to Joppa, and get Simon, who is surnamed Peter.
051006 He lodges with one Simon, a tanner, whose house is by the seaside."
051007 When the angel who spoke to him had departed, Cornelius called two of his household servants and a devout soldier of those who waited on him continually.
051008 Having explained everything to them, he sent them to Joppa.
051009 Now on the next day as they were on their journey, and got close to the city, Peter went up on the housetop to pray at about noon.
051010 He became hungry and desired to eat, but while they were preparing, he fell into a trance.
051011 He saw heaven opened and a certain container descending to him, like a great sheet let down by four corners on the earth,
051012 in which were all kinds of four-footed animals of the earth, wild animals, reptiles, and birds of the sky.
051013 A voice came to him, "Rise, Peter, kill and eat!"
051014 But Peter said, "Not so, Lord; for I have never eaten anything that is common or unclean."
051015 A voice came to him again the second time, "What God has cleansed, you must not call unclean."
051016 This was done three times, and immediately the vessel was received up into heaven.
051017 Now while Peter was very perplexed in himself what the vision which he had seen might mean, behold, the men who were sent by Cornelius, having made inquiry for Simon's house, stood before the gate,
051018 and called and asked whether Simon, who was surnamed Peter, was lodging there.
051019 While Peter was pondering the vision, the Spirit said to him, "Behold, three men seek you.
051020 But arise, get down, and go with them, doubting nothing; for I have sent them."
051021 Peter went down to the men, and said, "Behold, I am he whom you seek. Why have you come?"
051022 They said, "Cornelius, a centurion, a righteous man and one who fears God, and well spoken of by all the nation of the Jews, was directed by a holy angel to invite you to his house, and to listen to what you say."
051023 So he called them in and lodged them. On the next day Peter arose and went out with them, and some of the brothers from Joppa accompanied him.
051024 On the next day they entered into Caesarea. Cornelius was waiting for them, having called together his relatives and his near friends.
051025 When it happened that Peter entered, Cornelius met him, fell down at his feet, and worshiped him.
051026 But Peter raised him up, saying, "Stand up! I myself am also a man."
051027 As he talked with him, he went in and found many gathered together.
051028 He said to them, "You yourselves know how it is an unlawful thing for a man who is a Jew to join himself or come to one of another nation, but God has shown me that I shouldn't call any man unholy or unclean.
051029 Therefore also I came without complaint when I was sent for. I ask therefore, why did you send for me?"
051030 Cornelius said, "Four days ago, I was fasting until this hour, and at the ninth hour, I prayed in my house, and behold, a man stood before me in bright clothing,
051031 and said, 'Cornelius, your prayer is heard, and your gifts to the needy are remembered in the sight of God.
051032 Send therefore to Joppa, and summon Simon, who is surnamed Peter. He lodges in the house of Simon a tanner, by the seaside. When he comes, he will speak to you.'
051033 Therefore I sent to you at once, and it was good of you to come. Now therefore we are all here present in the sight of God to hear all things that have been commanded you by God."
051034 Peter opened his mouth and said, "Truly I perceive that God doesn't show favoritism;
051035 but in every nation he who fears him and works righteousness is acceptable to him.
051036 The word which he sent to the children of Israel, preaching good news of peace by Jesus Christ--he is Lord of all--
051037 that spoken word you yourselves know, which was proclaimed throughout all Judea, beginning from Galilee, after the baptism which John preached;
051038 even Jesus of Nazareth, how God anointed him with the Holy Spirit and with power, who went about doing good and healing all who were oppressed by the devil, for God was with him.
051039 We are witnesses of everything he did both in the country of the Jews, and in Jerusalem; whom they also killed, hanging him on a tree.
051040 God raised him up the third day, and gave him to be revealed,
051041 not to all the people, but to witnesses who were chosen before by God, to us, who ate and drank with him after he rose from the dead.
051042 He commanded us to preach to the people and to testify that this is he who is appointed by God as the Judge of the living and the dead.
051043 All the prophets testify about him, that through his name everyone who believes in him will receive remission of sins."
051044 While Peter was still speaking these words, the Holy Spirit fell on all those who heard the word.
051045 They of the circumcision who believed were amazed, as many as came with Peter, because the gift of the Holy Spirit was also poured out on the Gentiles.
051046 For they heard them speaking in other languages and magnifying God. Then Peter answered,
051047 "Can any man forbid the water, that these who have received the Holy Spirit as well as we should not be baptized?"
051048 He commanded them to be baptized in the name of Jesus Christ. Then they asked him to stay some days.
051101 Now the apostles and the brothers who were in Judea heard that the Gentiles had also received the word of God.
051102 When Peter had come up to Jerusalem, those who were of the circumcision contended with him,
051103 saying, "You went in to uncircumcised men, and ate with them!"
051104 But Peter began, and explained to them in order, saying,
051105 "I was in the city of Joppa praying, and in a trance I saw a vision: a certain container descending, like it was a great sheet let down from heaven by four corners. It came as far as me.
051106 When I had looked intently at it, I considered, and saw the four-footed animals of the earth, wild animals, creeping things, and birds of the sky.
051107 I also heard a voice saying to me, 'Rise, Peter, kill and eat!'
051108 But I said, 'Not so, Lord, for nothing unholy or unclean has ever entered into my mouth.'
051109 But a voice answered me the second time out of heaven, 'What God has cleansed, don't you call unclean.'
051110 This was done three times, and all were drawn up again into heaven.
051111 Behold, immediately three men stood before the house where I was, having been sent from Caesarea to me.
051112 The Spirit told me to go with them, without discriminating. These six brothers also accompanied me, and we entered into the man's house.
051113 He told us how he had seen the angel standing in his house, and saying to him, 'Send to Joppa, and get Simon, whose surname is Peter,
051114 who will speak to you words by which you will be saved, you and all your house.'
051115 As I began to speak, the Holy Spirit fell on them, even as on us at the beginning.
051116 I remembered the word of the Lord, how he said, 'John indeed baptized in water, but you will be baptized in the Holy Spirit.'
051117 If then God gave to them the same gift as us, when we believed in the Lord Jesus Christ, who was I, that I could withstand God?"
051118 When they heard these things, they held their peace, and glorified God, saying, "Then God has also granted to the Gentiles repentance to life!"
051119 They therefore who were scattered abroad by the oppression that arose about Stephen traveled as far as Phoenicia, Cyprus, and Antioch, speaking the word to no one except to Jews only.
051120 But there were some of them, men of Cyprus and Cyrene, who, when they had come to Antioch, spoke to the Hellenists, preaching the Lord Jesus.
051121 The hand of the Lord was with them, and a great number believed and turned to the Lord.
051122 The report concerning them came to the ears of the assembly which was in Jerusalem. They sent out Barnabas to go as far as Antioch,
051123 who, when he had come, and had seen the grace of God, was glad. He exhorted them all, that with purpose of heart they should remain near to the Lord.
051124 For he was a good man, and full of the Holy Spirit and of faith, and many people were added to the Lord.
051125 Barnabas went out to Tarsus to look for Saul.
051126 When he had found him, he brought him to Antioch. It happened, that for a whole year they were gathered together with the assembly, and taught many people. The disciples were first called Christians in Antioch.
051127 Now in these days, prophets came down from Jerusalem to Antioch.
051128 One of them named Agabus stood up, and indicated by the Spirit that there should be a great famine all over the world, which also happened in the days of Claudius.
051129 As any of the disciples had plenty, each determined to send relief to the brothers who lived in Judea;
051130 which they also did, sending it to the elders by the hands of Barnabas and Saul.
051201 Now about that time, King Herod stretched out his hands to oppress some of the assembly.
051202 He killed James, the brother of John, with the sword.
051203 When he saw that it pleased the Jews, he proceeded to seize Peter also. This was during the days of unleavened bread.
051204 When he had arrested him, he put him in prison, and delivered him to four squads of four soldiers each to guard him, intending to bring him out to the people after the Passover.
051205 Peter therefore was kept in the prison, but constant prayer was made by the assembly to God for him.
051206 The same night when Herod was about to bring him out, Peter was sleeping between two soldiers, bound with two chains. Guards in front of the door kept the prison.
051207 And behold, an angel of the Lord stood by him, and a light shone in the cell. He struck Peter on the side, and woke him up, saying, "Stand up quickly!" His chains fell off from his hands.
051208 The angel said to him, "Get dressed and put on your sandals." He did so. He said to him, "Put on your cloak, and follow me."
051209 And he went out and followed him. He didn't know that what was being done by the angel was real, but thought he saw a vision.
051210 When they were past the first and the second guard, they came to the iron gate that leads into the city, which opened to them by itself. They went out, and went down one street, and immediately the angel departed from him.
051211 When Peter had come to himself, he said, "Now I truly know that the Lord has sent out his angel and delivered me out of the hand of Herod, and from everything the Jewish people were expecting."
051212 Thinking about that, he came to the house of Mary, the mother of John whose surname was Mark, where many were gathered together and were praying.
051213 When Peter knocked at the door of the gate, a maid named Rhoda came to answer.
051214 When she recognized Peter's voice, she didn't open the gate for joy, but ran in, and reported that Peter was standing in front of the gate.
051215 They said to her, "You are crazy!" But she insisted that it was so. They said, "It is his angel."
051216 But Peter continued knocking. When they had opened, they saw him, and were amazed.
051217 But he, beckoning to them with his hand to be silent, declared to them how the Lord had brought him out of the prison. He said, "Tell these things to James, and to the brothers." Then he departed, and went to another place.
051218 Now as soon as it was day, there was no small stir among the soldiers about what had become of Peter.
051219 When Herod had sought for him, and didn't find him, he examined the guards, and commanded that they should be put to death. He went down from Judea to Caesarea, and stayed there.
051220 Now Herod was very angry with the people of Tyre and Sidon. They came with one accord to him, and, having made Blastus, the king's personal aide, their friend, they asked for peace, because their country depended on the king's country for food.
051221 On an appointed day, Herod dressed himself in royal clothing, sat on the throne, and gave a speech to them.
051222 The people shouted, "The voice of a god, and not of a man!"
051223 Immediately an angel of the Lord struck him, because he didn't give God the glory, and he was eaten by worms and died.
051224 But the word of God grew and multiplied.
051225 Barnabas and Saul returned to Jerusalem, when they had fulfilled their service, also taking with them John whose surname was Mark.
051301 Now in the assembly that was at Antioch there were some prophets and teachers: Barnabas, Simeon who was called Niger, Lucius of Cyrene, Manaen the foster brother of Herod the tetrarch, and Saul.
051302 As they served the Lord and fasted, the Holy Spirit said, "Separate Barnabas and Saul for me, for the work to which I have called them."
051303 Then, when they had fasted and prayed and laid their hands on them, they sent them away.
051304 So, being sent out by the Holy Spirit, they went down to Seleucia. From there they sailed to Cyprus.
051305 When they were at Salamis, they proclaimed the word of God in the Jewish synagogues. They had also John as their attendant.
051306 When they had gone through the island to Paphos, they found a certain sorcerer, a false prophet, a Jew, whose name was Bar Jesus,
051307 who was with the proconsul, Sergius Paulus, a man of understanding. This man summoned Barnabas and Saul, and sought to hear the word of God.
051308 But Elymas the sorcerer (for so is his name by interpretation) withstood them, seeking to turn aside the proconsul from the faith.
051309 But Saul, who is also called Paul, filled with the Holy Spirit, fastened his eyes on him,
051310 and said, "Full of all deceit and all cunning, you son of the devil, you enemy of all righteousness, will you not cease to pervert the right ways of the Lord?
051311 Now, behold, the hand of the Lord is on you, and you will be blind, not seeing the sun for a season!" Immediately a mist and darkness fell on him. He went around seeking someone to lead him by the hand.
051312 Then the proconsul, when he saw what was done, believed, being astonished at the teaching of the Lord.
051313 Now Paul and his company set sail from Paphos, and came to Perga in Pamphylia. John departed from them and returned to Jerusalem.
051314 But they, passing on from Perga, came to Antioch of Pisidia. They went into the synagogue on the Sabbath day, and sat down.
051315 After the reading of the law and the prophets, the rulers of the synagogue sent to them, saying, "Brothers, if you have any word of exhortation for the people, speak."
051316 Paul stood up, and beckoning with his hand said, "Men of Israel, and you who fear God, listen.
051317 The God of this people chose our fathers, and exalted the people when they stayed as aliens in the land of Egypt, and with an uplifted arm, he led them out of it.
051318 For a period of about forty years he put up with them in the wilderness.
051319 When he had destroyed seven nations in the land of Canaan, he gave them their land for an inheritance, for about four hundred fifty years.
051320 After these things he gave them judges until Samuel the prophet.
051321 Afterward they asked for a king, and God gave to them Saul the son of Kish, a man of the tribe of Benjamin, for forty years.
051322 When he had removed him, he raised up David to be their king, to whom he also testified, 'I have found David the son of Jesse, a man after my heart, who will do all my will.'
051323 From this man's seed, God has brought salvation to Israel according to his promise,
051324 before his coming, when John had first preached the baptism of repentance to Israel.
051325 As John was fulfilling his course, he said, 'What do you suppose that I am? I am not he. But behold, one comes after me the sandals of whose feet I am not worthy to untie.'
051326 Brothers, children of the stock of Abraham, and those among you who fear God, the word of this salvation is sent out to you.
051327 For those who dwell in Jerusalem, and their rulers, because they didn't know him, nor the voices of the prophets which are read every Sabbath, fulfilled them by condemning him.
051328 Though they found no cause for death, they still asked Pilate to have him killed.
051329 When they had fulfilled all things that were written about him, they took him down from the tree, and laid him in a tomb.
051330 But God raised him from the dead,
051331 and he was seen for many days by those who came up with him from Galilee to Jerusalem, who are his witnesses to the people.
051332 We bring you good news of the promise made to the fathers,
051333 that God has fulfilled the same to us, their children, in that he raised up Jesus. As it is also written in the second psalm, 'You are my Son. Today I have become your father.'
051334 "Concerning that he raised him up from the dead, now no more to return to corruption, he has spoken thus: 'I will give you the holy and sure blessings of David.'
051335 Therefore he says also in another psalm, 'You will not allow your Holy One to see decay.'
051336 For David, after he had in his own generation served the counsel of God, fell asleep, and was laid with his fathers, and saw decay.
051337 But he whom God raised up saw no decay.
051338 Be it known to you therefore, brothers, that through this man is proclaimed to you remission of sins,
051339 and by him everyone who believes is justified from all things, from which you could not be justified by the law of Moses.
051340 Beware therefore, lest that come on you which is spoken in the prophets:
051341 'Behold, you scoffers, and wonder, and perish; for I work a work in your days, a work which you will in no way believe, if one declares it to you.'"
051342 So when the Jews went out of the synagogue, the Gentiles begged that these words might be preached to them the next Sabbath.
051343 Now when the synagogue broke up, many of the Jews and of the devout proselytes followed Paul and Barnabas; who, speaking to them, urged them to continue in the grace of God.
051344 The next Sabbath almost the whole city was gathered together to hear the word of God.
051345 But when the Jews saw the multitudes, they were filled with jealousy, and contradicted the things which were spoken by Paul, and blasphemed.
051346 Paul and Barnabas spoke out boldly, and said, "It was necessary that God's word should be spoken to you first. Since indeed you thrust it from you, and judge yourselves unworthy of eternal life, behold, we turn to the Gentiles.
051347 For so has the Lord commanded us, saying, 'I have set you as a light for the Gentiles, that you should bring salvation to the uttermost parts of the earth.'"
051348 As the Gentiles heard this, they were glad, and glorified the word of God. As many as were appointed to eternal life believed.
051349 The Lord's word was spread abroad throughout all the region.
051350 But the Jews stirred up the devout and prominent women and the chief men of the city, and stirred up a persecution against Paul and Barnabas, and threw them out of their borders.
051351 But they shook off the dust of their feet against them, and came to Iconium.
051352 The disciples were filled with joy with the Holy Spirit.
051401 It happened in Iconium that they entered together into the synagogue of the Jews, and so spoke that a great multitude both of Jews and of Greeks believed.
051402 But the disbelieving Jews stirred up and embittered the souls of the Gentiles against the brothers.
051403 Therefore they stayed there a long time, speaking boldly in the Lord, who testified to the word of his grace, granting signs and wonders to be done by their hands.
051404 But the multitude of the city was divided. Part sided with the Jews, and part with the apostles.
051405 When some of both the Gentiles and the Jews, with their rulers, made a violent attempt to mistreat and stone them,
051406 they became aware of it, and fled to the cities of Lycaonia, Lystra, Derbe, and the surrounding region.
051407 There they preached the Good News.
051408 At Lystra a certain man sat, impotent in his feet, a cripple from his mother's womb, who never had walked.
051409 He was listening to Paul speaking, who, fastening eyes on him, and seeing that he had faith to be made whole,
051410 said with a loud voice, "Stand upright on your feet!" He leaped up and walked.
051411 When the multitude saw what Paul had done, they lifted up their voice, saying in the language of Lycaonia, "The gods have come down to us in the likeness of men!"
051412 They called Barnabas "Jupiter," and Paul "Mercury," because he was the chief speaker.
051413 The priest of Jupiter, whose temple was in front of their city, brought oxen and garlands to the gates, and would have made a sacrifice along with the multitudes.
051414 But when the apostles, Barnabas and Paul, heard of it, they tore their clothes, and sprang into the multitude, crying out,
051415 "Men, why are you doing these things? We also are men of like passions with you, and bring you good news, that you should turn from these vain things to the living God, who made the sky and the earth and the sea, and all that is in them;
051416 who in the generations gone by allowed all the nations to walk in their own ways.
051417 Yet he didn't leave himself without witness, in that he did good and gave you rains from the sky and fruitful seasons, filling our hearts with food and gladness."
051418 Even saying these things, they hardly stopped the multitudes from making a sacrifice to them.
051419 But some Jews from Antioch and Iconium came there, and having persuaded the multitudes, they stoned Paul, and dragged him out of the city, supposing that he was dead.
051420 But as the disciples stood around him, he rose up, and entered into the city. On the next day he went out with Barnabas to Derbe.
051421 When they had preached the Good News to that city, and had made many disciples, they returned to Lystra, Iconium, and Antioch,
051422 confirming the souls of the disciples, exhorting them to continue in the faith, and that through many afflictions we must enter into the Kingdom of God.
051423 When they had appointed elders for them in every assembly, and had prayed with fasting, they commended them to the Lord, on whom they had believed.
051424 They passed through Pisidia, and came to Pamphylia.
051425 When they had spoken the word in Perga, they went down to Attalia.
051426 From there they sailed to Antioch, from where they had been committed to the grace of God for the work which they had fulfilled.
051427 When they had arrived, and had gathered the assembly together, they reported all the things that God had done with them, and that he had opened a door of faith to the nations.
051428 They stayed there with the disciples for a long time.
051501 Some men came down from Judea and taught the brothers, "Unless you are circumcised after the custom of Moses, you can't be saved."
051502 Therefore when Paul and Barnabas had no small discord and discussion with them, they appointed Paul and Barnabas, and some others of them, to go up to Jerusalem to the apostles and elders about this question.
051503 They, being sent on their way by the assembly, passed through both Phoenicia and Samaria, declaring the conversion of the Gentiles. They caused great joy to all the brothers.
051504 When they had come to Jerusalem, they were received by the assembly and the apostles and the elders, and they reported all things that God had done with them.
051505 But some of the sect of the Pharisees who believed rose up, saying, "It is necessary to circumcise them, and to command them to keep the law of Moses."
051506 The apostles and the elders were gathered together to see about this matter.
051507 When there had been much discussion, Peter rose up and said to them, "Brothers, you know that a good while ago God made a choice among you, that by my mouth the nations should hear the word of the Good News, and believe.
051508 God, who knows the heart, testified about them, giving them the Holy Spirit, just like he did to us.
051509 He made no distinction between us and them, cleansing their hearts by faith.
051510 Now therefore why do you tempt God, that you should put a yoke on the neck of the disciples which neither our fathers nor we were able to bear?
051511 But we believe that we are saved through the grace of the Lord Jesus, just as they are."
051512 All the multitude kept silence, and they listened to Barnabas and Paul reporting what signs and wonders God had done among the nations through them.
051513 After they were silent, James answered, "Brothers, listen to me.
051514 Simeon has reported how God first visited the nations, to take out of them a people for his name.
051515 This agrees with the words of the prophets. As it is written,
051516 'After these things I will return. I will again build the tabernacle of David, which has fallen. I will again build its ruins. I will set it up,
051517 That the rest of men may seek after the Lord; All the Gentiles who are called by my name, Says the Lord, who does all these things.
051518 All his works are known to God from eternity.'
051519 "Therefore my judgment is that we don't trouble those from among the Gentiles who turn to God,
051520 but that we write to them that they abstain from the pollution of idols, from sexual immorality, from what is strangled, and from blood.
051521 For Moses from generations of old has in every city those who preach him, being read in the synagogues every Sabbath."
051522 Then it seemed good to the apostles and the elders, with the whole assembly, to choose men out of their company, and send them to Antioch with Paul and Barnabas: Judas called Barsabbas, and Silas, chief men among the brothers.
051523 They wrote these things by their hand: "The apostles, the elders, and the brothers, to the brothers who are of the Gentiles in Antioch, Syria, and Cilicia: greetings.
051524 Because we have heard that some who went out from us have troubled you with words, unsettling your souls, saying, 'You must be circumcised and keep the law,' to whom we gave no commandment;
051525 it seemed good to us, having come to one accord, to choose out men and send them to you with our beloved Barnabas and Paul,
051526 men who have risked their lives for the name of our Lord Jesus Christ.
051527 We have sent therefore Judas and Silas, who themselves will also tell you the same things by word of mouth.
051528 For it seemed good to the Holy Spirit, and to us, to lay no greater burden on you than these necessary things:
051529 that you abstain from things sacrificed to idols, from blood, from things strangled, and from sexual immorality, from which if you keep yourselves, it will be well with you. Farewell."
051530 So, when they were sent off, they came to Antioch. Having gathered the multitude together, they delivered the letter.
051531 When they had read it, they rejoiced over the encouragement.
051532 Judas and Silas, also being prophets themselves, encouraged the brothers with many words, and strengthened them.
051533 After they had spent some time there, they were sent back with greetings from the brothers to the apostles.
051534 
051535 But Paul and Barnabas stayed in Antioch, teaching and preaching the word of the Lord, with many others also.
051536 After some days Paul said to Barnabas, "Let's return now and visit our brothers in every city in which we proclaimed the word of the Lord, to see how they are doing."
051537 Barnabas planned to take John, who was called Mark, with them also.
051538 But Paul didn't think that it was a good idea to take with them someone who had withdrawn from them in Pamphylia, and didn't go with them to do the work.
051539 Then the contention grew so sharp that they separated from each other. Barnabas took Mark with him, and sailed away to Cyprus,
051540 but Paul chose Silas, and went out, being commended by the brothers to the grace of God.
051541 He went through Syria and Cilicia, strengthening the assemblies.
051601 He came to Derbe and Lystra: and behold, a certain disciple was there, named Timothy, the son of a Jewess who believed; but his father was a Greek.
051602 The brothers who were at Lystra and Iconium gave a good testimony about him.
051603 Paul wanted to have him go out with him, and he took and circumcised him because of the Jews who were in those parts; for they all knew that his father was a Greek.
051604 As they went on their way through the cities, they delivered the decrees to them to keep which had been ordained by the apostles and elders who were at Jerusalem.
051605 So the assemblies were strengthened in the faith, and increased in number daily.
051606 When they had gone through the region of Phrygia and Galatia, they were forbidden by the Holy Spirit to speak the word in Asia.
051607 When they had come opposite Mysia, they tried to go into Bithynia, but the Spirit didn't allow them.
051608 Passing by Mysia, they came down to Troas.
051609 A vision appeared to Paul in the night. There was a man of Macedonia standing, begging him, and saying, "Come over into Macedonia and help us."
051610 When he had seen the vision, immediately we sought to go out to Macedonia, concluding that the Lord had called us to preach the Good News to them.
051611 Setting sail therefore from Troas, we made a straight course to Samothrace, and the day following to Neapolis;
051612 and from there to Philippi, which is a city of Macedonia, the foremost of the district, a Roman colony. We were staying some days in this city.
051613 On the Sabbath day we went forth outside of the city by a riverside, where we supposed there was a place of prayer, and we sat down, and spoke to the women who had come together.
051614 A certain woman named Lydia, a seller of purple, of the city of Thyatira, one who worshiped God, heard us; whose heart the Lord opened to listen to the things which were spoken by Paul.
051615 When she and her household were baptized, she begged us, saying, "If you have judged me to be faithful to the Lord, come into my house, and stay." So she persuaded us.
051616 It happened, as we were going to prayer, that a certain girl having a spirit of divination met us, who brought her masters much gain by fortune telling.
051617 Following Paul and us, she cried out, "These men are servants of the Most High God, who proclaim to us a way of salvation!"
051618 She was doing this for many days. But Paul, becoming greatly annoyed, turned and said to the spirit, "I command you in the name of Jesus Christ to come out of her!" It came out that very hour.
051619 But when her masters saw that the hope of their gain was gone, they seized Paul and Silas, and dragged them into the marketplace before the rulers.
051620 When they had brought them to the magistrates, they said, "These men, being Jews, are agitating our city,
051621 and set forth customs which it is not lawful for us to accept or to observe, being Romans."
051622 The multitude rose up together against them, and the magistrates tore their clothes off of them, and commanded them to be beaten with rods.
051623 When they had laid many stripes on them, they threw them into prison, charging the jailer to keep them safely,
051624 who, having received such a command, threw them into the inner prison, and secured their feet in the stocks.
051625 But about midnight Paul and Silas were praying and singing hymns to God, and the prisoners were listening to them.
051626 Suddenly there was a great earthquake, so that the foundations of the prison were shaken; and immediately all the doors were opened, and everyone's bonds were loosened.
051627 The jailer, being roused out of sleep and seeing the prison doors open, drew his sword and was about to kill himself, supposing that the prisoners had escaped.
051628 But Paul cried with a loud voice, saying, "Don't harm yourself, for we are all here!"
051629 He called for lights and sprang in, and, fell down trembling before Paul and Silas,
051630 and brought them out and said, "Sirs, what must I do to be saved?"
051631 They said, "Believe in the Lord Jesus Christ, and you will be saved, you and your household."
051632 They spoke the word of the Lord to him, and to all who were in his house.
051633 He took them the same hour of the night, and washed their stripes, and was immediately baptized, he and all his household.
051634 He brought them up into his house, and set food before them, and rejoiced greatly, with all his household, having believed in God.
051635 But when it was day, the magistrates sent the sergeants, saying, "Let those men go."
051636 The jailer reported these words to Paul, saying, "The magistrates have sent to let you go; now therefore come out, and go in peace."
051637 But Paul said to them, "They have beaten us publicly, without a trial, men who are Romans, and have cast us into prison! Do they now release us secretly? No, most certainly, but let them come themselves and bring us out!"
051638 The sergeants reported these words to the magistrates, and they were afraid when they heard that they were Romans,
051639 and they came and begged them. When they had brought them out, they asked them to depart from the city.
051640 They went out of the prison, and entered into Lydia's house. When they had seen the brothers, they encouraged them, and departed.
051701 Now when they had passed through Amphipolis and Apollonia, they came to Thessalonica, where there was a Jewish synagogue.
051702 Paul, as was his custom, went in to them, and for three Sabbath days reasoned with them from the Scriptures,
051703 explaining and demonstrating that the Christ had to suffer and rise again from the dead, and saying, "This Jesus, whom I proclaim to you, is the Christ."
051704 Some of them were persuaded, and joined Paul and Silas, of the devout Greeks a great multitude, and not a few of the chief women.
051705 But the unpersuaded Jews took along some wicked men from the marketplace, and gathering a crowd, set the city in an uproar. Assaulting the house of Jason, they sought to bring them out to the people.
051706 When they didn't find them, they dragged Jason and certain brothers before the rulers of the city, crying, "These who have turned the world upside down have come here also,
051707 whom Jason has received. These all act contrary to the decrees of Caesar, saying that there is another king, Jesus!"
051708 The multitude and the rulers of the city were troubled when they heard these things.
051709 When they had taken security from Jason and the rest, they let them go.
051710 The brothers immediately sent Paul and Silas away by night to Beroea. When they arrived, they went into the Jewish synagogue.
051711 Now these were more noble than those in Thessalonica, in that they received the word with all readiness of the mind, examining the Scriptures daily to see whether these things were so.
051712 Many of them therefore believed; also of the prominent Greek women, and not a few men.
051713 But when the Jews of Thessalonica had knowledge that the word of God was proclaimed by Paul at Beroea also, they came there likewise, agitating the multitudes.
051714 Then the brothers immediately sent out Paul to go as far as to the sea, and Silas and Timothy still stayed there.
051715 But those who escorted Paul brought him as far as Athens. Receiving a commandment to Silas and Timothy that they should come to him very quickly, they departed.
051716 Now while Paul waited for them at Athens, his spirit was provoked within him as he saw the city full of idols.
051717 So he reasoned in the synagogue with the Jews and the devout persons, and in the marketplace every day with those who met him.
051718 Some of the Epicurean and Stoic philosophers also were conversing with him. Some said, "What does this babbler want to say?" Others said, "He seems to be advocating foreign deities," because he preached Jesus and the resurrection.
051719 They took hold of him, and brought him to the Areopagus, saying, "May we know what this new teaching is, which is spoken by you?
051720 For you bring certain strange things to our ears. We want to know therefore what these things mean."
051721 Now all the Athenians and the strangers living there spent their time in nothing else, but either to tell or to hear some new thing.
051722 Paul stood in the middle of the Areopagus, and said, "You men of Athens, I perceive that you are very religious in all things.
051723 For as I passed along, and observed the objects of your worship, I found also an altar with this inscription: 'TO AN UNKNOWN GOD.' What therefore you worship in ignorance, this I announce to you.
051724 The God who made the world and all things in it, he, being Lord of heaven and earth, doesn't dwell in temples made with hands,
051725 neither is he served by men's hands, as though he needed anything, seeing he himself gives to all life and breath, and all things.
051726 He made from one blood every nation of men to dwell on all the surface of the earth, having determined appointed seasons, and the boundaries of their dwellings,
051727 that they should seek the Lord, if perhaps they might reach out for him and find him, though he is not far from each one of us.
051728 'For in him we live, and move, and have our being.' As some of your own poets have said, 'For we are also his offspring.'
051729 Being then the offspring of God, we ought not to think that the Divine Nature is like gold, or silver, or stone, engraved by art and design of man.
051730 The times of ignorance therefore God overlooked. But now he commands that all people everywhere should repent,
051731 because he has appointed a day in which he will judge the world in righteousness by the man whom he has ordained; of which he has given assurance to all men, in that he has raised him from the dead."
051732 Now when they heard of the resurrection of the dead, some mocked; but others said, "We want to hear you again concerning this."
051733 Thus Paul went out from among them.
051734 But certain men joined with him, and believed, among whom also was Dionysius the Areopagite, and a woman named Damaris, and others with them.
051801 After these things Paul departed from Athens, and came to Corinth.
051802 He found a certain Jew named Aquila, a man of Pontus by race, who had recently come from Italy, with his wife Priscilla, because Claudius had commanded all the Jews to depart from Rome. He came to them,
051803 and because he practiced the same trade, he lived with them and worked, for by trade they were tent makers.
051804 He reasoned in the synagogue every Sabbath, and persuaded Jews and Greeks.
051805 But when Silas and Timothy came down from Macedonia, Paul was compelled by the Spirit, testifying to the Jews that Jesus was the Christ.
051806 When they opposed him and blasphemed, he shook out his clothing and said to them, "Your blood be on your own heads! I am clean. From now on, I will go to the Gentiles!"
051807 He departed there, and went into the house of a certain man named Justus, one who worshiped God, whose house was next door to the synagogue.
051808 Crispus, the ruler of the synagogue, believed in the Lord with all his house. Many of the Corinthians, when they heard, believed and were baptized.
051809 The Lord said to Paul in the night by a vision, "Don't be afraid, but speak and don't be silent;
051810 for I am with you, and no one will attack you to harm you, for I have many people in this city."
051811 He lived there a year and six months, teaching the word of God among them.
051812 But when Gallio was proconsul of Achaia, the Jews with one accord rose up against Paul and brought him before the judgment seat,
051813 saying, "This man persuades men to worship God contrary to the law."
051814 But when Paul was about to open his mouth, Gallio said to the Jews, "If indeed it were a matter of wrong or of wicked crime, you Jews, it would be reasonable that I should bear with you;
051815 but if they are questions about words and names and your own law, look to it yourselves. For I don't want to be a judge of these matters."
051816 He drove them from the judgment seat.
051817 Then all the Greeks laid hold on Sosthenes, the ruler of the synagogue, and beat him before the judgment seat. Gallio didn't care about any of these things.
051818 Paul, having stayed after this many more days, took his leave of the brothers, and sailed from there for Syria, together with Priscilla and Aquila. He shaved his head in Cenchreae, for he had a vow.
051819 He came to Ephesus, and he left them there; but he himself entered into the synagogue, and reasoned with the Jews.
051820 When they asked him to stay with them a longer time, he declined;
051821 but taking his leave of them, and saying, "I must by all means keep this coming feast in Jerusalem, but I will return again to you if God wills," he set sail from Ephesus.
051822 When he had landed at Caesarea, he went up and greeted the assembly, and went down to Antioch.
051823 Having spent some time there, he departed, and went through the region of Galatia, and Phrygia, in order, establishing all the disciples.
051824 Now a certain Jew named Apollos, an Alexandrian by race, an eloquent man, came to Ephesus. He was mighty in the Scriptures.
051825 This man had been instructed in the way of the Lord; and being fervent in spirit, he spoke and taught accurately the things concerning Jesus, although he knew only the baptism of John.
051826 He began to speak boldly in the synagogue. But when Priscilla and Aquila heard him, they took him aside, and explained to him the way of God more accurately.
051827 When he had determined to pass over into Achaia, the brothers encouraged him, and wrote to the disciples to receive him. When he had come, he greatly helped those who had believed through grace;
051828 for he powerfully refuted the Jews, publicly showing by the Scriptures that Jesus was the Christ.
051901 It happened that, while Apollos was at Corinth, Paul, having passed through the upper country, came to Ephesus, and found certain disciples.
051902 He said to them, "Did you receive the Holy Spirit when you believed?" They said to him, "No, we haven't even heard that there is a Holy Spirit."
051903 He said, "Into what then were you baptized?" They said, "Into John's baptism."
051904 Paul said, "John indeed baptized with the baptism of repentance, saying to the people that they should believe in the one who would come after him, that is, in Jesus."
051905 When they heard this, they were baptized in the name of the Lord Jesus.
051906 When Paul had laid his hands on them, the Holy Spirit came on them, and they spoke with other languages and prophesied.
051907 They were about twelve men in all.
051908 He entered into the synagogue, and spoke boldly for a period of three months, reasoning and persuading about the things concerning the Kingdom of God.
051909 But when some were hardened and disobedient, speaking evil of the Way before the multitude, he departed from them, and separated the disciples, reasoning daily in the school of Tyrannus.
051910 This continued for two years, so that all those who lived in Asia heard the word of the Lord Jesus, both Jews and Greeks.
051911 God worked special miracles by the hands of Paul,
051912 so that even handkerchiefs or aprons were carried away from his body to the sick, and the evil spirits went out.
051913 But some of the itinerant Jews, exorcists, took on themselves to invoke over those who had the evil spirits the name of the Lord Jesus, saying, "We adjure you by Jesus whom Paul preaches."
051914 There were seven sons of one Sceva, a Jewish chief priest, who did this.
051915 The evil spirit answered, "Jesus I know, and Paul I know, but who are you?"
051916 The man in whom the evil spirit was leaped on them, and overpowered them, and prevailed against them, so that they fled out of that house naked and wounded.
051917 This became known to all, both Jews and Greeks, who lived at Ephesus. Fear fell on them all, and the name of the Lord Jesus was magnified.
051918 Many also of those who had believed came, confessing, and declaring their deeds.
051919 Many of those who practiced magical arts brought their books together and burned them in the sight of all. They counted the price of them, and found it to be fifty thousand pieces of silver.
051920 So the word of the Lord was growing and becoming mighty.
051921 Now after these things had ended, Paul determined in the spirit, when he had passed through Macedonia and Achaia, to go to Jerusalem, saying, "After I have been there, I must also see Rome."
051922 Having sent into Macedonia two of those who served him, Timothy and Erastus, he himself stayed in Asia for a while.
051923 About that time there arose no small stir concerning the Way.
051924 For a certain man named Demetrius, a silversmith, who made silver shrines of Artemis, brought no little business to the craftsmen,
051925 whom he gathered together, with the workmen of like occupation, and said, "Sirs, you know that by this business we have our wealth.
051926 You see and hear, that not at Ephesus alone, but almost throughout all Asia, this Paul has persuaded and turned away many people, saying that they are no gods, that are made with hands.
051927 Not only is there danger that this our trade come into disrepute, but also that the temple of the great goddess Artemis will be counted as nothing, and her majesty destroyed, whom all Asia and the world worships."
051928 When they heard this they were filled with anger, and cried out, saying, "Great is Artemis of the Ephesians!"
051929 The whole city was filled with confusion, and they rushed with one accord into the theater, having seized Gaius and Aristarchus, men of Macedonia, Paul's companions in travel.
051930 When Paul wanted to enter in to the people, the disciples didn't allow him.
051931 Certain also of the Asiarchs, being his friends, sent to him and begged him not to venture into the theater.
051932 Some therefore cried one thing, and some another, for the assembly was in confusion. Most of them didn't know why they had come together.
051933 They brought Alexander out of the multitude, the Jews putting him forward. Alexander beckoned with his hand, and would have made a defense to the people.
051934 But when they perceived that he was a Jew, all with one voice for a time of about two hours cried out, "Great is Artemis of the Ephesians!"
051935 When the town clerk had quieted the multitude, he said, "You men of Ephesus, what man is there who doesn't know that the city of the Ephesians is temple keeper of the great goddess Artemis, and of the image which fell down from Zeus?
051936 Seeing then that these things can't be denied, you ought to be quiet, and to do nothing rash.
051937 For you have brought these men here, who are neither robbers of temples nor blasphemers of your goddess.
051938 If therefore Demetrius and the craftsmen who are with him have a matter against anyone, the courts are open, and there are proconsuls. Let them press charges against one another.
051939 But if you seek anything about other matters, it will be settled in the regular assembly.
051940 For indeed we are in danger of being accused concerning this day's riot, there being no cause. Concerning it, we wouldn't be able to give an account of this commotion."
051941 When he had thus spoken, he dismissed the assembly.
052001 After the uproar had ceased, Paul sent for the disciples, took leave of them, and departed to go into Macedonia.
052002 When he had gone through those parts, and had encouraged them with many words, he came into Greece.
052003 When he had spent three months there, and a plot was made against him by Jews as he was about to set sail for Syria, he determined to return through Macedonia.
052004 These accompanied him as far as Asia: Sopater of Beroea; Aristarchus and Secundus of the Thessalonians; Gaius of Derbe; Timothy; and Tychicus and Trophimus of Asia.
052005 But these had gone ahead, and were waiting for us at Troas.
052006 We sailed away from Philippi after the days of Unleavened Bread, and came to them at Troas in five days, where we stayed seven days.
052007 On the first day of the week, when the disciples were gathered together to break bread, Paul talked with them, intending to depart on the next day, and continued his speech until midnight.
052008 There were many lights in the upper chamber where we were gathered together.
052009 A certain young man named Eutychus sat in the window, weighed down with deep sleep. As Paul spoke still longer, being weighed down by his sleep, he fell down from the third story, and was taken up dead.
052010 Paul went down, and fell upon him, and embracing him said, "Don't be troubled, for his life is in him."
052011 When he had gone up, and had broken bread, and eaten, and had talked with them a long while, even until break of day, he departed.
052012 They brought the boy in alive, and were greatly comforted.
052013 But we who went ahead to the ship set sail for Assos, intending to take Paul aboard there, for he had so arranged, intending himself to go by land.
052014 When he met us at Assos, we took him aboard, and came to Mitylene.
052015 Sailing from there, we came the following day opposite Chios. The next day we touched at Samos and stayed at Trogyllium, and the day after we came to Miletus.
052016 For Paul had determined to sail past Ephesus, that he might not have to spend time in Asia; for he was hastening, if it were possible for him, to be in Jerusalem on the day of Pentecost.
052017 From Miletus he sent to Ephesus, and called to himself the elders of the assembly.
052018 When they had come to him, he said to them, "You yourselves know, from the first day that I set foot in Asia, how I was with you all the time,
052019 serving the Lord with all humility, with many tears, and with trials which happened to me by the plots of the Jews;
052020 how I didn't shrink from declaring to you anything that was profitable, teaching you publicly and from house to house,
052021 testifying both to Jews and to Greeks repentance toward God, and faith toward our Lord Jesus.
052022 Now, behold, I go bound by the Spirit to Jerusalem, not knowing what will happen to me there;
052023 except that the Holy Spirit testifies in every city, saying that bonds and afflictions wait for me.
052024 But these things don't count; nor do I hold my life dear to myself, so that I may finish my race with joy, and the ministry which I received from the Lord Jesus, to fully testify to the Good News of the grace of God.
052025 "Now, behold, I know that you all, among whom I went about preaching the Kingdom of God, will see my face no more.
052026 Therefore I testify to you this day that I am clean from the blood of all men,
052027 for I didn't shrink from declaring to you the whole counsel of God.
052028 Take heed, therefore, to yourselves, and to all the flock, in which the Holy Spirit has made you overseers, to shepherd the assembly of the Lord and God which he purchased with his own blood.
052029 For I know that after my departure, vicious wolves will enter in among you, not sparing the flock.
052030 Men will arise from among your own selves, speaking perverse things, to draw away the disciples after them.
052031 Therefore watch, remembering that for a period of three years I didn't cease to admonish everyone night and day with tears.
052032 Now, brothers, I entrust you to God, and to the word of his grace, which is able to build up, and to give you the inheritance among all those who are sanctified.
052033 I coveted no one's silver, or gold, or clothing.
052034 You yourselves know that these hands served my necessities, and those who were with me.
052035 In all things I gave you an example, that so laboring you ought to help the weak, and to remember the words of the Lord Jesus, that he himself said, 'It is more blessed to give than to receive.'"
052036 When he had spoken these things, he knelt down and prayed with them all.
052037 They all wept a lot, and fell on Paul's neck and kissed him,
052038 sorrowing most of all because of the word which he had spoken, that they should see his face no more. And they accompanied him to the ship.
052101 When it happened that we had parted from them and had set sail, we came with a straight course to Cos, and the next day to Rhodes, and from there to Patara.
052102 Having found a ship crossing over to Phoenicia, we went aboard, and set sail.
052103 When we had come in sight of Cyprus, leaving it on the left hand, we sailed to Syria, and landed at Tyre, for there the ship was to unload her cargo.
052104 Having found disciples, we stayed there seven days. These said to Paul through the Spirit, that he should not go up to Jerusalem.
052105 When it happened that we had accomplished the days, we departed and went on our journey. They all, with wives and children, brought us on our way until we were out of the city. Kneeling down on the beach, we prayed.
052106 After saying goodbye to each other, we went on board the ship, and they returned home again.
052107 When we had finished the voyage from Tyre, we arrived at Ptolemais. We greeted the brothers, and stayed with them one day.
052108 On the next day, we, who were Paul's companions, departed, and came to Caesarea. We entered into the house of Philip the evangelist, who was one of the seven, and stayed with him.
052109 Now this man had four virgin daughters who prophesied.
052110 As we stayed there some days, a certain prophet named Agabus came down from Judea.
052111 Coming to us, and taking Paul's belt, he bound his own feet and hands, and said, "Thus says the Holy Spirit: 'So will the Jews at Jerusalem bind the man who owns this belt, and will deliver him into the hands of the Gentiles.'"
052112 When we heard these things, both we and they of that place begged him not to go up to Jerusalem.
052113 Then Paul answered, "What are you doing, weeping and breaking my heart? For I am ready not only to be bound, but also to die at Jerusalem for the name of the Lord Jesus."
052114 When he would not be persuaded, we ceased, saying, "The Lord's will be done."
052115 After these days we took up our baggage and went up to Jerusalem.
052116 Some of the disciples from Caesarea also went with us, bringing one Mnason of Cyprus, an early disciple, with whom we would stay.
052117 When we had come to Jerusalem, the brothers received us gladly.
052118 The day following, Paul went in with us to James; and all the elders were present.
052119 When he had greeted them, he reported one by one the things which God had worked among the Gentiles through his ministry.
052120 They, when they heard it, glorified God. They said to him, "You see, brother, how many thousands there are among the Jews of those who have believed, and they are all zealous for the law.
052121 They have been informed about you, that you teach all the Jews who are among the Gentiles to forsake Moses, telling them not to circumcise their children neither to walk after the customs.
052122 What then? The assembly must certainly meet, for they will hear that you have come.
052123 Therefore do what we tell you. We have four men who have taken a vow.
052124 Take them, and purify yourself with them, and pay their expenses for them, that they may shave their heads. Then all will know that there is no truth in the things that they have been informed about you, but that you yourself also walk keeping the law.
052125 But concerning the Gentiles who believe, we have written our decision that they should observe no such thing, except that they should keep themselves from food offered to idols, from blood, from strangled things, and from sexual immorality."
052126 Then Paul took the men, and the next day, purified himself and went with them into the temple, declaring the fulfillment of the days of purification, until the offering was offered for every one of them.
052127 When the seven days were almost completed, the Jews from Asia, when they saw him in the temple, stirred up all the multitude and laid hands on him,
052128 crying out, "Men of Israel, help! This is the man who teaches all men everywhere against the people, and the law, and this place. Moreover, he also brought Greeks into the temple, and has defiled this holy place!"
052129 For they had seen Trophimus, the Ephesian, with him in the city, and they supposed that Paul had brought him into the temple.
052130 All the city was moved, and the people ran together. They seized Paul and dragged him out of the temple. Immediately the doors were shut.
052131 As they were trying to kill him, news came up to the commanding officer of the regiment that all Jerusalem was in an uproar.
052132 Immediately he took soldiers and centurions, and ran down to them. They, when they saw the chief captain and the soldiers, stopped beating Paul.
052133 Then the commanding officer came near, arrested him, commanded him to be bound with two chains, and inquired who he was and what he had done.
052134 Some shouted one thing, and some another, among the crowd. When he couldn't find out the truth because of the noise, he commanded him to be brought into the barracks.
052135 When he came to the stairs, it happened that he was carried by the soldiers because of the violence of the crowd;
052136 for the multitude of the people followed after, crying out, "Away with him!"
052137 As Paul was about to be brought into the barracks, he asked the commanding officer, "May I speak to you?" He said, "Do you know Greek?
052138 Aren't you then the Egyptian, who before these days stirred up to sedition and led out into the wilderness the four thousand men of the Assassins?"
052139 But Paul said, "I am a Jew, from Tarsus in Cilicia, a citizen of no insignificant city. I beg you, allow me to speak to the people."
052140 When he had given him permission, Paul, standing on the stairs, beckoned with his hand to the people. When there was a great silence, he spoke to them in the Hebrew language, saying,
052201 "Brothers and fathers, listen to the defense which I now make to you."
052202 When they heard that he spoke to them in the Hebrew language, they were even more quiet. He said,
052203 "I am indeed a Jew, born in Tarsus of Cilicia, but brought up in this city at the feet of Gamaliel, instructed according to the strict manner of the law of our fathers, being zealous for God, even as you all are this day.
052204 I persecuted this Way to the death, binding and delivering into prisons both men and women.
052205 As also the high priest and all the council of the elders testify, from whom also I received letters to the brothers, and traveled to Damascus to bring them also who were there to Jerusalem in bonds to be punished.
052206 It happened that, as I made my journey, and came close to Damascus, about noon, suddenly there shone from the sky a great light around me.
052207 I fell to the ground, and heard a voice saying to me, 'Saul, Saul, why are you persecuting me?'
052208 I answered, 'Who are you, Lord?' He said to me, 'I am Jesus of Nazareth, whom you persecute.'
052209 "Those who were with me indeed saw the light and were afraid, but they didn't understand the voice of him who spoke to me.
052210 I said, 'What shall I do, Lord?' The Lord said to me, 'Arise, and go into Damascus. There you will be told about all things which are appointed for you to do.'
052211 When I couldn't see for the glory of that light, being led by the hand of those who were with me, I came into Damascus.
052212 One Ananias, a devout man according to the law, well reported of by all the Jews who lived in Damascus,
052213 came to me, and standing by me said to me, 'Brother Saul, receive your sight!' In that very hour I looked up at him.
052214 He said, 'The God of our fathers has appointed you to know his will, and to see the Righteous One, and to hear a voice from his mouth.
052215 For you will be a witness for him to all men of what you have seen and heard.
052216 Now why do you wait? Arise, be baptized, and wash away your sins, calling on the name of the Lord.'
052217 "It happened that, when I had returned to Jerusalem, and while I prayed in the temple, I fell into a trance,
052218 and saw him saying to me, 'Hurry and get out of Jerusalem quickly, because they will not receive testimony concerning me from you.'
052219 I said, 'Lord, they themselves know that I imprisoned and beat in every synagogue those who believed in you.
052220 When the blood of Stephen, your witness, was shed, I also was standing by, and consenting to his death, and guarding the cloaks of those who killed him.'
052221 "He said to me, 'Depart, for I will send you out far from here to the Gentiles.'"
052222 They listened to him until he said that; then they lifted up their voice, and said, "Rid the earth of this fellow, for he isn't fit to live!"
052223 As they cried out, and threw off their cloaks, and threw dust into the air,
052224 the commanding officer commanded him to be brought into the barracks, ordering him to be examined by scourging, that he might know for what crime they shouted against him like that.
052225 When they had tied him up with thongs, Paul asked the centurion who stood by, "Is it lawful for you to scourge a man who is a Roman, and not found guilty?"
052226 When the centurion heard it, he went to the commanding officer and told him, "Watch what you are about to do, for this man is a Roman!"
052227 The commanding officer came and asked him, "Tell me, are you a Roman?" He said, "Yes."
052228 The commanding officer answered, "I bought my citizenship for a great price." Paul said, "But I was born a Roman."
052229 Immediately those who were about to examine him departed from him, and the commanding officer also was afraid when he realized that he was a Roman, because he had bound him.
052230 But on the next day, desiring to know the truth about why he was accused by the Jews, he freed him from the bonds, and commanded the chief priests and all the council to come together, and brought Paul down and set him before them.
052301 Paul, looking steadfastly at the council, said, "Brothers, I have lived before God in all good conscience until this day."
052302 The high priest, Ananias, commanded those who stood by him to strike him on the mouth.
052303 Then Paul said to him, "God will strike you, you whitewashed wall! Do you sit to judge me according to the law, and command me to be struck contrary to the law?"
052304 Those who stood by said, "Do you malign God's high priest?"
052305 Paul said, "I didn't know, brothers, that he was high priest. For it is written, 'You shall not speak evil of a ruler of your people.'"
052306 But when Paul perceived that the one part were Sadducees and the other Pharisees, he cried out in the council, "Men and brothers, I am a Pharisee, a son of Pharisees. Concerning the hope and resurrection of the dead I am being judged!"
052307 When he had said this, an argument arose between the Pharisees and Sadducees, and the assembly was divided.
052308 For the Sadducees say that there is no resurrection, nor angel, nor spirit; but the Pharisees confess all of these.
052309 A great clamor arose, and some of the scribes of the Pharisees part stood up, and contended, saying, "We find no evil in this man. But if a spirit or angel has spoken to him, let's not fight against God!"
052310 When a great argument arose, the commanding officer, fearing that Paul would be torn in pieces by them, commanded the soldiers to go down and take him by force from among them, and bring him into the barracks.
052311 The following night, the Lord stood by him, and said, "Cheer up, Paul, for as you have testified about me at Jerusalem, so you must testify also at Rome."
052312 When it was day, some of the Jews banded together, and bound themselves under a curse, saying that they would neither eat nor drink until they had killed Paul.
052313 There were more than forty people who had made this conspiracy.
052314 They came to the chief priests and the elders, and said, "We have bound ourselves under a great curse, to taste nothing until we have killed Paul.
052315 Now therefore, you with the council inform the commanding officer that he should bring him down to you tomorrow, as though you were going to judge his case more exactly. We are ready to kill him before he comes near."
052316 But Paul's sister's son heard of their lying in wait, and he came and entered into the barracks and told Paul.
052317 Paul summoned one of the centurions, and said, "Bring this young man to the commanding officer, for he has something to tell him."
052318 So he took him, and brought him to the commanding officer, and said, "Paul, the prisoner, summoned me and asked me to bring this young man to you, who has something to tell you."
052319 The commanding officer took him by the hand, and going aside, asked him privately, "What is it that you have to tell me?"
052320 He said, "The Jews have agreed to ask you to bring Paul down to the council tomorrow, as though intending to inquire somewhat more accurately concerning him.
052321 Therefore don't yield to them, for more than forty men lie in wait for him, who have bound themselves under a curse neither to eat nor to drink until they have killed him. Now they are ready, looking for the promise from you."
052322 So the commanding officer let the young man go, charging him, "Tell no one that you have revealed these things to me."
052323 He called to himself two of the centurions, and said, "Prepare two hundred soldiers to go as far as Caesarea, with seventy horsemen, and two hundred men armed with spears, at the third hour of the night."
052324 He asked them to provide animals, that they might set Paul on one, and bring him safely to Felix the governor.
052325 He wrote a letter like this:
052326 "Claudius Lysias to the most excellent governor Felix: Greetings.
052327 "This man was seized by the Jews, and was about to be killed by them, when I came with the soldiers and rescued him, having learned that he was a Roman.
052328 Desiring to know the cause why they accused him, I brought him down to their council.
052329 I found him to be accused about questions of their law, but not to be charged with anything worthy of death or of imprisonment.
052330 When I was told that the Jews lay in wait for the man, I sent him to you immediately, charging his accusers also to bring their accusations against him before you. Farewell."
052331 So the soldiers, carrying out their orders, took Paul and brought him by night to Antipatris.
052332 But on the next day they left the horsemen to go with him, and returned to the barracks.
