052333 When they came to Caesarea and delivered the letter to the governor, they also presented Paul to him.
052334 When the governor had read it, he asked what province he was from. When he understood that he was from Cilicia, he said,
052335 "I will hear you fully when your accusers also arrive." He commanded that he be kept in Herod's palace.
052401 After five days, the high priest, Ananias, came down with certain elders and an orator, one Tertullus. They informed the governor against Paul.
052402 When he was called, Tertullus began to accuse him, saying, "Seeing that by you we enjoy much peace, and that excellent measures are coming to this nation,
052403 we accept it in all ways and in all places, most excellent Felix, with all thankfulness.
052404 But, that I don't delay you, I entreat you to bear with us and hear a few words.
052405 For we have found this man to be a plague, an instigator of insurrections among all the Jews throughout the world, and a ringleader of the sect of the Nazarenes.
052406 He even tried to profane the temple, and we arrested him.
052407 
052408 By examining him yourself you may ascertain all these things of which we accuse him."
052409 The Jews also joined in the attack, affirming that these things were so.
052410 When the governor had beckoned to him to speak, Paul answered, "Because I know that you have been a judge of this nation for many years, I cheerfully make my defense,
052411 seeing that you can recognize that it is not more than twelve days since I went up to worship at Jerusalem.
052412 In the temple they didn't find me disputing with anyone or stirring up a crowd, either in the synagogues, or in the city.
052413 Nor can they prove to you the things of which they now accuse me.
052414 But this I confess to you, that after the Way, which they call a sect, so I serve the God of our fathers, believing all things which are according to the law, and which are written in the prophets;
052415 having hope toward God, which these also themselves look for, that there will be a resurrection of the dead, both of the just and unjust.
052416 Herein I also practice always having a conscience void of offense toward God and men.
052417 Now after some years, I came to bring gifts for the needy to my nation, and offerings;
052418 amid which certain Jews from Asia found me purified in the temple, not with a mob, nor with turmoil.
052419 They ought to have been here before you, and to make accusation, if they had anything against me.
052420 Or else let these men themselves say what injustice they found in me when I stood before the council,
052421 unless it is for this one thing that I cried standing among them, 'Concerning the resurrection of the dead I am being judged before you today!'"
052422 But Felix, having more exact knowledge concerning the Way, deferred them, saying, "When Lysias, the commanding officer, comes down, I will decide your case."
052423 He ordered the centurion that Paul should be kept in custody, and should have some privileges, and not to forbid any of his friends to serve him or to visit him.
052424 But after some days, Felix came with Drusilla, his wife, who was a Jewess, and sent for Paul, and heard him concerning the faith in Christ Jesus.
052425 As he reasoned about righteousness, self-control, and the judgment to come, Felix was terrified, and answered, "Go your way for this time, and when it is convenient for me, I will summon you."
052426 Meanwhile, he also hoped that money would be given to him by Paul, that he might release him. Therefore also he sent for him more often, and talked with him.
052427 But when two years were fulfilled, Felix was succeeded by Porcius Festus, and desiring to gain favor with the Jews, Felix left Paul in bonds.
052501 Festus therefore, having come into the province, after three days went up to Jerusalem from Caesarea.
052502 Then the high priest and the principal men of the Jews informed him against Paul, and they begged him,
052503 asking a favor against him, that he would summon him to Jerusalem; plotting to kill him on the way.
052504 However Festus answered that Paul should be kept in custody at Caesarea, and that he himself was about to depart shortly.
052505 "Let them therefore," said he, "that are in power among you go down with me, and if there is anything wrong in the man, let them accuse him."
052506 When he had stayed among them more than ten days, he went down to Caesarea, and on the next day he sat on the judgment seat, and commanded Paul to be brought.
052507 When he had come, the Jews who had come down from Jerusalem stood around him, bringing against him many and grievous charges which they could not prove,
052508 while he said in his defense, "Neither against the law of the Jews, nor against the temple, nor against Caesar, have I sinned at all."
052509 But Festus, desiring to gain favor with the Jews, answered Paul and said, "Are you willing to go up to Jerusalem, and be judged by me there concerning these things?"
052510 But Paul said, "I am standing before Caesar's judgment seat, where I ought to be tried. I have done no wrong to the Jews, as you also know very well.
052511 For if I have done wrong, and have committed anything worthy of death, I don't refuse to die; but if none of those things is true that they accuse me of, no one can give me up to them. I appeal to Caesar!"
052512 Then Festus, when he had conferred with the council, answered, "You have appealed to Caesar. To Caesar you shall go."
052513 Now when some days had passed, King Agrippa and Bernice arrived at Caesarea, and greeted Festus.
052514 As he stayed there many days, Festus laid Paul's case before the king, saying, "There is a certain man left a prisoner by Felix;
052515 about whom, when I was at Jerusalem, the chief priests and the elders of the Jews informed me, asking for a sentence against him.
052516 To whom I answered that it is not the custom of the Romans to give up any man to destruction, before the accused has met the accusers face to face, and has had opportunity to make his defense concerning the matter laid against him.
052517 When therefore they had come together here, I didn't delay, but on the next day sat on the judgment seat, and commanded the man to be brought.
052518 Concerning whom, when the accusers stood up, they brought no charge of such things as I supposed;
052519 but had certain questions against him about their own religion, and about one Jesus, who was dead, whom Paul affirmed to be alive.
052520 Being perplexed how to inquire concerning these things, I asked whether he was willing to go to Jerusalem and there be judged concerning these matters.
052521 But when Paul had appealed to be kept for the decision of the emperor, I commanded him to be kept until I could send him to Caesar."
052522 Agrippa said to Festus, "I also would like to hear the man myself." "Tomorrow," he said, "you shall hear him."
052523 So on the next day, when Agrippa and Bernice had come with great pomp, and they had entered into the place of hearing with the commanding officers and principal men of the city, at the command of Festus, Paul was brought in.
052524 Festus said, "King Agrippa, and all men who are here present with us, you see this man, about whom all the multitude of the Jews petitioned me, both at Jerusalem and here, crying that he ought not to live any longer.
052525 But when I found that he had committed nothing worthy of death, and as he himself appealed to the emperor I determined to send him.
052526 Of whom I have no certain thing to write to my lord. Therefore I have brought him forth before you, and especially before you, King Agrippa, that, after examination, I may have something to write.
052527 For it seems to me unreasonable, in sending a prisoner, not to also specify the charges against him."
052601 Agrippa said to Paul, "You may speak for yourself." Then Paul stretched out his hand, and made his defense.
052602 "I think myself happy, King Agrippa, that I am to make my defense before you this day concerning all the things that I am accused by the Jews,
052603 especially because you are expert in all customs and questions which are among the Jews. Therefore I beg you to hear me patiently.
052604 "Indeed, all the Jews know my way of life from my youth up, which was from the beginning among my own nation and at Jerusalem;
052605 having known me from the first, if they are willing to testify, that after the strictest sect of our religion I lived a Pharisee.
052606 Now I stand here to be judged for the hope of the promise made by God to our fathers,
052607 which our twelve tribes, earnestly serving night and day, hope to attain. Concerning this hope I am accused by the Jews, King Agrippa!
052608 Why is it judged incredible with you, if God does raise the dead?
052609 "I myself most certainly thought that I ought to do many things contrary to the name of Jesus of Nazareth.
052610 This I also did in Jerusalem. I both shut up many of the saints in prisons, having received authority from the chief priests, and when they were put to death I gave my vote against them.
052611 Punishing them often in all the synagogues, I tried to make them blaspheme. Being exceedingly enraged against them, I persecuted them even to foreign cities.
052612 "Whereupon as I traveled to Damascus with the authority and commission from the chief priests,
052613 at noon, O king, I saw on the way a light from the sky, brighter than the sun, shining around me and those who traveled with me.
052614 When we had all fallen to the earth, I heard a voice saying to me in the Hebrew language, 'Saul, Saul, why are you persecuting me? It is hard for you to kick against the goads.'
052615 "I said, 'Who are you, Lord?' "He said, 'I am Jesus, whom you are persecuting.
052616 But arise, and stand on your feet, for I have appeared to you for this purpose: to appoint you a servant and a witness both of the things which you have seen, and of the things which I will reveal to you;
052617 delivering you from the people, and from the Gentiles, to whom I send you,
052618 to open their eyes, that they may turn from darkness to light and from the power of Satan to God, that they may receive remission of sins and an inheritance among those who are sanctified by faith in me.'
052619 "Therefore, King Agrippa, I was not disobedient to the heavenly vision,
052620 but declared first to them of Damascus, at Jerusalem, and throughout all the country of Judea, and also to the Gentiles, that they should repent and turn to God, doing works worthy of repentance.
052621 For this reason the Jews seized me in the temple, and tried to kill me.
052622 Having therefore obtained the help that is from God, I stand to this day testifying both to small and great, saying nothing but what the prophets and Moses said would happen,
052623 how the Christ must suffer, and how, by the resurrection of the dead, he would be first to proclaim light both to these people and to the Gentiles."
052624 As he thus made his defense, Festus said with a loud voice, "Paul, you are crazy! Your great learning is driving you insane!"
052625 But he said, "I am not crazy, most excellent Festus, but boldly declare words of truth and reasonableness.
052626 For the king knows of these things, to whom also I speak freely. For I am persuaded that none of these things is hidden from him, for this has not been done in a corner.
052627 King Agrippa, do you believe the prophets? I know that you believe."
052628 Agrippa said to Paul, "With a little persuasion are you trying to make me a Christian?"
052629 Paul said, "I pray to God, that whether with little or with much, not only you, but also all that hear me this day, might become such as I am, except for these bonds."
052630 The king rose up with the governor, and Bernice, and those who sat with them.
052631 When they had withdrawn, they spoke one to another, saying, "This man does nothing worthy of death or of bonds."
052632 Agrippa said to Festus, "This man might have been set free if he had not appealed to Caesar."
052701 When it was determined that we should sail for Italy, they delivered Paul and certain other prisoners to a centurion named Julius, of the Augustan band.
052702 Embarking in a ship of Adramyttium, which was about to sail to places on the coast of Asia, we put to sea; Aristarchus, a Macedonian of Thessalonica, being with us.
052703 The next day, we touched at Sidon. Julius treated Paul kindly, and gave him permission to go to his friends and refresh himself.
052704 Putting to sea from there, we sailed under the lee of Cyprus, because the winds were contrary.
052705 When we had sailed across the sea which is off Cilicia and Pamphylia, we came to Myra, a city of Lycia.
052706 There the centurion found a ship of Alexandria sailing for Italy, and he put us on board.
052707 When we had sailed slowly many days, and had come with difficulty opposite Cnidus, the wind not allowing us further, we sailed under the lee of Crete, opposite Salmone.
052708 With difficulty sailing along it we came to a certain place called Fair Havens, near the city of Lasea.
052709 When much time had passed and the voyage was now dangerous, because the Fast had now already gone by, Paul admonished them,
052710 and said to them, "Sirs, I perceive that the voyage will be with injury and much loss, not only of the cargo and the ship, but also of our lives."
052711 But the centurion gave more heed to the master and to the owner of the ship than to those things which were spoken by Paul.
052712 Because the haven was not suitable to winter in, the majority advised going to sea from there, if by any means they could reach Phoenix, and winter there, which is a port of Crete, looking northeast and southeast.
052713 When the south wind blew softly, supposing that they had obtained their purpose, they weighed anchor and sailed along Crete, close to shore.
052714 But before long, a stormy wind beat down from shore, which is called Euroclydon.
052715 When the ship was caught, and couldn't face the wind, we gave way to it, and were driven along.
052716 Running under the lee of a small island called Clauda, we were able, with difficulty, to secure the boat.
052717 After they had hoisted it up, they used cables to help reinforce the ship. Fearing that they would run aground on the Syrtis sand bars, they lowered the sea anchor, and so were driven along.
052718 As we labored exceedingly with the storm, the next day they began to throw things overboard.
052719 On the third day, they threw out the ship's tackle with their own hands.
052720 When neither sun nor stars shone on us for many days, and no small storm pressed on us, all hope that we would be saved was now taken away.
052721 When they had been long without food, Paul stood up in the middle of them, and said, "Sirs, you should have listened to me, and not have set sail from Crete, and have gotten this injury and loss.
052722 Now I exhort you to cheer up, for there will be no loss of life among you, but only of the ship.
052723 For there stood by me this night an angel, belonging to the God whose I am and whom I serve,
052724 saying, 'Don't be afraid, Paul. You must stand before Caesar. Behold, God has granted you all those who sail with you.'
052725 Therefore, sirs, cheer up! For I believe God, that it will be just as it has been spoken to me.
052726 But we must run aground on a certain island."
052727 But when the fourteenth night had come, as we were driven back and forth in the Adriatic Sea, about midnight the sailors surmised that they were drawing near to some land.
052728 They took soundings, and found twenty fathoms. After a little while, they took soundings again, and found fifteen fathoms.
052729 Fearing that we would run aground on rocky ground, they let go four anchors from the stern, and wished for daylight.
052730 As the sailors were trying to flee out of the ship, and had lowered the boat into the sea, pretending that they would lay out anchors from the bow,
052731 Paul said to the centurion and to the soldiers, "Unless these stay in the ship, you can't be saved."
052732 Then the soldiers cut away the ropes of the boat, and let it fall off.
052733 While the day was coming on, Paul begged them all to take some food, saying, "This day is the fourteenth day that you wait and continue fasting, having taken nothing.
052734 Therefore I beg you to take some food, for this is for your safety; for not a hair will perish from any of your heads."
052735 When he had said this, and had taken bread, he gave thanks to God in the presence of all, and he broke it, and began to eat.
052736 Then they all cheered up, and they also took food.
052737 In all, we were two hundred seventy-six souls on the ship.
052738 When they had eaten enough, they lightened the ship, throwing out the wheat into the sea.
052739 When it was day, they didn't recognize the land, but they noticed a certain bay with a beach, and they decided to try to drive the ship onto it.
052740 Casting off the anchors, they left them in the sea, at the same time untying the rudder ropes. Hoisting up the foresail to the wind, they made for the beach.
052741 But coming to a place where two seas met, they ran the vessel aground. The bow struck and remained immovable, but the stern began to break up by the violence of the waves.
052742 The soldiers' counsel was to kill the prisoners, so that none of them would swim out and escape.
052743 But the centurion, desiring to save Paul, stopped them from their purpose, and commanded that those who could swim should throw themselves overboard first to go toward the land;
052744 and the rest should follow, some on planks, and some on other things from the ship. So it happened that they all escaped safely to the land.
052801 When we had escaped, then they learned that the island was called Malta.
052802 The natives showed us uncommon kindness; for they kindled a fire, and received us all, because of the present rain, and because of the cold.
052803 But when Paul had gathered a bundle of sticks and laid them on the fire, a viper came out because of the heat, and fastened on his hand.
052804 When the natives saw the creature hanging from his hand, they said one to another, "No doubt this man is a murderer, whom, though he has escaped from the sea, yet Justice has not allowed to live."
052805 However he shook off the creature into the fire, and wasn't harmed.
052806 But they expected that he would have swollen or fallen down dead suddenly, but when they watched for a long time and saw nothing bad happen to him, they changed their minds, and said that he was a god.
052807 Now in the neighborhood of that place were lands belonging to the chief man of the island, named Publius, who received us, and courteously entertained us for three days.
052808 It happened that the father of Publius lay sick of fever and dysentery. Paul entered in to him, prayed, and laying his hands on him, healed him.
052809 Then when this was done, the rest also who had diseases in the island came, and were cured.
052810 They also honored us with many honors, and when we sailed, they put on board the things that we needed.
052811 After three months, we set sail in a ship of Alexandria which had wintered in the island, whose sign was "The Twin Brothers."
052812 Touching at Syracuse, we stayed there three days.
052813 From there we circled around and arrived at Rhegium. After one day, a south wind sprang up, and on the second day we came to Puteoli,
052814 where we found brothers, and were entreated to stay with them for seven days. So we came to Rome.
052815 From there the brothers, when they heard of us, came to meet us as far as The Market of Appius and The Three Taverns. When Paul saw them, he thanked God, and took courage.
052816 When we entered into Rome, the centurion delivered the prisoners to the captain of the guard, but Paul was allowed to stay by himself with the soldier who guarded him.
052817 It happened that after three days Paul called together those who were the leaders of the Jews. When they had come together, he said to them, "I, brothers, though I had done nothing against the people, or the customs of our fathers, still was delivered prisoner from Jerusalem into the hands of the Romans,
052818 who, when they had examined me, desired to set me free, because there was no cause of death in me.
052819 But when the Jews spoke against it, I was constrained to appeal to Caesar, not that I had anything about which to accuse my nation.
052820 For this cause therefore I asked to see you and to speak with you. For because of the hope of Israel I am bound with this chain."
052821 They said to him, "We neither received letters from Judea concerning you, nor did any of the brothers come here and report or speak any evil of you.
052822 But we desire to hear from you what you think. For, as concerning this sect, it is known to us that everywhere it is spoken against."
052823 When they had appointed him a day, many people came to him at his lodging. He explained to them, testifying about the Kingdom of God, and persuading them concerning Jesus, both from the law of Moses and from the prophets, from morning until evening.
052824 Some believed the things which were spoken, and some disbelieved.
052825 When they didn't agree among themselves, they departed after Paul had spoken one word, "The Holy Spirit spoke rightly through Isaiah, the prophet, to our fathers,
052826 saying, 'Go to this people, and say, in hearing, you will hear, but will in no way understand. In seeing, you will see, but will in no way perceive.
052827 For this people's heart has grown callous. Their ears are dull of hearing. Their eyes they have closed. Lest they should see with their eyes, hear with their ears, understand with their heart, and would turn again, and I would heal them.'
052828 "Be it known therefore to you, that the salvation of God is sent to the nations. They will also listen."
052829 When he had said these words, the Jews departed, having a great dispute among themselves.
052830 Paul stayed two whole years in his own rented house, and received all who were coming to him,
052831 preaching the Kingdom of God, and teaching the things concerning the Lord Jesus Christ with all boldness, without hindrance.
060101 Paul, a servant of Jesus Christ, called to be an apostle, set apart for the Good News of God,
060102 which he promised before through his prophets in the holy Scriptures,
060103 concerning his Son, who was born of the seed of David according to the flesh,
060104 who was declared to be the Son of God with power, according to the Spirit of holiness, by the resurrection from the dead, Jesus Christ our Lord,
060105 through whom we received grace and apostleship, for obedience of faith among all the nations, for his name's sake;
060106 among whom you are also called to belong to Jesus Christ;
060107 to all who are in Rome, beloved of God, called to be saints: Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
060108 First, I thank my God through Jesus Christ for all of you, that your faith is proclaimed throughout the whole world.
060109 For God is my witness, whom I serve in my spirit in the Good News of his Son, how unceasingly I make mention of you always in my prayers,
060110 requesting, if by any means now at last I may be prospered by the will of God to come to you.
060111 For I long to see you, that I may impart to you some spiritual gift, to the end that you may be established;
060112 that is, that I with you may be encouraged in you, each of us by the other's faith, both yours and mine.
060113 Now I don't desire to have you unaware, brothers, that I often planned to come to you, and was hindered so far, that I might have some fruit among you also, even as among the rest of the Gentiles.
060114 I am debtor both to Greeks and to foreigners, both to the wise and to the foolish.
060115 So, as much as is in me, I am eager to preach the Good News to you also who are in Rome.
060116 For I am not ashamed of the Good News of Christ, for it is the power of God for salvation for everyone who believes; for the Jew first, and also for the Greek.
060117 For in it is revealed God's righteousness from faith to faith. As it is written, "But the righteous shall live by faith."
060118 For the wrath of God is revealed from heaven against all ungodliness and unrighteousness of men, who suppress the truth in unrighteousness,
060119 because that which is known of God is revealed in them, for God revealed it to them.
060120 For the invisible things of him since the creation of the world are clearly seen, being perceived through the things that are made, even his everlasting power and divinity; that they may be without excuse.
060121 Because, knowing God, they didn't glorify him as God, neither gave thanks, but became vain in their reasoning, and their senseless heart was darkened.
060122 Professing themselves to be wise, they became fools,
060123 and traded the glory of the incorruptible God for the likeness of an image of corruptible man, and of birds, and four-footed animals, and creeping things.
060124 Therefore God also gave them up in the lusts of their hearts to uncleanness, that their bodies should be dishonored among themselves,
060125 who exchanged the truth of God for a lie, and worshiped and served the creature rather than the Creator, who is blessed forever. Amen.
060126 For this reason, God gave them up to vile passions. For their women changed the natural function into that which is against nature.
060127 Likewise also the men, leaving the natural function of the woman, burned in their lust toward one another, men doing what is inappropriate with men, and receiving in themselves the due penalty of their error.
060128 Even as they refused to have God in their knowledge, God gave them up to a reprobate mind, to do those things which are not fitting;
060129 being filled with all unrighteousness, sexual immorality, wickedness, covetousness, malice; full of envy, murder, strife, deceit, evil habits, secret slanderers,
060130 backbiters, hateful to God, insolent, haughty, boastful, inventors of evil things, disobedient to parents,
060131 without understanding, covenant breakers, without natural affection, unforgiving, unmerciful;
060132 who, knowing the ordinance of God, that those who practice such things are worthy of death, not only do the same, but also approve of those who practice them.
060201 Therefore you are without excuse, O man, whoever you are who judge. For in that which you judge another, you condemn yourself. For you who judge practice the same things.
060202 We know that the judgment of God is according to truth against those who practice such things.
060203 Do you think this, O man who judges those who practice such things, and do the same, that you will escape the judgment of God?
060204 Or do you despise the riches of his goodness, forbearance, and patience, not knowing that the goodness of God leads you to repentance?
060205 But according to your hardness and unrepentant heart you are treasuring up for yourself wrath in the day of wrath, revelation, and of the righteous judgment of God;
060206 who "will pay back to everyone according to their works:"
060207 to those who by patience in well-doing seek for glory, honor, and incorruptibility, eternal life;
060208 but to those who are self-seeking, and don't obey the truth, but obey unrighteousness, will be wrath and indignation,
060209 oppression and anguish, on every soul of man who works evil, to the Jew first, and also to the Greek.
060210 But glory, honor, and peace go to every man who works good, to the Jew first, and also to the Greek.
060211 For there is no partiality with God.
060212 For as many as have sinned without law will also perish without the law. As many as have sinned under the law will be judged by the law.
060213 For it isn't the hearers of the law who are righteous before God, but the doers of the law will be justified
060214 (for when Gentiles who don't have the law do by nature the things of the law, these, not having the law, are a law to themselves,
060215 in that they show the work of the law written in their hearts, their conscience testifying with them, and their thoughts among themselves accusing or else excusing them)
060216 in the day when God will judge the secrets of men, according to my Good News, by Jesus Christ.
060217 Indeed you bear the name of a Jew, and rest on the law, and glory in God,
060218 and know his will, and approve the things that are excellent, being instructed out of the law,
060219 and are confident that you yourself are a guide of the blind, a light to those who are in darkness,
060220 a corrector of the foolish, a teacher of babies, having in the law the form of knowledge and of the truth.
060221 You therefore who teach another, don't you teach yourself? You who preach that a man shouldn't steal, do you steal?
060222 You who say a man shouldn't commit adultery. Do you commit adultery? You who abhor idols, do you rob temples?
060223 You who glory in the law, through your disobedience of the law do you dishonor God?
060224 For "the name of God is blasphemed among the Gentiles because of you," just as it is written.
060225 For circumcision indeed profits, if you are a doer of the law, but if you are a transgressor of the law, your circumcision has become uncircumcision.
060226 If therefore the uncircumcised keep the ordinances of the law, won't his uncircumcision be accounted as circumcision?
060227 Won't the uncircumcision which is by nature, if it fulfills the law, judge you, who with the letter and circumcision are a transgressor of the law?
060228 For he is not a Jew who is one outwardly, neither is that circumcision which is outward in the flesh;
060229 but he is a Jew who is one inwardly, and circumcision is that of the heart, in the spirit not in the letter; whose praise is not from men, but from God.
060301 Then what advantage does the Jew have? Or what is the profit of circumcision?
060302 Much in every way! Because first of all, they were entrusted with the oracles of God.
060303 For what if some were without faith? Will their lack of faith nullify the faithfulness of God?
060304 May it never be! Yes, let God be found true, but every man a liar. As it is written, "That you might be justified in your words, and might prevail when you come into judgment."
060305 But if our unrighteousness commends the righteousness of God, what will we say? Is God unrighteous who inflicts wrath? I speak like men do.
060306 May it never be! For then how will God judge the world?
060307 For if the truth of God through my lie abounded to his glory, why am I also still judged as a sinner?
060308 Why not (as we are slanderously reported, and as some affirm that we say), "Let us do evil, that good may come?" Those who say so are justly condemned.
060309 What then? Are we better than they? No, in no way. For we previously warned both Jews and Greeks, that they are all under sin.
060310 As it is written, "There is no one righteous; no, not one.
060311 There is no one who understands. There is no one who seeks after God.
060312 They have all turned aside. They have together become unprofitable. There is no one who does good, no, not, so much as one."
060313 "Their throat is an open tomb. With their tongues they have used deceit." "The poison of vipers is under their lips;"
060314 "Whose mouth is full of cursing and bitterness."
060315 "Their feet are swift to shed blood.
060316 Destruction and misery are in their ways.
060317 The way of peace, they haven't known."
060318 "There is no fear of God before their eyes."
060319 Now we know that whatever things the law says, it speaks to those who are under the law, that every mouth may be closed, and all the world may be brought under the judgment of God.
060320 Because by the works of the law, no flesh will be justified in his sight. For through the law comes the knowledge of sin.
060321 But now apart from the law, a righteousness of God has been revealed, being testified by the law and the prophets;
060322 even the righteousness of God through faith in Jesus Christ to all and on all those who believe. For there is no distinction,
060323 for all have sinned, and fall short of the glory of God;
060324 being justified freely by his grace through the redemption that is in Christ Jesus;
060325 whom God set forth to be an atoning sacrifice, through faith in his blood, for a demonstration of his righteousness through the passing over of prior sins, in God's forbearance;
060326 to demonstrate his righteousness at this present time; that he might himself be just, and the justifier of him who has faith in Jesus.
060327 Where then is the boasting? It is excluded. By what manner of law? Of works? No, but by a law of faith.
060328 We maintain therefore that a man is justified by faith apart from the works of the law.
060329 Or is God the God of Jews only? Isn't he the God of Gentiles also? Yes, of Gentiles also,
060330 since indeed there is one God who will justify the circumcised by faith, and the uncircumcised through faith.
060331 Do we then nullify the law through faith? May it never be! No, we establish the law.
060401 What then will we say that Abraham, our forefather, has found according to the flesh?
060402 For if Abraham was justified by works, he has something to boast about, but not toward God.
060403 For what does the Scripture say? "Abraham believed God, and it was accounted to him for righteousness."
060404 Now to him who works, the reward is not counted as grace, but as debt.
060405 But to him who doesn't work, but believes in him who justifies the ungodly, his faith is accounted for righteousness.
060406 Even as David also pronounces blessing on the man to whom God counts righteousness apart from works,
060407 "Blessed are they whose iniquities are forgiven, whose sins are covered.
060408 Blessed is the man whom the Lord will by no means charge with sin."
060409 Is this blessing then pronounced on the circumcised, or on the uncircumcised also? For we say that faith was accounted to Abraham for righteousness.
060410 How then was it counted? When he was in circumcision, or in uncircumcision? Not in circumcision, but in uncircumcision.
060411 He received the sign of circumcision, a seal of the righteousness of the faith which he had while he was in uncircumcision, that he might be the father of all those who believe, though they be in uncircumcision, that righteousness might also be accounted to them.
060412 The father of circumcision to those who not only are of the circumcision, but who also walk in the steps of that faith of our father Abraham, which he had in uncircumcision.
060413 For the promise to Abraham and to his seed that he should be heir of the world wasn't through the law, but through the righteousness of faith.
060414 For if those who are of the law are heirs, faith is made void, and the promise is made of no effect.
060415 For the law works wrath, for where there is no law, neither is there disobedience.
060416 For this cause it is of faith, that it may be according to grace, to the end that the promise may be sure to all the seed, not to that only which is of the law, but to that also which is of the faith of Abraham, who is the father of us all.
060417 As it is written, "I have made you a father of many nations." This is in the presence of him whom he believed: God, who gives life to the dead, and calls the things that are not, as though they were.
060418 Who in hope believed against hope, to the end that he might become a father of many nations, according to that which had been spoken, "So will your seed be."
060419 Without being weakened in faith, he didn't consider his own body, already having been worn out, (he being about a hundred years old), and the deadness of Sarah's womb.
060420 Yet, looking to the promise of God, he didn't waver through unbelief, but grew strong through faith, giving glory to God,
060421 and being fully assured that what he had promised, he was able also to perform.
060422 Therefore it also was "reckoned to him for righteousness."
060423 Now it was not written that it was accounted to him for his sake alone,
060424 but for our sake also, to whom it will be accounted, who believe in him who raised Jesus, our Lord, from the dead,
060425 who was delivered up for our trespasses, and was raised for our justification.
060501 Being therefore justified by faith, we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ;
060502 through whom we also have our access by faith into this grace in which we stand. We rejoice in hope of the glory of God.
060503 Not only this, but we also rejoice in our sufferings, knowing that suffering works perseverance;
060504 and perseverance, proven character; and proven character, hope:
060505 and hope doesn't disappoint us, because God's love has been poured out into our hearts through the Holy Spirit who was given to us.
060506 For while we were yet weak, at the right time Christ died for the ungodly.
060507 For one will hardly die for a righteous man. Yet perhaps for a righteous person someone would even dare to die.
060508 But God commends his own love toward us, in that while we were yet sinners, Christ died for us.
060509 Much more then, being now justified by his blood, we will be saved from God's wrath through him.
060510 For if, while we were enemies, we were reconciled to God through the death of his Son, much more, being reconciled, we will be saved by his life.
060511 Not only so, but we also rejoice in God through our Lord Jesus Christ, through whom we have now received the reconciliation.
060512 Therefore, as sin entered into the world through one man, and death through sin; and so death passed to all men, because all sinned.
060513 For until the law, sin was in the world; but sin is not charged when there is no law.
060514 Nevertheless death reigned from Adam until Moses, even over those whose sins weren't like Adam's disobedience, who is a foreshadowing of him who was to come.
060515 But the free gift isn't like the trespass. For if by the trespass of the one the many died, much more did the grace of God, and the gift by the grace of the one man, Jesus Christ, abound to the many.
060516 The gift is not as through one who sinned: for the judgment came by one to condemnation, but the free gift came of many trespasses to justification.
060517 For if by the trespass of the one, death reigned through the one; so much more will those who receive the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness reign in life through the one, Jesus Christ.
060518 So then as through one trespass, all men were condemned; even so through one act of righteousness, all men were justified to life.
060519 For as through the one man's disobedience many were made sinners, even so through the obedience of the one, many will be made righteous.
060520 The law came in besides, that the trespass might abound; but where sin abounded, grace abounded more exceedingly;
060521 that as sin reigned in death, even so grace might reign through righteousness to eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord.
060601 What shall we say then? Shall we continue in sin, that grace may abound?
060602 May it never be! We who died to sin, how could we live in it any longer?
060603 Or don't you know that all we who were baptized into Christ Jesus were baptized into his death?
060604 We were buried therefore with him through baptism to death, that just like Christ was raised from the dead through the glory of the Father, so we also might walk in newness of life.
060605 For if we have become united with him in the likeness of his death, we will also be part of his resurrection;
060606 knowing this, that our old man was crucified with him, that the body of sin might be done away with, so that we would no longer be in bondage to sin.
060607 For he who has died has been freed from sin.
060608 But if we died with Christ, we believe that we will also live with him;
060609 knowing that Christ, being raised from the dead, dies no more. Death no more has dominion over him!
060610 For the death that he died, he died to sin one time; but the life that he lives, he lives to God.
060611 Thus consider yourselves also to be dead to sin, but alive to God in Christ Jesus our Lord.
060612 Therefore don't let sin reign in your mortal body, that you should obey it in its lusts.
060613 Neither present your members to sin as instruments of unrighteousness, but present yourselves to God, as alive from the dead, and your members as instruments of righteousness to God.
060614 For sin will not have dominion over you. For you are not under law, but under grace.
060615 What then? Shall we sin, because we are not under law, but under grace? May it never be!
060616 Don't you know that to whom you present yourselves as servants to obedience, his servants you are whom you obey; whether of sin to death, or of obedience to righteousness?
060617 But thanks be to God, that, whereas you were bondservants of sin, you became obedient from the heart to that form of teaching whereunto you were delivered.
060618 Being made free from sin, you became bondservants of righteousness.
060619 I speak in human terms because of the weakness of your flesh, for as you presented your members as servants to uncleanness and to wickedness upon wickedness, even so now present your members as servants to righteousness for sanctification.
060620 For when you were servants of sin, you were free in regard to righteousness.
060621 What fruit then did you have at that time in the things of which you are now ashamed? For the end of those things is death.
060622 But now, being made free from sin, and having become servants of God, you have your fruit of sanctification, and the result of eternal life.
060623 For the wages of sin is death, but the free gift of God is eternal life in Christ Jesus our Lord.
060701 Or don't you know, brothers (for I speak to men who know the law), that the law has dominion over a man for as long as he lives?
060702 For the woman that has a husband is bound by law to the husband while he lives, but if the husband dies, she is discharged from the law of the husband.
060703 So then if, while the husband lives, she is joined to another man, she would be called an adulteress. But if the husband dies, she is free from the law, so that she is no adulteress, though she is joined to another man.
060704 Therefore, my brothers, you also were made dead to the law through the body of Christ, that you would be joined to another, to him who was raised from the dead, that we might bring forth fruit to God.
060705 For when we were in the flesh, the sinful passions which were through the law, worked in our members to bring forth fruit to death.
060706 But now we have been discharged from the law, having died to that in which we were held; so that we serve in newness of the spirit, and not in oldness of the letter.
060707 What shall we say then? Is the law sin? May it never be! However, I wouldn't have known sin, except through the law. For I wouldn't have known coveting, unless the law had said, "You shall not covet."
060708 But sin, finding occasion through the commandment, produced in me all kinds of coveting. For apart from the law, sin is dead.
060709 I was alive apart from the law once, but when the commandment came, sin revived, and I died.
060710 The commandment, which was for life, this I found to be for death;
060711 for sin, finding occasion through the commandment, deceived me, and through it killed me.
060712 Therefore the law indeed is holy, and the commandment holy, and righteous, and good.
060713 Did then that which is good become death to me? May it never be! But sin, that it might be shown to be sin, by working death to me through that which is good; that through the commandment sin might become exceeding sinful.
060714 For we know that the law is spiritual, but I am fleshly, sold under sin.
060715 For I don't know what I am doing. For I don't practice what I desire to do; but what I hate, that I do.
060716 But if what I don't desire, that I do, I consent to the law that it is good.
060717 So now it is no more I that do it, but sin which dwells in me.
060718 For I know that in me, that is, in my flesh, dwells no good thing. For desire is present with me, but I don't find it doing that which is good.
060719 For the good which I desire, I don't do; but the evil which I don't desire, that I practice.
060720 But if what I don't desire, that I do, it is no more I that do it, but sin which dwells in me.
060721 I find then the law, that, to me, while I desire to do good, evil is present.
060722 For I delight in God's law after the inward man,
060723 but I see a different law in my members, warring against the law of my mind, and bringing me into captivity under the law of sin which is in my members.
060724 What a wretched man I am! Who will deliver me out of the body of this death?
060725 I thank God through Jesus Christ, our Lord! So then with the mind, I myself serve God's law, but with the flesh, the sin's law.
060801 There is therefore now no condemnation to those who are in Christ Jesus, who don't walk according to the flesh, but according to the Spirit.
060802 For the law of the Spirit of life in Christ Jesus made me free from the law of sin and of death.
060803 For what the law couldn't do, in that it was weak through the flesh, God did, sending his own Son in the likeness of sinful flesh and for sin, he condemned sin in the flesh;
060804 that the ordinance of the law might be fulfilled in us, who walk not after the flesh, but after the Spirit.
060805 For those who live according to the flesh set their minds on the things of the flesh, but those who live according to the Spirit, the things of the Spirit.
060806 For the mind of the flesh is death, but the mind of the Spirit is life and peace;
060807 because the mind of the flesh is hostile towards God; for it is not subject to God's law, neither indeed can it be.
060808 Those who are in the flesh can't please God.
060809 But you are not in the flesh but in the Spirit, if it is so that the Spirit of God dwells in you. But if any man doesn't have the Spirit of Christ, he is not his.
060810 If Christ is in you, the body is dead because of sin, but the spirit is alive because of righteousness.
060811 But if the Spirit of him who raised up Jesus from the dead dwells in you, he who raised up Christ Jesus from the dead will also give life to your mortal bodies through his Spirit who dwells in you.
060812 So then, brothers, we are debtors, not to the flesh, to live after the flesh.
060813 For if you live after the flesh, you must die; but if by the Spirit you put to death the deeds of the body, you will live.
060814 For as many as are led by the Spirit of God, these are children of God.
060815 For you didn't receive the spirit of bondage again to fear, but you received the Spirit of adoption, by whom we cry, "Abba! Father!"
060816 The Spirit himself testifies with our spirit that we are children of God;
060817 and if children, then heirs; heirs of God, and joint heirs with Christ; if indeed we suffer with him, that we may also be glorified with him.
060818 For I consider that the sufferings of this present time are not worthy to be compared with the glory which will be revealed toward us.
060819 For the creation waits with eager expectation for the children of God to be revealed.
060820 For the creation was subjected to vanity, not of its own will, but because of him who subjected it, in hope
060821 that the creation itself also will be delivered from the bondage of decay into the liberty of the glory of the children of God.
060822 For we know that the whole creation groans and travails in pain together until now.
060823 Not only so, but ourselves also, who have the first fruits of the Spirit, even we ourselves groan within ourselves, waiting for adoption, the redemption of our body.
060824 For we were saved in hope, but hope that is seen is not hope. For who hopes for that which he sees?
060825 But if we hope for that which we don't see, we wait for it with patience.
060826 In the same way, the Spirit also helps our weaknesses, for we don't know how to pray as we ought. But the Spirit himself makes intercession for us with groanings which can't be uttered.
060827 He who searches the hearts knows what is on the Spirit's mind, because he makes intercession for the saints according to God.
060828 We know that all things work together for good for those who love God, to those who are called according to his purpose.
060829 For whom he foreknew, he also predestined to be conformed to the image of his Son, that he might be the firstborn among many brothers.
060830 Whom he predestined, those he also called. Whom he called, those he also justified. Whom he justified, those he also glorified.
060831 What then shall we say about these things? If God is for us, who can be against us?
060832 He who didn't spare his own Son, but delivered him up for us all, how would he not also with him freely give us all things?
060833 Who could bring a charge against God's chosen ones? It is God who justifies.
060834 Who is he who condemns? It is Christ who died, yes rather, who was raised from the dead, who is at the right hand of God, who also makes intercession for us.
060835 Who shall separate us from the love of Christ? Could oppression, or anguish, or persecution, or famine, or nakedness, or peril, or sword?
060836 Even as it is written, "For your sake we are killed all day long. We were accounted as sheep for the slaughter."
060837 No, in all these things, we are more than conquerors through him who loved us.
060838 For I am persuaded, that neither death, nor life, nor angels, nor principalities, nor things present, nor things to come, nor powers,
060839 nor height, nor depth, nor any other created thing, will be able to separate us from the love of God, which is in Christ Jesus our Lord.
060901 I tell the truth in Christ. I am not lying, my conscience testifying with me in the Holy Spirit,
060902 that I have great sorrow and unceasing pain in my heart.
060903 For I could wish that I myself were accursed from Christ for my brothers' sake, my relatives according to the flesh,
060904 who are Israelites; whose is the adoption, the glory, the covenants, the giving of the law, the service, and the promises;
060905 of whom are the fathers, and from whom is Christ as concerning the flesh, who is over all, God, blessed forever. Amen.
060906 But it is not as though the word of God has come to nothing. For they are not all Israel, that are of Israel.
060907 Neither, because they are Abraham's seed, are they all children. But, "In Isaac will your seed be called."
060908 That is, it is not the children of the flesh who are children of God, but the children of the promise are counted as a seed.
060909 For this is a word of promise, "At the appointed time I will come, and Sarah will have a son."
060910 Not only so, but Rebecca also conceived by one, by our father Isaac.
060911 For being not yet born, neither having done anything good or bad, that the purpose of God according to election might stand, not of works, but of him who calls,
060912 it was said to her, "The elder will serve the younger."
060913 Even as it is written, "Jacob I loved, but Esau I hated."
060914 What shall we say then? Is there unrighteousness with God? May it never be!
060915 For he said to Moses, "I will have mercy on whom I have mercy, and I will have compassion on whom I have compassion."
060916 So then it is not of him who wills, nor of him who runs, but of God who has mercy.
060917 For the Scripture says to Pharaoh, "For this very purpose I caused you to be raised up, that I might show in you my power, and that my name might be proclaimed in all the earth."
060918 So then, he has mercy on whom he desires, and he hardens whom he desires.
060919 You will say then to me, "Why does he still find fault? For who withstands his will?"
060920 But indeed, O man, who are you to reply against God? Will the thing formed ask him who formed it, "Why did you make me like this?"
060921 Or hasn't the potter a right over the clay, from the same lump to make one part a vessel for honor, and another for dishonor?
060922 What if God, willing to show his wrath, and to make his power known, endured with much patience vessels of wrath made for destruction,
060923 and that he might make known the riches of his glory on vessels of mercy, which he prepared beforehand for glory,
060924 us, whom he also called, not from the Jews only, but also from the Gentiles?
060925 As he says also in Hosea, "I will call them 'my people,' which were not my people; and her 'beloved,' who was not beloved."
060926 "It will be that in the place where it was said to them, 'You are not my people,' There they will be called 'children of the living God.'"
060927 Isaiah cries concerning Israel, "If the number of the children of Israel are as the sand of the sea, it is the remnant who will be saved;
060928 for He will finish the work and cut it short in righteousness, because the LORD will make a short work upon the earth."
060929 As Isaiah has said before, "Unless the Lord of Armies had left us a seed, we would have become like Sodom, and would have been made like Gomorrah."
060930 What shall we say then? That the Gentiles, who didn't follow after righteousness, attained to righteousness, even the righteousness which is of faith;
060931 but Israel, following after a law of righteousness, didn't arrive at the law of righteousness.
060932 Why? Because they didn't seek it by faith, but as it were by works of the law. They stumbled over the stumbling stone;
060933 even as it is written, "Behold, I lay in Zion a stumbling stone and a rock of offense; and no one who believes in him will be disappointed."
061001 Brothers, my heart's desire and my prayer to God is for Israel, that they may be saved.
061002 For I testify about them that they have a zeal for God, but not according to knowledge.
061003 For being ignorant of God's righteousness, and seeking to establish their own righteousness, they didn't subject themselves to the righteousness of God.
061004 For Christ is the fulfillment of the law for righteousness to everyone who believes.
061005 For Moses writes about the righteousness of the law, "The one who does them will live by them."
061006 But the righteousness which is of faith says this, "Don't say in your heart, 'Who will ascend into heaven?' (that is, to bring Christ down);
061007 or, 'Who will descend into the abyss?' (that is, to bring Christ up from the dead.)"
061008 But what does it say? "The word is near you, in your mouth, and in your heart;" that is, the word of faith, which we preach:
061009 that if you will confess with your mouth that Jesus is Lord, and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead, you will be saved.
061010 For with the heart, one believes unto righteousness; and with the mouth confession is made unto salvation.
061011 For the Scripture says, "Whoever believes in him will not be disappointed."
061012 For there is no distinction between Jew and Greek; for the same Lord is Lord of all, and is rich to all who call on him.
061013 For, "Whoever will call on the name of the Lord will be saved."
061014 How then will they call on him in whom they have not believed? How will they believe in him whom they have not heard? How will they hear without a preacher?
061015 And how will they preach unless they are sent? As it is written: "How beautiful are the feet of those who preach the Good News of peace, who bring glad tidings of good things!"
061016 But they didn't all listen to the glad news. For Isaiah says, "Lord, who has believed our report?"
061017 So faith comes by hearing, and hearing by the word of God.
061018 But I say, didn't they hear? Yes, most certainly, "Their sound went out into all the earth, their words to the ends of the world."
061019 But I ask, didn't Israel know? First Moses says, "I will provoke you to jealousy with that which is no nation, with a nation void of understanding I will make you angry."
061020 Isaiah is very bold, and says, "I was found by those who didn't seek me. I was revealed to those who didn't ask for me."
061021 But as to Israel he says, "All day long I stretched out my hands to a disobedient and contrary people."
061101 I ask then, did God reject his people? May it never be! For I also am an Israelite, a descendant of Abraham, of the tribe of Benjamin.
061102 God didn't reject his people, which he foreknew. Or don't you know what the Scripture says about Elijah? How he pleads with God against Israel:
061103 "Lord, they have killed your prophets, they have broken down your altars; and I am left alone, and they seek my life."
061104 But how does God answer him? "I have reserved for myself seven thousand men, who have not bowed the knee to Baal."
061105 Even so then at this present time also there is a remnant according to the election of grace.
061106 And if by grace, then it is no longer of works; otherwise grace is no longer grace. But if it is of works, it is no longer grace; otherwise work is no longer work.
061107 What then? That which Israel seeks for, that he didn't obtain, but the chosen ones obtained it, and the rest were hardened.
061108 According as it is written, "God gave them a spirit of stupor, eyes that they should not see, and ears that they should not hear, to this very day."
061109 David says, "Let their table be made a snare, and a trap, a stumbling block, and a retribution to them.
061110 Let their eyes be darkened, that they may not see. Bow down their back always."
061111 I ask then, did they stumble that they might fall? May it never be! But by their fall salvation has come to the Gentiles, to provoke them to jealousy.
061112 Now if their fall is the riches of the world, and their loss the riches of the Gentiles; how much more their fullness?
061113 For I speak to you who are Gentiles. Since then as I am an apostle to Gentiles, I glorify my ministry;
061114 if by any means I may provoke to jealousy those who are my flesh, and may save some of them.
061115 For if the rejection of them is the reconciling of the world, what would their acceptance be, but life from the dead?
061116 If the first fruit is holy, so is the lump. If the root is holy, so are the branches.
061117 But if some of the branches were broken off, and you, being a wild olive, were grafted in among them, and became partaker with them of the root and of the richness of the olive tree;
061118 don't boast over the branches. But if you boast, it is not you who support the root, but the root supports you.
061119 You will say then, "Branches were broken off, that I might be grafted in."
061120 True; by their unbelief they were broken off, and you stand by your faith. Don't be conceited, but fear;
061121 for if God didn't spare the natural branches, neither will he spare you.
061122 See then the goodness and severity of God. Toward those who fell, severity; but toward you, goodness, if you continue in his goodness; otherwise you also will be cut off.
061123 They also, if they don't continue in their unbelief, will be grafted in, for God is able to graft them in again.
061124 For if you were cut out of that which is by nature a wild olive tree, and were grafted contrary to nature into a good olive tree, how much more will these, which are the natural branches, be grafted into their own olive tree?
061125 For I don't desire you to be ignorant, brothers, of this mystery, so that you won't be wise in your own conceits, that a partial hardening has happened to Israel, until the fullness of the Gentiles has come in,
061126 and so all Israel will be saved. Even as it is written, "There will come out of Zion the Deliverer, and he will turn away ungodliness from Jacob.
061127 This is my covenant to them, when I will take away their sins."
061128 Concerning the Good News, they are enemies for your sake. But concerning the election, they are beloved for the fathers' sake.
061129 For the gifts and the calling of God are irrevocable.
061130 For as you in time past were disobedient to God, but now have obtained mercy by their disobedience,
061131 even so these also have now been disobedient, that by the mercy shown to you they may also obtain mercy.
061132 For God has shut up all to disobedience, that he might have mercy on all.
061133 Oh the depth of the riches both of the wisdom and the knowledge of God! How unsearchable are his judgments, and his ways past tracing out!
061134 "For who has known the mind of the Lord? Or who has been his counselor?"
061135 "Or who has first given to him, and it will be repaid to him again?"
061136 For of him, and through him, and to him, are all things. To him be the glory for ever! Amen.
061201 Therefore I urge you, brothers, by the mercies of God, to present your bodies a living sacrifice, holy, acceptable to God, which is your spiritual service.
061202 Don't be conformed to this world, but be transformed by the renewing of your mind, so that you may prove what is the good, well-pleasing, and perfect will of God.
061203 For I say, through the grace that was given me, to every man who is among you, not to think of himself more highly than he ought to think; but to think reasonably, as God has apportioned to each person a measure of faith.
061204 For even as we have many members in one body, and all the members don't have the same function,
061205 so we, who are many, are one body in Christ, and individually members one of another.
061206 Having gifts differing according to the grace that was given to us, if prophecy, let us prophesy according to the proportion of our faith;
061207 or service, let us give ourselves to service; or he who teaches, to his teaching;
061208 or he who exhorts, to his exhorting: he who gives, let him do it with liberality; he who rules, with diligence; he who shows mercy, with cheerfulness.
061209 Let love be without hypocrisy. Abhor that which is evil. Cling to that which is good.
061210 In love of the brothers be tenderly affectionate one to another; in honor preferring one another;
061211 not lagging in diligence; fervent in spirit; serving the Lord;
061212 rejoicing in hope; enduring in troubles; continuing steadfastly in prayer;
061213 contributing to the needs of the saints; given to hospitality.
061214 Bless those who persecute you; bless, and don't curse.
061215 Rejoice with those who rejoice. Weep with those who weep.
061216 Be of the same mind one toward another. Don't set your mind on high things, but associate with the humble. Don't be wise in your own conceits.
061217 Repay no one evil for evil. Respect what is honorable in the sight of all men.
061218 If it is possible, as much as it is up to you, be at peace with all men.
061219 Don't seek revenge yourselves, beloved, but give place to God's wrath. For it is written, "Vengeance belongs to me; I will repay, says the Lord."
061220 Therefore "If your enemy is hungry, feed him. If he is thirsty, give him a drink; for in doing so, you will heap coals of fire on his head."
061221 Don't be overcome by evil, but overcome evil with good.
061301 Let every soul be in subjection to the higher authorities, for there is no authority except from God, and those who exist are ordained by God.
061302 Therefore he who resists the authority, withstands the ordinance of God; and those who withstand will receive to themselves judgment.
061303 For rulers are not a terror to the good work, but to the evil. Do you desire to have no fear of the authority? Do that which is good, and you will have praise from the same,
061304 for he is a servant of God to you for good. But if you do that which is evil, be afraid, for he doesn't bear the sword in vain; for he is a servant of God, an avenger for wrath to him who does evil.
061305 Therefore you need to be in subjection, not only because of the wrath, but also for conscience' sake.
061306 For this reason you also pay taxes, for they are servants of God's service, attending continually on this very thing.
061307 Give therefore to everyone what you owe: taxes to whom taxes are due; customs to whom customs; respect to whom respect; honor to whom honor.
061308 Owe no one anything, except to love one another; for he who loves his neighbor has fulfilled the law.
061309 For the commandments, "You shall not commit adultery," "You shall not murder," "You shall not steal," "You shall not give false testimony," "You shall not covet," and whatever other commandments there are, are all summed up in this saying, namely, "You shall love your neighbor as yourself."
061310 Love doesn't harm a neighbor. Love therefore is the fulfillment of the law.
061311 Do this, knowing the time, that it is already time for you to awaken out of sleep, for salvation is now nearer to us than when we first believed.
061312 The night is far gone, and the day is near. Let's therefore throw off the works of darkness, and let's put on the armor of light.
061313 Let us walk properly, as in the day; not in reveling and drunkenness, not in sexual promiscuity and lustful acts, and not in strife and jealousy.
061314 But put on the Lord Jesus Christ, and make no provision for the flesh, for its lusts.
061401 Now accept one who is weak in faith, but not for disputes over opinions.
061402 One man has faith to eat all things, but he who is weak eats only vegetables.
061403 Don't let him who eats despise him who doesn't eat. Don't let him who doesn't eat judge him who eats, for God has accepted him.
061404 Who are you who judge another's servant? To his own lord he stands or falls. Yes, he will be made to stand, for God has power to make him stand.
061405 One man esteems one day as more important. Another esteems every day alike. Let each man be fully assured in his own mind.
061406 He who observes the day, observes it to the Lord; and he who does not observe the day, to the Lord he does not observe it. He who eats, eats to the Lord, for he gives God thanks. He who doesn't eat, to the Lord he doesn't eat, and gives God thanks.
061407 For none of us lives to himself, and none dies to himself.
061408 For if we live, we live to the Lord. Or if we die, we die to the Lord. If therefore we live or die, we are the Lord's.
061409 For to this end Christ died, rose, and lived again, that he might be Lord of both the dead and the living.
061410 But you, why do you judge your brother? Or you again, why do you despise your brother? For we will all stand before the judgment seat of Christ.
061411 For it is written, "'As I live,' says the Lord, 'to me every knee will bow. Every tongue will confess to God.'"
061412 So then each one of us will give account of himself to God.
061413 Therefore let's not judge one another any more, but judge this rather, that no man put a stumbling block in his brother's way, or an occasion for falling.
061414 I know, and am persuaded in the Lord Jesus, that nothing is unclean of itself; except that to him who considers anything to be unclean, to him it is unclean.
061415 Yet if because of food your brother is grieved, you walk no longer in love. Don't destroy with your food him for whom Christ died.
061416 Then don't let your good be slandered,
061417 for the Kingdom of God is not eating and drinking, but righteousness, peace, and joy in the Holy Spirit.
061418 For he who serves Christ in these things is acceptable to God and approved by men.
061419 So then, let us follow after things which make for peace, and things by which we may build one another up.
061420 Don't overthrow God's work for food's sake. All things indeed are clean, however it is evil for that man who creates a stumbling block by eating.
061421 It is good to not eat meat, drink wine, nor do anything by which your brother stumbles, is offended, or is made weak.
061422 Do you have faith? Have it to yourself before God. Happy is he who doesn't judge himself in that which he approves.
061423 But he who doubts is condemned if he eats, because it isn't of faith; and whatever is not of faith is sin.\NOTE: SEE Romans 16:25-16:27 for World English Bible Romans 14:24-14:26 (the translators had moved and renumbered these verses from their standard location of 16:25-27. They are left intact there for 1551 inter-Bible compatability).
061501 Now we who are strong ought to bear the weaknesses of the weak, and not to please ourselves.
061502 Let each one of us please his neighbor for that which is good, to be building him up.
061503 For even Christ didn't please himself. But, as it is written, "The reproaches of those who reproached you fell on me."
061504 For whatever things were written before were written for our learning, that through patience and through encouragement of the Scriptures we might have hope.
061505 Now the God of patience and of encouragement grant you to be of the same mind one with another according to Christ Jesus,
061506 that with one accord you may with one mouth glorify the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ.
061507 Therefore accept one another, even as Christ also accepted you, to the glory of God.
061508 Now I say that Christ has been made a servant of the circumcision for the truth of God, that he might confirm the promises given to the fathers,
061509 and that the Gentiles might glorify God for his mercy. As it is written, "Therefore will I give praise to you among the Gentiles, and sing to your name."
061510 Again he says, "Rejoice, you Gentiles, with his people."
061511 Again, "Praise the Lord, all you Gentiles! Let all the peoples praise him."
061512 Again, Isaiah says, "There will be the root of Jesse, he who arises to rule over the Gentiles; in him the Gentiles will hope."
061513 Now may the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace in believing, that you may abound in hope, in the power of the Holy Spirit.
061514 I myself am also persuaded about you, my brothers, that you yourselves are full of goodness, filled with all knowledge, able also to admonish others.
061515 But I write the more boldly to you in part, as reminding you, because of the grace that was given to me by God,
061516 that I should be a servant of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles, serving as a priest the Good News of God, that the offering up of the Gentiles might be made acceptable, sanctified by the Holy Spirit.
061517 I have therefore my boasting in Christ Jesus in things pertaining to God.
061518 For I will not dare to speak of any things except those which Christ worked through me, for the obedience of the Gentiles, by word and deed,
061519 in the power of signs and wonders, in the power of God's Spirit; so that from Jerusalem, and around as far as to Illyricum, I have fully preached the Good News of Christ;
061520 yes, making it my aim to preach the Good News, not where Christ was already named, that I might not build on another's foundation.
061521 But, as it is written, "They will see, to whom no news of him came. They who haven't heard will understand."
061522 Therefore also I was hindered these many times from coming to you,
061523 but now, no longer having any place in these regions, and having these many years a longing to come to you,
061524 whenever I journey to Spain, I will come to you. For I hope to see you on my journey, and to be helped on my way there by you, if first I may enjoy your company for a while.
061525 But now, I say, I am going to Jerusalem, serving the saints.
061526 For it has been the good pleasure of Macedonia and Achaia to make a certain contribution for the poor among the saints who are at Jerusalem.
061527 Yes, it has been their good pleasure, and they are their debtors. For if the Gentiles have been made partakers of their spiritual things, they owe it to them also to serve them in fleshly things.
061528 When therefore I have accomplished this, and have sealed to them this fruit, I will go on by way of you to Spain.
061529 I know that, when I come to you, I will come in the fullness of the blessing of the Good News of Christ.
061530 Now I beg you, brothers, by our Lord Jesus Christ, and by the love of the Spirit, that you strive together with me in your prayers to God for me,
061531 that I may be delivered from those who are disobedient in Judea, and that my service which I have for Jerusalem may be acceptable to the saints;
061532 that I may come to you in joy through the will of God, and together with you, find rest.
061533 Now the God of peace be with you all. Amen.
061601 I commend to you Phoebe, our sister, who is a servant of the assembly that is at Cenchreae,
061602 that you receive her in the Lord, in a way worthy of the saints, and that you assist her in whatever matter she may need from you, for she herself also has been a helper of many, and of my own self.
061603 Greet Prisca and Aquila, my fellow workers in Christ Jesus,
061604 who for my life, laid down their own necks; to whom not only I give thanks, but also all the assemblies of the Gentiles.
061605 Greet the assembly that is in their house. Greet Epaenetus, my beloved, who is the first fruits of Achaia to Christ.
061606 Greet Mary, who labored much for us.
061607 Greet Andronicus and Junias, my relatives and my fellow prisoners, who are notable among the apostles, who also were in Christ before me.
061608 Greet Amplias, my beloved in the Lord.
061609 Greet Urbanus, our fellow worker in Christ, and Stachys, my beloved.
061610 Greet Apelles, the approved in Christ. Greet those who are of the household of Aristobulus.
061611 Greet Herodion, my kinsman. Greet them of the household of Narcissus, who are in the Lord.
061612 Greet Tryphaena and Tryphosa, who labor in the Lord. Greet Persis, the beloved, who labored much in the Lord.
061613 Greet Rufus, the chosen in the Lord, and his mother and mine.
061614 Greet Asyncritus, Phlegon, Hermes, Patrobas, Hermas, and the brothers who are with them.
061615 Greet Philologus and Julia, Nereus and his sister, and Olympas, and all the saints who are with them.
061616 Greet one another with a holy kiss. The assemblies of Christ greet you.
061617 Now I beg you, brothers, look out for those who are causing the divisions and occasions of stumbling, contrary to the doctrine which you learned, and turn away from them.
061618 For those who are such don't serve our Lord, Jesus Christ, but their own belly; and by their smooth and flattering speech, they deceive the hearts of the innocent.
061619 For your obedience has become known to all. I rejoice therefore over you. But I desire to have you wise in that which is good, but innocent in that which is evil.
061620 And the God of peace will quickly crush Satan under your feet. The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you.
061621 Timothy, my fellow worker, greets you, as do Lucius, Jason, and Sosipater, my relatives.
061622 I, Tertius, who write the letter, greet you in the Lord.
061623 Gaius, my host and host of the whole assembly, greets you. Erastus, the treasurer of the city, greets you, as does Quartus, the brother.
061624 The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ be with you all! Amen.
061625 (The World English Bible moved this verse to 14:24) [14:24] Now to him who is able to establish you according to my Good News and the preaching of Jesus Christ, according to the revelation of the mystery which has been kept secret through long ages,
061626 (The World English Bible moved this verse to 14:25) [14:25] but now is revealed, and by the Scriptures of the prophets, according to the commandment of the eternal God, is made known for obedience of faith to all the nations;
061627 (The World English Bible moved this verse to 14:26) [14:26] to the only wise God, through Jesus Christ, to whom be the glory forever! Amen.
070101 Paul, called to be an apostle of Jesus Christ through the will of God, and our brother Sosthenes,
070102 to the assembly of God which is at Corinth; those who are sanctified in Christ Jesus, called to be saints, with all who call on the name of our Lord Jesus Christ in every place, both theirs and ours:
070103 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
070104 I always thank my God concerning you, for the grace of God which was given you in Christ Jesus;
070105 that in everything you were enriched in him, in all speech and all knowledge;
070106 even as the testimony of Christ was confirmed in you:
070107 so that you come behind in no gift; waiting for the revelation of our Lord Jesus Christ;
070108 who will also confirm you until the end, blameless in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ.
070109 God is faithful, through whom you were called into the fellowship of his Son, Jesus Christ, our Lord.
070110 Now I beg you, brothers, through the name of our Lord, Jesus Christ, that you all speak the same thing and that there be no divisions among you, but that you be perfected together in the same mind and in the same judgment.
070111 For it has been reported to me concerning you, my brothers, by those who are from Chloe's household, that there are contentions among you.
070112 Now I mean this, that each one of you says, "I follow Paul," "I follow Apollos," "I follow Cephas," and, "I follow Christ."
070113 Is Christ divided? Was Paul crucified for you? Or were you baptized into the name of Paul?
070114 I thank God that I baptized none of you, except Crispus and Gaius,
070115 so that no one should say that I had baptized you into my own name.
070116 (I also baptized the household of Stephanas; besides them, I don't know whether I baptized any other.)
070117 For Christ sent me not to baptize, but to preach the Good News--not in wisdom of words, so that the cross of Christ wouldn't be made void.
070118 For the word of the cross is foolishness to those who are dying, but to us who are saved it is the power of God.
070119 For it is written, "I will destroy the wisdom of the wise, I will bring the discernment of the discerning to nothing."
070120 Where is the wise? Where is the scribe? Where is the lawyer of this world? Hasn't God made foolish the wisdom of this world?
070121 For seeing that in the wisdom of God, the world through its wisdom didn't know God, it was God's good pleasure through the foolishness of the preaching to save those who believe.
070122 For Jews ask for signs, Greeks seek after wisdom,
070123 but we preach Christ crucified; a stumbling block to Jews, and foolishness to Greeks,
070124 but to those who are called, both Jews and Greeks, Christ is the power of God and the wisdom of God.
070125 Because the foolishness of God is wiser than men, and the weakness of God is stronger than men.
070126 For you see your calling, brothers, that not many are wise according to the flesh, not many mighty, and not many noble;
070127 but God chose the foolish things of the world that he might put to shame those who are wise. God chose the weak things of the world, that he might put to shame the things that are strong;
070128 and God chose the lowly things of the world, and the things that are despised, and the things that are not, that he might bring to nothing the things that are:
070129 that no flesh should boast before God.
070130 But of him, you are in Christ Jesus, who was made to us wisdom from God, and righteousness and sanctification, and redemption:
070131 that, according as it is written, "He who boasts, let him boast in the Lord."
070201 When I came to you, brothers, I didn't come with excellence of speech or of wisdom, proclaiming to you the testimony of God.
070202 For I determined not to know anything among you, except Jesus Christ, and him crucified.
070203 I was with you in weakness, in fear, and in much trembling.
