070204 My speech and my preaching were not in persuasive words of human wisdom, but in demonstration of the Spirit and of power,
070205 that your faith wouldn't stand in the wisdom of men, but in the power of God.
070206 We speak wisdom, however, among those who are full grown; yet a wisdom not of this world, nor of the rulers of this world, who are coming to nothing.
070207 But we speak God's wisdom in a mystery, the wisdom that has been hidden, which God foreordained before the worlds for our glory,
070208 which none of the rulers of this world has known. For had they known it, they wouldn't have crucified the Lord of glory.
070209 But as it is written, "Things which an eye didn't see, and an ear didn't hear, which didn't enter into the heart of man, these God has prepared for those who love him."
070210 But to us, God revealed them through the Spirit. For the Spirit searches all things, yes, the deep things of God.
070211 For who among men knows the things of a man, except the spirit of the man, which is in him? Even so, no one knows the things of God, except God's Spirit.
070212 But we received, not the spirit of the world, but the Spirit which is from God, that we might know the things that were freely given to us by God.
070213 Which things also we speak, not in words which man's wisdom teaches, but which the Holy Spirit teaches, comparing spiritual things with spiritual things.
070214 Now the natural man doesn't receive the things of God's Spirit, for they are foolishness to him, and he can't know them, because they are spiritually discerned.
070215 But he who is spiritual discerns all things, and he himself is judged by no one.
070216 "For who has known the mind of the Lord, that he should instruct him?" But we have Christ's mind.
070301 Brothers, I couldn't speak to you as to spiritual, but as to fleshly, as to babies in Christ.
070302 I fed you with milk, not with meat; for you weren't yet ready. Indeed, not even now are you ready,
070303 for you are still fleshly. For insofar as there is jealousy, strife, and factions among you, aren't you fleshly, and don't you walk in the ways of men?
070304 For when one says, "I follow Paul," and another, "I follow Apollos," aren't you fleshly?
070305 Who then is Apollos, and who is Paul, but servants through whom you believed; and each as the Lord gave to him?
070306 I planted. Apollos watered. But God gave the increase.
070307 So then neither he who plants is anything, nor he who waters, but God who gives the increase.
070308 Now he who plants and he who waters are the same, but each will receive his own reward according to his own labor.
070309 For we are God's fellow workers. You are God's farming, God's building.
070310 According to the grace of God which was given to me, as a wise master builder I laid a foundation, and another builds on it. But let each man be careful how he builds on it.
070311 For no one can lay any other foundation than that which has been laid, which is Jesus Christ.
070312 But if anyone builds on the foundation with gold, silver, costly stones, wood, hay, or stubble;
070313 each man's work will be revealed. For the Day will declare it, because it is revealed in fire; and the fire itself will test what sort of work each man's work is.
070314 If any man's work remains which he built on it, he will receive a reward.
070315 If any man's work is burned, he will suffer loss, but he himself will be saved, but as through fire.
070316 Don't you know that you are a temple of God, and that God's Spirit lives in you?
070317 If anyone destroys the temple of God, God will destroy him; for God's temple is holy, which you are.
070318 Let no one deceive himself. If anyone thinks that he is wise among you in this world, let him become a fool, that he may become wise.
070319 For the wisdom of this world is foolishness with God. For it is written, "He has taken the wise in their craftiness."
070320 And again, "The Lord knows the reasoning of the wise, that it is worthless."
070321 Therefore let no one boast in men. For all things are yours,
070322 whether Paul, or Apollos, or Cephas, or the world, or life, or death, or things present, or things to come. All are yours,
070323 and you are Christ's, and Christ is God's.
070401 So let a man think of us as Christ's servants, and stewards of God's mysteries.
070402 Here, moreover, it is required of stewards, that they be found faithful.
070403 But with me it is a very small thing that I should be judged by you, or by man's judgment. Yes, I don't judge my own self.
070404 For I know nothing against myself. Yet I am not justified by this, but he who judges me is the Lord.
070405 Therefore judge nothing before the time, until the Lord comes, who will both bring to light the hidden things of darkness, and reveal the counsels of the hearts. Then each man will get his praise from God.
070406 Now these things, brothers, I have in a figure transferred to myself and Apollos for your sakes, that in us you might learn not to think beyond the things which are written, that none of you be puffed up against one another.
070407 For who makes you different? And what do you have that you didn't receive? But if you did receive it, why do you boast as if you had not received it?
070408 You are already filled. You have already become rich. You have come to reign without us. Yes, and I wish that you did reign, that we also might reign with you.
070409 For, I think that God has displayed us, the apostles, last of all, like men sentenced to death. For we are made a spectacle to the world, both to angels and men.
070410 We are fools for Christ's sake, but you are wise in Christ. We are weak, but you are strong. You have honor, but we have dishonor.
070411 Even to this present hour we hunger, thirst, are naked, are beaten, and have no certain dwelling place.
070412 We toil, working with our own hands. When people curse us, we bless. Being persecuted, we endure.
070413 Being defamed, we entreat. We are made as the filth of the world, the dirt wiped off by all, even until now.
070414 I don't write these things to shame you, but to admonish you as my beloved children.
070415 For though you have ten thousand tutors in Christ, yet not many fathers. For in Christ Jesus, I became your father through the Good News.
070416 I beg you therefore, be imitators of me.
070417 Because of this I have sent Timothy to you, who is my beloved and faithful child in the Lord, who will remind you of my ways which are in Christ, even as I teach everywhere in every assembly.
070418 Now some are puffed up, as though I were not coming to you.
070419 But I will come to you shortly, if the Lord is willing. And I will know, not the word of those who are puffed up, but the power.
070420 For the Kingdom of God is not in word, but in power.
070421 What do you want? Shall I come to you with a rod, or in love and a spirit of gentleness?
070501 It is actually reported that there is sexual immorality among you, and such sexual immorality as is not even named among the Gentiles, that one has his father's wife.
070502 You are puffed up, and didn't rather mourn, that he who had done this deed might be removed from among you.
070503 For I most certainly, as being absent in body but present in spirit, have already, as though I were present, judged him who has done this thing.
070504 In the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, you being gathered together, and my spirit, with the power of our Lord Jesus Christ,
070505 are to deliver such a one to Satan for the destruction of the flesh, that the spirit may be saved in the day of the Lord Jesus.
070506 Your boasting is not good. Don't you know that a little yeast leavens the whole lump?
070507 Purge out the old yeast, that you may be a new lump, even as you are unleavened. For indeed Christ, our Passover, has been sacrificed in our place.
070508 Therefore let us keep the feast, not with old yeast, neither with the yeast of malice and wickedness, but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth.
070509 I wrote to you in my letter to have no company with sexual sinners;
070510 yet not at all meaning with the sexual sinners of this world, or with the covetous and extortioners, or with idolaters; for then you would have to leave the world.
070511 But as it is, I wrote to you not to associate with anyone who is called a brother who is a sexual sinner, or covetous, or an idolater, or a slanderer, or a drunkard, or an extortioner. Don't even eat with such a person.
070512 For what have I to do with also judging those who are outside? Don't you judge those who are within?
070513 But those who are outside, God judges. "Put away the wicked man from among yourselves."
070601 Dare any of you, having a matter against his neighbor, go to law before the unrighteous, and not before the saints?
070602 Don't you know that the saints will judge the world? And if the world is judged by you, are you unworthy to judge the smallest matters?
070603 Don't you know that we will judge angels? How much more, things that pertain to this life?
070604 If then, you have to judge things pertaining to this life, do you set them to judge who are of no account in the assembly?
070605 I say this to move you to shame. Isn't there even one wise man among you who would be able to decide between his brothers?
070606 But brother goes to law with brother, and that before unbelievers!
070607 Therefore it is already altogether a defect in you, that you have lawsuits one with another. Why not rather be wronged? Why not rather be defrauded?
070608 No, but you yourselves do wrong, and defraud, and that against your brothers.
070609 Or don't you know that the unrighteous will not inherit the Kingdom of God? Don't be deceived. Neither the sexually immoral, nor idolaters, nor adulterers, nor male prostitutes, nor homosexuals,
070610 nor thieves, nor covetous, nor drunkards, nor slanderers, nor extortioners, will inherit the Kingdom of God.
070611 Such were some of you, but you were washed. But you were sanctified. But you were justified in the name of the Lord Jesus, and in the Spirit of our God.
070612 "All things are lawful for me," but not all things are expedient. "All things are lawful for me," but I will not be brought under the power of anything.
070613 "Foods for the belly, and the belly for foods," but God will bring to nothing both it and them. But the body is not for sexual immorality, but for the Lord; and the Lord for the body.
070614 Now God raised up the Lord, and will also raise us up by his power.
070615 Don't you know that your bodies are members of Christ? Shall I then take the members of Christ, and make them members of a prostitute? May it never be!
070616 Or don't you know that he who is joined to a prostitute is one body? For, "The two," says he, "will become one flesh."
070617 But he who is joined to the Lord is one spirit.
070618 Flee sexual immorality! "Every sin that a man does is outside the body," but he who commits sexual immorality sins against his own body.
070619 Or don't you know that your body is a temple of the Holy Spirit which is in you, which you have from God? You are not your own,
070620 for you were bought with a price. Therefore glorify God in your body and in your spirit, which are God's.
070701 Now concerning the things about which you wrote to me: it is good for a man not to touch a woman.
070702 But, because of sexual immoralities, let each man have his own wife, and let each woman have her own husband.
070703 Let the husband render to his wife the affection owed her, and likewise also the wife to her husband.
070704 The wife doesn't have authority over her own body, but the husband. Likewise also the husband doesn't have authority over his own body, but the wife.
070705 Don't deprive one another, unless it is by consent for a season, that you may give yourselves to fasting and prayer, and may be together again, that Satan doesn't tempt you because of your lack of self-control.
070706 But this I say by way of concession, not of commandment.
070707 Yet I wish that all men were like me. However each man has his own gift from God, one of this kind, and another of that kind.
070708 But I say to the unmarried and to widows, it is good for them if they remain even as I am.
070709 But if they don't have self-control, let them marry. For it's better to marry than to burn.
070710 But to the married I command--not I, but the Lord--that the wife not leave her husband
070711 (but if she departs, let her remain unmarried, or else be reconciled to her husband), and that the husband not leave his wife.
070712 But to the rest I--not the Lord--say, if any brother has an unbelieving wife, and she is content to live with him, let him not leave her.
070713 The woman who has an unbelieving husband, and he is content to live with her, let her not leave her husband.
070714 For the unbelieving husband is sanctified in the wife, and the unbelieving wife is sanctified in the husband. Otherwise your children would be unclean, but now they are holy.
070715 Yet if the unbeliever departs, let there be separation. The brother or the sister is not under bondage in such cases, but God has called us in peace.
070716 For how do you know, wife, whether you will save your husband? Or how do you know, husband, whether you will save your wife?
070717 Only, as the Lord has distributed to each man, as God has called each, so let him walk. So I command in all the assemblies.
070718 Was anyone called having been circumcised? Let him not become uncircumcised. Has anyone been called in uncircumcision? Let him not be circumcised.
070719 Circumcision is nothing, and uncircumcision is nothing, but the keeping of the commandments of God.
070720 Let each man stay in that calling in which he was called.
070721 Were you called being a bondservant? Don't let that bother you, but if you get an opportunity to become free, use it.
070722 For he who was called in the Lord being a bondservant is the Lord's free man. Likewise he who was called being free is Christ's bondservant.
070723 You were bought with a price. Don't become bondservants of men.
070724 Brothers, let each man, in whatever condition he was called, stay in that condition with God.
070725 Now concerning virgins, I have no commandment from the Lord, but I give my judgment as one who has obtained mercy from the Lord to be trustworthy.
070726 I think that it is good therefore, because of the distress that is on us, that it is good for a man to be as he is.
070727 Are you bound to a wife? Don't seek to be freed. Are you free from a wife? Don't seek a wife.
070728 But if you marry, you have not sinned. If a virgin marries, she has not sinned. Yet such will have oppression in the flesh, and I want to spare you.
070729 But I say this, brothers: the time is short, that from now on, both those who have wives may be as though they had none;
070730 and those who weep, as though they didn't weep; and those who rejoice, as though they didn't rejoice; and those who buy, as though they didn't possess;
070731 and those who use the world, as not using it to the fullest. For the mode of this world passes away.
070732 But I desire to have you to be free from cares. He who is unmarried is concerned for the things of the Lord, how he may please the Lord;
070733 but he who is married is concerned about the things of the world, how he may please his wife.
070734 There is also a difference between a wife and a virgin. The unmarried woman cares about the things of the Lord, that she may be holy both in body and in spirit. But she who is married cares about the things of the world--how she may please her husband.
070735 This I say for your own profit; not that I may ensnare you, but for that which is appropriate, and that you may attend to the Lord without distraction.
070736 But if any man thinks that he is behaving inappropriately toward his virgin, if she is past the flower of her age, and if need so requires, let him do what he desires. He doesn't sin. Let them marry.
070737 But he who stands steadfast in his heart, having no necessity, but has power over his own heart, to keep his own virgin, does well.
070738 So then both he who gives his own virgin in marriage does well, and he who doesn't give her in marriage does better.
070739 A wife is bound by law for as long as her husband lives; but if the husband is dead, she is free to be married to whoever she desires, only in the Lord.
070740 But she is happier if she stays as she is, in my judgment, and I think that I also have God's Spirit.
070801 Now concerning things sacrificed to idols: We know that we all have knowledge. Knowledge puffs up, but love builds up.
070802 But if anyone thinks that he knows anything, he doesn't yet know as he ought to know.
070803 But if anyone loves God, the same is known by him.
070804 Therefore concerning the eating of things sacrificed to idols, we know that no idol is anything in the world, and that there is no other God but one.
070805 For though there are things that are called "gods," whether in the heavens or on earth; as there are many "gods" and many "lords;"
070806 yet to us there is one God, the Father, of whom are all things, and we for him; and one Lord, Jesus Christ, through whom are all things, and we live through him.
070807 However, that knowledge isn't in all men. But some, with consciousness of the idol until now, eat as of a thing sacrificed to an idol, and their conscience, being weak, is defiled.
070808 But food will not commend us to God. For neither, if we don't eat, are we the worse; nor, if we eat, are we the better.
070809 But be careful that by no means does this liberty of yours become a stumbling block to the weak.
070810 For if a man sees you who have knowledge sitting in an idol's temple, won't his conscience, if he is weak, be emboldened to eat things sacrificed to idols?
070811 And through your knowledge, he who is weak perishes, the brother for whose sake Christ died.
070812 Thus, sinning against the brothers, and wounding their conscience when it is weak, you sin against Christ.
070813 Therefore, if food causes my brother to stumble, I will eat no meat forevermore, that I don't cause my brother to stumble.
070901 Am I not free? Am I not an apostle? Haven't I seen Jesus Christ, our Lord? Aren't you my work in the Lord?
070902 If to others I am not an apostle, yet at least I am to you; for you are the seal of my apostleship in the Lord.
070903 My defense to those who examine me is this.
070904 Have we no right to eat and to drink?
070905 Have we no right to take along a wife who is a believer, even as the rest of the apostles, and the brothers of the Lord, and Cephas?
070906 Or have only Barnabas and I no right to not work?
070907 What soldier ever serves at his own expense? Who plants a vineyard, and doesn't eat of its fruit? Or who feeds a flock, and doesn't drink from the flock's milk?
070908 Do I speak these things according to the ways of men? Or doesn't the law also say the same thing?
070909 For it is written in the law of Moses, "You shall not muzzle an ox while it treads out the grain." Is it for the oxen that God cares,
070910 or does he say it assuredly for our sake? Yes, it was written for our sake, because he who plows ought to plow in hope, and he who threshes in hope should partake of his hope.
070911 If we sowed to you spiritual things, is it a great thing if we reap your fleshly things?
070912 If others partake of this right over you, don't we yet more? Nevertheless we did not use this right, but we bear all things, that we may cause no hindrance to the Good News of Christ.
070913 Don't you know that those who serve around sacred things eat from the things of the temple, and those who wait on the altar have their portion with the altar?
070914 Even so the Lord ordained that those who proclaim the Good News should live from the Good News.
070915 But I have used none of these things, and I don't write these things that it may be done so in my case; for I would rather die, than that anyone should make my boasting void.
070916 For if I preach the Good News, I have nothing to boast about; for necessity is laid on me; but woe is to me, if I don't preach the Good News.
070917 For if I do this of my own will, I have a reward. But if not of my own will, I have a stewardship entrusted to me.
070918 What then is my reward? That, when I preach the Good News, I may present the Good News of Christ without charge, so as not to abuse my authority in the Good News.
070919 For though I was free from all, I brought myself under bondage to all, that I might gain the more.
070920 To the Jews I became as a Jew, that I might gain Jews; to those who are under the law, as under the law, that I might gain those who are under the law;
070921 to those who are without law, as without law (not being without law toward God, but under law toward Christ), that I might win those who are without law.
070922 To the weak I became as weak, that I might gain the weak. I have become all things to all men, that I may by all means save some.
070923 Now I do this for the sake of the Good News, that I may be a joint partaker of it.
070924 Don't you know that those who run in a race all run, but one receives the prize? Run like that, that you may win.
070925 Every man who strives in the games exercises self-control in all things. Now they do it to receive a corruptible crown, but we an incorruptible.
070926 I therefore run like that, as not uncertainly. I fight like that, as not beating the air,
070927 but I beat my body and bring it into submission, lest by any means, after I have preached to others, I myself should be rejected.
071001 Now I would not have you ignorant, brothers, that our fathers were all under the cloud, and all passed through the sea;
071002 and were all baptized into Moses in the cloud and in the sea;
071003 and all ate the same spiritual food;
071004 and all drank the same spiritual drink. For they drank of a spiritual rock that followed them, and the rock was Christ.
071005 However with most of them, God was not well pleased, for they were overthrown in the wilderness.
071006 Now these things were our examples, to the intent we should not lust after evil things, as they also lusted.
071007 Neither be idolaters, as some of them were. As it is written, "The people sat down to eat and drink, and rose up to play."
071008 Neither let us commit sexual immorality, as some of them committed, and in one day twenty-three thousand fell.
071009 Neither let us test the Lord, as some of them tested, and perished by the serpents.
071010 Neither grumble, as some of them also grumbled, and perished by the destroyer.
071011 Now all these things happened to them by way of example, and they were written for our admonition, on whom the ends of the ages have come.
071012 Therefore let him who thinks he stands be careful that he doesn't fall.
071013 No temptation has taken you except what is common to man. God is faithful, who will not allow you to be tempted above what you are able, but will with the temptation also make the way of escape, that you may be able to endure it.
071014 Therefore, my beloved, flee from idolatry.
071015 I speak as to wise men. Judge what I say.
071016 The cup of blessing which we bless, isn't it a sharing of the blood of Christ? The bread which we break, isn't it a sharing of the body of Christ?
071017 Because there is one loaf of bread, we, who are many, are one body; for we all partake of the one loaf of bread.
071018 Consider Israel according to the flesh. Don't those who eat the sacrifices participate in the altar?
071019 What am I saying then? That a thing sacrificed to idols is anything, or that an idol is anything?
071020 But I say that the things which the Gentiles sacrifice, they sacrifice to demons, and not to God, and I don't desire that you would have fellowship with demons.
071021 You can't both drink the cup of the Lord and the cup of demons. You can't both partake of the table of the Lord, and of the table of demons.
071022 Or do we provoke the Lord to jealousy? Are we stronger than he?
071023 "All things are lawful for me," but not all things are profitable. "All things are lawful for me," but not all things build up.
071024 Let no one seek his own, but each one his neighbor's good.
071025 Whatever is sold in the butcher shop, eat, asking no question for the sake of conscience,
071026 for "the earth is the Lord's, and its fullness."
071027 But if one of those who don't believe invites you to a meal, and you are inclined to go, eat whatever is set before you, asking no questions for the sake of conscience.
071028 But if anyone says to you, "This was offered to idols," don't eat it for the sake of the one who told you, and for the sake of conscience. For "the earth is the Lord's, and all its fullness."
071029 Conscience, I say, not your own, but the other's conscience. For why is my liberty judged by another conscience?
071030 If I partake with thankfulness, why am I denounced for that for which I give thanks?
071031 Whether therefore you eat, or drink, or whatever you do, do all to the glory of God.
071032 Give no occasions for stumbling, either to Jews, or to Greeks, or to the assembly of God;
071033 even as I also please all men in all things, not seeking my own profit, but the profit of the many, that they may be saved.
071101 Be imitators of me, even as I also am of Christ.
071102 Now I praise you, brothers, that you remember me in all things, and hold firm the traditions, even as I delivered them to you.
071103 But I would have you know that the head of every man is Christ, and the head of the woman is the man, and the head of Christ is God.
071104 Every man praying or prophesying, having his head covered, dishonors his head.
071105 But every woman praying or prophesying with her head unveiled dishonors her head. For it is one and the same thing as if she were shaved.
071106 For if a woman is not covered, let her also be shorn. But if it is shameful for a woman to be shorn or shaved, let her be covered.
071107 For a man indeed ought not to have his head covered, because he is the image and glory of God, but the woman is the glory of the man.
071108 For man is not from woman, but woman from man;
071109 for neither was man created for the woman, but woman for the man.
071110 For this cause the woman ought to have authority on her head, because of the angels.
071111 Nevertheless, neither is the woman independent of the man, nor the man independent of the woman, in the Lord.
071112 For as woman came from man, so a man also comes through a woman; but all things are from God.
071113 Judge for yourselves. Is it appropriate that a woman pray to God unveiled?
071114 Doesn't even nature itself teach you that if a man has long hair, it is a dishonor to him?
071115 But if a woman has long hair, it is a glory to her, for her hair is given to her for a covering.
071116 But if any man seems to be contentious, we have no such custom, neither do God's assemblies.
071117 But in giving you this command, I don't praise you, that you come together not for the better but for the worse.
071118 For first of all, when you come together in the assembly, I hear that divisions exist among you, and I partly believe it.
071119 For there also must be factions among you, that those who are approved may be revealed among you.
071120 When therefore you assemble yourselves together, it is not the Lord's supper that you eat.
071121 For in your eating each one takes his own supper first. One is hungry, and another is drunken.
071122 What, don't you have houses to eat and to drink in? Or do you despise God's assembly, and put them to shame who don't have? What shall I tell you? Shall I praise you? In this I don't praise you.
071123 For I received from the Lord that which also I delivered to you, that the Lord Jesus on the night in which he was betrayed took bread.
071124 When he had given thanks, he broke it, and said, "Take, eat. This is my body, which is broken for you. Do this in memory of me."
071125 In the same way he also took the cup, after supper, saying, "This cup is the new covenant in my blood. Do this, as often as you drink, in memory of me."
071126 For as often as you eat this bread and drink this cup, you proclaim the Lord's death until he comes.
071127 Therefore whoever eats this bread or drinks the Lord's cup in a manner unworthy of the Lord will be guilty of the body and the blood of the Lord.
071128 But let a man examine himself, and so let him eat of the bread, and drink of the cup.
071129 For he who eats and drinks in an unworthy manner eats and drinks judgment to himself, if he doesn't discern the Lord's body.
071130 For this cause many among you are weak and sickly, and not a few sleep.
071131 For if we discerned ourselves, we wouldn't be judged.
071132 But when we are judged, we are punished by the Lord, that we may not be condemned with the world.
071133 Therefore, my brothers, when you come together to eat, wait one for another.
071134 But if anyone is hungry, let him eat at home, lest your coming together be for judgment. The rest I will set in order whenever I come.
071201 Now concerning spiritual things, brothers, I don't want you to be ignorant.
071202 You know that when you were heathen, you were led away to those mute idols, however you might be led.
071203 Therefore I make known to you that no man speaking by God's Spirit says, "Jesus is accursed." No one can say, "Jesus is Lord," but by the Holy Spirit.
071204 Now there are various kinds of gifts, but the same Spirit.
071205 There are various kinds of service, and the same Lord.
071206 There are various kinds of workings, but the same God, who works all things in all.
071207 But to each one is given the manifestation of the Spirit for the profit of all.
071208 For to one is given through the Spirit the word of wisdom, and to another the word of knowledge, according to the same Spirit;
071209 to another faith, by the same Spirit; and to another gifts of healings, by the same Spirit;
071210 and to another workings of miracles; and to another prophecy; and to another discerning of spirits; to another different kinds of languages; and to another the interpretation of languages.
071211 But the one and the same Spirit works all of these, distributing to each one separately as he desires.
071212 For as the body is one, and has many members, and all the members of the body, being many, are one body; so also is Christ.
071213 For in one Spirit we were all baptized into one body, whether Jews or Greeks, whether bond or free; and were all given to drink into one Spirit.
071214 For the body is not one member, but many.
071215 If the foot would say, "Because I'm not the hand, I'm not part of the body," it is not therefore not part of the body.
071216 If the ear would say, "Because I'm not the eye, I'm not part of the body," it's not therefore not part of the body.
071217 If the whole body were an eye, where would the hearing be? If the whole were hearing, where would the smelling be?
071218 But now God has set the members, each one of them, in the body, just as he desired.
071219 If they were all one member, where would the body be?
071220 But now they are many members, but one body.
071221 The eye can't tell the hand, "I have no need for you," or again the head to the feet, "I have no need for you."
071222 No, much rather, those members of the body which seem to be weaker are necessary.
071223 Those parts of the body which we think to be less honorable, on those we bestow more abundant honor; and our unpresentable parts have more abundant propriety;
071224 whereas our presentable parts have no such need. But God composed the body together, giving more abundant honor to the inferior part,
071225 that there should be no division in the body, but that the members should have the same care for one another.
071226 When one member suffers, all the members suffer with it. Or when one member is honored, all the members rejoice with it.
071227 Now you are the body of Christ, and members individually.
071228 God has set some in the assembly: first apostles, second prophets, third teachers, then miracle workers, then gifts of healings, helps, governments, and various kinds of languages.
071229 Are all apostles? Are all prophets? Are all teachers? Are all miracle workers?
071230 Do all have gifts of healings? Do all speak with various languages? Do all interpret?
071231 But earnestly desire the best gifts. Moreover, I show a most excellent way to you.
071301 If I speak with the languages of men and of angels, but don't have love, I have become sounding brass, or a clanging cymbal.
071302 If I have the gift of prophecy, and know all mysteries and all knowledge; and if I have all faith, so as to remove mountains, but don't have love, I am nothing.
071303 If I dole out all my goods to feed the poor, and if I give my body to be burned, but don't have love, it profits me nothing.
071304 Love is patient and is kind; love doesn't envy. Love doesn't brag, is not proud,
071305 doesn't behave itself inappropriately, doesn't seek its own way, is not provoked, takes no account of evil;
071306 doesn't rejoice in unrighteousness, but rejoices with the truth;
071307 bears all things, believes all things, hopes all things, endures all things.
071308 Love never fails. But where there are prophecies, they will be done away with. Where there are various languages, they will cease. Where there is knowledge, it will be done away with.
071309 For we know in part, and we prophesy in part;
071310 but when that which is complete has come, then that which is partial will be done away with.
071311 When I was a child, I spoke as a child, I felt as a child, I thought as a child. Now that I have become a man, I have put away childish things.
071312 For now we see in a mirror, dimly, but then face to face. Now I know in part, but then I will know fully, even as I was also fully known.
071313 But now faith, hope, and love remain--these three. The greatest of these is love.
071401 Follow after love, and earnestly desire spiritual gifts, but especially that you may prophesy.
071402 For he who speaks in another language speaks not to men, but to God; for no one understands; but in the Spirit he speaks mysteries.
071403 But he who prophesies speaks to men for their edification, exhortation, and consolation.
071404 He who speaks in another language edifies himself, but he who prophesies edifies the assembly.
071405 Now I desire to have you all speak with other languages, but rather that you would prophesy. For he is greater who prophesies than he who speaks with other languages, unless he interprets, that the assembly may be built up.
071406 But now, brothers, if I come to you speaking with other languages, what would I profit you, unless I speak to you either by way of revelation, or of knowledge, or of prophesying, or of teaching?
071407 Even things without life, giving a voice, whether pipe or harp, if they didn't give a distinction in the sounds, how would it be known what is piped or harped?
071408 For if the trumpet gave an uncertain sound, who would prepare himself for war?
071409 So also you, unless you uttered by the tongue words easy to understand, how would it be known what is spoken? For you would be speaking into the air.
071410 There are, it may be, so many kinds of sounds in the world, and none of them is without meaning.
071411 If then I don't know the meaning of the sound, I would be to him who speaks a foreigner, and he who speaks would be a foreigner to me.
071412 So also you, since you are zealous for spiritual gifts, seek that you may abound to the building up of the assembly.
071413 Therefore let him who speaks in another language pray that he may interpret.
071414 For if I pray in another language, my spirit prays, but my understanding is unfruitful.
071415 What is it then? I will pray with the spirit, and I will pray with the understanding also. I will sing with the spirit, and I will sing with the understanding also.
071416 Otherwise if you bless with the spirit, how will he who fills the place of the unlearned say the "Amen" at your giving of thanks, seeing he doesn't know what you say?
071417 For you most certainly give thanks well, but the other person is not built up.
071418 I thank my God, I speak with other languages more than you all.
071419 However in the assembly I would rather speak five words with my understanding, that I might instruct others also, than ten thousand words in another language.
071420 Brothers, don't be children in thoughts, yet in malice be babies, but in thoughts be mature.
071421 In the law it is written, "By men of strange languages and by the lips of strangers I will speak to this people. Not even thus will they hear me, says the Lord."
071422 Therefore other languages are for a sign, not to those who believe, but to the unbelieving; but prophesying is for a sign, not to the unbelieving, but to those who believe.
071423 If therefore the whole assembly is assembled together and all speak with other languages, and unlearned or unbelieving people come in, won't they say that you are crazy?
071424 But if all prophesy, and someone unbelieving or unlearned comes in, he is reproved by all, and he is judged by all.
071425 And thus the secrets of his heart are revealed. So he will fall down on his face and worship God, declaring that God is among you indeed.
071426 What is it then, brothers? When you come together, each one of you has a psalm, has a teaching, has a revelation, has another language, has an interpretation. Let all things be done to build each other up.
071427 If any man speaks in another language, let it be two, or at the most three, and in turn; and let one interpret.
071428 But if there is no interpreter, let him keep silent in the assembly, and let him speak to himself, and to God.
071429 Let the prophets speak, two or three, and let the others discern.
071430 But if a revelation is made to another sitting by, let the first keep silent.
071431 For you all can prophesy one by one, that all may learn, and all may be exhorted.
071432 The spirits of the prophets are subject to the prophets,
071433 for God is not a God of confusion, but of peace. As in all the assemblies of the saints,
071434 let your wives keep silent in the assemblies, for it has not been permitted for them to speak; but let them be in subjection, as the law also says.
071435 If they desire to learn anything, let them ask their own husbands at home, for it is shameful for a woman to chatter in the assembly.
071436 What? Was it from you that the word of God went out? Or did it come to you alone?
071437 If any man thinks himself to be a prophet, or spiritual, let him recognize the things which I write to you, that they are the commandment of the Lord.
071438 But if anyone is ignorant, let him be ignorant.
071439 Therefore, brothers, desire earnestly to prophesy, and don't forbid speaking with other languages.
071440 Let all things be done decently and in order.
071501 Now I declare to you, brothers, the Good News which I preached to you, which also you received, in which you also stand,
071502 by which also you are saved, if you hold firmly the word which I preached to you--unless you believed in vain.
071503 For I delivered to you first of all that which I also received: that Christ died for our sins according to the Scriptures,
071504 that he was buried, that he was raised on the third day according to the Scriptures,
071505 and that he appeared to Cephas, then to the twelve.
071506 Then he appeared to over five hundred brothers at once, most of whom remain until now, but some have also fallen asleep.
071507 Then he appeared to James, then to all the apostles,
071508 and last of all, as to the child born at the wrong time, he appeared to me also.
071509 For I am the least of the apostles, who is not worthy to be called an apostle, because I persecuted the assembly of God.
071510 But by the grace of God I am what I am. His grace which was bestowed on me was not futile, but I worked more than all of them; yet not I, but the grace of God which was with me.
071511 Whether then it is I or they, so we preach, and so you believed.
071512 Now if Christ is preached, that he has been raised from the dead, how do some among you say that there is no resurrection of the dead?
071513 But if there is no resurrection of the dead, neither has Christ been raised.
071514 If Christ has not been raised, then our preaching is in vain, and your faith also is in vain.
071515 Yes, we are found false witnesses of God, because we testified about God that he raised up Christ, whom he didn't raise up, if it is so that the dead are not raised.
071516 For if the dead aren't raised, neither has Christ been raised.
071517 If Christ has not been raised, your faith is vain; you are still in your sins.
071518 Then they also who are fallen asleep in Christ have perished.
071519 If we have only hoped in Christ in this life, we are of all men most pitiable.
071520 But now Christ has been raised from the dead. He became the first fruits of those who are asleep.
071521 For since death came by man, the resurrection of the dead also came by man.
071522 For as in Adam all die, so also in Christ all will be made alive.
071523 But each in his own order: Christ the first fruits, then those who are Christ's, at his coming.
071524 Then the end comes, when he will deliver up the Kingdom to God, even the Father; when he will have abolished all rule and all authority and power.
071525 For he must reign until he has put all his enemies under his feet.
071526 The last enemy that will be abolished is death.
071527 For, "He put all things in subjection under his feet." But when he says, "All things are put in subjection," it is evident that he is excepted who subjected all things to him.
071528 When all things have been subjected to him, then the Son will also himself be subjected to him who subjected all things to him, that God may be all in all.
071529 Or else what will they do who are baptized for the dead? If the dead aren't raised at all, why then are they baptized for the dead?
071530 Why do we also stand in jeopardy every hour?
071531 I affirm, by the boasting in you which I have in Christ Jesus our Lord, I die daily.
071532 If I fought with animals at Ephesus for human purposes, what does it profit me? If the dead are not raised, then "let us eat and drink, for tomorrow we die."
071533 Don't be deceived! "Evil companionships corrupt good morals."
071534 Wake up righteously, and don't sin, for some have no knowledge of God. I say this to your shame.
071535 But someone will say, "How are the dead raised?" and, "With what kind of body do they come?"
071536 You foolish one, that which you yourself sow is not made alive unless it dies.
071537 That which you sow, you don't sow the body that will be, but a bare grain, maybe of wheat, or of some other kind.
071538 But God gives it a body even as it pleased him, and to each seed a body of its own.
071539 All flesh is not the same flesh, but there is one flesh of men, another flesh of animals, another of fish, and another of birds.
071540 There are also celestial bodies, and terrestrial bodies; but the glory of the celestial differs from that of the terrestrial.
071541 There is one glory of the sun, another glory of the moon, and another glory of the stars; for one star differs from another star in glory.
071542 So also is the resurrection of the dead. It is sown in corruption; it is raised in incorruption.
071543 It is sown in dishonor; it is raised in glory. It is sown in weakness; it is raised in power.
071544 It is sown a natural body; it is raised a spiritual body. There is a natural body and there is also a spiritual body.
071545 So also it is written, "The first man, Adam, became a living soul." The last Adam became a life-giving spirit.
071546 However that which is spiritual isn't first, but that which is natural, then that which is spiritual.
071547 The first man is of the earth, made of dust. The second man is the Lord from heaven.
071548 As is the one made of dust, such are those who are also made of dust; and as is the heavenly, such are they also that are heavenly.
071549 As we have borne the image of those made of dust, let's also bear the image of the heavenly.
071550 Now I say this, brothers, that flesh and blood can't inherit the Kingdom of God; neither does corruption inherit incorruption.
071551 Behold, I tell you a mystery. We will not all sleep, but we will all be changed,
071552 in a moment, in the twinkling of an eye, at the last trumpet. For the trumpet will sound, and the dead will be raised incorruptible, and we will be changed.
071553 For this corruptible must put on incorruption, and this mortal must put on immortality.
071554 But when this corruptible will have put on incorruption, and this mortal will have put on immortality, then what is written will happen: "Death is swallowed up in victory."
071555 "Death, where is your sting? Hades, where is your victory?"
071556 The sting of death is sin, and the power of sin is the law.
071557 But thanks be to God, who gives us the victory through our Lord Jesus Christ.
071558 Therefore, my beloved brothers, be steadfast, immovable, always abounding in the Lord's work, because you know that your labor is not in vain in the Lord.
071601 Now concerning the collection for the saints, as I commanded the assemblies of Galatia, you do likewise.
071602 On the first day of the week, let each one of you save, as he may prosper, that no collections be made when I come.
071603 When I arrive, I will send whoever you approve with letters to carry your gracious gift to Jerusalem.
071604 If it is appropriate for me to go also, they will go with me.
071605 But I will come to you when I have passed through Macedonia, for I am passing through Macedonia.
071606 But with you it may be that I will stay, or even winter, that you may send me on my journey wherever I go.
071607 For I do not wish to see you now in passing, but I hope to stay a while with you, if the Lord permits.
071608 But I will stay at Ephesus until Pentecost,
071609 for a great and effective door has opened to me, and there are many adversaries.
071610 Now if Timothy comes, see that he is with you without fear, for he does the work of the Lord, as I also do.
071611 Therefore let no one despise him. But set him forward on his journey in peace, that he may come to me; for I expect him with the brothers.
071612 Now concerning Apollos, the brother, I strongly urged him to come to you with the brothers; and it was not at all his desire to come now; but he will come when he has an opportunity.
071613 Watch! Stand firm in the faith! Be courageous! Be strong!
071614 Let all that you do be done in love.
071615 Now I beg you, brothers (you know the house of Stephanas, that it is the first fruits of Achaia, and that they have set themselves to serve the saints),
071616 that you also be in subjection to such, and to everyone who helps in the work and labors.
071617 I rejoice at the coming of Stephanas, Fortunatus, and Achaicus; for that which was lacking on your part, they supplied.
071618 For they refreshed my spirit and yours. Therefore acknowledge those who are like that.
071619 The assemblies of Asia greet you. Aquila and Priscilla greet you much in the Lord, together with the assembly that is in their house.
071620 All the brothers greet you. Greet one another with a holy kiss.
071621 This greeting is by me, Paul, with my own hand.
071622 If any man doesn't love the Lord Jesus Christ, let him be accursed. Come, Lord!
071623 The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with you.
071624 My love to all of you in Christ Jesus. Amen.
080101 Paul, an apostle of Christ Jesus through the will of God, and Timothy our brother, to the assembly of God which is at Corinth, with all the saints who are in the whole of Achaia:
080102 Grace to you and peace from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ.
080103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Father of mercies and God of all comfort;
080104 who comforts us in all our affliction, that we may be able to comfort those who are in any affliction, through the comfort with which we ourselves are comforted by God.
080105 For as the sufferings of Christ abound to us, even so our comfort also abounds through Christ.
080106 But if we are afflicted, it is for your comfort and salvation. If we are comforted, it is for your comfort, which produces in you the patient enduring of the same sufferings which we also suffer.
080107 Our hope for you is steadfast, knowing that, since you are partakers of the sufferings, so also are you of the comfort.
080108 For we don't desire to have you uninformed, brothers, concerning our affliction which happened to us in Asia, that we were weighed down exceedingly, beyond our power, so much that we despaired even of life.
080109 Yes, we ourselves have had the sentence of death within ourselves, that we should not trust in ourselves, but in God who raises the dead,
080110 who delivered us out of so great a death, and does deliver; on whom we have set our hope that he will also still deliver us;
080111 you also helping together on our behalf by your supplication; that, for the gift bestowed on us by means of many, thanks may be given by many persons on your behalf.
080112 For our boasting is this: the testimony of our conscience, that in holiness and sincerity of God, not in fleshly wisdom but in the grace of God we behaved ourselves in the world, and more abundantly toward you.
080113 For we write no other things to you, than what you read or even acknowledge, and I hope you will acknowledge to the end;
080114 as also you acknowledged us in part, that we are your boasting, even as you also are ours, in the day of our Lord Jesus.
080115 In this confidence, I was determined to come first to you, that you might have a second benefit;
080116 and by you to pass into Macedonia, and again from Macedonia to come to you, and to be sent forward by you on my journey to Judea.
080117 When I therefore was thus determined, did I show fickleness? Or the things that I purpose, do I purpose according to the flesh, that with me there should be the "Yes, yes" and the "No, no?"
080118 But as God is faithful, our word toward you was not "Yes and no."
080119 For the Son of God, Jesus Christ, who was preached among you by us, by me, Silvanus, and Timothy, was not "Yes and no," but in him is "Yes."
080120 For however many are the promises of God, in him is the "Yes." Therefore also through him is the "Amen," to the glory of God through us.
080121 Now he who establishes us with you in Christ, and anointed us, is God;
080122 who also sealed us, and gave us the down payment of the Spirit in our hearts.
080123 But I call God for a witness to my soul, that I didn't come to Corinth to spare you.
080124 Not that we have lordship over your faith, but are fellow workers with you for your joy. For you stand firm in faith.
080201 But I determined this for myself, that I would not come to you again in sorrow.
080202 For if I make you sorry, then who will make me glad but he who is made sorry by me?
080203 And I wrote this very thing to you, so that, when I came, I wouldn't have sorrow from them of whom I ought to rejoice; having confidence in you all, that my joy would be shared by all of you.
080204 For out of much affliction and anguish of heart I wrote to you with many tears, not that you should be made sorry, but that you might know the love that I have so abundantly for you.
080205 But if any has caused sorrow, he has caused sorrow, not to me, but in part (that I not press too heavily) to you all.
080206 Sufficient to such a one is this punishment which was inflicted by the many;
080207 so that on the contrary you should rather forgive him and comfort him, lest by any means such a one should be swallowed up with his excessive sorrow.
080208 Therefore I beg you to confirm your love toward him.
080209 For to this end I also wrote, that I might know the proof of you, whether you are obedient in all things.
080210 Now I also forgive whomever you forgive anything. For if indeed I have forgiven anything, I have forgiven that one for your sakes in the presence of Christ,
080211 that no advantage may be gained over us by Satan; for we are not ignorant of his schemes.
080212 Now when I came to Troas for the Good News of Christ, and when a door was opened to me in the Lord,
080213 I had no relief for my spirit, because I didn't find Titus, my brother, but taking my leave of them, I went out into Macedonia.
080214 Now thanks be to God, who always leads us in triumph in Christ, and reveals through us the sweet aroma of his knowledge in every place.
080215 For we are a sweet aroma of Christ to God, in those who are saved, and in those who perish;
080216 to the one a stench from death to death; to the other a sweet aroma from life to life. Who is sufficient for these things?
080217 For we are not as so many, peddling the word of God. But as of sincerity, but as of God, in the sight of God, we speak in Christ.
080301 Are we beginning again to commend ourselves? Or do we need, as do some, letters of commendation to you or from you?
080302 You are our letter, written in our hearts, known and read by all men;
080303 being revealed that you are a letter of Christ, served by us, written not with ink, but with the Spirit of the living God; not in tablets of stone, but in tablets that are hearts of flesh.
080304 Such confidence we have through Christ toward God;
080305 not that we are sufficient of ourselves, to account anything as from ourselves; but our sufficiency is from God;
080306 who also made us sufficient as servants of a new covenant; not of the letter, but of the Spirit. For the letter kills, but the Spirit gives life.
080307 But if the service of death, written engraved on stones, came with glory, so that the children of Israel could not look steadfastly on the face of Moses for the glory of his face; which was passing away:
080308 won't service of the Spirit be with much more glory?
080309 For if the service of condemnation has glory, the service of righteousness exceeds much more in glory.
080310 For most certainly that which has been made glorious has not been made glorious in this respect, by reason of the glory that surpasses.
080311 For if that which passes away was with glory, much more that which remains is in glory.
080312 Having therefore such a hope, we use great boldness of speech,
080313 and not as Moses, who put a veil on his face, that the children of Israel wouldn't look steadfastly on the end of that which was passing away.
080314 But their minds were hardened, for until this very day at the reading of the old covenant the same veil remains, because in Christ it passes away.
080315 But to this day, when Moses is read, a veil lies on their heart.
080316 But whenever one turns to the Lord, the veil is taken away.
080317 Now the Lord is the Spirit and where the Spirit of the Lord is, there is liberty.
080318 But we all, with unveiled face beholding as in a mirror the glory of the Lord, are transformed into the same image from glory to glory, even as from the Lord, the Spirit.
080401 Therefore seeing we have this ministry, even as we obtained mercy, we don't faint.
080402 But we have renounced the hidden things of shame, not walking in craftiness, nor handling the word of God deceitfully; but by the manifestation of the truth commending ourselves to every man's conscience in the sight of God.
080403 Even if our Good News is veiled, it is veiled in those who perish;
080404 in whom the god of this world has blinded the minds of the unbelieving, that the light of the Good News of the glory of Christ, who is the image of God, should not dawn on them.
080405 For we don't preach ourselves, but Christ Jesus as Lord, and ourselves as your servants for Jesus' sake;
080406 seeing it is God who said, "Light will shine out of darkness," who has shone in our hearts, to give the light of the knowledge of the glory of God in the face of Jesus Christ.
080407 But we have this treasure in clay vessels, that the exceeding greatness of the power may be of God, and not from ourselves.
080408 We are pressed on every side, yet not crushed; perplexed, yet not to despair;
080409 pursued, yet not forsaken; struck down, yet not destroyed;
080410 always carrying in the body the putting to death of the Lord Jesus, that the life of Jesus may also be revealed in our body.
080411 For we who live are always delivered to death for Jesus' sake, that the life also of Jesus may be revealed in our mortal flesh.
080412 So then death works in us, but life in you.
080413 But having the same spirit of faith, according to that which is written, "I believed, and therefore I spoke." We also believe, and therefore also we speak;
080414 knowing that he who raised the Lord Jesus will raise us also with Jesus, and will present us with you.
080415 For all things are for your sakes, that the grace, being multiplied through the many, may cause the thanksgiving to abound to the glory of God.
080416 Therefore we don't faint, but though our outward man is decaying, yet our inward man is renewed day by day.
080417 For our light affliction, which is for the moment, works for us more and more exceedingly an eternal weight of glory;
080418 while we don't look at the things which are seen, but at the things which are not seen. For the things which are seen are temporal, but the things which are not seen are eternal.
080501 For we know that if the earthly house of our tent is dissolved, we have a building from God, a house not made with hands, eternal, in the heavens.
080502 For most certainly in this we groan, longing to be clothed with our habitation which is from heaven;
080503 if so be that being clothed we will not be found naked.
080504 For indeed we who are in this tent do groan, being burdened; not that we desire to be unclothed, but that we desire to be clothed, that what is mortal may be swallowed up by life.
080505 Now he who made us for this very thing is God, who also gave to us the down payment of the Spirit.
080506 Therefore, we are always confident and know that while we are at home in the body, we are absent from the Lord;
080507 for we walk by faith, not by sight.
080508 We are of good courage, I say, and are willing rather to be absent from the body, and to be at home with the Lord.
080509 Therefore also we make it our aim, whether at home or absent, to be well pleasing to him.
080510 For we must all be revealed before the judgment seat of Christ; that each one may receive the things in the body, according to what he has done, whether good or bad.
080511 Knowing therefore the fear of the Lord, we persuade men, but we are revealed to God; and I hope that we are revealed also in your consciences.
080512 For we are not commending ourselves to you again, but speak as giving you occasion of boasting on our behalf, that you may have something to answer those who boast in appearance, and not in heart.
080513 For if we are beside ourselves, it is for God. Or if we are of sober mind, it is for you.
080514 For the love of Christ constrains us; because we judge thus, that one died for all, therefore all died.
080515 He died for all, that those who live should no longer live to themselves, but to him who for their sakes died and rose again.
080516 Therefore we know no one after the flesh from now on. Even though we have known Christ after the flesh, yet now we know him so no more.
080517 Therefore if anyone is in Christ, he is a new creation. The old things have passed away. Behold, all things have become new.
080518 But all things are of God, who reconciled us to himself through Jesus Christ, and gave to us the ministry of reconciliation;
080519 namely, that God was in Christ reconciling the world to himself, not reckoning to them their trespasses, and having committed to us the word of reconciliation.
080520 We are therefore ambassadors on behalf of Christ, as though God were entreating by us: we beg you on behalf of Christ, be reconciled to God.
080521 For him who knew no sin he made to be sin on our behalf; so that in him we might become the righteousness of God.
080601 Working together, we entreat also that you not receive the grace of God in vain,
080602 for he says, "At an acceptable time I listened to you, in a day of salvation I helped you." Behold, now is the acceptable time. Behold, now is the day of salvation.
080603 We give no occasion of stumbling in anything, that our service may not be blamed,
080604 but in everything commending ourselves, as servants of God, in great endurance, in afflictions, in hardships, in distresses,
080605 in beatings, in imprisonments, in riots, in labors, in watchings, in fastings;
080606 in pureness, in knowledge, in patience, in kindness, in the Holy Spirit, in sincere love,
080607 in the word of truth, in the power of God; by the armor of righteousness on the right hand and on the left,
080608 by glory and dishonor, by evil report and good report; as deceivers, and yet true;
080609 as unknown, and yet well known; as dying, and behold, we live; as punished, and not killed;
080610 as sorrowful, yet always rejoicing; as poor, yet making many rich; as having nothing, and yet possessing all things.
080611 Our mouth is open to you, Corinthians. Our heart is enlarged.
080612 You are not restricted by us, but you are restricted by your own affections.
080613 Now in return, I speak as to my children, you also be open wide.
080614 Don't be unequally yoked with unbelievers, for what fellowship have righteousness and iniquity? Or what fellowship has light with darkness?
080615 What agreement has Christ with Belial? Or what portion has a believer with an unbeliever?
080616 What agreement has a temple of God with idols? For you are a temple of the living God. Even as God said, "I will dwell in them, and walk in them; and I will be their God, and they will be my people."
080617 Therefore, "'Come out from among them, and be separate,' says the Lord. 'Touch no unclean thing. I will receive you.
080618 I will be to you a Father. You will be to me sons and daughters,' says the Lord Almighty."
080701 Having therefore these promises, beloved, let us cleanse ourselves from all defilement of flesh and spirit, perfecting holiness in the fear of God.
080702 Open your hearts to us. We wronged no one. We corrupted no one. We took advantage of no one.
080703 I say this not to condemn you, for I have said before, that you are in our hearts to die together and live together.
080704 Great is my boldness of speech toward you. Great is my boasting on your behalf. I am filled with comfort. I overflow with joy in all our affliction.
080705 For even when we had come into Macedonia, our flesh had no relief, but we were afflicted on every side. Fightings were outside. Fear was inside.
080706 Nevertheless, he who comforts the lowly, God, comforted us by the coming of Titus;
080707 and not by his coming only, but also by the comfort with which he was comforted in you, while he told us of your longing, your mourning, and your zeal for me; so that I rejoiced still more.
080708 For though I made you sorry with my letter, I do not regret it, though I did regret it. For I see that my letter made you sorry, though just for a while.
080709 I now rejoice, not that you were made sorry, but that you were made sorry to repentance. For you were made sorry in a godly way, that you might suffer loss by us in nothing.
080710 For godly sorrow works repentance to salvation, which brings no regret. But the sorrow of the world works death.
080711 For behold, this same thing, that you were made sorry in a godly way, what earnest care it worked in you. Yes, what defense, indignation, fear, longing, zeal, and vengeance! In everything you demonstrated yourselves to be pure in the matter.
080712 So although I wrote to you, I wrote not for his cause that did the wrong, nor for his cause that suffered the wrong, but that your earnest care for us might be revealed in you in the sight of God.
080713 Therefore we have been comforted. In our comfort we rejoiced the more exceedingly for the joy of Titus, because his spirit has been refreshed by you all.
080714 For if in anything I have boasted to him on your behalf, I was not disappointed. But as we spoke all things to you in truth, so our glorying also which I made before Titus was found to be truth.
080715 His affection is more abundantly toward you, while he remembers all of your obedience, how with fear and trembling you received him.
080716 I rejoice that in everything I am of good courage concerning you.
080801 Moreover, brothers, we make known to you the grace of God which has been given in the assemblies of Macedonia;
080802 how that in much proof of affliction the abundance of their joy and their deep poverty abounded to the riches of their liberality.
080803 For according to their power, I testify, yes and beyond their power, they gave of their own accord,
080804 begging us with much entreaty to receive this grace and the fellowship in the service to the saints.
080805 This was not as we had hoped, but first they gave their own selves to the Lord, and to us through the will of God.
080806 So we urged Titus, that as he made a beginning before, so he would also complete in you this grace.
080807 But as you abound in everything, in faith, utterance, knowledge, all earnestness, and in your love to us, see that you also abound in this grace.
080808 I speak not by way of commandment, but as proving through the earnestness of others the sincerity also of your love.
080809 For you know the grace of our Lord Jesus Christ, that, though he was rich, yet for your sakes he became poor, that you through his poverty might become rich.
080810 I give a judgment in this: for this is expedient for you, who were the first to start a year ago, not only to do, but also to be willing.
080811 But now complete the doing also, that as there was the readiness to be willing, so there may be the completion also out of your ability.
080812 For if the readiness is there, it is acceptable according to what you have, not according to what you don't have.
080813 For this is not that others may be eased and you distressed,
080814 but for equality. Your abundance at this present time supplies their lack, that their abundance also may become a supply for your lack; that there may be equality.
080815 As it is written, "He who gathered much had nothing left over, and he who gathered little had no lack."
080816 But thanks be to God, who puts the same earnest care for you into the heart of Titus.
080817 For he indeed accepted our exhortation, but being himself very earnest, he went out to you of his own accord.
080818 We have sent together with him the brother whose praise in the Good News is known through all the assemblies.
080819 Not only so, but who was also appointed by the assemblies to travel with us in this grace, which is served by us to the glory of the Lord himself, and to show our readiness.
080820 We are avoiding this, that any man should blame us concerning this abundance which is administered by us.
080821 Having regard for honorable things, not only in the sight of the Lord, but also in the sight of men.
080822 We have sent with them our brother, whom we have many times proved earnest in many things, but now much more earnest, by reason of the great confidence which he has in you.
080823 As for Titus, he is my partner and fellow worker for you. As for our brothers, they are the apostles of the assemblies, the glory of Christ.
080824 Therefore show the proof of your love to them in front of the assemblies, and of our boasting on your behalf.
080901 It is indeed unnecessary for me to write to you concerning the service to the saints,
080902 for I know your readiness, of which I boast on your behalf to them of Macedonia, that Achaia has been prepared for a year past. Your zeal has stirred up very many of them.
080903 But I have sent the brothers that our boasting on your behalf may not be in vain in this respect, that, just as I said, you may be prepared,
080904 so that I won't by any means, if there come with me any of Macedonia and find you unprepared, we (to say nothing of you) should be disappointed in this confident boasting.
080905 I thought it necessary therefore to entreat the brothers that they would go before to you, and arrange ahead of time the generous gift that you promised before, that the same might be ready as a matter of generosity, and not of greediness.
080906 Remember this: he who sows sparingly will also reap sparingly. He who sows bountifully will also reap bountifully.
080907 Let each man give according as he has determined in his heart; not grudgingly, or under compulsion; for God loves a cheerful giver.
080908 And God is able to make all grace abound to you, that you, always having all sufficiency in everything, may abound to every good work.
080909 As it is written, "He has scattered abroad, he has given to the poor. His righteousness remains forever."
080910 Now may he who supplies seed to the sower and bread for food, supply and multiply your seed for sowing, and increase the fruits of your righteousness;
080911 you being enriched in everything to all liberality, which works through us thanksgiving to God.
080912 For this service of giving that you perform not only makes up for lack among the saints, but abounds also through many givings of thanks to God;
080913 seeing that through the proof given by this service, they glorify God for the obedience of your confession to the Good News of Christ, and for the liberality of your contribution to them and to all;
080914 while they themselves also, with supplication on your behalf, yearn for you by reason of the exceeding grace of God in you.
080915 Now thanks be to God for his unspeakable gift!
081001 Now I Paul, myself, entreat you by the humility and gentleness of Christ; I who in your presence am lowly among you, but being absent am of good courage toward you.
081002 Yes, I beg you that I may not, when present, show courage with the confidence with which I intend to be bold against some, who consider us to be walking according to the flesh.
081003 For though we walk in the flesh, we don't wage war according to the flesh;
081004 for the weapons of our warfare are not of the flesh, but mighty before God to the throwing down of strongholds,
081005 throwing down imaginations and every high thing that is exalted against the knowledge of God, and bringing every thought into captivity to the obedience of Christ;
081006 and being in readiness to avenge all disobedience, when your obedience will be made full.
081007 Do you look at things only as they appear in front of your face? If anyone trusts in himself that he is Christ's, let him consider this again with himself, that, even as he is Christ's, so also we are Christ's.
081008 For though I should boast somewhat abundantly concerning our authority, (which the Lord gave for building you up, and not for casting you down) I will not be disappointed,
081009 that I may not seem as if I desire to terrify you by my letters.
081010 For, "His letters," they say, "are weighty and strong, but his bodily presence is weak, and his speech is despised."
081011 Let such a person consider this, that what we are in word by letters when we are absent, such are we also in deed when we are present.
081012 For we are not bold to number or compare ourselves with some of those who commend themselves. But they themselves, measuring themselves by themselves, and comparing themselves with themselves, are without understanding.
081013 But we will not boast beyond proper limits, but within the boundaries with which God appointed to us, which reach even to you.
081014 For we don't stretch ourselves too much, as though we didn't reach to you. For we came even as far as to you with the Good News of Christ,
081015 not boasting beyond proper limits in other men's labors, but having hope that as your faith grows, we will be abundantly enlarged by you in our sphere of influence,
081016 so as to preach the Good News even to the parts beyond you, not to boast in what someone else has already done.
081017 But "he who boasts, let him boast in the Lord."
081018 For it isn't he who commends himself who is approved, but whom the Lord commends.
081101 I wish that you would bear with me in a little foolishness, but indeed you do bear with me.
081102 For I am jealous over you with a godly jealousy. For I married you to one husband, that I might present you as a pure virgin to Christ.
081103 But I am afraid that somehow, as the serpent deceived Eve in his craftiness, so your minds might be corrupted from the simplicity that is in Christ.
081104 For if he who comes preaches another Jesus, whom we did not preach, or if you receive a different spirit, which you did not receive, or a different "good news", which you did not accept, you put up with that well enough.
081105 For I reckon that I am not at all behind the very best apostles.
081106 But though I am unskilled in speech, yet I am not unskilled in knowledge. No, in every way we have been revealed to you in all things.
081107 Or did I commit a sin in humbling myself that you might be exalted, because I preached to you God's Good News free of charge?
081108 I robbed other assemblies, taking wages from them that I might serve you.
081109 When I was present with you and was in need, I wasn't a burden on anyone, for the brothers, when they came from Macedonia, supplied the measure of my need. In everything I kept myself from being burdensome to you, and I will continue to do so.
081110 As the truth of Christ is in me, no one will stop me from this boasting in the regions of Achaia.
081111 Why? Because I don't love you? God knows.
081112 But what I do, that I will do, that I may cut off occasion from them that desire an occasion, that in which they boast, they may be found even as we.
081113 For such men are false apostles, deceitful workers, masquerading as Christ's apostles.
081114 And no wonder, for even Satan masquerades as an angel of light.
081115 It is no great thing therefore if his servants also masquerade as servants of righteousness, whose end will be according to their works.
081116 I say again, let no one think me foolish. But if so, yet receive me as foolish, that I also may boast a little.
081117 That which I speak, I don't speak according to the Lord, but as in foolishness, in this confidence of boasting.
081118 Seeing that many boast after the flesh, I will also boast.
081119 For you bear with the foolish gladly, being wise.
081120 For you bear with a man, if he brings you into bondage, if he devours you, if he takes you captive, if he exalts himself, if he strikes you on the face.
081121 I speak by way of disparagement, as though we had been weak. Yet however any is bold (I speak in foolishness), I am bold also.
081122 Are they Hebrews? So am I. Are they Israelites? So am I. Are they the seed of Abraham? So am I.
081123 Are they servants of Christ? (I speak as one beside himself) I am more so; in labors more abundantly, in prisons more abundantly, in stripes above measure, in deaths often.
081124 Five times from the Jews I received forty stripes minus one.
081125 Three times I was beaten with rods. Once I was stoned. Three times I suffered shipwreck. I have been a night and a day in the deep.
081126 I have been in travels often, perils of rivers, perils of robbers, perils from my countrymen, perils from the Gentiles, perils in the city, perils in the wilderness, perils in the sea, perils among false brothers;
081127 in labor and travail, in watchings often, in hunger and thirst, in fastings often, and in cold and nakedness.
081128 Besides those things that are outside, there is that which presses on me daily, anxiety for all the assemblies.
081129 Who is weak, and I am not weak? Who is caused to stumble, and I don't burn with indignation?
081130 If I must boast, I will boast of the things that concern my weakness.
081131 The God and Father of the Lord Jesus Christ, he who is blessed forevermore, knows that I don't lie.
081132 In Damascus the governor under King Aretas guarded the city of the Damascenes desiring to arrest me.
081133 Through a window I was let down in a basket by the wall, and escaped his hands.
081201 It is doubtless not profitable for me to boast. For I will come to visions and revelations of the Lord.
081202 I know a man in Christ, fourteen years ago (whether in the body, I don't know, or whether out of the body, I don't know; God knows), such a one caught up into the third heaven.
081203 I know such a man (whether in the body, or outside of the body, I don't know; God knows),
081204 how he was caught up into Paradise, and heard unspeakable words, which it is not lawful for a man to utter.
081205 On behalf of such a one I will boast, but on my own behalf I will not boast, except in my weaknesses.
081206 For if I would desire to boast, I will not be foolish; for I will speak the truth. But I refrain, so that no man may think more of me than that which he sees in me, or hears from me.
081207 By reason of the exceeding greatness of the revelations, that I should not be exalted excessively, there was given to me a thorn in the flesh, a messenger of Satan to torment me, that I should not be exalted excessively.
081208 Concerning this thing, I begged the Lord three times that it might depart from me.
081209 He has said to me, "My grace is sufficient for you, for my power is made perfect in weakness." Most gladly therefore I will rather glory in my weaknesses, that the power of Christ may rest on me.
081210 Therefore I take pleasure in weaknesses, in injuries, in necessities, in persecutions, in distresses, for Christ's sake. For when I am weak, then am I strong.
081211 I have become foolish in boasting. You compelled me, for I ought to have been commended by you, for in nothing was I inferior to the very best apostles, though I am nothing.
081212 Truly the signs of an apostle were worked among you in all patience, in signs and wonders and mighty works.
081213 For what is there in which you were made inferior to the rest of the assemblies, unless it is that I myself was not a burden to you? Forgive me this wrong.
081214 Behold, this is the third time I am ready to come to you, and I will not be a burden to you; for I seek not your possessions, but you. For the children ought not to save up for the parents, but the parents for the children.
081215 I will most gladly spend and be spent for your souls. If I love you more abundantly, am I loved the less?
081216 But be it so, I did not myself burden you. But, being crafty, I caught you with deception.
081217 Did I take advantage of you by anyone of them whom I have sent to you?
081218 I exhorted Titus, and I sent the brother with him. Did Titus take any advantage of you? Didn't we walk in the same spirit? Didn't we walk in the same steps?
081219 Again, do you think that we are excusing ourselves to you? In the sight of God we speak in Christ. But all things, beloved, are for your edifying.
081220 For I am afraid that by any means, when I come, I might find you not the way I want to, and that I might be found by you as you don't desire; that by any means there would be strife, jealousy, outbursts of anger, factions, slander, whisperings, proud thoughts, riots;
081221 that again when I come my God would humble me before you, and I would mourn for many of those who have sinned before now, and not repented of the uncleanness and sexual immorality and lustfulness which they committed.
