210101 Peter, an apostle of Jesus Christ, to the chosen ones who are living as foreigners in the Dispersion in Pontus, Galatia, Cappadocia, Asia, and Bithynia,
210102 according to the foreknowledge of God the Father, in sanctification of the Spirit, that you may obey Jesus Christ and be sprinkled with his blood: Grace to you and peace be multiplied.
210103 Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, who according to his great mercy became our father again to a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead,
210104 to an incorruptible and undefiled inheritance that doesn't fade away, reserved in Heaven for you,
210105 who by the power of God are guarded through faith for a salvation ready to be revealed in the last time.
210106 Wherein you greatly rejoice, though now for a little while, if need be, you have been put to grief in various trials,
210107 that the proof of your faith, which is more precious than gold that perishes even though it is tested by fire, may be found to result in praise, glory, and honor at the revelation of Jesus Christ--
210108 whom not having known you love; in whom, though now you don't see him, yet believing, you rejoice greatly with joy unspeakable and full of glory--
210109 receiving the result of your faith, the salvation of your souls.
210110 Concerning this salvation, the prophets sought and searched diligently, who prophesied of the grace that would come to you,
210111 searching for who or what kind of time the Spirit of Christ, which was in them, pointed to, when he predicted the sufferings of Christ, and the glories that would follow them.
210112 To them it was revealed, that not to themselves, but to you, they ministered these things, which now have been announced to you through those who preached the Good News to you by the Holy Spirit sent out from heaven; which things angels desire to look into.
210113 Therefore, prepare your minds for action, be sober and set your hope fully on the grace that will be brought to you at the revelation of Jesus Christ--
210114 as children of obedience, not conforming yourselves according to your former lusts as in your ignorance,
210115 but just as he who called you is holy, you yourselves also be holy in all of your behavior;
210116 because it is written, "You shall be holy; for I am holy."
210117 If you call on him as Father, who without respect of persons judges according to each man's work, pass the time of your living as foreigners here in reverent fear:
210118 knowing that you were redeemed, not with corruptible things, with silver or gold, from the useless way of life handed down from your fathers,
210119 but with precious blood, as of a faultless and pure lamb, the blood of Christ;
210120 who was foreknown indeed before the foundation of the world, but was revealed at the end of times for your sake,
210121 who through him are believers in God, who raised him from the dead, and gave him glory; so that your faith and hope might be in God.
210122 Seeing you have purified your souls in your obedience to the truth through the Spirit in sincere brotherly affection, love one another from the heart fervently:
210123 having been born again, not of corruptible seed, but of incorruptible, through the word of God, which lives and remains forever.
210124 For, "All flesh is like grass, and all of man's glory like the flower in the grass. The grass withers, and its flower falls;
210125 but the Lord's word endures forever." This is the word of Good News which was preached to you.
210201 Putting away therefore all wickedness, all deceit, hypocrisies, envies, and all evil speaking,
210202 as newborn babies, long for the pure milk of the Word, that you may grow thereby,
210203 if indeed you have tasted that the Lord is gracious:
210204 coming to him, a living stone, rejected indeed by men, but chosen by God, precious.
210205 You also, as living stones, are built up as a spiritual house, to be a holy priesthood, to offer up spiritual sacrifices, acceptable to God through Jesus Christ.
210206 Because it is contained in Scripture, "Behold, I lay in Zion a chief cornerstone, chosen, and precious: He who believes in him will not be disappointed."
210207 For you who believe therefore is the honor, but for those who are disobedient, "The stone which the builders rejected, has become the chief cornerstone,"
210208 and, "a stone of stumbling, and a rock of offense." For they stumble at the word, being disobedient, to which also they were appointed.
210209 But you are a chosen race, a royal priesthood, a holy nation, a people for God's own possession, that you may proclaim the excellence of him who called you out of darkness into his marvelous light:
210210 who in time past were no people, but now are God's people, who had not obtained mercy, but now have obtained mercy.
210211 Beloved, I beg you as foreigners and pilgrims, to abstain from fleshly lusts, which war against the soul;
210212 having good behavior among the nations, so in that of which they speak against you as evildoers, they may by your good works, which they see, glorify God in the day of visitation.
210213 Therefore subject yourselves to every ordinance of man for the Lord's sake: whether to the king, as supreme;
210214 or to governors, as sent by him for vengeance on evildoers and for praise to those who do well.
210215 For this is the will of God, that by well-doing you should put to silence the ignorance of foolish men:
210216 as free, and not using your freedom for a cloak of wickedness, but as bondservants of God.
210217 Honor all men. Love the brotherhood. Fear God. Honor the king.
210218 Servants, be in subjection to your masters with all fear; not only to the good and gentle, but also to the wicked.
210219 For it is commendable if someone endures pain, suffering unjustly, because of conscience toward God.
210220 For what glory is it if, when you sin, you patiently endure beating? But if, when you do well, you patiently endure suffering, this is commendable with God.
210221 For to this you were called, because Christ also suffered for us, leaving you an example, that you should follow his steps,
210222 who did not sin, "neither was deceit found in his mouth."
210223 Who, when he was cursed, didn't curse back. When he suffered, didn't threaten, but committed himself to him who judges righteously;
210224 who his own self bore our sins in his body on the tree, that we, having died to sins, might live to righteousness; by whose stripes you were healed.
210225 For you were going astray like sheep; but now have returned to the Shepherd and Overseer of your souls.
210301 In like manner, wives, be in subjection to your own husbands; so that, even if any don't obey the Word, they may be won by the behavior of their wives without a word;
210302 seeing your pure behavior in fear.
210303 Let your beauty be not just the outward adorning of braiding the hair, and of wearing jewels of gold, or of putting on fine clothing;
210304 but in the hidden person of the heart, in the incorruptible adornment of a gentle and quiet spirit, which is in the sight of God very precious.
210305 For this is how the holy women before, who hoped in God also adorned themselves, being in subjection to their own husbands:
210306 as Sarah obeyed Abraham, calling him lord, whose children you now are, if you do well, and are not put in fear by any terror.
210307 You husbands, in like manner, live with your wives according to knowledge, giving honor to the woman, as to the weaker vessel, as being also joint heirs of the grace of life; that your prayers may not be hindered.
210308 Finally, be all like-minded, compassionate, loving as brothers, tenderhearted, courteous,
210309 not rendering evil for evil, or reviling for reviling; but instead blessing; knowing that to this were you called, that you may inherit a blessing.
210310 For, "He who would love life, and see good days, let him keep his tongue from evil, and his lips from speaking deceit.
210311 Let him turn away from evil, and do good. Let him seek peace, and pursue it.
210312 For the eyes of the Lord are on the righteous, and his ears open to their prayer; but the face of the Lord is against those who do evil."
210313 Now who is he who will harm you, if you become imitators of that which is good?
210314 But even if you should suffer for righteousness' sake, you are blessed. "Don't fear what they fear, neither be troubled."
210315 But sanctify the Lord God in your hearts; and always be ready to give an answer to everyone who asks you a reason concerning the hope that is in you, with humility and fear:
210316 having a good conscience; that, while you are spoken against as evildoers, they may be disappointed who curse your good manner of life in Christ.
210317 For it is better, if it is God's will, that you suffer for doing well than for doing evil.
210318 Because Christ also suffered for sins once, the righteous for the unrighteous, that he might bring you to God; being put to death in the flesh, but made alive in the spirit;
210319 in which he also went and preached to the spirits in prison,
210320 who before were disobedient, when God waited patiently in the days of Noah, while the ship was being built. In it, few, that is, eight souls, were saved through water.
210321 This is a symbol of baptism, which now saves you--not the putting away of the filth of the flesh, but the answer of a good conscience toward God, through the resurrection of Jesus Christ,
210322 who is at the right hand of God, having gone into heaven, angels and authorities and powers being made subject to him.
210401 Forasmuch then as Christ suffered for us in the flesh, arm yourselves also with the same mind; for he who has suffered in the flesh has ceased from sin;
210402 that you no longer should live the rest of your time in the flesh for the lusts of men, but for the will of God.
210403 For we have spent enough of our past time doing the desire of the Gentiles, and having walked in lewdness, lusts, drunken binges, orgies, carousings, and abominable idolatries.
210404 They think it is strange that you don't run with them into the same excess of riot, blaspheming:
210405 who will give account to him who is ready to judge the living and the dead.
210406 For to this end the Good News was preached even to the dead, that they might be judged indeed as men in the flesh, but live as to God in the spirit.
210407 But the end of all things is near. Therefore be of sound mind, self-controlled, and sober in prayer.
210408 And above all things be earnest in your love among yourselves, for love covers a multitude of sins.
210409 Be hospitable to one another without grumbling.
210410 As each has received a gift, employ it in serving one another, as good managers of the grace of God in its various forms.
210411 If anyone speaks, let it be as it were the very words of God. If anyone serves, let it be as of the strength which God supplies, that in all things God may be glorified through Jesus Christ, to whom belong the glory and the dominion forever and ever. Amen.
210412 Beloved, don't be astonished at the fiery trial which has come upon you, to test you, as though a strange thing happened to you.
210413 But because you are partakers of Christ's sufferings, rejoice; that at the revelation of his glory you also may rejoice with exceeding joy.
210414 If you are insulted for the name of Christ, you are blessed; because the Spirit of glory and of God rests on you. On their part he is blasphemed, but on your part he is glorified.
210415 For let none of you suffer as a murderer, or a thief, or an evil doer, or a meddler in other men's matters.
210416 But if one of you suffers for being a Christian, let him not be ashamed; but let him glorify God in this matter.
210417 For the time has come for judgment to begin with the household of God. If it begins first with us, what will happen to those who don't obey the Good News of God?
210418 "If it is hard for the righteous to be saved, what will happen to the ungodly and the sinner?"
210419 Therefore let them also who suffer according to the will of God in doing good entrust their souls to him, as to a faithful Creator.
210501 I exhort the elders among you, as a fellow elder, and a witness of the sufferings of Christ, and who will also share in the glory that will be revealed.
210502 Shepherd the flock of God which is among you, exercising the oversight, not under compulsion, but voluntarily, not for dishonest gain, but willingly;
210503 neither as lording it over those entrusted to you, but making yourselves examples to the flock.
210504 When the chief Shepherd is revealed, you will receive the crown of glory that doesn't fade away.
210505 Likewise, you younger ones, be subject to the elder. Yes, all of you gird yourselves with humility, to subject yourselves to one another; for "God resists the proud, but gives grace to the humble."
210506 Humble yourselves therefore under the mighty hand of God, that he may exalt you in due time;
210507 casting all your worries on him, because he cares for you.
210508 Be sober and self-controlled. Be watchful. Your adversary the devil, walks around like a roaring lion, seeking whom he may devour.
210509 Withstand him steadfast in your faith, knowing that your brothers who are in the world are undergoing the same sufferings.
210510 But may the God of all grace, who called you to his eternal glory by Christ Jesus, after you have suffered a little while, perfect, establish, strengthen, and settle you.
210511 To him be the glory and the power forever and ever. Amen.
210512 Through Silvanus, our faithful brother, as I consider him, I have written to you briefly, exhorting, and testifying that this is the true grace of God in which you stand.
210513 She who is in Babylon, chosen together with you, greets you; and so does Mark, my son.
210514 Greet one another with a kiss of love. Peace be to you all who are in Christ Jesus. Amen.
220101 Simon Peter, a servant and apostle of Jesus Christ, to those who have obtained a like precious faith with us in the righteousness of our God and Savior, Jesus Christ:
220102 Grace to you and peace be multiplied in the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord,
220103 seeing that his divine power has granted to us all things that pertain to life and godliness, through the knowledge of him who called us by his own glory and virtue;
220104 by which he has granted to us his precious and exceedingly great promises; that through these you may become partakers of the divine nature, having escaped from the corruption that is in the world by lust.
220105 Yes, and for this very cause adding on your part all diligence, in your faith supply moral excellence; and in moral excellence, knowledge;
220106 and in knowledge, self-control; and in self-control patience; and in patience godliness;
220107 and in godliness brotherly affection; and in brotherly affection, love.
220108 For if these things are yours and abound, they make you to be not idle nor unfruitful to the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ.
220109 For he who lacks these things is blind, seeing only what is near, having forgotten the cleansing from his old sins.
220110 Therefore, brothers, be more diligent to make your calling and election sure. For if you do these things, you will never stumble.
220111 For thus you will be richly supplied with the entrance into the eternal Kingdom of our Lord and Savior, Jesus Christ.
220112 Therefore I will not be negligent to remind you of these things, though you know them, and are established in the present truth.
220113 I think it right, as long as I am in this tent, to stir you up by reminding you;
220114 knowing that the putting off of my tent comes swiftly, even as our Lord Jesus Christ made clear to me.
220115 Yes, I will make every effort that you may always be able to remember these things even after my departure.
220116 For we did not follow cunningly devised fables, when we made known to you the power and coming of our Lord Jesus Christ, but we were eyewitnesses of his majesty.
220117 For he received from God the Father honor and glory, when the voice came to him from the Majestic Glory, "This is my beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased."
220118 We heard this voice come out of heaven when we were with him on the holy mountain.
220119 We have the more sure word of prophecy; and you do well that you heed it, as to a lamp shining in a dark place, until the day dawns, and the morning star arises in your hearts:
220120 knowing this first, that no prophecy of Scripture is of private interpretation.
220121 For no prophecy ever came by the will of man: but holy men of God spoke, being moved by the Holy Spirit.
220201 But false prophets also arose among the people, as false teachers will also be among you, who will secretly bring in destructive heresies, denying even the Master who bought them, bringing on themselves swift destruction.
220202 Many will follow their immoral ways, and as a result, the way of the truth will be maligned.
220203 In covetousness they will exploit you with deceptive words: whose sentence now from of old doesn't linger, and their destruction will not slumber.
220204 For if God didn't spare angels when they sinned, but cast them down to Tartarus, and committed them to pits of darkness, to be reserved for judgment;
220205 and didn't spare the ancient world, but preserved Noah with seven others, a preacher of righteousness, when he brought a flood on the world of the ungodly;
220206 and turning the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah into ashes, condemned them to destruction, having made them an example to those who would live ungodly;
220207 and delivered righteous Lot, who was very distressed by the lustful life of the wicked
220208 (for that righteous man dwelling among them, was tormented in his righteous soul from day to day with seeing and hearing lawless deeds):
220209 the Lord knows how to deliver the godly out of temptation and to keep the unrighteous under punishment for the day of judgment;
220210 but chiefly those who walk after the flesh in the lust of defilement, and despise authority. Daring, self-willed, they are not afraid to speak evil of dignitaries;
220211 whereas angels, though greater in might and power, don't bring a railing judgment against them before the Lord.
220212 But these, as unreasoning creatures, born natural animals to be taken and destroyed, speaking evil in matters about which they are ignorant, will in their destroying surely be destroyed,
220213 receiving the wages of unrighteousness; people who count it pleasure to revel in the daytime, spots and blemishes, reveling in their deceit while they feast with you;
220214 having eyes full of adultery, and who can't cease from sin; enticing unsettled souls; having a heart trained in greed; children of cursing;
220215 forsaking the right way, they went astray, having followed the way of Balaam the son of Beor, who loved the wages of wrongdoing;
220216 but he was rebuked for his own disobedience. A mute donkey spoke with a man's voice and stopped the madness of the prophet.
220217 These are wells without water, clouds driven by a storm; for whom the blackness of darkness has been reserved forever.
220218 For, uttering great swelling words of emptiness, they entice in the lusts of the flesh, by licentiousness, those who are indeed escaping from those who live in error;
220219 promising them liberty, while they themselves are bondservants of corruption; for a man is brought into bondage by whoever overcomes him.
220220 For if, after they have escaped the defilement of the world through the knowledge of the Lord and Savior Jesus Christ, they are again entangled in it and overcome, the last state has become worse for them than the first.
220221 For it would be better for them not to have known the way of righteousness, than, after knowing it, to turn back from the holy commandment delivered to them.
220222 But it has happened to them according to the true proverb, "The dog turns to his own vomit again," and "the sow that has washed to wallowing in the mire."
220301 This is now, beloved, the second letter that I have written to you; and in both of them I stir up your sincere mind by reminding you;
220302 that you should remember the words which were spoken before by the holy prophets, and the commandments of us, the apostles of the Lord and Savior:
220303 knowing this first, that in the last days mockers will come, walking after their own lusts,
220304 and saying, "Where is the promise of his coming? For, from the day that the fathers fell asleep, all things continue as they were from the beginning of the creation."
220305 For this they willfully forget, that there were heavens from of old, and an earth formed out of water and amid water, by the word of God;
220306 by which means the world that then was, being overflowed with water, perished.
220307 But the heavens that now are, and the earth, by the same word have been stored up for fire, being reserved against the day of judgment and destruction of ungodly men.
220308 But don't forget this one thing, beloved, that one day is with the Lord as a thousand years, and a thousand years as one day.
220309 The Lord is not slow concerning his promise, as some count slowness; but is patient with us, not wishing that any should perish, but that all should come to repentance.
220310 But the day of the Lord will come as a thief in the night; in which the heavens will pass away with a great noise, and the elements will be dissolved with fervent heat, and the earth and the works that are in it will be burned up.
220311 Therefore since all these things will be destroyed like this, what kind of people ought you to be in holy living and godliness,
220312 looking for and earnestly desiring the coming of the day of God, which will cause the burning heavens to be dissolved, and the elements will melt with fervent heat?
220313 But, according to his promise, we look for new heavens and a new earth, in which righteousness dwells.
220314 Therefore, beloved, seeing that you look for these things, be diligent to be found in peace, without blemish and blameless in his sight.
220315 Regard the patience of our Lord as salvation; even as our beloved brother Paul also, according to the wisdom given to him, wrote to you;
220316 as also in all of his letters, speaking in them of these things. In those, there are some things that are hard to understand, which the ignorant and unsettled twist, as they also do to the other Scriptures, to their own destruction.
220317 You therefore, beloved, knowing these things beforehand, beware, lest being carried away with the error of the wicked, you fall from your own steadfastness.
220318 But grow in the grace and knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ. To him be the glory both now and forever. Amen.
230101 That which was from the beginning, that which we have heard, that which we have seen with our eyes, that which we saw, and our hands touched, concerning the Word of life
230102 (and the life was revealed, and we have seen, and testify, and declare to you the life, the eternal life, which was with the Father, and was revealed to us);
230103 that which we have seen and heard we declare to you, that you also may have fellowship with us. Yes, and our fellowship is with the Father, and with his Son, Jesus Christ.
230104 And we write these things to you, that our joy may be fulfilled.
230105 This is the message which we have heard from him and announce to you, that God is light, and in him is no darkness at all.
230106 If we say that we have fellowship with him and walk in the darkness, we lie, and don't tell the truth.
230107 But if we walk in the light, as he is in the light, we have fellowship with one another, and the blood of Jesus Christ, his Son, cleanses us from all sin.
230108 If we say that we have no sin, we deceive ourselves, and the truth is not in us.
230109 If we confess our sins, he is faithful and righteous to forgive us the sins, and to cleanse us from all unrighteousness.
230110 If we say that we haven't sinned, we make him a liar, and his word is not in us.
230201 My little children, I write these things to you so that you may not sin. If anyone sins, we have a Counselor with the Father, Jesus Christ, the righteous.
230202 And he is the atoning sacrifice for our sins, and not for ours only, but also for the whole world.
230203 This is how we know that we know him: if we keep his commandments.
230204 One who says, "I know him," and doesn't keep his commandments, is a liar, and the truth isn't in him.
230205 But whoever keeps his word, God's love has most certainly been perfected in him. This is how we know that we are in him:
230206 he who says he remains in him ought himself also to walk just like he walked.
230207 Brothers, I write no new commandment to you, but an old commandment which you had from the beginning. The old commandment is the word which you heard from the beginning.
230208 Again, I write a new commandment to you, which is true in him and in you; because the darkness is passing away, and the true light already shines.
230209 He who says he is in the light and hates his brother, is in the darkness even until now.
230210 He who loves his brother remains in the light, and there is no occasion for stumbling in him.
230211 But he who hates his brother is in the darkness, and walks in the darkness, and doesn't know where he is going, because the darkness has blinded his eyes.
230212 I write to you, little children, because your sins are forgiven you for his name's sake.
230213 I write to you, fathers, because you know him who is from the beginning. I write to you, young men, because you have overcome the evil one. I write to you, little children, because you know the Father.
230214 I have written to you, fathers, because you know him who is from the beginning. I have written to you, young men, because you are strong, and the word of God remains in you, and you have overcome the evil one.
230215 Don't love the world, neither the things that are in the world. If anyone loves the world, the Father's love isn't in him.
230216 For all that is in the world, the lust of the flesh, the lust of the eyes, and the pride of life, isn't the Father's, but is the world's.
230217 The world is passing away with its lusts, but he who does God's will remains forever.
230218 Little children, these are the end times, and as you heard that the Antichrist is coming, even now many antichrists have arisen. By this we know that it is the final hour.
230219 They went out from us, but they didn't belong to us; for if they had belonged to us, they would have continued with us. But they left, that they might be revealed that none of them belong to us.
230220 You have an anointing from the Holy One, and you all have knowledge.
230221 I have not written to you because you don't know the truth, but because you know it, and because no lie is of the truth.
230222 Who is the liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ? This is the Antichrist, he who denies the Father and the Son.
230223 Whoever denies the Son, the same doesn't have the Father. He who confesses the Son has the Father also.
230224 Therefore, as for you, let that remain in you which you heard from the beginning. If that which you heard from the beginning remains in you, you also will remain in the Son, and in the Father.
230225 This is the promise which he promised us, the eternal life.
230226 These things I have written to you concerning those who would lead you astray.
230227 As for you, the anointing which you received from him remains in you, and you don't need for anyone to teach you. But as his anointing teaches you concerning all things, and is true, and is no lie, and even as it taught you, you will remain in him.
230228 Now, little children, remain in him, that when he appears, we may have boldness, and not be ashamed before him at his coming.
230229 If you know that he is righteous, you know that everyone who practices righteousness is born of him.
230301 Behold, how great a love the Father has bestowed on us, that we should be called children of God! For this cause the world doesn't know us, because it didn't know him.
230302 Beloved, now we are children of God, and it is not yet revealed what we will be. But we know that, when he is revealed, we will be like him; for we will see him just as he is.
230303 Everyone who has this hope set on him purifies himself, even as he is pure.
230304 Everyone who sins also commits lawlessness. Sin is lawlessness.
230305 You know that he was revealed to take away our sins, and in him is no sin.
230306 Whoever remains in him doesn't sin. Whoever sins hasn't seen him, neither knows him.
230307 Little children, let no one lead you astray. He who does righteousness is righteous, even as he is righteous.
230308 He who sins is of the devil, for the devil has been sinning from the beginning. To this end the Son of God was revealed, that he might destroy the works of the devil.
230309 Whoever is born of God doesn't commit sin, because his seed remains in him; and he can't sin, because he is born of God.
230310 In this the children of God are revealed, and the children of the devil. Whoever doesn't do righteousness is not of God, neither is he who doesn't love his brother.
230311 For this is the message which you heard from the beginning, that we should love one another;
230312 unlike Cain, who was of the evil one, and killed his brother. Why did he kill him? Because his works were evil, and his brother's righteous.
230313 Don't be surprised, my brothers, if the world hates you.
230314 We know that we have passed out of death into life, because we love the brothers. He who doesn't love his brother remains in death.
230315 Whoever hates his brother is a murderer, and you know that no murderer has eternal life remaining in him.
230316 By this we know love, because he laid down his life for us. And we ought to lay down our lives for the brothers.
230317 But whoever has the world's goods, and sees his brother in need, and closes his heart of compassion against him, how does the love of God remain in him?
230318 My little children, let's not love in word only, neither with the tongue only, but in deed and truth.
230319 And by this we know that we are of the truth, and persuade our hearts before him,
230320 because if our heart condemns us, God is greater than our heart, and knows all things.
230321 Beloved, if our hearts don't condemn us, we have boldness toward God;
230322 and whatever we ask, we receive from him, because we keep his commandments and do the things that are pleasing in his sight.
230323 This is his commandment, that we should believe in the name of his Son, Jesus Christ, and love one another, even as he commanded.
230324 He who keeps his commandments remains in him, and he in him. By this we know that he remains in us, by the Spirit which he gave us.
230401 Beloved, don't believe every spirit, but test the spirits, whether they are of God, because many false prophets have gone out into the world.
230402 By this you know the Spirit of God: every spirit who confesses that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is of God,
230403 and every spirit who doesn't confess that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is not of God, and this is the spirit of the Antichrist, of whom you have heard that it comes. Now it is in the world already.
230404 You are of God, little children, and have overcome them; because greater is he who is in you than he who is in the world.
230405 They are of the world. Therefore they speak of the world, and the world hears them.
230406 We are of God. He who knows God listens to us. He who is not of God doesn't listen to us. By this we know the spirit of truth, and the spirit of error.
230407 Beloved, let us love one another, for love is of God; and everyone who loves is born of God, and knows God.
230408 He who doesn't love doesn't know God, for God is love.
230409 By this God's love was revealed in us, that God has sent his one and only Son into the world that we might live through him.
230410 In this is love, not that we loved God, but that he loved us, and sent his Son as the atoning sacrifice for our sins.
230411 Beloved, if God loved us in this way, we also ought to love one another.
230412 No one has seen God at any time. If we love one another, God remains in us, and his love has been perfected in us.
230413 By this we know that we remain in him and he in us, because he has given us of his Spirit.
230414 We have seen and testify that the Father has sent the Son as the Savior of the world.
230415 Whoever confesses that Jesus is the Son of God, God remains in him, and he in God.
230416 We know and have believed the love which God has for us. God is love, and he who remains in love remains in God, and God remains in him.
230417 In this love has been made perfect among us, that we may have boldness in the day of judgment, because as he is, even so are we in this world.
230418 There is no fear in love; but perfect love casts out fear, because fear has punishment. He who fears is not made perfect in love.
230419 We love him, because he first loved us.
230420 If a man says, "I love God," and hates his brother, he is a liar; for he who doesn't love his brother whom he has seen, how can he love God whom he has not seen?
230421 This commandment we have from him, that he who loves God should also love his brother.
230501 Whoever believes that Jesus is the Christ is born of God. Whoever loves the Father also loves the child who is born of him.
230502 By this we know that we love the children of God, when we love God and keep his commandments.
230503 For this is the love of God, that we keep his commandments. His commandments are not grievous.
230504 For whatever is born of God overcomes the world. This is the victory that has overcome the world: your faith.
230505 Who is he who overcomes the world, but he who believes that Jesus is the Son of God?
230506 This is he who came by water and blood, Jesus Christ; not with the water only, but with the water and the blood. It is the Spirit who testifies, because the Spirit is the truth.
230507 For there are three who testify:
230508 the Spirit, the water, and the blood; and the three agree as one.
230509 If we receive the witness of men, the witness of God is greater; for this is God's testimony which he has testified concerning his Son.
230510 He who believes in the Son of God has the testimony in himself. He who doesn't believe God has made him a liar, because he has not believed in the testimony that God has given concerning his Son.
230511 The testimony is this, that God gave to us eternal life, and this life is in his Son.
230512 He who has the Son has the life. He who doesn't have God's Son doesn't have the life.
230513 These things I have written to you who believe in the name of the Son of God, that you may know that you have eternal life, and that you may continue to believe in the name of the Son of God.
230514 This is the boldness which we have toward him, that, if we ask anything according to his will, he listens to us.
230515 And if we know that he listens to us, whatever we ask, we know that we have the petitions which we have asked of him.
230516 If anyone sees his brother sinning a sin not leading to death, he shall ask, and God will give him life for those who sin not leading to death. There is a sin leading to death. I don't say that he should make a request concerning this.
230517 All unrighteousness is sin, and there is a sin not leading to death.
230518 We know that whoever is born of God doesn't sin, but he who was born of God keeps himself, and the evil one doesn't touch him.
230519 We know that we are of God, and the whole world lies in the power of the evil one.
230520 We know that the Son of God has come, and has given us an understanding, that we know him who is true, and we are in him who is true, in his Son Jesus Christ. This is the true God, and eternal life.
230521 Little children, keep yourselves from idols.
240101 The elder, to the chosen lady and her children, whom I love in truth; and not I only, but also all those who know the truth;
240102 for the truth's sake, which remains in us, and it will be with us forever:
240103 Grace, mercy, and peace will be with us, from God the Father, and from the Lord Jesus Christ, the Son of the Father, in truth and love.
240104 I rejoice greatly that I have found some of your children walking in truth, even as we have been commanded by the Father.
240105 Now I beg you, dear lady, not as though I wrote to you a new commandment, but that which we had from the beginning, that we love one another.
240106 This is love, that we should walk according to his commandments. This is the commandment, even as you heard from the beginning, that you should walk in it.
240107 For many deceivers have gone out into the world, those who don't confess that Jesus Christ came in the flesh. This is the deceiver and the Antichrist.
240108 Watch yourselves, that we don't lose the things which we have accomplished, but that we receive a full reward.
240109 Whoever transgresses and doesn't remain in the teaching of Christ, doesn't have God. He who remains in the teaching, the same has both the Father and the Son.
240110 If anyone comes to you, and doesn't bring this teaching, don't receive him into your house, and don't welcome him,
240111 for he who welcomes him participates in his evil works.
240112 Having many things to write to you, I don't want to do so with paper and ink, but I hope to come to you, and to speak face to face, that our joy may be made full.
240113 The children of your chosen sister greet you. Amen.
250101 The elder to Gaius the beloved, whom I love in truth.
250102 Beloved, I pray that you may prosper in all things and be healthy, even as your soul prospers.
250103 For I rejoiced greatly, when brothers came and testified about your truth, even as you walk in truth.
250104 I have no greater joy than this, to hear about my children walking in truth.
250105 Beloved, you do a faithful work in whatever you accomplish for those who are brothers and strangers.
250106 They have testified about your love before the assembly. You will do well to send them forward on their journey in a manner worthy of God,
250107 because for the sake of the Name they went out, taking nothing from the Gentiles.
250108 We therefore ought to receive such, that we may be fellow workers for the truth.
250109 I wrote to the assembly, but Diotrephes, who loves to be first among them, doesn't accept what we say.
250110 Therefore, if I come, I will call attention to his deeds which he does, unjustly accusing us with wicked words. Not content with this, neither does he himself receive the brothers, and those who would, he forbids and throws out of the assembly.
250111 Beloved, don't imitate that which is evil, but that which is good. He who does good is of God. He who does evil hasn't seen God.
250112 Demetrius has the testimony of all, and of the truth itself; yes, we also testify, and you know that our testimony is true.
250113 I had many things to write to you, but I am unwilling to write to you with ink and pen;
250114 but I hope to see you soon, and we will speak face to face. Peace be to you. The friends greet you. Greet the friends by name.
260101 Jude, a servant of Jesus Christ, and brother of James, to those who are called, sanctified by God the Father, and kept for Jesus Christ:
260102 Mercy to you and peace and love be multiplied.
260103 Beloved, while I was very eager to write to you about our common salvation, I was constrained to write to you exhorting you to contend earnestly for the faith which was once for all delivered to the saints.
260104 For there are certain men who crept in secretly, even those who were long ago written about for this condemnation: ungodly men, turning the grace of our God into indecency, and denying our only Master, God, and Lord, Jesus Christ.
260105 Now I desire to remind you, though you already know this, that the Lord, having saved a people out of the land of Egypt, afterward destroyed those who didn't believe.
260106 Angels who didn't keep their first domain, but deserted their own dwelling place, he has kept in everlasting bonds under darkness for the judgment of the great day.
260107 Even as Sodom and Gomorrah, and the cities around them, having, in the same way as these, given themselves over to sexual immorality and gone after strange flesh, are set forth as an example, suffering the punishment of eternal fire.
260108 Yet in like manner these also in their dreaming defile the flesh, despise authority, and slander celestial beings.
260109 But Michael, the archangel, when contending with the devil and arguing about the body of Moses, dared not bring against him an abusive condemnation, but said, "May the Lord rebuke you!"
260110 But these speak evil of whatever things they don't know. What they understand naturally, like the creatures without reason, they are destroyed in these things.
260111 Woe to them! For they went in the way of Cain, and ran riotously in the error of Balaam for hire, and perished in Korah's rebellion.
260112 These are hidden rocky reefs in your love feasts when they feast with you, shepherds who without fear feed themselves; clouds without water, carried along by winds; autumn leaves without fruit, twice dead, plucked up by the roots;
260113 wild waves of the sea, foaming out their own shame; wandering stars, for whom the blackness of darkness has been reserved forever.
260114 About these also Enoch, the seventh from Adam, prophesied, saying, "Behold, the Lord came with ten thousands of his holy ones,
260115 to execute judgment on all, and to convict all the ungodly of all their works of ungodliness which they have done in an ungodly way, and of all the hard things which ungodly sinners have spoken against him."
260116 These are murmurers and complainers, walking after their lusts (and their mouth speaks proud things), showing respect of persons to gain advantage.
260117 But you, beloved, remember the words which have been spoken before by the apostles of our Lord Jesus Christ.
260118 They said to you that "In the last time there will be mockers, walking after their own ungodly lusts."
260119 These are they who cause divisions, and are sensual, not having the Spirit.
260120 But you, beloved, keep building up yourselves on your most holy faith, praying in the Holy Spirit.
260121 Keep yourselves in the love of God, looking for the mercy of our Lord Jesus Christ to eternal life.
260122 On some have compassion, making a distinction,
260123 and some save, snatching them out of the fire with fear, hating even the clothing stained by the flesh.
260124 Now to him who is able to keep them from stumbling, and to present you faultless before the presence of his glory in great joy,
260125 to God our Savior, who alone is wise, be glory and majesty, dominion and power, both now and forever. Amen.
270101 This is the Revelation of Jesus Christ, which God gave him to show to his servants the things which must happen soon, which he sent and made known by his angel to his servant, John,
270102 who testified to God's word, and of the testimony of Jesus Christ, about everything that he saw.
270103 Blessed is he who reads and those who hear the words of the prophecy, and keep the things that are written in it, for the time is at hand.
270104 John, to the seven assemblies that are in Asia: Grace to you and peace, from God, who is and who was and who is to come; and from the seven Spirits who are before his throne;
270105 and from Jesus Christ, the faithful witness, the firstborn of the dead, and the ruler of the kings of the earth. To him who loves us, and washed us from our sins by his blood;
270106 and he made us to be a Kingdom, priests to his God and Father; to him be the glory and the dominion forever and ever. Amen.
270107 Behold, he is coming with the clouds, and every eye will see him, including those who pierced him. All the tribes of the earth will mourn over him. Even so, Amen.
270108 "I am the Alpha and the Omega," says the Lord God, "who is and who was and who is to come, the Almighty."
270109 I John, your brother and partner with you in oppression, Kingdom, and perseverance in Christ Jesus, was on the isle that is called Patmos because of God's Word and the testimony of Jesus Christ.
270110 I was in the Spirit on the Lord's day, and I heard behind me a loud voice, like a trumpet
270111 saying, "What you see, write in a book and send to the seven assemblies: to Ephesus, Smyrna, Pergamum, Thyatira, Sardis, Philadelphia, and to Laodicea."
270112 I turned to see the voice that spoke with me. Having turned, I saw seven golden lampstands.
270113 And among the lampstands was one like a son of man, clothed with a robe reaching down to his feet, and with a golden sash around his chest.
270114 His head and his hair were white as white wool, like snow. His eyes were like a flame of fire.
270115 His feet were like burnished brass, as if it had been refined in a furnace. His voice was like the voice of many waters.
270116 He had seven stars in his right hand. Out of his mouth proceeded a sharp two-edged sword. His face was like the sun shining at its brightest.
270117 When I saw him, I fell at his feet like a dead man. He laid his right hand on me, saying, "Don't be afraid. I am the first and the last,
270118 and the Living one. I was dead, and behold, I am alive forevermore. Amen. I have the keys of Death and of Hades.
270119 Write therefore the things which you have seen, and the things which are, and the things which will happen hereafter;
270120 the mystery of the seven stars which you saw in my right hand, and the seven golden lampstands. The seven stars are the angels of the seven assemblies. The seven lampstands are seven assemblies.
270201 "To the angel of the assembly in Ephesus write: "He who holds the seven stars in his right hand, he who walks among the seven golden lampstands says these things:
270202 "I know your works, and your toil and perseverance, and that you can't tolerate evil men, and have tested those who call themselves apostles, and they are not, and found them false.
270203 You have perseverance and have endured for my name's sake, and have not grown weary.
270204 But I have this against you, that you left your first love.
270205 Remember therefore from where you have fallen, and repent and do the first works; or else I am coming to you swiftly, and will move your lampstand out of its place, unless you repent.
270206 But this you have, that you hate the works of the Nicolaitans, which I also hate.
270207 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies. To him who overcomes I will give to eat of the tree of life, which is in the Paradise of my God.
270208 "To the angel of the assembly in Smyrna write: "The first and the last, who was dead, and has come to life says these things:
270209 "I know your works, oppression, and your poverty (but you are rich), and the blasphemy of those who say they are Jews, and they are not, but are a synagogue of Satan.
270210 Don't be afraid of the things which you are about to suffer. Behold, the devil is about to throw some of you into prison, that you may be tested; and you will have oppression for ten days. Be faithful to death, and I will give you the crown of life.
270211 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies. He who overcomes won't be harmed by the second death.
270212 "To the angel of the assembly in Pergamum write: "He who has the sharp two-edged sword says these things:
270213 "I know your works and where you dwell, where Satan's throne is. You hold firmly to my name, and didn't deny my faith in the days of Antipas my witness, my faithful one, who was killed among you, where Satan dwells.
270214 But I have a few things against you, because you have there some who hold the teaching of Balaam, who taught Balak to throw a stumbling block before the children of Israel, to eat things sacrificed to idols, and to commit sexual immorality.
270215 So you also have some who hold to the teaching of the Nicolaitans likewise.
270216 Repent therefore, or else I am coming to you quickly, and I will make war against them with the sword of my mouth.
270217 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies. To him who overcomes, to him I will give of the hidden manna, and I will give him a white stone, and on the stone a new name written, which no one knows but he who receives it.
270218 "To the angel of the assembly in Thyatira write: "The Son of God, who has his eyes like a flame of fire, and his feet are like burnished brass, says these things:
270219 "I know your works, your love, faith, service, patient endurance, and that your last works are more than the first.
270220 But I have this against you, that you tolerate your woman, Jezebel, who calls herself a prophetess. She teaches and seduces my servants to commit sexual immorality, and to eat things sacrificed to idols.
270221 I gave her time to repent, but she refuses to repent of her sexual immorality.
270222 Behold, I will throw her into a bed, and those who commit adultery with her into great oppression, unless they repent of her works.
270223 I will kill her children with Death, and all the assemblies will know that I am he who searches the minds and hearts. I will give to each one of you according to your deeds.
270224 But to you I say, to the rest who are in Thyatira, as many as don't have this teaching, who don't know what some call 'the deep things of Satan,' to you I say, I am not putting any other burden on you.
270225 Nevertheless, hold that which you have firmly until I come.
270226 He who overcomes, and he who keeps my works to the end, to him I will give authority over the nations.
270227 He will rule them with a rod of iron, shattering them like clay pots; as I also have received of my Father:
270228 and I will give him the morning star.
270229 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies.
270301 "And to the angel of the assembly in Sardis write: "He who has the seven Spirits of God, and the seven stars says these things: "I know your works, that you have a reputation of being alive, but you are dead.
270302 Wake up, and keep the things that remain, which you were about to throw away, for I have found no works of yours perfected before my God.
270303 Remember therefore how you have received and heard. Keep it, and repent. If therefore you won't watch, I will come as a thief, and you won't know what hour I will come upon you.
270304 Nevertheless you have a few names in Sardis that did not defile their garments. They will walk with me in white, for they are worthy.
270305 He who overcomes will be arrayed in white garments, and I will in no way blot his name out of the book of life, and I will confess his name before my Father, and before his angels.
270306 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies.
270307 "To the angel of the assembly in Philadelphia write: "He who is holy, he who is true, he who has the key of David, he who opens and no one can shut, and who shuts and no one opens, says these things:
270308 "I know your works (behold, I have set before you an open door, which no one can shut), that you have a little power, and kept my word, and didn't deny my name.
270309 Behold, I give of the synagogue of Satan, of those who say they are Jews, and they are not, but lie. Behold, I will make them to come and worship before your feet, and to know that I have loved you.
270310 Because you kept my command to endure, I also will keep you from the hour of testing, which is to come on the whole world, to test those who dwell on the earth.
270311 I am coming quickly! Hold firmly that which you have, so that no one takes your crown.
270312 He who overcomes, I will make him a pillar in the temple of my God, and he will go out from there no more. I will write on him the name of my God, and the name of the city of my God, the new Jerusalem, which comes down out of heaven from my God, and my own new name.
270313 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies.
270314 "To the angel of the assembly in Laodicea write: "The Amen, the Faithful and True Witness, the Head of God's creation, says these things:
270315 "I know your works, that you are neither cold nor hot. I wish you were cold or hot.
270316 So, because you are lukewarm, and neither hot nor cold, I will vomit you out of my mouth.
270317 Because you say, 'I am rich, and have gotten riches, and have need of nothing;' and don't know that you are the wretched one, miserable, poor, blind, and naked;
270318 I counsel you to buy from me gold refined by fire, that you may become rich; and white garments, that you may clothe yourself, and that the shame of your nakedness may not be revealed; and eye salve to anoint your eyes, that you may see.
270319 As many as I love, I reprove and chasten. Be zealous therefore, and repent.
270320 Behold, I stand at the door and knock. If anyone hears my voice and opens the door, then I will come in to him, and will dine with him, and he with me.
270321 He who overcomes, I will give to him to sit down with me on my throne, as I also overcame, and sat down with my Father on his throne.
270322 He who has an ear, let him hear what the Spirit says to the assemblies."
270401 After these things I looked and saw a door opened in heaven, and the first voice that I heard, like a trumpet speaking with me, was one saying, "Come up here, and I will show you the things which must happen after this."
270402 Immediately I was in the Spirit. Behold, there was a throne set in heaven, and one sitting on the throne
270403 that looked like a jasper stone and a sardius. There was a rainbow around the throne, like an emerald to look at.
270404 Around the throne were twenty-four thrones. On the thrones were twenty-four elders sitting, dressed in white garments, with crowns of gold on their heads.
270405 Out of the throne proceed lightnings, sounds, and thunders. There were seven lamps of fire burning before his throne, which are the seven Spirits of God.
270406 Before the throne was something like a sea of glass, similar to crystal. In the midst of the throne, and around the throne were four living creatures full of eyes before and behind.
270407 The first creature was like a lion, and the second creature like a calf, and the third creature had a face like a man, and the fourth was like a flying eagle.
270408 The four living creatures, each one of them having six wings, are full of eyes around and within. They have no rest day and night, saying, "Holy, holy, holy is the Lord God, the Almighty, who was and who is and who is to come!"
270409 When the living creatures give glory, honor, and thanks to him who sits on the throne, to him who lives forever and ever,
270410 the twenty-four elders fall down before him who sits on the throne, and worship him who lives forever and ever, and throw their crowns before the throne, saying,
270411 "Worthy are you, our Lord and God, the Holy One, to receive the glory, the honor, and the power, for you created all things, and because of your desire they existed, and were created!"
270501 I saw, in the right hand of him who sat on the throne, a book written inside and outside, sealed shut with seven seals.
270502 I saw a mighty angel proclaiming with a loud voice, "Who is worthy to open the book, and to break its seals?"
270503 No one in heaven above, or on the earth, or under the earth, was able to open the book, or to look in it.
270504 And I wept much, because no one was found worthy to open the book, or to look in it.
270505 One of the elders said to me, "Don't weep. Behold, the Lion who is of the tribe of Judah, the Root of David, has overcome; he who opens the book and its seven seals."
270506 I saw in the midst of the throne and of the four living creatures, and in the midst of the elders, a Lamb standing, as though it had been slain, having seven horns, and seven eyes, which are the seven Spirits of God, sent out into all the earth.
270507 Then he came, and he took it out of the right hand of him who sat on the throne.
270508 Now when he had taken the book, the four living creatures and the twenty-four elders fell down before the Lamb, each one having a harp, and golden bowls full of incense, which are the prayers of the saints.
270509 They sang a new song, saying, "You are worthy to take the book, and to open its seals: for you were killed, and bought us for God with your blood, out of every tribe, language, people, and nation,
270510 and made us kings and priests to our God, and we will reign on earth."
270511 I saw, and I heard something like a voice of many angels around the throne, the living creatures, and the elders; and the number of them was ten thousands of ten thousands, and thousands of thousands;
270512 saying with a loud voice, "Worthy is the Lamb who has been killed to receive the power, wealth, wisdom, strength, honor, glory, and blessing!"
270513 I heard every created thing which is in heaven, on the earth, under the earth, on the sea, and everything in them, saying, "To him who sits on the throne, and to the Lamb be the blessing, the honor, the glory, and the dominion, forever and ever! Amen!"
270514 The four living creatures said, "Amen!" The elders fell down and worshiped.
270601 I saw that the Lamb opened one of the seven seals, and I heard one of the four living creatures saying, as with a voice of thunder, "Come and see!"
270602 And behold, a white horse, and he who sat on it had a bow. A crown was given to him, and he came forth conquering, and to conquer.
270603 When he opened the second seal, I heard the second living creature saying, "Come!"
270604 Another came forth, a red horse. To him who sat on it was given power to take peace from the earth, and that they should kill one another. There was given to him a great sword.
270605 When he opened the third seal, I heard the third living creature saying, "Come and see!" And behold, a black horse, and he who sat on it had a balance in his hand.
270606 I heard a voice in the midst of the four living creatures saying, "A choenix of wheat for a denarius, and three choenix of barley for a denarius! Don't damage the oil and the wine!"
270607 When he opened the fourth seal, I heard the fourth living creature saying, "Come and see!"
270608 And behold, a pale horse, and he who sat on it, his name was Death. Hades followed with him. Authority over one fourth of the earth, to kill with the sword, with famine, with death, and by the wild animals of the earth was given to him.
270609 When he opened the fifth seal, I saw underneath the altar the souls of those who had been killed for the Word of God, and for the testimony of the Lamb which they had.
270610 They cried with a loud voice, saying, "How long, Master, the holy and true, until you judge and avenge our blood on those who dwell on the earth?"
270611 A long white robe was given to each of them. They were told that they should rest yet for a while, until their fellow servants and their brothers, who would also be killed even as they were, should complete their course.
270612 I saw when he opened the sixth seal, and there was a great earthquake. The sun became black as sackcloth made of hair, and the whole moon became as blood.
270613 The stars of the sky fell to the earth, like a fig tree dropping its unripe figs when it is shaken by a great wind.
270614 The sky was removed like a scroll when it is rolled up. Every mountain and island were moved out of their places.
270615 The kings of the earth, the princes, the commanding officers, the rich, the strong, and every slave and free person, hid themselves in the caves and in the rocks of the mountains.
270616 They told the mountains and the rocks, "Fall on us, and hide us from the face of him who sits on the throne, and from the wrath of the Lamb,
270617 for the great day of his wrath has come; and who is able to stand?"
270701 After this, I saw four angels standing at the four corners of the earth, holding the four winds of the earth, so that no wind would blow on the earth, or on the sea, or on any tree.
270702 I saw another angel ascend from the sunrise, having the seal of the living God. He cried with a loud voice to the four angels to whom it was given to harm the earth and the sea,
270703 saying, "Don't harm the earth, neither the sea, nor the trees, until we have sealed the bondservants of our God on their foreheads!"
270704 I heard the number of those who were sealed, one hundred forty-four thousand, sealed out of every tribe of the children of Israel:
270705 of the tribe of Judah were sealed twelve thousand, of the tribe of Reuben twelve thousand, of the tribe of Gad twelve thousand,
270706 of the tribe of Asher twelve thousand, of the tribe of Naphtali twelve thousand, of the tribe of Manasseh twelve thousand,
270707 of the tribe of Simeon twelve thousand, of the tribe of Levi twelve thousand, of the tribe of Issachar twelve thousand,
270708 of the tribe of Zebulun twelve thousand, of the tribe of Joseph twelve thousand, of the tribe of Benjamin were sealed twelve thousand.
270709 After these things I looked, and behold, a great multitude, which no man could number, out of every nation and of all tribes, peoples, and languages, standing before the throne and before the Lamb, dressed in white robes, with palm branches in their hands.
270710 They cried with a loud voice, saying, "Salvation be to our God, who sits on the throne, and to the Lamb!"
270711 All the angels were standing around the throne, the elders, and the four living creatures; and they fell on their faces before his throne, and worshiped God,
270712 saying, "Amen! Blessing, glory, wisdom, thanksgiving, honor, power, and might, be to our God forever and ever! Amen."
270713 One of the elders answered, saying to me, "These who are arrayed in white robes, who are they, and from where did they come?"
270714 I told him, "My lord, you know." He said to me, "These are those who came out of the great tribulation. They washed their robes, and made them white in the Lamb's blood.
270715 Therefore they are before the throne of God, they serve him day and night in his temple. He who sits on the throne will spread his tabernacle over them.
270716 They will never be hungry, neither thirsty any more; neither will the sun beat on them, nor any heat;
270717 for the Lamb who is in the midst of the throne shepherds them, and leads them to springs of waters of life. And God will wipe away every tear from their eyes."
270801 When he opened the seventh seal, there was silence in heaven for about half an hour.
270802 I saw the seven angels who stand before God, and seven trumpets were given to them.
270803 Another angel came and stood over the altar, having a golden censer. Much incense was given to him, that he should add it to the prayers of all the saints on the golden altar which was before the throne.
270804 The smoke of the incense, with the prayers of the saints, went up before God out of the angel's hand.
270805 The angel took the censer, and he filled it with the fire of the altar, and threw it on the earth. There followed thunders, sounds, lightnings, and an earthquake.
270806 The seven angels who had the seven trumpets prepared themselves to sound.
270807 The first sounded, and there followed hail and fire, mixed with blood, and they were thrown to the earth. One third of the earth was burnt up, and one third of the trees were burnt up, and all green grass was burnt up.
270808 The second angel sounded, and something like a great burning mountain was thrown into the sea. One third of the sea became blood,
270809 and one third of the living creatures which were in the sea died. One third of the ships were destroyed.
270810 The third angel sounded, and a great star fell from the sky, burning like a torch, and it fell on one third of the rivers, and on the springs of the waters.
270811 The name of the star is called "Wormwood." One third of the waters became wormwood. Many people died from the waters, because they were made bitter.
270812 The fourth angel sounded, and one third of the sun was struck, and one third of the moon, and one third of the stars; so that one third of them would be darkened, and the day wouldn't shine for one third of it, and the night in the same way.
270813 I saw, and I heard an eagle, flying in mid heaven, saying with a loud voice, "Woe! Woe! Woe for those who dwell on the earth, because of the other voices of the trumpets of the three angels, who are yet to sound!"
270901 The fifth angel sounded, and I saw a star from the sky which had fallen to the earth. The key to the pit of the abyss was given to him.
270902 He opened the pit of the abyss, and smoke went up out of the pit, like the smoke from a burning furnace. The sun and the air were darkened because of the smoke from the pit.
270903 Then out of the smoke came forth locusts on the earth, and power was given to them, as the scorpions of the earth have power.
270904 They were told that they should not hurt the grass of the earth, neither any green thing, neither any tree, but only those people who don't have God's seal on their foreheads.
270905 They were given power not to kill them, but to torment them for five months. Their torment was like the torment of a scorpion, when it strikes a person.
270906 In those days people will seek death, and will in no way find it. They will desire to die, and death will flee from them.
270907 The shapes of the locusts were like horses prepared for war. On their heads were something like golden crowns, and their faces were like people's faces.
270908 They had hair like women's hair, and their teeth were like those of lions.
270909 They had breastplates, like breastplates of iron. The sound of their wings was like the sound of chariots, or of many horses rushing to war.
270910 They have tails like those of scorpions, and stings. In their tails they have power to harm men for five months.
270911 They have over them as king the angel of the abyss. His name in Hebrew is "Abaddon," but in Greek, he has the name "Apollyon."
270912 The first woe is past. Behold, there are still two woes coming after this.
270913 The sixth angel sounded. I heard a voice from the horns of the golden altar which is before God,
270914 saying to the sixth angel who had one trumpet, "Free the four angels who are bound at the great river Euphrates!"
270915 The four angels were freed who had been prepared for that hour and day and month and year, so that they might kill one third of mankind.
270916 The number of the armies of the horsemen was two hundred million. I heard the number of them.
270917 Thus I saw the horses in the vision, and those who sat on them, having breastplates of fiery red, hyacinth blue, and sulfur yellow; and the heads of lions. Out of their mouths proceed fire, smoke, and sulfur.
270918 By these three plagues were one third of mankind killed: by the fire, the smoke, and the sulfur, which proceeded out of their mouths.
270919 For the power of the horses is in their mouths, and in their tails. For their tails are like serpents, and have heads, and with them they harm.
270920 The rest of mankind, who were not killed with these plagues, didn't repent of the works of their hands, that they wouldn't worship demons, and the idols of gold, and of silver, and of brass, and of stone, and of wood; which can neither see, nor hear, nor walk.
270921 They didn't repent of their murders, nor of their sorceries, nor of their sexual immorality, nor of their thefts.
271001 I saw a mighty angel coming down out of the sky, clothed with a cloud. A rainbow was on his head. His face was like the sun, and his feet like pillars of fire.
271002 He had in his hand a little open book. He set his right foot on the sea, and his left on the land.
271003 He cried with a loud voice, as a lion roars. When he cried, the seven thunders uttered their voices.
271004 When the seven thunders sounded, I was about to write; but I heard a voice from the sky saying, "Seal up the things which the seven thunders said, and don't write them."
271005 The angel who I saw standing on the sea and on the land lifted up his right hand to the sky,
271006 and swore by him who lives forever and ever, who created heaven and the things that are in it, the earth and the things that are in it, and the sea and the things that are in it, that there will no longer be delay,
271007 but in the days of the voice of the seventh angel, when he is about to sound, then the mystery of God is finished, as he declared to his servants, the prophets.
271008 The voice which I heard from heaven, again speaking with me, said, "Go, take the book which is open in the hand of the angel who stands on the sea and on the land."
271009 I went to the angel, telling him to give me the little book. He said to me, "Take it, and eat it up. It will make your stomach bitter, but in your mouth it will be as sweet as honey."
271010 I took the little book out of the angel's hand, and ate it up. It was as sweet as honey in my mouth. When I had eaten it, my stomach was made bitter.
271011 They told me, "You must prophesy again over many peoples, nations, languages, and kings."
271101 A reed like a rod was given to me. Someone said, "Rise, and measure God's temple, and the altar, and those who worship in it.
271102 Leave out the court which is outside of the temple, and don't measure it, for it has been given to the nations. They will tread the holy city under foot for forty-two months.
271103 I will give power to my two witnesses, and they will prophesy one thousand two hundred sixty days, clothed in sackcloth."
271104 These are the two olive trees and the two lampstands, standing before the Lord of the earth.
271105 If anyone desires to harm them, fire proceeds out of their mouth and devours their enemies. If anyone desires to harm them, he must be killed in this way.
271106 These have the power to shut up the sky, that it may not rain during the days of their prophecy. They have power over the waters, to turn them into blood, and to strike the earth with every plague, as often as they desire.
271107 When they have finished their testimony, the beast that comes up out of the abyss will make war with them, and overcome them, and kill them.
271108 Their dead bodies will be in the street of the great city, which spiritually is called Sodom and Egypt, where also their Lord was crucified.
271109 From among the peoples, tribes, languages, and nations people will look at their dead bodies for three and a half days, and will not allow their dead bodies to be laid in a tomb.
271110 Those who dwell on the earth rejoice over them, and they will be glad. They will give gifts to one another, because these two prophets tormented those who dwell on the earth.
271111 After the three and a half days, the breath of life from God entered into them, and they stood on their feet. Great fear fell on those who saw them.
271112 I heard a loud voice from heaven saying to them, "Come up here!" They went up into heaven in the cloud, and their enemies saw them.
271113 In that day there was a great earthquake, and a tenth of the city fell. Seven thousand people were killed in the earthquake, and the rest were terrified, and gave glory to the God of heaven.
271114 The second woe is past. Behold, the third woe comes quickly.
271115 The seventh angel sounded, and great voices in heaven followed, saying, "The kingdom of the world has become the Kingdom of our Lord, and of his Christ. He will reign forever and ever!"
271116 The twenty-four elders, who sit on their thrones before God's throne, fell on their faces and worshiped God,
271117 saying: "We give you thanks, Lord God, the Almighty, the one who is and who was; because you have taken your great power, and reigned.
271118 The nations were angry, and your wrath came, as did the time for the dead to be judged, and to give your bondservants the prophets, their reward, as well as to the saints, and those who fear your name, to the small and the great; and to destroy those who destroy the earth."
271119 God's temple that is in heaven was opened, and the ark of the Lord's covenant was seen in his temple. Lightnings, sounds, thunders, an earthquake, and great hail followed.
271201 A great sign was seen in heaven: a woman clothed with the sun, and the moon under her feet, and on her head a crown of twelve stars.
271202 She was with child. She cried out in pain, laboring to give birth.
271203 Another sign was seen in heaven. Behold, a great red dragon, having seven heads and ten horns, and on his heads seven crowns.
271204 His tail drew one third of the stars of the sky, and threw them to the earth. The dragon stood before the woman who was about to give birth, so that when she gave birth he might devour her child.
271205 She gave birth to a son, a male child, who is to rule all the nations with a rod of iron. Her child was caught up to God, and to his throne.
271206 The woman fled into the wilderness, where she has a place prepared by God, that there they may nourish her one thousand two hundred sixty days.
271207 There was war in the sky. Michael and his angels made war on the dragon. The dragon and his angels made war.
271208 They didn't prevail, neither was a place found for him any more in heaven.
271209 The great dragon was thrown down, the old serpent, he who is called the devil and Satan, the deceiver of the whole world. He was thrown down to the earth, and his angels were thrown down with him.
271210 I heard a loud voice in heaven, saying, "Now is come the salvation, the power, and the Kingdom of our God, and the authority of his Christ; for the accuser of our brothers has been thrown down, who accuses them before our God day and night.
271211 They overcame him because of the Lamb's blood, and because of the word of their testimony. They didn't love their life, even to death.
271212 Therefore rejoice, heavens, and you who dwell in them. Woe to the earth and to the sea, because the devil has gone down to you, having great wrath, knowing that he has but a short time."
271213 When the dragon saw that he was thrown down to the earth, he persecuted the woman who gave birth to the male child.
271214 Two wings of the great eagle were given to the woman, that she might fly into the wilderness to her place, so that she might be nourished for a time, and times, and half a time, from the face of the serpent.
271215 The serpent spewed water out of his mouth after the woman like a river, that he might cause her to be carried away by the stream.
271216 The earth helped the woman, and the earth opened its mouth and swallowed up the river which the dragon spewed out of his mouth.
271217 The dragon grew angry with the woman, and went away to make war with the rest of her seed, who keep God's commandments and hold Jesus' testimony.
271301 Then I stood on the sand of the sea. I saw a beast coming up out of the sea, having ten horns and seven heads. On his horns were ten crowns, and on his heads, blasphemous names.
271302 The beast which I saw was like a leopard, and his feet were like those of a bear, and his mouth like the mouth of a lion. The dragon gave him his power, his throne, and great authority.
271303 One of his heads looked like it had been wounded fatally. His fatal wound was healed, and the whole earth marveled at the beast.
271304 They worshiped the dragon, because he gave his authority to the beast, and they worshiped the beast, saying, "Who is like the beast? Who is able to make war with him?"
271305 A mouth speaking great things and blasphemy was given to him. Authority to make war for forty-two months was given to him.
271306 He opened his mouth for blasphemy against God, to blaspheme his name, and his dwelling, those who dwell in heaven.
271307 It was given to him to make war with the saints, and to overcome them. Authority over every tribe, people, language, and nation was given to him.
271308 All who dwell on the earth will worship him, everyone whose name has not been written from the foundation of the world in the book of life of the Lamb who has been killed.
271309 If anyone has an ear, let him hear.
271310 If anyone has captivity, he will go into captivity. If anyone is with the sword, he must be killed. Here is the endurance and the faith of the saints.
271311 I saw another beast coming up out of the earth. He had two horns like a lamb, and he spoke like a dragon.
271312 He exercises all the authority of the first beast in his presence. He makes the earth and those who dwell in it to worship the first beast, whose fatal wound was healed.
271313 He performs great signs, even making fire come down out of the sky to the earth in the sight of people.
271314 He deceives my own people who dwell on the earth because of the signs he was granted to do in front of the beast; saying to those who dwell on the earth, that they should make an image to the beast who had the sword wound and lived.
271315 It was given to him to give breath to it, to the image of the beast, that the image of the beast should both speak, and cause as many as wouldn't worship the image of the beast to be killed.
271316 He causes all, the small and the great, the rich and the poor, and the free and the slave, to be given marks on their right hands, or on their foreheads;
271317 and that no one would be able to buy or to sell, unless he has that mark, the name of the beast or the number of his name.
271318 Here is wisdom. He who has understanding, let him calculate the number of the beast, for it is the number of a man. His number is six hundred sixty-six.
271401 I saw, and behold, the Lamb standing on Mount Zion, and with him a number, one hundred forty-four thousand, having his name, and the name of his Father, written on their foreheads.
271402 I heard a sound from heaven, like the sound of many waters, and like the sound of a great thunder. The sound which I heard was like that of harpists playing on their harps.
271403 They sing a new song before the throne, and before the four living creatures and the elders. No one could learn the song except the one hundred forty-four thousand, those who had been redeemed out of the earth.
271404 These are those who were not defiled with women, for they are virgins. These are those who follow the Lamb wherever he goes. These were redeemed by Jesus from among men, the first fruits to God and to the Lamb.
271405 In their mouth was found no lie, for they are blameless.
271406 I saw an angel flying in mid heaven, having an eternal Good News to proclaim to those who dwell on the earth, and to every nation, tribe, language, and people.
271407 He said with a loud voice, "Fear the Lord, and give him glory; for the hour of his judgment has come. Worship him who made the heaven, the earth, the sea, and the springs of waters!"
271408 Another, a second angel, followed, saying, "Babylon the great has fallen, which has made all the nations to drink of the wine of the wrath of her sexual immorality."
271409 Another angel, a third, followed them, saying with a great voice, "If anyone worships the beast and his image, and receives a mark on his forehead, or on his hand,
271410 he also will drink of the wine of the wrath of God, which is prepared unmixed in the cup of his anger. He will be tormented with fire and sulfur in the presence of the holy angels, and in the presence of the Lamb.
