271411 The smoke of their torment goes up forever and ever. They have no rest day and night, those who worship the beast and his image, and whoever receives the mark of his name.
271412 Here is the patience of the saints, those who keep the commandments of God, and the faith of Jesus."
271413 I heard the voice from heaven saying, "Write, 'Blessed are the dead who die in the Lord from now on.'" "Yes," says the Spirit, "that they may rest from their labors; for their works follow with them."
271414 I looked, and behold, a white cloud; and on the cloud one sitting like a son of man, having on his head a golden crown, and in his hand a sharp sickle.
271415 Another angel came out from the temple, crying with a loud voice to him who sat on the cloud, "Send forth your sickle, and reap; for the hour to reap has come; for the harvest of the earth is ripe!"
271416 He who sat on the cloud thrust his sickle on the earth, and the earth was reaped.
271417 Another angel came out from the temple which is in heaven. He also had a sharp sickle.
271418 Another angel came out from the altar, he who has power over fire, and he called with a great voice to him who had the sharp sickle, saying, "Send forth your sharp sickle, and gather the clusters of the vine of the earth, for the earth's grapes are fully ripe!"
271419 The angel thrust his sickle into the earth, and gathered the vintage of the earth, and threw it into the great winepress of the wrath of God.
271420 The winepress was trodden outside of the city, and blood came out from the winepress, even to the bridles of the horses, as far as one thousand six hundred stadia.
271501 I saw another great and marvelous sign in the sky: seven angels having the seven last plagues, for in them God's wrath is finished.
271502 I saw something like a sea of glass mixed with fire, and those who overcame the beast, his image, and the number of his name, standing on the sea of glass, having harps of God.
271503 They sang the song of Moses, the servant of God, and the song of the Lamb, saying, "Great and marvelous are your works, Lord God, the Almighty! Righteous and true are your ways, you King of the nations.
271504 Who wouldn't fear you, Lord, and glorify your name? For you only are holy. For all the nations will come and worship before you. For your righteous acts have been revealed."
271505 After these things I looked, and the temple of the tabernacle of the testimony in heaven was opened.
271506 The seven angels who had the seven plagues came out, clothed with pure, bright linen, and wearing golden sashes around their breasts.
271507 One of the four living creatures gave to the seven angels seven golden bowls full of the wrath of God, who lives forever and ever.
271508 The temple was filled with smoke from the glory of God, and from his power. No one was able to enter into the temple, until the seven plagues of the seven angels would be finished.
271601 I heard a loud voice out of the temple, saying to the seven angels, "Go and pour out the seven bowls of the wrath of God on the earth!"
271602 The first went, and poured out his bowl into the earth, and it became a harmful and evil sore on the people who had the mark of the beast, and who worshiped his image.
271603 The second angel poured out his bowl into the sea, and it became blood as of a dead man. Every living thing in the sea died.
271604 The third poured out his bowl into the rivers and springs of water, and they became blood.
271605 I heard the angel of the waters saying, "You are righteous, who are and who were, you Holy One, because you have judged these things.
271606 For they poured out the blood of the saints and the prophets, and you have given them blood to drink. They deserve this."
271607 I heard the altar saying, "Yes, Lord God, the Almighty, true and righteous are your judgments."
271608 The fourth poured out his bowl on the sun, and it was given to him to scorch men with fire.
271609 People were scorched with great heat, and people blasphemed the name of God who has the power over these plagues. They didn't repent and give him glory.
271610 The fifth poured out his bowl on the throne of the beast, and his kingdom was darkened. They gnawed their tongues because of the pain,
271611 and they blasphemed the God of heaven because of their pains and their sores. They didn't repent of their works.
271612 The sixth poured out his bowl on the great river, the Euphrates. Its water was dried up, that the way might be made ready for the kings that come from the sunrise.
271613 I saw coming out of the mouth of the dragon, and out of the mouth of the beast, and out of the mouth of the false prophet, three unclean spirits, something like frogs;
271614 for they are spirits of demons, performing signs; which go forth to the kings of the whole inhabited earth, to gather them together for the war of that great day of God, the Almighty.
271615 "Behold, I come like a thief. Blessed is he who watches, and keeps his clothes, so that he doesn't walk naked, and they see his shame."
271616 He gathered them together into the place which is called in Hebrew, Megiddo.
271617 The seventh poured out his bowl into the air. A loud voice came forth out of the temple of heaven, from the throne, saying, "It is done!"
271618 There were lightnings, sounds, and thunders; and there was a great earthquake, such as was not since there were men on the earth, so great an earthquake, so mighty.
271619 The great city was divided into three parts, and the cities of the nations fell. Babylon the great was remembered in the sight of God, to give to her the cup of the wine of the fierceness of his wrath.
271620 Every island fled away, and the mountains were not found.
271621 Great hailstones, about the weight of a talent, came down out of the sky on people. People blasphemed God because of the plague of the hail, for this plague is exceedingly severe.
271701 One of the seven angels who had the seven bowls came and spoke with me, saying, "Come here. I will show you the judgment of the great prostitute who sits on many waters,
271702 with whom the kings of the earth committed sexual immorality, and those who dwell in the earth were made drunken with the wine of her sexual immorality."
271703 He carried me away in the Spirit into a wilderness. I saw a woman sitting on a scarlet-colored animal, full of blasphemous names, having seven heads and ten horns.
271704 The woman was dressed in purple and scarlet, and decked with gold and precious stones and pearls, having in her hand a golden cup full of abominations and the impurities of the sexual immorality of the earth.
271705 And on her forehead a name was written, "MYSTERY, BABYLON THE GREAT, THE MOTHER OF THE PROSTITUTES AND OF THE ABOMINATIONS OF THE EARTH."
271706 I saw the woman drunken with the blood of the saints, and with the blood of the martyrs of Jesus. When I saw her, I wondered with great amazement.
271707 The angel said to me, "Why do you wonder? I will tell you the mystery of the woman, and of the beast that carries her, which has the seven heads and the ten horns.
271708 The beast that you saw was, and is not; and is about to come up out of the abyss and to go into destruction. Those who dwell on the earth and whose names have not been written in the book of life from the foundation of the world will marvel when they see that the beast was, and is not, and shall be present.
271709 Here is the mind that has wisdom. The seven heads are seven mountains, on which the woman sits.
271710 They are seven kings. Five have fallen, the one is, the other has not yet come. When he comes, he must continue a little while.
271711 The beast that was, and is not, is himself also an eighth, and is of the seven; and he goes to destruction.
271712 The ten horns that you saw are ten kings who have received no kingdom as yet, but they receive authority as kings, with the beast, for one hour.
271713 These have one mind, and they give their power and authority to the beast.
271714 These will war against the Lamb, and the Lamb will overcome them, for he is Lord of lords, and King of kings. They also will overcome who are with him, called and chosen and faithful."
271715 He said to me, "The waters which you saw, where the prostitute sits, are peoples, multitudes, nations, and languages.
271716 The ten horns which you saw, and the beast, these will hate the prostitute, and will make her desolate, and will make her naked, and will eat her flesh, and will burn her utterly with fire.
271717 For God has put in their hearts to do what he has in mind, and to be of one mind, and to give their kingdom to the beast, until the words of God should be accomplished.
271718 The woman whom you saw is the great city, which reigns over the kings of the earth."
271801 After these things, I saw another angel coming down out of the sky, having great authority. The earth was illuminated with his glory.
271802 He cried with a mighty voice, saying, "Fallen, fallen is Babylon the great, and she has become a habitation of demons, a prison of every unclean spirit, and a prison of every unclean and hateful bird!
271803 For all the nations have drunk of the wine of the wrath of her sexual immorality, the kings of the earth committed sexual immorality with her, and the merchants of the earth grew rich from the abundance of her luxury."
271804 I heard another voice from heaven, saying, "Come out of her, my people, that you have no participation in her sins, and that you don't receive of her plagues,
271805 for her sins have reached to the sky, and God has remembered her iniquities.
271806 Return to her just as she returned, and repay her double as she did, and according to her works. In the cup which she mixed, mix to her double.
271807 However much she glorified herself, and grew wanton, so much give her of torment and mourning. For she says in her heart, 'I sit a queen, and am no widow, and will in no way see mourning.'
271808 Therefore in one day her plagues will come: death, mourning, and famine; and she will be utterly burned with fire; for the Lord God who has judged her is strong.
271809 The kings of the earth, who committed sexual immorality and lived wantonly with her, will weep and wail over her, when they look at the smoke of her burning,
271810 standing far away for the fear of her torment, saying, 'Woe, woe, the great city, Babylon, the strong city! For your judgment has come in one hour.'
271811 The merchants of the earth weep and mourn over her, for no one buys their merchandise any more;
271812 merchandise of gold, silver, precious stones, pearls, fine linen, purple, silk, scarlet, all expensive wood, every vessel of ivory, every vessel made of most precious wood, and of brass, and iron, and marble;
271813 and cinnamon, incense, perfume, frankincense, wine, olive oil, fine flour, wheat, sheep, horses, chariots, and people's bodies and souls.
271814 The fruits which your soul lusted after have been lost to you, and all things that were dainty and sumptuous have perished from you, and you will find them no more at all.
271815 The merchants of these things, who were made rich by her, will stand far away for the fear of her torment, weeping and mourning;
271816 saying, 'Woe, woe, the great city, she who was dressed in fine linen, purple, and scarlet, and decked with gold and precious stones and pearls!
271817 For in an hour such great riches are made desolate.' Every shipmaster, and everyone who sails anywhere, and mariners, and as many as gain their living by sea, stood far away,
271818 and cried out as they looked at the smoke of her burning, saying, 'What is like the great city?'
271819 They cast dust on their heads, and cried, weeping and mourning, saying, 'Woe, woe, the great city, in which all who had their ships in the sea were made rich by reason of her great wealth!' For in one hour is she made desolate.
271820 "Rejoice over her, O heaven, you saints, apostles, and prophets; for God has judged your judgment on her."
271821 A mighty angel took up a stone like a great millstone and cast it into the sea, saying, "Thus with violence will Babylon, the great city, be thrown down, and will be found no more at all.
271822 The voice of harpists, minstrels, flute players, and trumpeters will be heard no more at all in you. No craftsman, of whatever craft, will be found any more at all in you. The sound of a mill will be heard no more at all in you.
271823 The light of a lamp will shine no more at all in you. The voice of the bridegroom and of the bride will be heard no more at all in you; for your merchants were the princes of the earth; for with your sorcery all the nations were deceived.
271824 In her was found the blood of prophets and of saints, and of all who have been slain on the earth."
271901 After these things I heard something like a loud voice of a great multitude in heaven, saying, "Hallelujah! Salvation, power, and glory belong to our God:
271902 for true and righteous are his judgments. For he has judged the great prostitute, who corrupted the earth with her sexual immorality, and he has avenged the blood of his servants at her hand."
271903 A second said, "Hallelujah! Her smoke goes up forever and ever."
271904 The twenty-four elders and the four living creatures fell down and worshiped God who sits on the throne, saying, "Amen! Hallelujah!"
271905 A voice came forth from the throne, saying, "Give praise to our God, all you his servants, you who fear him, the small and the great!"
271906 I heard something like the voice of a great multitude, and like the voice of many waters, and like the voice of mighty thunders, saying, "Hallelujah! For the Lord our God, the Almighty, reigns!
271907 Let us rejoice and be exceedingly glad, and let us give the glory to him. For the marriage of the Lamb has come, and his wife has made herself ready."
271908 It was given to her that she would array herself in bright, pure, fine linen: for the fine linen is the righteous acts of the saints.
271909 He said to me, "Write, 'Blessed are those who are invited to the marriage supper of the Lamb.'" He said to me, "These are true words of God."
271910 I fell down before his feet to worship him. He said to me, "Look! Don't do it! I am a fellow bondservant with you and with your brothers who hold the testimony of Jesus. Worship God, for the testimony of Jesus is the Spirit of Prophecy."
271911 I saw the heaven opened, and behold, a white horse, and he who sat on it is called Faithful and True. In righteousness he judges and makes war.
271912 His eyes are a flame of fire, and on his head are many crowns. He has names written and a name written which no one knows but he himself.
271913 He is clothed in a garment sprinkled with blood. His name is called "The Word of God."
271914 The armies which are in heaven followed him on white horses, clothed in white, pure, fine linen.
271915 Out of his mouth proceeds a sharp, double-edged sword, that with it he should strike the nations. He will rule them with an iron rod. He treads the winepress of the fierceness of the wrath of God, the Almighty.
271916 He has on his garment and on his thigh a name written, "KING OF KINGS, AND LORD OF LORDS."
271917 I saw an angel standing in the sun. He cried with a loud voice, saying to all the birds that fly in the sky, "Come! Be gathered together to the great supper of God,
271918 that you may eat the flesh of kings, the flesh of captains, the flesh of mighty men, and the flesh of horses and of those who sit on them, and the flesh of all men, both free and slave, and small and great."
271919 I saw the beast, and the kings of the earth, and their armies, gathered together to make war against him who sat on the horse, and against his army.
271920 The beast was taken, and with him the false prophet who worked the signs in his sight, with which he deceived those who had received the mark of the beast and those who worshiped his image. These two were thrown alive into the lake of fire that burns with sulfur.
271921 The rest were killed with the sword of him who sat on the horse, the sword which came forth out of his mouth. All the birds were filled with their flesh.
272001 I saw an angel coming down out of heaven, having the key of the abyss and a great chain in his hand.
272002 He seized the dragon, the old serpent, which is the devil and Satan, who deceives the whole inhabited earth, and bound him for a thousand years,
272003 and cast him into the abyss, and shut it, and sealed it over him, that he should deceive the nations no more, until the thousand years were finished. After this, he must be freed for a short time.
272004 I saw thrones, and they sat on them, and judgment was given to them. I saw the souls of those who had been beheaded for the testimony of Jesus, and for the word of God, and such as didn't worship the beast nor his image, and didn't receive the mark on their forehead and on their hand. They lived, and reigned with Christ for a thousand years.
272005 The rest of the dead didn't live until the thousand years were finished. This is the first resurrection.
272006 Blessed and holy is he who has part in the first resurrection. Over these, the second death has no power, but they will be priests of God and of Christ, and will reign with him one thousand years.
272007 And after the thousand years, Satan will be released from his prison,
272008 and he will come out to deceive the nations which are in the four corners of the earth, Gog and Magog, to gather them together to the war; the number of whom is as the sand of the sea.
272009 They went up over the breadth of the earth, and surrounded the camp of the saints, and the beloved city. Fire came down out of heaven from God, and devoured them.
272010 The devil who deceived them was thrown into the lake of fire and sulfur, where the beast and the false prophet are also. They will be tormented day and night forever and ever.
272011 I saw a great white throne, and him who sat on it, from whose face the earth and the heaven fled away. There was found no place for them.
272012 I saw the dead, the great and the small, standing before the throne, and they opened books. Another book was opened, which is the book of life. The dead were judged out of the things which were written in the books, according to their works.
272013 The sea gave up the dead who were in it. Death and Hades gave up the dead who were in them. They were judged, each one according to his works.
272014 Death and Hades were thrown into the lake of fire. This is the second death, the lake of fire.
272015 If anyone was not found written in the book of life, he was cast into the lake of fire.
272101 I saw a new heaven and a new earth: for the first heaven and the first earth have passed away, and the sea is no more.
272102 I saw the holy city, New Jerusalem, coming down out of heaven from God, made ready like a bride adorned for her husband.
272103 I heard a loud voice out of heaven saying, "Behold, God's dwelling is with people, and he will dwell with them, and they will be his people, and God himself will be with them as their God.
272104 He will wipe away from them every tear from their eyes. Death will be no more; neither will there be mourning, nor crying, nor pain, any more. The first things have passed away."
272105 He who sits on the throne said, "Behold, I am making all things new." He said, "Write, for these words of God are faithful and true."
272106 He said to me, "It is done! I am the Alpha and the Omega, the Beginning and the End. I will give freely to him who is thirsty from the spring of the water of life.
272107 He who overcomes, I will give him these things. I will be his God, and he will be my son.
272108 But for the cowardly, unbelieving, sinners, abominable, murderers, sexually immoral, sorcerers, idolaters, and all liars, their part is in the lake that burns with fire and sulfur, which is the second death."
272109 One of the seven angels who had the seven bowls, who were loaded with the seven last plagues came, and he spoke with me, saying, "Come here. I will show you the wife, the Lamb's bride."
272110 He carried me away in the Spirit to a great and high mountain, and showed me the holy city, Jerusalem, coming down out of heaven from God,
272111 having the glory of God. Her light was like a most precious stone, as if it was a jasper stone, clear as crystal;
272112 having a great and high wall; having twelve gates, and at the gates twelve angels; and names written on them, which are the names of the twelve tribes of the children of Israel.
272113 On the east were three gates; and on the north three gates; and on the south three gates; and on the west three gates.
272114 The wall of the city had twelve foundations, and on them twelve names of the twelve Apostles of the Lamb.
272115 He who spoke with me had for a measure, a golden reed, to measure the city, its gates, and its walls.
272116 The city lies foursquare, and its length is as great as its breadth. He measured the city with the reed, Twelve thousand twelve stadia. Its length, breadth, and height are equal.
272117 Its wall is one hundred forty-four cubits, by the measure of a man, that is, of an angel.
272118 The construction of its wall was jasper. The city was pure gold, like pure glass.
272119 The foundations of the city's wall were adorned with all kinds of precious stones. The first foundation was jasper; the second, sapphire; the third, chalcedony; the fourth, emerald;
272120 the fifth, sardonyx; the sixth, sardius; the seventh, chrysolite; the eighth, beryl; the ninth, topaz; the tenth, chrysoprasus; the eleventh, jacinth; and the twelfth, amethyst.
272121 The twelve gates were twelve pearls. Each one of the gates was made of one pearl. The street of the city was pure gold, like transparent glass.
272122 I saw no temple in it, for the Lord God, the Almighty, and the Lamb, are its temple.
272123 The city has no need for the sun, neither of the moon, to shine, for the very glory of God illuminated it, and its lamp is the Lamb.
272124 The nations will walk in its light. The kings of the earth bring the glory and honor of the nations into it.
272125 Its gates will in no way be shut by day (for there will be no night there),
272126 and they shall bring the glory and the honor of the nations into it so that they may enter.
272127 There will in no way enter into it anything profane, or one who causes an abomination or a lie, but only those who are written in the Lamb's book of life.
272201 He showed me a river of water of life, clear as crystal, proceeding out of the throne of God and of the Lamb,
272202 in the middle of its street. On this side of the river and on that was the tree of life, bearing twelve kinds of fruits, yielding its fruit every month. The leaves of the tree were for the healing of the nations.
272203 There will be no curse any more. The throne of God and of the Lamb will be in it, and his servants serve him.
272204 They will see his face, and his name will be on their foreheads.
272205 There will be no night, and they need no lamp light; for the Lord God will illuminate them. They will reign forever and ever.
272206 He said to me, "These words are faithful and true. The Lord God of the spirits of the prophets sent his angel to show to his bondservants the things which must happen soon."
272207 "Behold, I come quickly. Blessed is he who keeps the words of the prophecy of this book."
272208 Now I, John, am the one who heard and saw these things. When I heard and saw, I fell down to worship before the feet of the angel who had shown me these things.
272209 He said to me, "See you don't do it! I am a fellow bondservant with you and with your brothers, the prophets, and with those who keep the words of this book. Worship God."
272210 He said to me, "Don't seal up the words of the prophecy of this book, for the time is at hand.
272211 He who acts unjustly, let him act unjustly still. He who is filthy, let him be filthy still. He who is righteous, let him do righteousness still. He who is holy, let him be holy still."
272212 "Behold, I come quickly. My reward is with me, to repay to each man according to his work.
272213 I am the Alpha and the Omega, the First and the Last, the Beginning and the End.
272214 Blessed are those who do his commandments, that they may have the right to the tree of life, and may enter in by the gates into the city.
272215 Outside are the dogs, the sorcerers, the sexually immoral, the murderers, the idolaters, and everyone who loves and practices falsehood.
272216 I, Jesus, have sent my angel to testify these things to you for the assemblies. I am the root and the offspring of David; the Bright and Morning Star."
272217 The Spirit and the bride say, "Come!" He who hears, let him say, "Come!" He who is thirsty, let him come. He who desires, let him take the water of life freely.
272218 I testify to everyone who hears the words of the prophecy of this book, if anyone adds to them, may God add to him the plagues which are written in this book.
272219 If anyone takes away from the words of the book of this prophecy, may God take away his part from the tree of life, and out of the holy city, which are written in this book.
272220 He who testifies these things says, "Yes, I come quickly." Amen! Yes, come, Lord Jesus.
272221 The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ be with all the saints. Amen.
